MAT 1:1 Enna ewela azaa beting be Yeso Kiristi, kena ka Daoda, kena ka Ibraheng.
MAT 1:2 Ibraheng ate a Ishaku, Ishaku ate a Yakubu, a Yakubu ate a Yahuda kaa arone awai alome.
MAT 1:3 Yahuda ate a Perez kaa Zera andaaka iini onea waye Tamar, Perez ate a Hezron, a Hezron ate a Aram.
MAT 1:4 Aram ate a Aminadab, Aminadab ate a Nashon, aa Nashon ate a Salmon.
MAT 1:5 Salmon ate a Bowaza ka iini wai waye Rahab. Bowaza ate a Obed ka iini wai waye Rut, Obed ate a Yese,
MAT 1:6 a Yese ate a Ogomo Daoda. Daoda ate a Suleimanu ka iini wai waye Batsheba, ondaye Uriya o samba.
MAT 1:7 Suleimanu ate a Rehobowam, Rehobowam ate a Abija, Abija ate a Asa,
MAT 1:8 Asa ate a Yehoshapat, Yehoshapat ate a Yehoram, Yehoram ate a Uziya,
MAT 1:9 Uziya ate a Yotam, Yotam ate a Ahaz, Ahaz ate a Hezekiya,
MAT 1:10 Hezekiya ate a Manase, Manase ate a Amon, Amon ate a Yosiya,
MAT 1:11 aa Yosiya ate a Yekoniya ka arone awai, a were aka a bese maYahuda a ale a lezara a Babila.
MAT 1:12 Malo besa one a lezara a Babila, Yekoniya ate a Sheyaltiyel, Sheyaltiyel ate a Zerubabel,
MAT 1:13 Zerubabel ate a Abihud, Abihud ate a Eliyakim, Eliyakim ate a Azor,
MAT 1:14 Azor ate a Zadok, Zadok ate a Akim, Akim ate a Aliyud,
MAT 1:15 Aliyud ate a Eleyazar, Eleyazar ate a Mattan, Mattan ate a Yakubu,
MAT 1:16 aa Yakubu ate a Yusupu ondaleme Mariya, Mariya kamea ka ngmeng Yeso ka a beya kai na Kiristi.
MAT 1:17 Obena pate sepeza a era Ibraheng a alea Daoda, sepeza betuurua ka she naaze. O era Daoda a alea awere amea a bese maYahuda a alea lezara a Babila, sepeza betuurua ka she naaze, o era were lezara a Babila kangza a ale o ngmenga Kiristi, sepeza betuurua ka she naaze.
MAT 1:18 Nannaa ongmenga o Yeso Kiristi waze. Awere aka Yusupu waya caasa Mariya kamea ka ngmeng Yeso, zongka wa ana kai, na manaa ka ana etumǝ a surǝ a Obere Ashili.
MAT 1:19 Yusupu ondasau kai waye ka boome ba Ashili na wata yeme o kare okai ezǝng a nyimi aromone, nawa eze madoola ma baya kai a suk.
MAT 1:20 Nangka waya madoola ma nyimi, na otoma Ashili o dera lepung o Ateokora deya awai atolau. Awa bena, “Yusupu kena ka Daoda, tana okone boome bo ana Mariya ka ka itǝ ondaye one, obena etumǝ ka ka ana, e surea Obere Ashilia.
MAT 1:21 Kayo ngmenga kena ka lome, oyo nya kai leze na Yeso, o bena kayo boza aromo aza madinǝ mane.”
MAT 1:22 A eze pate nyimia adorana angmǝ Ateokora pene ka Ondo beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili Ishaya beke.
MAT 1:23 “Laka! Kagala yo ya etumǝ, ka ka ngmeng kena kalome, ka ayo nya kai leze na Emanuwel, o wore obena Ashili ya legwa ka ro.”
MAT 1:24 Nangka Yusupu wa ere atolau, nawa tare epaaka otoma Ashili o dera lepung me wa ote wai na waye, aa wa ana Mariya naka itǝ ondaye wai.
MAT 1:25 Pate ka nyimi, wata wa more ka kai ne, se malo ngmenga kena ka kai. Nawa nya kena kame leze na Yeso.
MAT 2:1 Malo ngmenga Yeso a Baitalami o makeke ma Yahudiya, awere togomo te Hiridus ogomo Ogong, ana orosa ne surea adizi nane deya a Urushalima ane pirkǝ na,
MAT 2:2 “Ondooka a ngmeng, ogomo ma Yahuda ya babaa? Te laka bewerewere be wai a dizi na te deya kate eze kai makili ma Ashili.”
MAT 2:3 Nangka Ogomo Hiridus wa kone nyimi nawa kone oburǝ ka apate aromo a Urushalima.
MAT 2:4 Nawa kurki pate andaamoole magame ma Ashili ka ana obaala angmǝ aka Ashili a nya Mosa, awa pirkǝ ne na, a ruwǝme abena aya ngmenga Kiristi?
MAT 2:5 Nane kabare wai na, “Apeng Betalami a makeke ma Yahudiya,” Ane kang bena, “Nyimia ondo obeya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili wa wele,
MAT 2:6 “‘Bo Betalami o makeke ma Yahudiya ota baate ne a nyimi makeke ma togomo ma Yahudiya, ka ogomo yo surǝa nyimi au ka waya eza togomo azaa aromo ang maIsrela.’”’
MAT 2:7 Na Hiridus rare ana orosa name asuk adorana wa rose awere aka bewerewere beme be suri.
MAT 2:8 Nawa tong ne a Betalami na, “Ale na ka esoole kena kame a dede. Eedate ka ecǝ kai, deyana ka ebeleng, adorana mima ang ale kang eze makili ma Ashili a begeshe be kai.”
MAT 2:9 Malooka ne mara okona angmǝ ogomo, nane lya izi ka teweno tene, a bewerewere beeka be surǝ ane obora kale ane ba izi a ale araaka kena kame zane.
MAT 2:10 Nangka ne laka bewerewere beme, nane pene ka okona oleba maleu.
MAT 2:11 Ko lyǝ a kwilǝ me ane laka kena kame ka iini kai Mariya, nane girwǝ aa ne eze kai makili ma Ashili. Zaa nyimi nane pǝri majeketa ma emate mane ane nya kai magogoro, mazenare, madangku ma lubban kaa ma omur.
MAT 2:12 Aza obena Obere Ashili wa windi ne toto a nyimi tolau na tana ne kuri ara Hiridus ne, nane tare orona yende a kurǝ a makeke mane.
MAT 2:13 Malooka ana orosa me ne ale, otoma Ashili o dera lepung wa suri a Yusupu a tolau. Awa bekaana, “Era o ana kena kame ka iini kai o alea wogo a Masar. Oo cikǝ a saname seena ba kone eyapa mi, aza obena Hiridus ya gera kena kame kawa wong kai.”
MAT 2:14 Na Yusupu ere a lelyaare leme, nawa ana kena kame ka iini kai a alea Masar,
MAT 2:15 arakanamea ne cikǝ ne a ale ogwǝ o Hiridus. Nyimi apanza angmǝ Ashili ka a beke o ngmǝ otoma ai o lepung na, “Ma rare kena kang ka ka suri a Masar.”
MAT 2:16 Nangka Hiridus wa laka obena ana orosa ne kala wai a izi, na o nyong caro wai maleu. Nawa ote na a wongze pate ayana a batebate alome ka neya Betalami ka oringǝri o ai, aa deya senai se leere aa jǝpi, a akap nangka ne kone ara ana orosa name.
MAT 2:17 Awere namea angmǝ Ashili ka Irimiya beke a pena na,
MAT 2:18 “A kona lengmelo a Rama, lengmelo le okona oburǝ ka oruuzi a jǝng, Rahila ya ruuzi azaa ayana kai aka nyana kona okoo ogwǝ, aza obena a wongza ne.”
MAT 2:19 Malooka Hiridus wa gbwi, na otoma Ashili o dera lepung deya a Yusupu a nyimi tolau a Masar
MAT 2:20 awa bekaana, “Era, ka o ana kena ka iini kai o ale a makeke ma Isrela, andaaka neya yeme o wongnga kena kame ne gbwizǝ.”
MAT 2:21 Nawa ere, aa wa ana kena kame ka iini kai aa wa ale a makeke ma Isrela.
MAT 2:22 Nangka wa kone obena oyana o Hiridus, Arkilayus wa zala togomo a bengmǝ ba ate wai, nawa kone boome bo ale a saname. Azaa obena a windi wai teto a nyimi tolau, nawa dare awa ale a makeke ma Galili,
MAT 2:23 Wa ale nawa cikǝ a kapeng ka yende ka a rareze kai na Nazarat. Adorana apanza angmǝ Ashili ka ana obeya a ngmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili ne beke, “Ayo rara kai karomo ka Nazarat.”
MAT 3:1 A nyimi tomore tonname a Yohana o batisma wa suri awa ya zoola a nyimi wake o makeke ma Yahudiya,
MAT 3:2 aa wa beyana, “Kurǝ na Ashili, obena togomo te shili te amara.”
MAT 3:3 Ondoonaa Ishaya ondo beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili wa beke angmǝ azaa wai na: “Lengmelo ya rara owake ale beya na, ‘Babara Ateokora orona, babara na marona ma wai.’ ”
MAT 3:4 A soo madibi ma Yohana ka sezǝru se orongkoomea, awa tera o tinǝ owai ka lejǝng le ongma. A epaolya wai eya ekangdang ka mato ma esheng.
MAT 3:5 Na aromo a Urushalima, kaa a makeke ma Yahudiya a pate, kaa a pate ana makeke ma Obeno Urdung ne deese ara a kai,
MAT 3:6 ane beeze madinǝ mane, aa wa ezene obatisma Obeno Urdung.
MAT 3:7 Pate ka nyimi nangka Yohana wa laka maParisa ka maSadukiya araaka waya eza aromo obatisma, nawa bekaa ne na, “Ying okurkǝnǝng ewa eburu! Mana wa zoola aying na esong o gǝǝzǝ o Ashili ka waya deya?
MAT 3:8 Ezana epaaka eyo ale akap ka ewore obena e kurǝ Ashili aying.
MAT 3:9 Kangza tane ole begeshe na, ‘Ibraheng waya ate aro ne.’ Ang bele ying na, Ashili aye ka obare o sǝǝrǝ Ibraheng ayana a nyimi a caleena.
MAT 3:10 A samba o eke betemo aa madǝrǝ ma o mati, kangza pate uti ka wata ngmengza ayana a rerene, ayo genda wai ka tare a nyimi ola.
MAT 3:11 “Mi ang ezeze ying o batisma ka manyia o wore o kurǝ a Ashili aying. Malo ong ondo ya deya kawa kalang o bare, tekakau te wai ma era anta bare ang monte ne. Wayo eza ying o batisma ka Obere Ashili ka ola.
MAT 3:12 Waya onta upkwi owai a taara, aa wa keleke epaolya wai, aa wa kare o eyo me a nyimi lebengga, aa wa ese masuni mame ka ola ka wata lambuzu ne.”
MAT 3:13 A were name na Yeso deya ka suri a Galili a ale a Urdung ara Yohana adorana wa eze kai o batisma.
MAT 3:14 Na Yohana yeme o nara kai, awa bekaana, “Mi ang gwara obekaana bo oyeng o batisma, eyaaka bo ba deya ara ang?”
MAT 3:15 Na Yeso kabare wai na, “Baya wa itǝ nyimi nanname, aza obena nyimi a kala orera ka te panza epa e sangsang eeka Ashili ya yeme me.” Na Yohana kabare, aa wa ye kai o batisma.
MAT 3:16 Malo o eza Yeso o batisma, ka osurǝ kai a nyimi manyi naname, a saseya na zaa shili banggalanu, aka laka Obere o Ashili a jǝpi na kagoma, aka jǝpi ukpwei kai.
MAT 3:17 Na kone lengmelo a surǝ zaa shili na, “Kannaa kena kang, kamea ang yeme, kamea ang kone oleba kai maleu.”
MAT 4:1 Na Obere Ashili tare kaa Yeso a ale owake ka ogomo o bere o buru kedeya kai.
MAT 4:2 Aka meke ongmǝ o tomore tuuru naaze, lelyaare ka letereme, na ekomo meke kai.
MAT 4:3 Na ogomo obere o buru deya kai awa bekaana, “Boa baaya Kena ka Ashili, ote lecale leena ka le itǝ oborode.”
MAT 4:4 Na Yeso kabare na, “Angmǝ Ashili a bekaana, “Epaolya belle ta ongtaza oromo ne, seena ka koonang angmǝ ka susi ongmǝ Ashili.”
MAT 4:5 Na ogomo o bere oburu, ale ka kai a Urushalima apeng a odera madinǝ, nawa zalara kai araa o kala bezaati a akwilǝ Ashili.
MAT 4:6 Na wa bena, “Bo kena ka Ashili kaaza, cangko ka otaru a deze, obena a wele na, ‘Wayo ote atoma wai a kazo o, kane woboo ka taara tene nangka oto jukǝ tobona to ocale ne.”
MAT 4:7 Na Yeso kabare wai na, “A wele na, ‘Tana okedeya Ateokora Ashili au ne.’ ”
MAT 4:8 Kangza na ogomo obere oburu ale ka kai oyara o zaati awa wore kai pate togomo te lerambo leena ka o gongha te.
MAT 4:9 Awa kang bena, “Pate tenna eyang nyau, ba girwǝ a begeshe beng o ezeng makili ma Ashili.”
MAT 4:10 Na Yeso bekaa wai na, “Era arakaana, Shetan! A wele na, ‘Eza Ashili Ateokora au makili ma ai, kangza aiya belle oyo saba.’ ”
MAT 4:11 Na ogomo obere o buru ale awa baya kai, na atoma Ashili o dera lepung de nane kangkama kai.
MAT 4:12 Nangka Yeso ka kone obena a meke Yohana na apate akwilǝ andaleme, naka ere naka ale a Galili.
MAT 4:13 Ko baya Nazarat, naka ale a Kaparnahum ka ocikǝ, apeng amea aya bengmǝ bo beno, a bekazo be makeke ma Zebulung ka Naptali,
MAT 4:14 adorana a panza epaaka ondo obeya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili Ishaya wa beke,
MAT 4:15 “A makeke ma Zebulung ka ma Naptali, orona o alea obeno ogong a alea bekazo be obeno Urdung, a makeke ma Galili araaka a worme acake cikǝ ne,
MAT 4:16 aromo kane cikǝ amaring, ne laka masanto ma gong, ana ocikǝ makeke ma o ululu o gbwǝ kangza, masanto ma tara ane.”
MAT 4:17 O era were name, na Yeso bore ozoola aka beyaana, “Kurǝ na Ashili aza obena togomo te shili te amara.”
MAT 4:18 Yeso kaya yenga edǝki o beno gong o Galili naname, naka laka arone a leere, Siman ka a rare wai na Biturusu ka orone owai Andarawus. Neya tara majara ma o meese ekwala obeno, obena ogole one o meese ekwala waze.
MAT 4:19 Na Yeso bekaane na, “Deyana ka etareng, eyang ote ying ka e itǝ ana o deesa ka aromo a mi.”
MAT 4:20 A saseya nane baya majara mane aa ne tare kai.
MAT 4:21 Ko lya izi a baate, naka laka arone leere kangza, Yakubu kena ka Zabadi, ka orone kai Yohana. Neya nyimi o onggo o manyi ka ate ane Zabadi, aneya babara majara mane ma o meese ekwala. Na Yeso rare ne.
MAT 4:22 A saseya nane baya o onggo o manyi mame ka ate ane, aa ne tare kai.
MAT 4:23 Yeso ka ringgari pate makeke ma Galili, aka baale a nyimi odandaro o gwarzanang maYahuda, aka zoole aa ne aza angmǝ a lebo a togomo te Ashili. Kangza aaka womza pate makono ka odera o kona zake ka aromo ya zitǝ ka mai.
MAT 4:24 Na orooka azaa kai ale a kurǝwǝ a nyimi makeke ma Suriya pate. Na aromo casa kai pate andaaka neya kono ka andaaka neya zitǝ ka kombela makono, ka ana o kona o poba a jǝng, andaaka obere o buru wa taba ne, ana letaranggi, andaaka apung ane aa gbwǝ a sara yende, pate naka womza ne.
MAT 4:25 Na aromo a cake ne tare kai, kane suri a Galili, ka ana o surǝ a Dekapolis, ka Urushalima, ka makeke ma Yahudiya, a ale cakate obeno Urdung.
MAT 5:1 Nangka Yeso ka laka aromo ane kurkǝnǝng, naka zale oyara aa ka cikǝ a saname. Na atoma kai deya kai,
MAT 5:2 aka bore o baala one na.
MAT 5:3 “Ana okona olebaa aromo aaka ne rose o sawa one a nyimi o tare Ashili, aza o bena togomo te shili taate nea te.
MAT 5:4 Ana okona oleba ana o caro anyong, ayo nata ne anyong.
MAT 5:5 Ana okona olebaa ana o nata ukpwei, lerambo leena yo itǝ lalene.
MAT 5:6 Ana okona olebaa andaaka neya kona ekomo ka lewe le cikǝ o sangsang, obena neyo tiyǝ.
MAT 5:7 Ana okona olebaa andaaka ne kone egonegone, ayo wore ne egonegone.
MAT 5:8 Ana okona olebaa andaaka neya sangsang a nyimia nyong, obena neyo laka Ashili.
MAT 5:9 Ana okona olebaa andaaka ne gere o cikǝ o cammo, obena ayo rara ne na ayana Ashili.
MAT 5:10 Ana okona olebaa andaaka a nyana ne azaa be sangsang bene, obena togomo te shili taa tene te.
MAT 5:11 Ana okona olebaa ying awere aka aromo ne eske ying, ane nyalang ka ying ane kang beya kombela rendaza ma buru aza oying, obena ying e tareng.
MAT 5:12 Konana oleba e zante ajǝng, o bena bengmǝ bee ying yo gongha aa cak azaa shili, nyimia aromome ne gǝǝzǝ ana obeya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili kane kaana ying.”
MAT 5:13 Yingnga ogalu makeke maana. A ogalu wa arnang ka olento owai, eya ayo ya ka wa kang olento? Wa itǝ wata kang ya ka edang ne, soona a oke wai a itǝzǝ ne.
MAT 5:14 Yingnga masanto ma lerambo. Apeng aka a sowa ai azaa ka zalo, a era ta baasa ne.
MAT 5:15 Nyimi a aromo ne era neta diki beru be masanto aa ne pate be ka oso ne. Seena eke be ara azaati o eese be, nangka beyo nya pate aromo akwilǝ me masanto.
MAT 5:16 Nyimi a kangza bayana ee itǝ ana masanto a aromo, adorana nee laka teweno teying te rere ka eya ezame, aa ne sabe Ate aying ooka waya nyimi azaa shili.
MAT 5:17 Tane laka na ma deya kang dinggi makili ma Mosa ka ewela ana obeya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili. Anta ma deya kang dinggi ne soona ang panza mai.
MAT 5:18 Eyang dongdong bele oying, azaa shili ka makeke maana yo maro, otengke o baate ewela makili ma Mosa wato maro ne, seeka a panza ekeeya apat.
MAT 5:19 A zaa nyimi pate ondooka wa cakate o yende o kala a bebaate a nyimi makili ma Ashili maana, aa wa baale ana ondo na neye nyimi, ayo beka ondo me na wa kala be baate a nyimia togomo te o zaa shili. Ondooka wa tare mai kangza aa wa baale ana ondo o tare o mai, ayo rara wai na ondo ogong a togomo te shili.
MAT 5:20 Eyang baalo ying eta kala ana obaala angmǝ ka Ashili anya Mosa ka maParisa aa eza epa e sangsang ne, eto lyǝ a togomo te ozaa shili ne.
MAT 5:21 “E kone obena a beka aromo ko rabo na, ‘Tano wong ondo ne, pate ondooka wa wongngha ondo, ayo gǝǝzǝ wai.’
MAT 5:22 Mi eyang bele oying, ondooka wa munggi ka arone wai, ayo gǝǝzǝ wai. Ondooka wa rare arone wai na, eta ka edang ne, ayo ale ka wai ara o cora angmǝ. Komana kangza wa rare arone wai na, eta ka edang ne, wa itǝ kap ka akwilǝ ola.
MAT 5:23 “Nyimia kangza, baya nya Ashili eyapa a nyimi akwilǝ ai ara o esaza Ashili mapapa ma owaze, o ringtǝ o bena arone au neye ka bo a lenyong,
MAT 5:24 baya epaaka oya nya Ashili a ting ara o esaza Ashili mapapa mo waze. Bora ka o ale ka o babare kane, o ama o de ka onya Ashili epaaka baaya nyame.
MAT 5:25 Ondo wa ale ka bo ara o cora angmǝ, yangkanna a saseya ka ebabare ka wai e tata o orona o ale zongka e dukǝ. Bata ya nyimi ne, wayo gwaarau ka ondoo cora angmǝ, aa ondoo cora angmǝ kangza wayo gwaarau ka ana o tesa geza ka a pateo a akwilǝ andaleme.
MAT 5:26 Ang dongdong bele o epeng, zongka o sǝǝrǝu arakaname, seena ba are pate emate eeka ataro.
MAT 5:27 “Ba kone a bekaana, ‘Tana o eze leyau ne.’
MAT 5:28 Eyang beya ying na, pate ondooka wa gonta ondaaye, kawa kone o eza leyau ka wai, wa samba o eza me ka wai naname a nyimi lenyong le wai.
MAT 5:29 Liizi le oree leo leeyo ote ka o rizi, lopa le ka o pere. Mara o dere sara yende a lepung leo ko bena a tare pate lepung leo a nyimi akwilǝ ola.
MAT 5:30 O ara oree wa ote ka o rizi, core wai ka o pere. Mara o dere sara yende a lepung leo ko bena a tare pate lepung leo a nyimi akwilǝ ola.
MAT 5:31 “Akang samba obena, ‘Ondooka wa pere ondaaye wai, awa dongdong nya wai ewela o pere o awai.
MAT 5:32 Aa maa bekaa ying na pate ondooka wa pere ondaaye wai, aa wata wa meke wai ka leyau ne, wa ote wai orona o leyau naname, kangza pate ondooka wa ana wai, wa eza leyau naname.
MAT 5:33 “Kangza, ekone a samba o bekea aromo ko rabo na, ‘Tana o tono a rendaza ne, o eze epaaka ba tono ne aa begeshe Ateokora.’
MAT 5:34 Mi eyang beya yingna, tana e tono dakememe ne, ka azaa shili, obena arakanamea lǝdǝngdǝ le Ashili zene,
MAT 5:35 nyimia tane tono ka adeze ne, arakaname Ashili eeshe tobona te ai ne, koona ka Urushalima obena aya apeng ogomo ogong.
MAT 5:36 Kangza tana otono ka ukpwei o ne, azaa obena ba era ota ote lepkwai le yende kale itǝ leepeng koona leebo ne.
MAT 5:37 Pate epaaka wa gwara o beke belle eya ‘Eeye’ koona ‘Aa,’ eyapa e kala nyimi, e surea ara ondoo burua.
MAT 5:38 “E kone a samba o bekaa me na, ‘Liizi a bengmǝ be liizi, a liini a bengmǝ be liini.’
MAT 5:39 Na mi eyang beya ying na, tana enyane ondoo eza oying epa eburu ne. Ondo wa tabau a letamo lo ore wanggare wai lo guri kawa tabe kangza.
MAT 5:40 Ondo wa ale ka bo ara o cora angmǝ ka wa jeke odibi o, nya wai ulǝ o urnǝzǝ o kangza.
MAT 5:41 A ondo wa oteu na o eze teweno te omele yende, o ale ka wai o mamele maleere.
MAT 5:42 Ondo wa bosa eyapa abo, o nya wai. Ondo kangza wa deya aa kope eyapa abo, tana o nare wai ne.
MAT 5:43 “E kone a samba o bekaa na, ‘Yeme ondooka waya ating o, o nyane ondooka wata yeme oo ne.’
MAT 5:44 A mi eyang beya aying na, yeme na ana o nyana oying e bosazana Ashili azaa andaaka ne gǝǝzǝ ying,
MAT 5:45 adorana e itǝ ayana Ate aying o zaa shili. Ondooka wa oteze ongme ka wa ye masanto ara ana edang kaa ana o dera edang, awa kang deesa ka olyi ara ana nyong a sangsang ka ana nyong a buru.
MAT 5:46 Ba yeme ana o yeme owa belle, aya taasa o ka eya? Ana o eesa emate makeke kaa ana madinǝ, nyimia ne ezeze.
MAT 5:47 Ba beeza aromo au okoo belle, eya o ezeze erere ke kala ena ondo? Andaame maYahuda taza ne nyimia ne ezeze.
MAT 5:48 Azaa nyimi, itǝ na ana edang nangka Ate aying o zaa shili waye ka edang.
MAT 6:1 “Ezana a sauwo tana ogole oying orere wa itǝ ogongta a yizi ne. Azaa obena e eza nyimi, eto cǝ o taasa o woma araa Ate aying o zaa shili ne.
MAT 6:2 “Nyimia baaya nya ana odera, tana o ara lengmelo ajǝng ka komana kone ne, ana o ara ukpwei ezeze nyimi odandaro o gwarzanang maYahuda ka azaa marona adora aromo sabe ne. Eyang dongdong bele oying, ne samba ocǝ o taasa o woma one pat.
MAT 6:3 Aa bayaa nya ondo odera eyapa, tana o baya o ara oguri wa rose epaaka o ara ore ya eza me ne,
MAT 6:4 adorana nyaza oying itǝ epa esuk. Arakaname Ate aying, ka wa gongte epaaka aya ezaa me aa asuk, wayo taasau akap.
MAT 6:5 “Aa baaya beya angmǝ ka Ashili, tana oye na ana o ara ukpwei ne, ne yeme o beya angmǝ ka Ashili a itǝ a madandaro ma ogwarzanang maYahuda ka edǝki marona ka aromo laka ne. Eyang dongdong bele oying epeng, ne samba o emba o taasa one a pat.
MAT 6:6 Nyimia waaza, baya beya angmǝ ka Ashili, ale a nyimi odo o, pate abuudu me o beye angmǝ ka Ate au aaka ata gonta ai ne, aa Ate au ka agonte pate epaaka a eze a suk, ayo taasau.
MAT 6:7 “A eeya beya angmǝ ka Ashili, tana wa eweo na aworme ka neta rosa Ashili ne, andaame neya gonta na ne beya angmǝ a ewo waya yo ote ka kone ne.
MAT 6:8 Tane itǝ na nee ne, Ate ying rosa epaaka e gwara ka ying zongka e pirkǝ ai.
MAT 6:9 E beya angmǝ ka Ashili nanna, “Ate aro ozaa shili, a monte leze leo a sangsang.
MAT 6:10 A togomo to de, aa eze epaaka oya yeme me a lerambo leena, nangka ezeze azaa shili.
MAT 6:11 Nyaro epaolya o ngmeengme.
MAT 6:12 O pisi ro madinǝ maro, nangka te pisizi andaaka ne ezeze ro madinǝ.
MAT 6:13 Tana o ale kaaro ara o kedeya ne, o wobe ro a taara te ogomo o bere o buru ona.’
MAT 6:14 “E pisǝ aromo aaka ne ezeze ying epa eburu, Ate aying o zaa shili yo pisǝ maying’.
MAT 6:15 Aa eeta pisǝ ana ondo madinǝ mane ne, Ate ying to pisǝ epa eburu eeying ne.”
MAT 6:16 “Eeya meke o ngmǝ, tane care mayinu nangka ana o ara ukpwei ezeze ne. Ne care mayinu kane wore aromo bekaana neya eza opate o ngmǝ. Ang dongdong bele oying, ne samba ocǝ o taasa one naname.
MAT 6:17 Aa baaya pate o ngmǝ, kwizǝ mayinu mau, o saane mai manau,
MAT 6:18 adorana tana rosa o bena oya eza o pate o ngmǝ ne. Ate au kaa ta gonta ne, ooka kangza wa gonte pate epaaka a ezeze a suk, wayo taasau.
MAT 6:19 “Tana e kuri tukpwei toying ocǝ a lerambo leena araaka egau kaa orengkaka yo cara wai ne, araaka akǝri neyo pora ka ne lyǝ ne kpwi.
MAT 6:20 Soona e kuri tukpwei toying ocǝ azaa shili, araaka egau ka orengkaka to cara wai ne, araaka kangza, akǝri to lyǝ ka ne eze bekǝri ne.
MAT 6:21 Araaka ocǝ o zene, sanamea lenyong leo zene kangza.
MAT 6:22 “Liizi leya beru be masanto ma lepung, liizi leo leeya cammo, pate lepung leo yo pena ka masanto.
MAT 6:23 A liizi leo leeta cammo ne, pate lepung leo yo dera masanto. Masanto ma lepung leo ma itǝ maring, maring yo dongdong gongha!
MAT 6:24 “Ondo wa era wata eza lezara ateakoro leere ne, baya nyimi oyo nyana o yende o yeme o yende, koona o tare o yende o zeele o leere me. Ba era ota tare Ashili kaa emate awere yende ne.”
MAT 6:25 Azaa nyimi eyang bele oying, tana e gare tukpwei toying azaa epaaka eya lyame, koona eya sa me, koona nangka eyo cǝ madibi ma o amba. Ebeene kala epaolya sang? Aa lepung kangza kala madibi sang?
MAT 6:26 Laka na engmeng o zaa shili, neta eza o shebeka koona ne shende kane eke a bengga ne. Pate ka nyimi Ate ying o zaa shili lyeeze ka ne. Ying e kala ne edang sang?
MAT 6:27 Mana a nyimi oying a kazo gara ukpwei wai wa era wa wale lemore le yende a nyimi tomore to wai?
MAT 6:28 “Na eyaka eya gara tukpwei toying azaa madibi ma o amba? Laka nangka eburu o wake e gongze, neta eza gole yende ne.
MAT 6:29 Pate ka nyimi eyang belo oying na ogomo Suleimanu ka ocǝ wai wata wa amba madibi maa gong na ondo a nyimi one ne.
MAT 6:30 Nyimia Ashili eze mawake ma owake bejaga nanna, maaka maya arakana o ngmeengme, a leere a ese mai ka ola, shibari ying? Ying ana o dera o kabare kaa Ashili!
MAT 6:31 Azaa nyimi tana e gare tukpwei toying a beyana, ‘Eya taya lya me?’ Koona ‘Eya teya sa me?’ Koona ‘Eya teya amba me?’
MAT 6:32 A worme ana o dera o rosa Ashili neya gare tukpwei tone azaa o gera nyimi. Kangza Ate aying o zaa shili a rose o bena eya yeme mapapa maana.
MAT 6:33 Epa e woma o bora eya, e nya Ashili tukpwei toying, e eze epa e togomo te Ashili, ka o gera epa ee sangsang ai, ayo nya ying kaa pate ma mapapa maana kangza.
MAT 6:34 Zaa nyimia tana e gare tukpwei toying azaa leere ne, leere yo deya ka ebelo gara le. Konang lengme ya ka ozitǝ ka waya kap ka le.
MAT 7:1 “Tana e core angmǝ azaa ondo ne, adorana tana a core angmǝ azaa oying ne.
MAT 7:2 Nangka e core angmǝ azaa na ondo, nyimia ayo core angmǝ aza oying. Kangza ka epa ogoshe ooka e ezane, ka wai ya ayo eza ying ne.
MAT 7:3 “Eyaka oya gonta kapa a liizi le orone o, oota ba laka okuturu a liizi leo ne?
MAT 7:4 Ba wǝnia o bekaa orone o na, ‘Bayang lopau kapa a nyimi liizi leo,’ abo oya ka okuturu a liizi leo?
MAT 7:5 Bo ondo ara ukpwei, bora ka o lope okuturu a liizi leo, arakaname oyo laka maleu ko ama o lopa kapa a liizi le orone o.
MAT 7:6 “Tana e nya e'ere epa e sangsang ne, tana e tare odembashe akwilǝ acale edang aying ne. Nee era ne itǝzǝ ne ka tobona, ane kuri kane daare ying a lekeleke.”
MAT 7:7 “Pirǝ na ayo nya ying, geraza na eyo cǝ, gwarazana ayo pari ying abuudu.
MAT 7:8 Pate ondooka wa pirǝ ayo nya wai, ondooka wa gera wayo cǝ, kangza pate ondooka wa gwara, ayo pari wai abuudu.
MAT 7:9 Mana nyimi oying ana ate, kena ka wai ka bosa oborode, awa nya kai lecale?
MAT 7:10 Koona ka bose bekwala, awa nya kai owa?
MAT 7:11 Na ying ana ara aburu e rose nangka eyo nyaza ayana ying mapapa ma rere, shebari Ate aying o zaa shili wato kala ying aa ama o nyaza mapapa ma rere andaaka ne pirzi ai sang!
MAT 7:12 Azaa nyimi, eza aromo epaaka oya yeme ane ezo, obena ennaa beyo be makili ma Mosa ka ana obeya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili.”
MAT 7:13 Lyǝ na abuudu a seto. Obena abuudu a patarke kaa kang gongha a aleze ka aromo akwilǝ ola, aromo a cake lyǝzǝ a ai.
MAT 7:14 Nyimia orona o cǝsǝ ebeene o dera o maro, waya seto awa kang ya baate, andaa baate ya kalea ai.
MAT 7:15 “Ezana a sauwo ka ana beya angmǝ ka mawo rendaza. Ne deese aying ka madibi ma emande epeng, a nyimi one neye na enama orambo o kala ara aburu.
MAT 7:16 Ebelo ogole ane wayo ote ka rose ne. Ara cǝ ayana inabi uti ekana na, koona ayana osaya a uti ekana?
MAT 7:17 Nyimia konang uti orere wa kareze ayana rere, aa uti oburu wa kareze ayana aburu.
MAT 7:18 Uti orere wa era wata kare ayana aburu ne, anyimia kangza uti oburu wa era wata kare ayana aa rere ne.
MAT 7:19 Pate uti ka wata kare ayana aa rere ne, ayo core wai a tare wai a nyimi ola.
MAT 7:20 Nyimia ayana ane yo ote ka erose ne.”
MAT 7:21 Pate ondooka wa beya mi na, ‘Ateokora, Ateokora’ waya to lyǝ a nyimi togomo to zaa shili ne. Soona ondooka wa eza epaaka Ate ang o nyimia o zaa shili ya yeme me.
MAT 7:22 A lengme lenname aromo acake yo beya me na, ‘Ateokora, Ateokora!’ Cai! Te zoole aa nyimi leze leo sang? Te sǝrsǝzǝ mabere maa buru anyimi leze leo sang? Kangza, a nyimi leze leo wa te eze mapapa mo tera ukpwei sang?
MAT 7:23 A were namea eyang bekaa ne a begeshe be komana na, ‘Anta tukǝ orosa oying ne. Arnang na ka me, ying ana o eza epa e buru.’
MAT 7:24 “Azaa nyimi pate ondooka wa kona angmǝ ang aana, ka wa eze ogole ka ai, waye na ondoo rosa ka wa sowa akwilǝ wai azaa opoo.
MAT 7:25 Nangka olyi wa ngmeze, na mabeno penze a ngmet, obere kang era nawa tabe akwilǝ me, nyimia na ata oko ne, obena oting ai ya azaa opoo.
MAT 7:26 A pate ondooka wa kona a ngmǝ ang aana, ka wata eza ogole ka ai ne, waye na ondoo dera orosa ka wa so akwilǝ azaa egengge.
MAT 7:27 Na olyi ngmeze, a mabeno penze, kangza obere ere nawa tabe akwilǝ name, naa oko a nyokonyoko.”
MAT 7:28 Nangka Yeso ka mare o beya mapapa ma name, na epame tere leguki le aromo ukpwei azaa ambela obaala kai.
MAT 7:29 Azaa obena ka baale ne naa ondooka waye ka obare, na ana o baala makili ma Mosa tazane.
MAT 8:1 Nangka Yeso ka jǝpi aza oyara, na aromo cake ne tare kai.
MAT 8:2 Na ogangca yende deya a kai nawa tunggunu aa begeshe be kai awa bena, “Ateokora, oya ka obare o womzang ong kang itǝ a sangsang.”
MAT 8:3 Na Yeso nayi o ara kai naka meke wai aka bekaana, “Ma kabare ma womzau, itǝ a sangsang.” A saseya nawa woma ka leganca le ma.
MAT 8:4 Na Yeso beka a wai, “Kona, tana o bekea ondo epa eka ee manau ne, ale ka o wore ukpwei o ondo magame ma Ashili, oo kang nya epa eka a yo esa nangka Ashili a bele Mosa. Ya nyimi ka o wore aromo bekaana ba woma.
MAT 8:5 Nangka Yeso ka lyǝ a Kaparnahum, Na ondo o gong o tesa geza omole o Roma bose kai na,
MAT 8:6 “Ateokora, ozara ong ya tete akwilǝ, a lepung lewai lee gbwǝ aa waya kona o poba ajǝng.”
MAT 8:7 Na Yeso bekaa wai na, “Eyang deya kang womza wai.”
MAT 8:8 Ondo o gong o tesa geza omole name bekena, “Ateokora ang ta bare odeya akwilǝ ang ne, soona o sokoo bekaa angmǝ, ozara ong wayo woma.
MAT 8:9 Mi ang ya taara te ondo, kangza ka ana o tesa geza a moole ba taara tong, maa kang bekaa ondo na, “Ale, awa ale, ondo kangza ang bekaa na, “Deya,” awa de, ang kang bekaa ozara ong na, “Ya epana,” a wa ye.
MAT 8:10 Nangka Yeso ka kone nyimi, na epame tere kai ukpwei, aa ka beka ana o tarea kai na, “Ang dongdong bele ying epeng me, anta ma cǝ ondo a nyimi Isrela kawa o kabare kaa Ashili na oromo na ne.
MAT 8:11 Eyang belo ying, aromo a cake ne yo deesa a dizi ka aza ka ne cikǝ a ne lye epaolya legwa kaa Ibraheng, kaa Ishaku aa Yakubu a nyimi togomo te o zaa shili.
MAT 8:12 Bangka nyimi, ayo gǝǝzǝ ayana togomo ogomo obere oburu a nyimi maring maa bitibiti. Ara aaka ne yo ruuzi ka o nonza tuuni.
MAT 8:13 Na Yeso bekaa ondo o gong o tesa geza o moole o Roma na, “Ale, ayo yau nangka o kabare ka Ashili au ze.” Na o ngmere liizi na ozara me woma.
MAT 8:14 Nangka Yeso ka lyǝ akwilǝ a Biturusu naka mana ondawa wai a wata zake ne.
MAT 8:15 Na Yeso meke o ara wai, nawa woma, aa wa era nawa sele kai epaolya.
MAT 8:16 Nangka ulyǝlu waye, na aromo deese kaa aromo a cake ka ogomo o bere o buru wa taba ne. Kaa angmǝ ka ka beke belle, ka sǝǝrǝ obere oburu me, aka kang womza pate ana o dera o kona a cammo.
MAT 8:17 Ka ye nyimia adorana a panza epa eka ondo beya ngmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili Ishaya wa beke na, “Ka ana makono maro, kaa pate odera o kona aa zake aro.”
MAT 8:18 Nangka Yeso ka laka aromo a cake aa nee ringgǝri kai, naka ote nee na ne kuri owulu obeno niini.
MAT 8:19 Na ondo baala angmǝ aaka Ashili nya Mosa wa de nawa beka kai na, “Ondo baala, eyang tare o apate araaka oya ale ne.”
MAT 8:20 Na Yeso kabare wai na, “E ere o wake neye ka she'o, engmeng o zaa shili kangza neye ka todo, aa Kena ka o Oromo kata ka ara o mora ne.”
MAT 8:21 Na ondo nyimi ana o tare o Yeso bekena, Ateokora, baya ang ale kang taase ate ang suri.”
MAT 8:22 Na Yeso bekaa wai na, “Tareng, baya andaaka ne gbwizǝ ne taase andaaka ne gbwizǝ.”
MAT 8:23 Nangka Yeso lyǝ a nyimi o onggo o taara manyi, na ana o tare o Yeso ale legwa ka kai.
MAT 8:24 Na o bere ogong era a lepong leme, na sejǝng sheme ere ka legoone na manyi bore o lyǝzǝ a nyimi onggo me, aa Yeso ya malau.
MAT 8:25 Na atoma kai ale nane ara kai, aa ne bekaa kai na, “Ateokora, boza ro, manyi ya lya oro.”
MAT 8:26 Na ka bekaa ne na, “Eyaka e kerke nyimi? O kabare kaa Ashili aying me baba? Naka ere, aaka zurki obere ka lejǝng le manyi mame. Na keeya itǝ a tiiyi.
MAT 8:27 Na epame tere aromo ukpwei, aa ne beke na, “Mana waana ka o bere ka lejǝng le manyi kone kai aane tare kai?”
MAT 8:28 Nangka ne de owulu o makeke ma Garasina, na aromo leere ane suri a macau aaka obere o buru wa taba ne, ne wobe Yeso. Legoone lene le itǝ epa e boome maleu nangka aromo ta tareze orona me ne.
MAT 8:29 Na ne rurayi aa ne bekaa Yeso na, “Eya manyi mau kaaro, bo Kena ka Ashili? Ba deya ko ka gǝǝzǝ ro, a were ta aya ne na?”
MAT 8:30 Aa ma'amo kaa ne edembashe akwilǝ ne rene a cake a neya lya epaolya.
MAT 8:31 Na obere oburu name bose Yeso na, “Baa sǝǝrǝ ro o turki ro a nyimia edembashe akwilǝ me.”
MAT 8:32 Naka bekaa ne na, “Ale na.” Na ne suri aa ne lyǝ edembashe akwilǝ me. Na edembashe me ne ere ka tesong na ne tǝǝru a lepong leme na manyi lye ne apat.
MAT 8:33 Na ana o soola edembashe me ne ere ka tosong, aa ne ale apeng, aa ne baale pate epa eka e mane ne, kaa epa eka ee mane ana obere o buru me.
MAT 8:34 Na pate aromo apeng me ne suri na ne wobe Yeso. Nangka ne laka kai, na ne bose kai na ka baya makeke mane.
MAT 9:1 Nangka Yeso ka lyǝ o onggo manyi, naka tare a Kaparnahum apeng aaka ka gong ne.
MAT 9:2 Na ca kai ondo ka lepung le wai le gbwi aa waya tete a kapengge. Nangka Yeso ka laka okabare kaa Ashili ane, naka bekaa ondooka lepung lewai le gbwǝ na, “Kena kang, zanta, a pisǝ madinǝ mau.”
MAT 9:3 Na ana o baala ngmǝ aaka Ashili nya Mosa ne bekaa a tukpwei tone na, “Karomo kaana ka tambo Ashili!”
MAT 9:4 Aa Yeso ka orosa madoola mane, naka pirkǝ na, “Eyaaka eya eza madoola maburu a nyong aying nanna?
MAT 9:5 Eya kala o dera o poba, o beka na, “O bena a pisǝ madinǝ mau na, ‘Koona era ka oyeng na?
MAT 9:6 Eyang yeme e rose obena Kena ka o Oromo kaye ka obare o pisǝ madinǝ a lerambo.’ Naka bekaa ondooka lepung le wai le gbwǝ na, “Era ka o jeke kapengge kau o ale akwilǝ.”
MAT 9:7 Na oromo me ere, nawa ale akwilǝ.
MAT 9:8 Nangka aromo a cake ne laka nyimi, nane kone boome, aa ne sabe Ashili, aaka aa nya aromo ebelo obare oona.
MAT 9:9 Nangka Yeso ka lyǝ izi ka teweno, naka laka oromo yende kaa rareze wai na Matiyu, aa waya cikǝ awa eze ogole ara o eese emate makeke. Naka bekaa wai na, “Tareng.” Nawa ere aa wa tare kai.
MAT 9:10 Malo nyimi aa Yeso ya lya epaolya akwilǝ a Matiyu, na ana o eesa emate makeke ka ana madinǝ a cake ne de, na ne cikǝ ka kai kaa ana o tare o kai.
MAT 9:11 Nangka maParisa ne laka nyimi, na ne bekaa atoma kai na, “Eyaka ka ondo obaala o ying waya lya epaolya kaa ana o eesa emate makeke kaa na madinǝ?”
MAT 9:12 Nangka Yeso ka kone nyimi na ka bekaa na, “Andaaka neya kona azake ta gera ondo onyaza makang ne, seekoona ana o kono.
MAT 9:13 Azaa nyimi ale na ka e gere orosa epaaka nyimi, ‘Egonegonea mi ang yeme aying, onyaza eyapaa tazane.’ Antaa ma deya kang rare andaa woma ne, seena ana madinǝ.”
MAT 9:14 Na ana otare Yohana o batisma ne deya Yeso na ne beka kai na, “Awiinia ro ka maParisa te pate o ngmǝ, a na otare o ta ezaza ne?”
MAT 9:15 Na Yeso kabare nee na, “Anyong a era caro ajaa ondooka wa sure ana ondaye osau a neye legwa na? Tomore ya deya ka ayo jeka ondoo ana ondaaye osau a baya ne. A tomore tonname neyo pate o ngmǝ.
MAT 9:16 “Ondo wa ere wata manka ozani osau ka wa naane odibi oo kozo ne, o naane me yo dara odibi me kawa kala o samba o burǝ.
MAT 9:17 Kangza, ondo wa era wata kare manyi ma o inabi ma sau aa boboto a kozo ne. Waya nyimi a boboto me yo poso ka manyi ma o inabi me oko, a boboto me caro. Manyi ma o inabi ma sau, a kare mai a boboto a sau. Adorana a bisi kaa pate maleere mame.”
MAT 9:18 Yeso kaya za obeya nyimi naname, na ondoono o dandaro o gwarzanang maYahuda, wa de aa wa tunggunu ating kai aa wa bekaa na, “Nanname na kagala kang surǝ aa gbwǝ, deya ka o eke taara to azaa kai, ka yo era.”
MAT 9:19 Na Yeso ere legwa kaa ana otare kai, nane ale ka oromo me.
MAT 9:20 Ondaaye yende wa zene arame aa wa ye shenai betuuru ka she leere aa waya kono o ooso manyau, nawa deya a sauwo a dimǝ Yeso nawa eke o ara a bengmǝ be odibi kai.
MAT 9:21 Aa wa bekaa lenyong lewai na, “Maa eke o ara odibi kai belle, eyang woma.”
MAT 9:22 Nangka Yeso ka ringgǝnu naka laka wai, naka bekaana, “Ondaaye, zanta, o kabare kaa Ashili au, wa womzau.” A saseya na ondaaye me woma.
MAT 9:23 Nangka Yeso ka de akwilǝ ondoono dandaro gwarzanang maYahuda, naka mana aromo acak aa neya ulbǝ esherowa ka seleera she ma'ade.
MAT 9:24 Naka bekaana, “Erana arakaana! Ogala me taa wa gbwǝ ne waya malauwa belle.” Nane zoze, aa ne zeele kai.
MAT 9:25 Nangka asǝǝrǝ aromo me o yanga, naka lyǝ aa nyimi aa ka meke o ara ogala me, aaka ara kai.
MAT 9:26 Na orooka me wa ale a kuruwǝ a pate makeke mame.
MAT 9:27 Yeso kaya baya ara me naname, na arǝ aleere tare kai aa ne rare ajǝng na, “Kena ka Daoda kona egonegone ero!”
MAT 9:28 Nangka ka lyǝ akwilǝ yende na arǝ me deya kai, na Yeso me bekaa ne na, “Ee kabare ka Ashili obena maa erang womza ying na?” Na ne kabare kai na, “Eeye, Ateokora.”
MAT 9:29 Naka a eke o ara kai aa yizi ane, aaka bekaa na, “Azaa o kabare ka Ashili aying, aa womza ying.”
MAT 9:30 Na a yizi ane pǝrnu. Aa Yeso windi ne teto maleu na, “Tana e bele ondo orooka na ne.”
MAT 9:31 Pate ka nyimi, na ne suri, aane baale orooka kai aa kuruwǝ aa makeke ma me.
MAT 9:32 Nangka neya ale, na ca kai orakare yende ka obere oburu wa tabe wai.
MAT 9:33 Malo oka a sǝǝrǝ obere o buru me, na orakare me wa obeke angmǝ. Na epa me tere aromo cak tukpwei aane beyaa na, “Ata aa tuku laka ebelo epa eena a nyimi a Isrela ne.”
MAT 9:34 Na maParisa bekaana, “Ka legoone le ogomo obere o burua wa ya sǝrsǝzǝ mabere maburu.”
MAT 9:35 Na Yeso ka aleze a topepeng, aaka baale angmǝ a lebo a madandaro ma ogwarzanang maYahuda, aaka zoole azaa togomo te Ashili, aaka womza aromo azaa kombela makono ka o dera o kona a zake.
MAT 9:36 Nangka ka laka o kurkǝnǝng aromo naka kone egonegone, obena neya zitǝ azaa o dera ondo o kangkama, neye na emande epeng zora ondo otare ka ne.
MAT 9:37 Aka bekaa ana o tare o akai na, “O shende arame gong, aa na o shende me ta gongnga ne.
MAT 9:38 Azaa nyimi, bosana ateokora o shende me kawa tong ana ogole kane shende.”
MAT 10:1 Na Yeso zake ana o tare o akai betuuru kaa leere, a ka nya ne legoone lo sǝǝrǝ mabere maburu, ka o womza koonang makono kaa o dera o kona azake.
MAT 10:2 Shennaa seze she atoma Yeso betuuru: Obora waya Siman ka a beya wai na Biturusu, Kaa orone wai Andarawus, Kaa Yakubu kena kaa Zabadi, Kaa orone wai Yohana,
MAT 10:3 Kaa Pilibus, Kaa Batilomi, Kaa Toma, Kaa Matiyu ondo eesa emate makeke, Kaa Yakubu kena ka Halpa, Kaa Tadiyus,
MAT 10:4 Kaa Siman karomo ka Kan'na ka beya kai na kaye kale nyong le makeke ma kai, Kangza kaa Yahuda Iskariyoti ooka wa nya Yeso.
MAT 10:5 Nee betuuru kaa leere namea Yeso ka tong, aaka bekaa nee na, “Tana ne ale a makeke ma aworme ne, na koonang apeng a Samariya,
MAT 10:6 soona e ale emande epeng ka e wilǝ, aromo a Isrela.
MAT 10:7 A nyimi teweno teying e zoole na, ‘Togomo te zaa shili te amara.’
MAT 10:8 Ee womza ana makono, ee arsaza andaaka ne gbwizǝ, a womza agangca, ee sǝǝrǝ mabere maburu. A nyaza ying zora onya eyapa, ying ma nyaza na nyimi.
MAT 10:9 Kane monte emate o ozinari, na azorpa, emate epeng a nyimi lejǝng le le'eke.
MAT 10:10 Kangza kane jeke ojeketa a teweno toying ne, kane jeke madibi maleere ne, na tokakau, na lebenda, obena ondo ogole gwara ka epaolya wai.
MAT 10:11 Pate apeng aaka e lyǝ ne, ee gere oromo edang ka e jǝpi akwilǝ wai, a ale a were o baya apeng me.
MAT 10:12 Eeya lyǝ a akwilǝ me ee bekaa na, ‘O cikǝ o cammo itǝ oying.’
MAT 10:13 Akwilǝ me edang aaza, oo cikǝ o cammo ying wa cikǝ ai. Kangza edang waata zane, aa wa kuri a ying.
MAT 10:14 Pate ondooka wa nyana o emba oying, koona wa nyana o kona angmǝ aying, eeya surǝ akwilǝ me, na apeng me e zazame ma sorma ma tobona toying.
MAT 10:15 “Eyang dongdong obele oying, a lengme lo core angmǝ ayo kona egonegone makeke ma Sadoma ka ma Gwamrata azaa apeng na.”
MAT 10:16 “Laka na, ma tonga ying naa emande epeng a nyimi egana. Azaa nyimi cikǝ na ka o rosana na ewa, kangza e itǝ ana epa erere naa egoma.
MAT 10:17 Ezana a sauwo ka aromo, neyo ale ying abegeshe ana o cora ngmǝ, aane ole ying ane eze ying teyong aa madandaro ma ogwarzanang maYahuda.
MAT 10:18 Aza ong Kangza neyo aleze ka ying abegeshe be andaano kaa agomo, ka e beke angmǝ a lebo aza ong abegeshe be aworme.
MAT 10:19 Awereaka ne meke ying kane ale kaa ying aana togomo, tane gare tukpwei toying aza epa eeka eyo beka, kaa nangka eyo beka ne, ayo nya ying epa eka eyo beka awere me.
MAT 10:20 Aza obena ying ngha ta beya angmǝ ne, Obere orere Ate a ying waya ya beya angmǝ aa tongmǝ toying.
MAT 10:21 “Orone wayo nya orone wai ka wong, nyimia ate yo ya ka kena ka wai. Ayana kangza neyo girǝ ana ate ane, ane ote ka wongze ne.
MAT 10:22 Aromo neyo nyana ying azaa leze leng. Pate ondooka wa motana aa ale omaare, wayo bisǝ.
MAT 10:23 Nee gǝǝzǝ ying apeng aana, songhana ka e alea apeng a izi. Epeng emea eyang dongdong belo oying, eto mara o aleze a topepeng te Isrela ne, aa Kena ka o Oromo yo deya.
MAT 10:24 “Ondo tare wata kala ondo baala wai ne, ozara kangza wata kala ateokora wai ne.
MAT 10:25 Wa gwara ondooka a baale wai aa wa itǝ na ondo o baala wai, ozara kangza waye na ateokora wai. Aa ne rare ateokora na Ba'alzebul, nannia aromo akwilǝ wai kangza?”
MAT 10:26 “Azaa nyimi kane kone boome bene ne, obena eyapa tazene ka a pate, ka atoo pǝri e ne, kangza eyapa ta zene ka aa baasa ka atoo rosa ee ne.
MAT 10:27 Epa eeka eyang baala oying asuk, beke na e aa pantalang. Aa epa eeka a bele ying a toto, zoola na azaa e ajǝng aa betǝnkǝrǝ.
MAT 10:28 Tana e kone boome be andaaka ne wonze oromo ne, a neta ama o wonga bebuu be wai ne. Soona e kone boome be ondooka waye ka legoone le o wonga bebuu ka lepung apat akwilǝ ola.
MAT 10:29 A lisǝzǝ engmeng e leere okobo sang? Kayende ka era aa kata tǝru aa deze ka ka gbwǝ dera orosa a Ate aying ne.
MAT 10:30 Nyimia waaza pate shepkwai she ying a bala.
MAT 10:31 Azaa nyimi tane kone boome ne. Obena edang eying e kala engmeng acak.”
MAT 10:32 “Pate ondooka wa kabare kaa mi a begeshe be aromo, mi ma eyang kabare kaa wai a begeshe be Ate ang o zaa shili.
MAT 10:33 Apate ondooka wa sangga o rosa ong a begeshe be aromo, mi ma eyang sangga o rosa wai a begeshe be Ate ang o zaa shili.”
MAT 10:34 “Tane eke obena ma deya ka o cikǝ a cammo a lerambo leena ne. Anta ma deya ka o cikǝ ocammo ne, soona okara.
MAT 10:35 Ma deya, Kang gwara oromo kaa ate wai, Ang gwaara okara kagala kaa iini kai, aa iini ka ogiri wai.
MAT 10:36 Kangza wa itǝ bena ondoo nyana o wa ya nyimi a kwilǝ au.
MAT 10:37 Pate ondooka wa kala yeme ate, na iini wai o kala ong, wata gwara awa itǝ a ong ne. Kangza ondooka wa kala yeme ayana wai alome ka a ai o kala ong, wata gwara awa itǝ aa ong ne.
MAT 10:38 Nyimia ondooka waata ana uti o gendare o wai a wa tareng ne, wata gwara a wa itǝ a ong ne.
MAT 10:39 Pate ondooka wa yeme ebeene wai, wayo dera e. Aa pate ondooka wa dera ebeene wai azaa ong, wayo cǝ e.
MAT 10:40 “Ondooka wa kabare kaa ying, wa kabare kami naname. Kangza, ondooka wa kabare kaa mi wa kabare kaa ondooka wa tongang.
MAT 10:41 Ondooka wa emba ondo obeya angmǝ ka mawo Ashili, ka leze le obena wai ondo obeya ngmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili wai, wayo cǝ o taasa ondo obeya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili. Ondooka wa kabare kaa ondo o sangsang, ka leze le obena wai ondo o woma wai, wayo cǝ o taasa ondo o sangsang.
MAT 10:42 Komana wa nya kena ka yende a nyimi ayana aa batebate naa kaso kaa manyi, ka leze le obena wai ondo tare ong nga wai wato dongdong dera o taasa wai ne.”
MAT 11:1 Malooka Yeso ka mare ozoola a atoma kai betuuru ka leere name, na ka ere aa rana me na ka ale aaka baale ka o zoola a topepeng to Galili.
MAT 11:2 A were me Yohana ko batisma kaya apate aa kwilǝ ana o ezaza epa eburu, nawa kone epa eka Almasipu ya eza me, nawa tong ana o tare o wai ara Yeso
MAT 11:3 kane pirkǝ wai na, “Boa ondooka waya deya na, na te kare ayizi a ondo na?”
MAT 11:4 Na Yeso kabare nee na, “Kurǝna ka e bekaa Yohana epa eeka ee laka kangza ka ee kaa ekone,
MAT 11:5 obena arǝ na cǝ o laka ara, aa agǝdǝ neya teyeno, agangca ne kurǝ a sangsang, arara neya konaza ngmǝ, aa ya arsaza andaaka na gbwizǝ kangza a nya ana o dera cǝ oroka o lebo.
MAT 11:6 Ondo okona oleba ondooka waata cǝwǝ aa zaa o eke lenyong le wai aza ong ne.”
MAT 11:7 Nangka ne ale, na Yeso bore obeya angmǝ ka aromo a cake a zaa Yohana na, “E ale owake nee laka eya? E laka mawake maaka obere ya paba me na?
MAT 11:8 Na ee surǝ ka e laka eya? Ondo ka wa amba madibi maa rere na? Aromo akwilǝ ogomo neya ambaza madibi maa rere.
MAT 11:9 Na eya ee surǝ a laka me? Ondo obeya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili na? Nyimia, eyang bele oying na, wa dongdong kala ondo obeya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili.
MAT 11:10 Ondo ona a wele aa zaa wai na, “Laka na, ma tong ka o otoma ong kawa kala a izi au, ondooka wayo babarau orona zongka o de.
MAT 11:11 Eyang dongdong belle oying, ata a tukǝ o ngmenga ondo a nyimi lerambo leena ka wa dukǝ Yohana o batisma ogonga ne, pate kaa nyimi, ondooka kala a be baate a togomo te zaa shili wa kala wai.
MAT 11:12 O era a were o Yohana o batisma a deya o ngmeengme togomo te zaa shili teya kala o ara ozitǝ, ana o ote o zitǝ me neya yeme o emba togomo teme ka legoone.
MAT 11:13 Nyimia apate ana o baya ngmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili kaa makili maa kaa Ashili a nya Mosa ne beke angmǝ aa zaa togomo te me zongka Yohana de.
MAT 11:14 Kangza ee yo kabare ka letoma leena, Yohana waya a beka angmǝ aa zaa wai kaa a bena Iliya ya deya.
MAT 11:15 Pate ondo teto to kona, awa kone.
MAT 11:16 “Ma erang kedeya aromo awere na keeya? Naa ayana aka neya cikǝ ara ejamane, aane rare eja eceya ene aane beyana,
MAT 11:17 “‘Te ulubǝ ying tejebe, na eta e yowa leera ne, te beya leera le ma'ade na eta ee ruuzi ne.
MAT 11:18 Lakana, Yohana wa de wata wa lyeeze aa wa soze ne, nane bekaana, ‘Cai! Waya ka o obere oburu.’
MAT 11:19 Nangka Kena ka Oromo ka de na ka lyeeze aka soze nane bekaana, ‘Laka na ondo okala o ara o lyeeza ka o soza, beja bena o eesa emate makeke ka ana madinǝ!’ Pate kaa nyimi, a ebelo orosa Ashili, aa zaa gole o ai waya a rose edang.”
MAT 11:20 Naka bore ozurki a topepeng teeka ka kala ara o eza ogole o kai o tera ukpwei ne, obena aromo me neta ne kuri aa Ashili ne.
MAT 11:21 E lyǝ udi Korasiya! E lyǝ udi Betsaida! Obekaana ogole o tera ukpwei ooka a eze a nyimi ying aa ezea Taya ka Sidon, eeya nee samba o kurǝ aa Ashili ka o rabo aane amba majankale ka o kareze mato apung ane.
MAT 11:22 Azaa nyimi, eyang belo ying, a lengme lo core angmǝ, ayo kala aa kona egonegone aromo a Taya ka Sidon azaa oying.
MAT 11:23 Bo ma Kaparnahum, oya gonta o bena aya zalara o aa zaa shili na? Nyimia taza ne, aya jǝpǝrǝ o araaka ana o gbwizǝ zene. Epa otera ukpwei ka a eze aa nyimi oo, eya aa eze a Sadoma, Sadoma me waayo tata a deya o ngmeengme.
MAT 11:24 Aza nyimi, eyang bele oying, a lengme le o core angmǝ, ayo kala aa kona egonegone o makeke ma Sadoma baa zaa o.”
MAT 11:25 A were namea Yeso ka bekaana, “Ate maa kona oleba o, Ateokora o zaa shili kaa deze, aa zaa obena ba baasa epaana a na o ama ka o rosa, na ba pari ara andaaka neta rosa eyapa ne.
MAT 11:26 Nyimia Ate, enna eya epa eeka e kala o rera aa bo.
MAT 11:27 Ate ang wa nya ekeeya aa taara tong. Ondo ta rosa kena kame ne soona Ate me, kangza ondo ta rosa Ate me ne soona kena kame, kaa pate ondooka kena kame kaa yeme owore o wai.
MAT 11:28 Deyana me pate o ying ana o zitǝ, ying ana o kona kaa be dengdeng, eyang nya ying o teseke.
MAT 11:29 Lyǝ na a lezara leng, ee eze epa eeka ang eze, obena mi ondo o nata ukpwei ya wai, ondooka wata ara ukpwei ne, eyo cǝ o nata anyong.
MAT 11:30 Obena lezara leng ta poba ne, magogoro mang kangza ta dengdeng ne.”
MAT 12:1 A were name a lengme le o teseke le maYahuda, Yeso ka dare aa nyimi turu te eyuu. Atoma kai neya kona ekomo, na ne torbe makpwe ma eyuu na ne lye.
MAT 12:2 Nangka maParisa ne laka nyimi, na ne beka kai na, “Ba laka atoma au neya eza epa eeka makili ma Mosa ma nare eze a lengme le o teseke le maYahuda.”
MAT 12:3 Naka bekaa nee na, “Eta e kone epa eeka Daoda ye a were aka ka kone ekomo, kai kaa aja teweno te kai sang?
MAT 12:4 Nangka ka lyǝ akwilǝ Ashili naka lye borode emea kata gwara aaka lye, na aja teweno te kai ne lye ne, soona ana magame ma Ashili belle.
MAT 12:5 Ying eta e soole a ngmǝ aaka Ashili nya Mosa, nangka ana magame ma Ashili, aa akwilǝ Ashili ne cakate makili ma lengme lo teseke maYahuda aa zaa nyimi ne tambo na?
MAT 12:6 Eyang bele oying, kando kamea ka kala akwilǝ Ashili kaana.
MAT 12:7 Ayya e rose epa eeka a ngmǝ Ashili ya beyame, ‘Mi o cikǝ egonegonea mi ang yeme aying, o nayi Ashili enama tazane,’ etaa eeyo laka madinǝ mana odera madinǝ ne.
MAT 12:8 Obena Kena ka Oromo kaya Ateokora o lengme le o teseke le maYahuda.”
MAT 12:9 Na Yeso baya araname aaka lyǝ odandaro o gwarzanang maYahuda.
MAT 12:10 Aa mana oromo yende a rame ooka o ara wai wa waka. Nane pirkǝ Yeso na, “Obaala Mosa wa wore obena wa gwara a womza a lengme le o teseke le maYahuda na?” Ne pirkǝ kai nyimia adorana ne cǝ kai ka o tambo.
MAT 12:11 Naka bekaa nee na, “Mana a nyimi oying waaya ka omande openg, na wa taru a leo a lengme lo teseke le maYahuda, wato meke wai kawa sǝǝrǝ ne na?
MAT 12:12 Oromo kala omande epeng edang maleu. Azaa nyimi ata aa nara ogole o rere aa lengme teseke maYahuda ne.”
MAT 12:13 Naka bekaa oromo me na, “Niyi o ara o!” Nawa niyi ora me, aa wa kuri a zak na o leere me.
MAT 12:14 Na maParisa suri, a ne gwaara madoola ma nangka neyo wongha kai.
MAT 12:15 Nangka Yeso rose nyimi, na ka ere arame. Na aromo acake tare kai naka womza ne apat.
MAT 12:16 Aa ka windi ne toto na kana ne bele ana ondo ne.
MAT 12:17 Aye nyimia ka panza o bekaa ondo beya ngmǝ ka mawo Ashili Ishaya na,
MAT 12:18 “Kazara kang ang kaana kamea ma zake! Epa oyeme ong, kamea ang kone oleba kai ba cak. Eyang nya kai o bere ong, aa kayo beka ngmǝ a masanto a makeke ma aworme.
MAT 12:19 Ka too beya masanggo koona ka beye angmǝ a jǝng ne, Kangza ondo too kona lengmelo le kai aza orona ne.
MAT 12:20 Legaaga leeme le tunggunu katoo pora leene, Beru be masanto bemea bee amara ka o lambu katoo limbǝ be ne, Ka ka ote epeng eme ke lya izi.
MAT 12:21 Aa nyimi leze le kai aworme kangza neyo eke lenyong a kai.”
MAT 12:22 Na ca Yeso orakare ka urǝ waze ka wa kang ya ka obere o buru, naka womza wai, nawa bore beya ngmǝ awa kang gonta ara.
MAT 12:23 Na epame tere aromo me ukpwei, na ne bekaana, “Kanna Kena Daoda tazane na?”
MAT 12:24 Nangka maParisa ne kone nyimi na ne bekaana, ka legoone le Ba'alzebul ogomo obere oburua kando kaana kaya sǝrsǝzǝ mabere maburu.”
MAT 12:25 Nangka Yeso ka rose madoola mane, naka bekaa nee na, “Pate togomo teeka te arnang to dǝkǝni to leere a neya kara ka tukpwei, teyo caro. Kangza apeng koona akwilǝ aaka a arnang to dǝkǝni to leere a neya kara ka tukpwei, ayo rizi.
MAT 12:26 O Shetan wa sǝǝrǝ o Shetan waya kara ka ukpwei wai naname. Togomo te wai yoya legoone nannia?
MAT 12:27 Ma sǝrsǝzǝ obere oburu ka legoone le Ba'alzebul, ana o tare o ying ne sǝrsǝzǝ ka legoone le mana? Aa zaa nyimi ana otare oying neya yo core ying angmǝ me.
MAT 12:28 A ma sǝrsǝzǝ bere o buru ka legoone le obere Ashili na togomo te Ashili te deya aying naname.
MAT 12:29 A era ta lyǝ aa kwilǝ ondo legoone ka bese magogoro ma wai ne, soona a tese wai suri, aa amaa ama o besa magogoro ma akwilǝ a wai.
MAT 12:30 Ondooka wata ya legwa kami, ondo o nyana ong nga wai. Kangza ondooka wata kangkamang a kurǝ me ne, waya bacakaraa.
MAT 12:31 Aa zaa nyimi eyang bele oying, ayo pisǝ madinǝ ma aromo apat, ondooka wa sopa o obere Ashili, a to pisǝ madinǝ ma wai ne.
MAT 12:32 Ondooka wa beya a ngmǝ ma zeelakong aa Kena ka Oromo, ayo pisǝ madinǝ ma wai. Ondooka wa beya a ngmǝ ma zeelakong aa obere Ashili, a to pisǝ madinǝ ma wai a nyimi lerambo leena nanname ka o ale a izi ne.
MAT 12:33 Uti o rere wa ngmenze ayana a rere. Uti oburu wa ngmenze ayana aburu. A rose uti ayana wai ya.
MAT 12:34 Ying okurkǝnǝng ewa ee buru! Ee wiinia ee beye angmǝ edang, a ying naana ana ara buru ne? Obena epa emea eya nyimi lenyong eya susi o ngmǝ.
MAT 12:35 Oromo edang, a nyimi lenyong le wai wa eke epa eeke eye ka edang, ondo ara buru o eke lenyong lewai le eburu eya susi a lenyong le wai.
MAT 12:36 Eyang bele oying, aa lengme le o core angmǝ, pate angmǝ aburu ka oromo wa beya ayo pirkǝ wai.
MAT 12:37 Angmǝ au aya ayo sǝǝrǝu, aa kangza aya ayo core angmǝ aza o.
MAT 12:38 Na ana obaala angmǝ aaka Ashili nya Mosa kaa maParisa ne bekaa kai na, “Ondo baala, teya yeme aa te laka epa otera ukpwei aa bo.”
MAT 12:39 Naka kabare na, “Ying aromo tomore teena, ana leyau ka ara aburu, neya gera o laka epa otera ukpwei, a era ta wore ne epa otera ukpwei ne! Soona epa o tera ukpwei ondo obeya angmǝ ka mawo Ashili Yonana.
MAT 12:40 Nangka Yonana wa more awa were ka taaro a nyimi lebangi le bekwala bee gong, nyimia Kena ka Oromo kayo ya tomore to taro nyimi ocau.
MAT 12:41 A lengme le core angmǝ aromo o Neneba neyo era ka aromo tomore teena, ka ne toze aromo a tomore teena kane ta ne ya epa e woma ne, azaa o bena nee kurǝa Ashili aa kazo o ozoola o Yonana. Kangza ondo ka wa kala Yonana waya raana.
MAT 12:42 A Lengme le o core angmǝ, Aya ogong o makeke ma o Sheba wayo era kaa aromo a tomore teena, ka wa toze ne, o bena wa deya a wa suri a macangcang ma lerambo leena, kawa kone o rosa ogomo Suleimanu. Ondo ka wa kala Suleimanu naana.
MAT 12:43 Obere o buru wa surǝ nyimi oromo, aa wa kaale araaka manyi ta zane ne azaa o gera ara o teseke. Aa wa ta ocǝ ne,
MAT 12:44 malo nyimi aa wa bekaana, “Eyang kurǝ akwilǝ aa kaa maa surǝ ne.’ Wa kurǝ wayo mana akwilǝ amea zora ondo nyimi me aa a besa ai aa babare aa sangsang.
MAT 12:45 A wayo kurǝ kawa jeke mabere maa buru o sondaare maaka ma kala o bora me ara aburu, kane lyǝ ba oromo me aa ne cikǝ a nyimi owai. O maare oromo me wayo kala o bora wai o buru. Nyimia wayo itǝ kaa ana ara aburu a tomore teena.”
MAT 12:46 Nangka Yeso kaya beya angmǝ kaa aromo a cak naa mana iini ka arone kai aa neya itǝ oo yanga, a neya yeme o beya a ngmǝ kaa kai.”
MAT 12:47 Na oromo yende bekaa kai na, “Iini kaa arone au, neya oo yanga aa neya yeme o beya a ngmǝ kaa bo.”
MAT 12:48 Na Yeso kabare na, “Mana iini ong, kaa arone ang?”
MAT 12:49 Naka niyi o ara kai ana o tare kai, aa ka bekaana, “Andaana iini ong kaa arone ang.”
MAT 12:50 Komana wa eza epa eeka Ate ang o zaa shili waya yeme me, waya arone ang kaa iini ong.”
MAT 13:1 A lengme leme na Yeso suri akwilǝ me, naka ale aa ka cikǝ o wulu o lepong.
MAT 13:2 Na leguki le aromo leegong deya a kai, naka lyǝ o onggo o tara manyi naka cikǝ. Aa leguki le aromo me kangza ne itǝ o wulu lepong le me.
MAT 13:3 Naka bele ne mapapa cake aa nyimi angmǝ a gerpo na, “Ondo ogole ara yende wa ale ara aa waale ebelo.
MAT 13:4 Nangka waya waale me, na ebelo eyende taru a za orona, na engmeng de nane donge e.
MAT 13:5 Na eyende taru aa za acale araaka makeke ta gongha ne. Na e suri a saseya obena makeke arame taa gerpo ne.
MAT 13:6 Nangka ongme wa tamana na ma ya rauwo, na ma waka obena madǝrǝ mame taa gerpo ne.
MAT 13:7 Ee belo yende kangza taru a nyimi ekana, na ekana me gong na e gatakale e.
MAT 13:8 Ee yende kangza taru a makeke ma rere, na ekare eyo, na eye eyo liwinu, liwunu, eyende etuuru taashe, taashe, eyende kangza etuuru taaro, taaro.
MAT 13:9 Pate ondooka waye ka toto to konaza a wa kone angmǝ aa na.”
MAT 13:10 Na atoma Yeso de, aa ne pirkǝ kai na, “Eyaaka o beya angmǝ aa gerpo ka aromo?”
MAT 13:11 Naka kabare ne na, “Ying aa kabare o bena e rose o ela o togomo te Ashili, aa ne ata a nya nee ne.
MAT 13:12 O bena ondooka waya ka eyapa waya ayo wala wai ne, ka wa cǝ a cake. Kangza ondo odera eyapa, ee baate kawa ye ka e, ayo emba e a wai.
MAT 13:13 Epa eeka e ote na eyang beya ngmǝ gerpo kane, ‘Adorana na ne gonte a neta laka ne, aa ne rakara a neta a kona ne, obena epa eme e lyǝ aane amaring.’
MAT 13:14 Azaa one ayo panza epa eeka ondo beya ngmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili Ishaya wa beke na, “Eyo konaza, aa eto rosa ne dakememe, eyo kang gonta aa eto laka ne ko babate.
MAT 13:15 Obena anyong aromo ana aya katakau, aa teto tene ta konaza ne. Kangza ne pate ayizi ane, obena kana ne gonte ka ayizi ane ne, kana ne kone ka teto tene ne, obena kana ne cǝ orosa ne, kane kuri a mi kang womza nee ne.’
MAT 13:16 Ana o kona oleba ying obena ayizi aying aya gonta, a teto teying kangza taya konaza.
MAT 13:17 Eyang dongdong baala oying ana obeya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili ka ana o kona boome Ashili a cake ne yeme olaka epana eeya gonta me, na ne ta laka ne, aa ne kone epa eeka eya konaza me, na ne ta kona ne.
MAT 13:18 “Anna masanto ma angmǝ a gerpo ondo o waale ebelo na.
MAT 13:19 Pate ondooka wa kona ngmǝ a togomo nawa ta rosa ne, ogomo o bere oburu deese kawa kwagale epaaka a waale a lenyong le wai. Enna ebelo eeka a wale a za orona.
MAT 13:20 Ebelo eeka ee tǝru ara acale, eya naa ondooka wa kona angmǝ Ashili, nawa embe ka o kona o leba.
MAT 13:21 Oo bena wata ka oting ne, nawa ta rabo aa cake ne. A were aka o kedeya na opoba wa era, azaa a ngmǝ Ashili, aa oromo me kuri sidimǝ.
MAT 13:22 Ebelo ee ka e taru a nyimi ekana, eya na ondooka wa kona ngmǝ Ashili, na madoola ma ocǝ ka o kona oleba awere na a nare angmǝ o gongha, ka ngmǝ me itǝ o dera edang.
MAT 13:23 Ebelo eemea ee tǝru a makeke ma rere, waya na ondooka wa kone ngmǝ Ashili na wa rose ai, awa eze ogole ka ai. Kangza awa cǝ eyapa aza ame, eyende lewinu, lewinu, eyende etuuru taashe, taashe, ee yende etuuru taaro, taaro.”
MAT 13:24 Na Yeso kang bele ne angmǝ a gerpo yende na, “Ayo kedeya togomo ta shili ka oromo ooka wa waale ebelo e rere ara awai.
MAT 13:25 Awere aka aromo neya malau, na oja okara wai ale na wa waale a belo o wake yende ara o alkama me, awa sokoo ale.
MAT 13:26 Nangka ebelo me e ere na eye eyo, na owake me kang gongha.
MAT 13:27 Na azara ateakwilǝ me ne de, na ne bekaa wai na, ‘Ateakwilǝ, teya beya na ebelo erere ba waale ara au sang? A wiinia na mawake ma surǝ ara ame?
MAT 13:28 Nawa kabare ne na, ‘Oja okara waya nyimi.’ Na azara me pirkǝ wai na, ‘Oya yeme aa te ale kate lope mawake mame na?
MAT 13:29 Aa wa bekaa nee na, ‘Nyimia dai, bayana, tana azaa olopa mawake e gwaara ka o alkama me ne.
MAT 13:30 Baya na ne aa gong legwa a ale awere o shende. A were o shende me kangza eyang bekaa ana o shende me, kane bore ka oshende mawake mame, a ne kurki mawake mame, aane tese kane ese, aane shende o alkama me ka ne kare aa benga.’ ”
MAT 13:31 Na Yeso bekaa ne a ngmǝ a gerpo kangza na, “Togomo te shili teya baate na beyo be o mosta, emea oromo yende wa ale kawa kpeene ara awai.
MAT 13:32 Eya kala a bee baate a nyimi eyo, aa ee gongha, e kala kombela uti o marane, kawa itǝ uti oo gong, ka engmeng soze todo ee bana me.
MAT 13:33 Kangza Yeso ka bele ne angmǝ gerpo yende na, “Togomo te Ashili teye na o yisti, ooka ondaye yende wa jeke nawa sakale ka maso ma taaro ma'ena ma o alkama, na ma sakalnang ka ma o yisti me.
MAT 13:34 Na Yeso bele okurkǝnǝng aromo, pate epaname a nyimi angmǝ aa gerpo. Kata ka baaleze eyapa ne soona aa nyimi angmǝ gerpo.
MAT 13:35 Aye nyimia ka panza o bekaa ondo beya ngmǝ mawo Ashili Ishaya na, “Eyang beya angmǝ a nyimi ngmǝ a gerpo, Eyang beka epa eeka a baasa obora lerambo.”
MAT 13:36 Na Yeso baya aromo acake me, aaka lyǝ akwilǝ. Na atoma kai kangza ne deya kai, na ne bekaa na, “Bele ro masanto ma angmǝ gerpo aza mawake ara.”
MAT 13:37 Aaka kabare na, “Ondo owaale ebelo erere name, waya Kena ka Oromo.
MAT 13:38 Aa ara ame, aya lerambo leena, ebelo erere name, neya ayana a togomo te Ashili, kangza mawake mame maya ayana ogomo ara a buru.
MAT 13:39 Oja okara ka wa waale owake, waya ogomo ara a buru. Awere oshende me aya lengme le maare o lerambo leena, ana o shende me neya atoma Ashili o surǝ azaa shili.
MAT 13:40 Nangka kurki mawake ka ese mai, nyimia wayo itǝ a lengme le omaare.
MAT 13:41 Kena ka Oromo kayo tonga atoma kai o surǝ azaa shili, kane shende ana o ote aromo kane rizi, kangza kaa pate ana o eza epa eburu, kane sǝǝrǝ ne a nyimi togomo te kai,
MAT 13:42 kangza kane tare ne a nyimi ola o kpwaiye. A saname neya ruuzi ka o nonza tuuni.
MAT 13:43 A were namea ana o eza epa erere, masanto mane mayo surǝ na ongme a nyimi togomo te Ate ane. Ondooka waya ka toto to kona, awa kone.”
MAT 13:44 Togomo te Ashili teye na ocǝa ka a baasa nyimi ara, ooka ondo wa cǝ nawa kang baasa. A nyimi zanta wai, nawa ale nawa lishi pate epa eeka waye ka e nawa embe ara me.”
MAT 13:45 Kangza togomo te Ashili teye na ondo ejamanea, ooka waya gera acale aa rere ka aye kaa emate.
MAT 13:46 Nangka wa cǝ lecale le yende lee rere acak, na wa ale nawa lishi pate epa eeka waye ka e, na wa embe ai.”
MAT 13:47 Kangza Togomo te Ashili teye na ojara o meese ekwala ooka tare a lepong, nawa meke kombela ekwala.
MAT 13:48 Nangka wa pene, naa windi wai o wulu lepong, nane cikǝ ane zake e kwala ee rere e me nane kare a nyimi o kende, aa ne oke eburu me.
MAT 13:49 Nyimia wayo itǝ a lengme le omare. Atoma Ashili o surǝ azaa shili neyo sǝǝrǝ ana ara aburu nyimi aromo a rere.
MAT 13:50 Ka ne tare ana ara aburu a nyimi ola o kpwaiye, aa sanamea neyo ruuzi ko nonza tuuni.
MAT 13:51 “E rose epaena pate na?” Na ne kabare na “Eeye.”
MAT 13:52 Naka bekaa nee na, “Pate ondo o baala angmǝ aaka Ashili nya Mosa wa itǝ ondo tare togomo te Ashili, wa itǝ na ateakwilǝ, ondooka wa mangka ocǝ osau ka o kozo ara a le'eke lewai.”
MAT 13:53 Nangka Yeso ka mare obeya angmǝ aa gerpo name naka baya arame.
MAT 13:54 Ko deya a peng kai, naka bore o baala aromo oo dandaro o ogwarzanang one. Na epa me tere ne ukpwei na ne beke na, “Karomo kaana ka cǝ orosa ka epa o tera ukpwei aa ba?
MAT 13:55 Teya beyana kanna, kena ka o ondo cocoza sang? Iini kai kaya Mariya sang? Arone kai neya Yakubu, Yusupu, ka Saminu, kangza kaa Yahuda sang?
MAT 13:56 Arone kai andaye neya ara yendea kaa ro sang? Karomo kaana ka cǝ epa eena ba?
MAT 13:57 Na ne kone oburǝ okai. Na Yeso bekaanee na, “Ondo obeya ngmǝ ka mawo Ashili ata kabare ka wai a nyimi apeng awai kaa kwilǝ awai ne.
MAT 13:58 Naka ta eza epa otera ukpwei a cake a saname ne, a za odera okabare ka Ashili one.
MAT 14:1 A were name Ogomo Hiridus Antipas wa kone oroka azaa Yeso.
MAT 14:2 Nawa bekaa azara wai na, “Ondoonaa Yohana o Batisma, waya a ara wai malo ogwǝ, nyimia wa ote na waya kaa o bare o eza epa otera ukpwei na.”
MAT 14:3 Obena Hiridus wa meke Yohana na tere wai, aa ote wai a akwilǝ andaleme azaa Herodiya ondaye orone owai Pilibus.
MAT 14:4 Azaa bena Yohana wa beeze awai na wa ta gwara awa ana Herodiya ka ka itǝ ondaye wai ne.
MAT 14:5 Pate ka o bena Hiridus waya yeme wonga Yohana, aa waya kona boome be aromo, aa ne jeke o bena Yohana ondo beya ngmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili wai.
MAT 14:6 Nangka lengme le o ngmenga o Hiridus le dukǝ, na kagala ka Herodiya ka yo leera a begeshe be aromo kane de ara o zǝnggǝ me, na Hiridus kone oleba maleo,
MAT 14:7 nawa tono a kai na wayo nya kai pate epa eeka ka bosa.
MAT 14:8 Na iini kai bekaa kai na ale ka o bekaana, “A nyau ukpwei o Yohana o Batisma nannameena a nyimi oso.”
MAT 14:9 Na ogomo kone oburu, aza obena wa tono abegeshe be ageng wai, nawa ote na a nya kai epa eeka kaa bosa.
MAT 14:10 Nawa tong na core ukpwei o Yohana a akwilǝ andaleme,
MAT 14:11 na de ka ukpwei me a nyimi oso na nya kagala ka me, na ka ca iini kai.
MAT 14:12 Na ana o tare Yohana de nane ana ekeze me, na ne taashe, aa ne ale na ne beka Yeso.
MAT 14:13 Nangka Yeso ka kone nyimi, naka ere naka lyǝ o onggo o taara manyi aaka ale ara aaka aromo ta rene ne ka ka cikǝ a yende. Nangka aromo acak ne kone nyimi, na ne surǝ a topepeng na ne tare kai a tobona.
MAT 14:14 Ka o surǝ kai o onggo o tara manyi naka laka leguki le aromo. Naka kone egonegone o ne, naka womza ana makono nyimi o ne.
MAT 14:15 Nangka ulyǝlu waye, na atoma kai de akai na ne bekaa na, “Ara na a aromo ta rene ne, a waana ulyǝlu waya. Baya aromo ana ane ale a topepeng kane gere tukpwei tone epaolya.”
MAT 14:16 Na Yeso bekaa ne na, “Wata gwara aane ale ne, nyana ne eyapa ka ne lye.”
MAT 14:17 Na ne kabare na, “Teta ka eyapa arakaname, soona maborode esu ka ekwala e leere.”
MAT 14:18 Na ka bekaa na, “Deyana ka e arakaana.”
MAT 14:19 Aaka ote aromo me na ne cikǝ azaa mawake. Naka jeke, maborode esu ka ekwala leere, naka ara ukpwei aaza shili, aaka sabe Ashili, naka pose maborode mame aaka nyaza atoma kai, a atoma me kangza aa ne nyaza aromo.
MAT 14:20 A pate one ne lye na ne tiyǝ, na ne kurki o dangare me, nawa panza makende betuuru ka maleere.
MAT 14:21 Andaaka ne lye ne dukǝ andaleme magu esu bangka andaye ka ayana.
MAT 14:22 Ka o mara me naka ote atoma kai na ne lyǝ o onggo o tara manyi ka ne kaana kai a ale owulu o sara yende. Aa kai ka itǝ a dimǝ ka ka laka o aleze a tokwilǝ te aromo me.
MAT 14:23 Malo ale aromo me, naka zale oyara kai a yende kaka beye angmǝ ka Ashili. Na ulyǝlu ye aa kaya yende saname.
MAT 14:24 A wereme o onggo o taara manyi waya tera lepong, na sejǝng se manyi se ere ka legoone, obena obere me waya kara ka ne.
MAT 14:25 Aa ra aa dukǝ beru bo taaro be lelere, na Yeso yeng azaa manyi aaka dore ne.
MAT 14:26 Nangka atoma ne laka kai aa yenga azaa manyi na boome meke ne nane bekaana, “Bebua be!” Nane gware bekoko azaa obena nee kona boome.
MAT 14:27 A saseya naka bekaa nee na, “Kane kone boome ne Mea. Kane kone boome ne.”
MAT 14:28 Na Biturusu kabare wai na, “Ateokora boa baaza, oteng kang deya bo aa yenga azaa manyi.”
MAT 14:29 Na Yeso bekaa wai na, “Deya.” Na Biturusu suri o onggo o taara manyi, nawa yeng azaa manyi a wa dore Yeso.
MAT 14:30 Awereaka wa laka obere wa ere a jǝng nawa kone boome. Nangka manyi ma bore dongha wai nawa rurai, awa bekaa na, “Ateokora bozang!”
MAT 14:31 Aa saseya na Yeso nayi o ara naka meke wai, aaka bekaa wai na, “Bo o kabare ka Ashili au wa sawa, eya e ote na ba dambaraza?”
MAT 14:32 Ka o lyǝ one o onggo o taara manyi na obere me tete.
MAT 14:33 Andaaka neya a nyimi onggo o tara manyi ma me na ne girwǝ ane bekaa na, “Bo dongdong, Kena ka Ashili kai!”
MAT 14:34 Nangka ne tare opong ome, na ne lyǝ a makeke ma Janasarata.
MAT 14:35 Nangka aromo apeng me ne rose bena Yesoa kai, na ne tongze a kombela aromo apat a topepeng te ma'amo, na ne casa kai ana makono,
MAT 14:36 Na ne boshe kai na ka kabare aa ne cocome edǝki odibi kai. Pate andaaka ne cocome na ne woma.
MAT 15:1 Na ana ondo ba nyimi maParisa kaa ana o baala angmǝ aka Ashili a nya Mosa nane deya Yeso a ne surǝ ba Urushalima nane bekaa na,
MAT 15:2 “Eyaaka atoma au neta tare makili mana Anateandaasau ne? O bena neta sabozo zongka ne lye epaolya ne.”
MAT 15:3 Na Yeso kabare nee na, “Eyaaka ying eta tare makili ma Ashili ne e tare makili maying?
MAT 15:4 Ashili a bekaa na, ‘Tare ate au, ka iini au, kangza pate ondooka wa zeela ate ka iini wai wa gwara aa wongha wai.’
MAT 15:5 Ying e baale na, ‘Pate ondooka wa bekaa ate ka iini wai na, epaaka maa ya kankama oying ka e, ma nya Ashili,’
MAT 15:6 wa nyana otare ate kaa iini wai ka e ne, azaa nyimi ee cakate angmǝ Ashili azaa makili maying naname.
MAT 15:7 Ying ana rendaza, Ishaya ondo beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili wa beke oroka Ashili aza oying aa kap na,
MAT 15:8 “Aromo ana, ne tareng ka ongmǝ belle, aa nyimi anyong ane neya macangcang kaa mi.
MAT 15:9 O girwǝ one aa mi taa ka edang ne, obaala one o tare makili ma aromo, o bena aya angmǝ Ashili.”
MAT 15:10 Na Yeso rare o kurkǝnǝng aromo acak, aa ka bekaa nee na, “Konana ekang rosa.
MAT 15:11 Epa eeka e lyǝzǝ ongmǝ oromo eta ote ka wa ye ka madinǝ ne, soona epa eeka e susi ba ongmǝ eya ote ka oromo wa itǝ ka madinǝ.”
MAT 15:12 Na atoma kai ne deya kai nane bekaa kai na, “Orose obena maParisa ne kona o burǝ ka ne kona a angmǝ aa na?”
MAT 15:13 Na Yeso kabare na, “Pate epa eeka Ate ang o zaa shili ta wa gata ne, ayo mukǝ.
MAT 15:14 Arnang ka ne, ne arǝ ne ka neya windǝ arǝ lebenda. Urǝ wa windǝ urǝ lebenda, pate one neya kala a le'o.”
MAT 15:15 Na Biturusu bekaa na, “Bele ro masanto ma angmǝ aa gerpo ana ka ba beka.”
MAT 15:16 Na Yeso pirkǝ nee na, “A alea aa were aana e tata a maring na?
MAT 15:17 Eta rosa obena pate epa eeka e lyǝ ongmǝ e ale a lebangi e suri ba lepung sang?
MAT 15:18 A epaaka e susi ba ongmǝ e suri ba lenyong. Epa o susǝ a lenyong leme eya ote oromo ka wa itǝ ka madinǝ a begeshe ba Ashili.
MAT 15:19 Azaa o bena aa nyimi lenyong leyaa sǝrsǝzǝ madoola maa buru. Naa, o wongha oromo, o mora kaa ondaye ondo, o mora kaa Ogala, o eza bekǝri, o ana angmǝ, ka o cara leze.
MAT 15:20 Ennaa ote oromo kawa itǝ ka madinǝ a begeshe ba Ashili, o lya epa olya zora o sabo waya ta ote ka oromo waye ka madinǝ a begeshe ba Ashili ne.”
MAT 15:21 Nangka Yeso ka baya arakaname, naka ale a makeke ma Taya ka Sidon.
MAT 15:22 Na ondaye yende ka makeke ma Kan'ana deya a Yeso ka oruuzi na, “Kona egonegone eng Ateokora, kena ka Daoda, bozang, kagala kang obere o buru ooka waya nyimi kai waya zo gara kai.”
MAT 15:23 Na Yeso ta beka eyapa a wai ne. Aza nyimi na atoma kai ne deya a kai nane bosa kai na, “Tarangga wai kawa ale waya tare oro awa gare ro ka be koko.”
MAT 15:24 Naka kabare na, “Mi aa tonghang azaa emande epeng e Isrela kane wilǝ belle.”
MAT 15:25 Na ondaye ome wa deya nawa girwǝ ba ting kai aaka bose kai kangza na, “Ateokora kangkamang!”
MAT 15:26 Na Yeso kabare na, “Wata gwara a jeke epa olya ayana ka kare e ere ne.”
MAT 15:27 Na ondaaye me bekaa na, “Nyimia Ateokora, pate kaa nyimi, e ere donge ma ngmeskarong maaka ma taaru ba deze araaka ateakwilǝ lyeeze epa olya ne.”
MAT 15:28 Na Yeso kabare naka bekaa ondaye me na, “Ondaye o eke lenyong leo ba Ashili wa gong, baya epa eeka oya gera me, e itǝ nyimi.” Ka o bekaa nyimi na obere oburu me wa arnang ka kagala kame.
MAT 15:29 Nangka Yeso ka baya a rame naka tare bee dǝki lepong le Galili. Naka zale ba zaa oyara naka cikǝ ba saname.
MAT 15:30 Na aromo acak ne deya kai. Nane de kaa ana ozantǝ, arǝ, agǝdǝ, ka arara, aa ana ondo ba cak, nane eke ne aa begeshe be Yeso naka womza ne.
MAT 15:31 Na epame tere apate aromo tukpwei azaa obena arara neya beya ngmǝ, agǝdǝ ya teweno, arǝ neya gonta, na pate one ne saba Ashili a maIsrela.
MAT 15:32 Azaa nyimi na Yeso ka rare atoma o kai naka bekaa nee na, “Eyang kona egonegone aromo aana, tomore to taaro naana o ngmeengme teye legwa kaane aa neta ne lya epa olya ne, kangza anta yeme o baya one aane ale ekomo ne adorana tana ne sau orona ne.”
MAT 15:33 Na atoma kai ne kabare nane bekaa kai na, “A baba te era a te cǝ epaolya a nyimi lerambo leena kate nya aromo acake aana?”
MAT 15:34 Na Yeso pirkǝ nee na, “Ma borode ma wondaa eye kaa mai?” Nane kabare na, “O sondaare kaa ekwala a baate.”
MAT 15:35 Naka ote aromo aa cake name nane cikǝ ba deze,
MAT 15:36 Nangka ka jeke maborode o sondaare ka ekwala me, naka wore o kona oleba ba Ashili, aaka pose mai aaka nya atoma kai, na nee kangza ne arseze aromo amea ne kurkǝnǝng.
MAT 15:37 Pate one ne lye na komana one tii, na atoma kurki ma ngmeskarong maaka ma lyǝ nama panza makende ma moole sondaare.
MAT 15:38 O gongha aromo aaka ne lye epaolya me ne dukǝ andaleme magu ma naaze bangka andaye kaa ayana.
MAT 15:39 Malo arnang ka aromo me, naka zale o onggo o taara manyi naka ale a makeke ma magadan.
MAT 16:1 Na maParisa kaa maSadukiya ne deya a Yeso adorana ne kedeya kai, nane bose kai ka ka wore ne epa o tera ukpwei ooka wayo wore o bare o kai.
MAT 16:2 Naka kabare nee na, “Ulyǝlu waaya, ke laka azaa shili aaya aa ganggo e bekaana, ‘Ahaa, ara yo ya aa sangsang leere.’
MAT 16:3 Ara a sana a leleere kangza e laka azaa shili aya a ganggo, na masanto mame maa kabare kuruwǝ ee bena, ‘Ulyi wayo ngmeza o ngmeengme.’ E ama orosa nangka zaa shili ze, aa eta ama orosa epaeka awere ana ya nyimi me ne.
MAT 16:4 Aromo awere ana, ana odera o tare Ashili, ana leyau, ana a nyong aburu, ana ogera epa otera ukpwei, aa ato wore ne epa o tera ukpwei ne, soona e Yonana. Na Yeso arnang ka ne a ka ale.
MAT 16:5 Nangka atoma Yeso ne cakate aa ale owulu lepong leme, nane winǝ o jeka oborode.
MAT 16:6 Na Yeso bekaa ne naa, “Eza na ba sauwo, ka o yisti o maParisa kaa o maSadukiya.”
MAT 16:7 Na ne bore o pirǝ tukpwei tone na, “Ka beka epaana ba eza azaa obena teta te deya ko borode ne na?”
MAT 16:8 Nangka Yeso ka laka nyimi, a ka rose madoola mane naka beka nee na, “Ying ana o kabare kaa mi aa baate, eyaaka eya masanggo obena eta ka o borode ne?
MAT 16:9 Aa deya wereena e tata a maring na? E winǝ nangka ma lye ka aromo magu esu ka a agwataka ma o borode maaname esu sang? Makende ma wonda e panza kaa maa epa eeka e lyǝ?
MAT 16:10 Koona awere aaka ma lye ka aromo magu ma naaze ka ma borode o sondaare, makende ma wonda e panza kaa epa eeka e lyǝ?
MAT 16:11 Eyaka eta ama o rosa obena anta beya oroka aza o borode ne? Epa eka eyang yeme e rose eya ezana ba sauwo ka o yisti o maParisa kaa maSadukiya.”
MAT 16:12 Arakanamea atoma Yeso ne rose obena kataa beya a zo yisti o kareze ba o borode ne, aa kaya beya kane eza ba sauwo kaa obaala maParisa kaa maSadukiya.
MAT 16:13 Nangka Yeso ka de aa bekazo be makeke ma Kaisariya o Pilibi, naka pirkǝ atoma kai na, “Aromo ne beya kena ka oromo na mana kai?”
MAT 16:14 Na ne kabare na, “Ana ondo ne beya na Yohana o Batisma, aana ondo beya na Iliya, aana ondo kangza beya naa, Irimiya, na ondo ba nyimi ana o beya angmǝ kama mawo ma Ashili.”
MAT 16:15 Naka pirkǝ nee na, “A ying pa, e beye na mia mana?”
MAT 16:16 Na Siman Biturusu kabare na, “Boa Almasipu, Kena ka Ashili ondo ebeene.”
MAT 16:17 Na Yeso kabare naka bekaa wai na, “Bo ondo kona oleba wai, Siman kena ka Yonana! Obena oromo ka lepung ka manyau waya ta waa belo ne, soona Ate ang omea waya nyimia shili.
MAT 16:18 Eyang bele au, boa Biturusu, azaa lecale leena eyang sowa akwilǝ ang, aaka legoone le ogbwǝ leto ama kaa ai ne.
MAT 16:19 Eyang nyau becapa be togomo to shili. Kangza epaaka ba tera a lerambo leena, eyo itǝ nyimi ba zaa shili, a epaaka ba dinggǝ a lerambo leena eyo itǝ ka o dinggǝ a nyimia shili.”
MAT 16:20 Naka windi atoma kai toto na tana ne bele ondo na kai ya Almasipu ne.
MAT 16:21 Oo era lengme lenname na ka bore o wore atoma kai na kayo dongdong ale ba Urushalima, a sanamea kayo lyǝ kombela o zitǝ aa taara te anateandasau, kaa ana magame ma Ashili, kaa ana obaala angmǝ ka Ashili a nya Mosa, kangza aane wongha kai, aa lengme le o taaro aaka era ka ebeene.”
MAT 16:22 Na Biturusu kuri ka Yeso aa sara yende nawa zurki kai na, “Tana Ashili baya epaana eye ne, Ateokora! Enna to manau ne.”
MAT 16:23 Na Yeso ringgarnu naka beka a Biturusu na, “Arnang kaa mi, Shetan! Bo epaa o ote ong kang cǝwǝ, bo o eze madoola mau ma oromoa, ma Ashili ta za ne.”
MAT 16:24 Na Yeso ka bekaa atoma kai na, “Pate ondooka waya yeme o tare ong, awa nyane ukpwei o wai a wa ana uti o gendare o wai a wa tareng.
MAT 16:25 Pate ondooka waya yeme o boza ebeene e wai, wayo dera e. Aa ondooka wayo dera ebeene e wai a za ong, wayo cǝ e.
MAT 16:26 Ebelo epa edang ngha oromo yo cǝ, wa cǝ pate lerambo leena a wa dera ebene e wai? Eya oromo wa era wa nya aa bekazo be ebeene e wai?
MAT 16:27 Kena ka oromo kaya deya ka togomo te Ate o kai kaa aa toma ozaa shili, kangza kayo nya komana epaaka e itǝ e wai a zo ogole omea komana wa eza.
MAT 16:28 “Ang dongdong bele ying, ana ondo ka neya itǝ arakana neto gbwǝ ne, seeka ne laka o deya kena ka Oromo ba nyimi togomo te kai.”
MAT 17:1 Malo tomore o taashe na Yeso ka jeke Biturusu, ka Yakubu, a orone kai oka a beya wai na Yohana, naka ale kaa ne o oyara o yende oo zaati, na ne cikǝ saname ne belle.
MAT 17:2 Na nangka kaze, sara aa begeshe bene, na mainu ma kai ma santo na ongme, aa madibi maaka ka amba, na ma itǝ maa peng.
MAT 17:3 Na ongmere liizi, na ana o beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili Mosa ka Iliya ne surǝ baa tera one a neya beya angmǝ ka Yeso.
MAT 17:4 Na Biturusu beka Yeso na, “Ateokora, wa gwara ka teye arakana. Ba kabare ang sowa mapuki ma taaro arakana, oyende a au, a oyende o Mosa a oyende kangza o Iliya.”
MAT 17:5 Waya zo beya angmǝ naname na owere yende oma santo wa urǝ ne, aane kone lengmelo le yende ba nyimi owere me a le beka na, “Kando kaana kena kang, ka oyeme ong maleo, ang kang kona oleba kai. Konana kai!”
MAT 17:6 Nangka atoma kai ne kone nyimi na boome moke ne maleu, na ne rizi baa deze.
MAT 17:7 Na Yeso ka de naka cokome ne aaka bekaa nee na, “Erana a itǝ, tane kone boome ne.”
MAT 17:8 Nangka ne ara tukpwei, nane ta laka ondo ne soona Yeso kai aa yende.
MAT 17:9 Aa neya zo jipi oyara me, na Yeso ka windi ne toto na, “Tane bele ondo epaaka e laka ne, soona aa ara Kena ka Oromo malo ogbwǝ kai.”
MAT 17:10 Na atoma kai ne pirkǝ kai na, “Nyimia waaza, eyaka ana o baala angmǝ aaka Ashili a nyana Mosa ne beeze na dongdong Otoma Ashili Iliya waya yaa deya o bora?”
MAT 17:11 Na Yeso kabare na, “Iliya wayo dongdong deya kawa babara ekeeya.
MAT 17:12 Pate ka nyimi eyang bele oying, Iliya wa samba o deya, na eta ee rose naa waya ne, nane eze wai epaaka ne ama o ezaa me. Nyimia kangza Kena ka Oromo yo zitǝ ba taara tone.”
MAT 17:13 Na atoma Yeso ne rose obena kaya beya one a ngmǝ ba zaa Yohana ondo batisma.
MAT 17:14 Nangka ne dukǝ araaka aromo ne gwarnang ne, na oromo yende wa deya Yeso nawa girwǝ ba begeshe be kai awa bekaa na,
MAT 17:15 “Ateokora, kona egonegone kena kang, ka ya ka letaranggi, kangza leya gǝǝzǝ kai maleo. Le rabo aa peere okai a nyimi ola kaa nyimi manyi.
MAT 17:16 Nang ale ka kai a atoma au, nane ta ama o womza kai ne.”
MAT 17:17 Na Yeso kabare naka bekaa na, “Ying aromo awereena, ana o dera o kabare ka Ashili, kangza ana ara aburu! Aa alea aa werea yemea eyang cikǝ ba nyimi oying? Aa alea aa werea yemea ang motana ka ying? Deyana ka kai arakana.”
MAT 17:18 Na Yeso ka zurki obere oburu me, na obere oburu me wa arnang ka kena kame. Na o ngmere liizi na kena kame ka woma.
MAT 17:19 Na atoma Yeso ne deya kai ba sara yende, na ne pirkǝ kai na, “Eyaka teta te ama o sǝǝrǝ obere oburu me ne?”
MAT 17:20 Na Yeso bekaa nee na, “O kabare ka Ashili oying wata gongha ne. Eyang dongdong bele oying, eeya ka o kabare kaa Ashili na beyo bee baate be o mosta, eyo ama bekaa oyara na wa mukuru araaka wa zene, kawa ye nyimi. Eyapa eto girǝ ying ne.
MAT 17:21 Ebelo onname, wata susǝ ne soona ka obeya angmǝ ka Ashili kangza ka opate ongmǝ.”
MAT 17:22 Nangka atoma Yeso ne kurkǝnǝng a makeke ma Galili, na Yeso ka bekaa nee na, “Ayo nya Kena ka Oromo ba taara ta aromo,
MAT 17:23 neyo wongha kai. Aa lengme lo taaro kangza ayo ara kai.” Na pate one ne kone oburǝ.
MAT 17:24 Malooka Yeso kaa atoma kai ne dukǝ Kaparnahum, na ana o eesa e mate akwilǝ Ashili nane mana Biturusu, na ne pirkǝ wai na, “Ondo baala oying wata nyaza emate akwilǝ Ashili ne na?”
MAT 17:25 Nawa bekaa na, “Ka arseze. “Nangka wa kurǝ ba akwilǝ, na Yeso bora o beya angmǝ ka wai naka beka na, “Ba laka nannia Siman Biturusu azaa be pirǝ beena? Aana mana agomo lerambo leena ne eesa emate e makeke ne, ara ayana anea naa, ana ondoai?”
MAT 17:26 Na Biturusu kabare na, “Aana ondo,” na Yeso bekaa na, “Obena ayana ane ta arsaza ne.
MAT 17:27 Pate ka nyimi, adorana tana aromo me ne mungi kaa ro ne, ale ba lepong ka o tare beruu be omeese ekwala, bekwala beeka baa bora a moke me o pǝri ongmǝ be oyo cǝ emate eeka eyo bare. O jeke mate me ka o are e mate makeke mau kaa a‘eng.”
MAT 18:1 Awere name na atoma Yeso ne deya akai, nane pirkǝ na, “Mana kala o gongha a nyimi togomo te zaa shili?”
MAT 18:2 Naka rare kena ka baate ka yende, naka eke kai baa tera one,
MAT 18:3 aka bekaa na, “Eyang dongdong bele oying, eeta kurǝ ka e itǝ naa abana ayana aana ne, eto lyǝ ba togomo ta zaa shili ne.
MAT 18:4 Pate ondooka wa jipǝrǝ ukpwei wai naa ka bana kena kaana, waya wa kala o gongha a togomo te zaa shili.
MAT 18:5 Pate ondooka wa kabare ka kabana kena naa kaana, mia wa embang.”
MAT 18:6 Pate ka nyimi, ondooka wa ote kena ka yende ba nyimi abana ayana aaka ne kabare kaa mi ka ka ye madinǝ, wayo kala aa tere wai onyanto aa lengmelo, a tare wai ba nyimi o pong o gerpo.”
MAT 18:7 Ee lyǝ udi lerambo, aza epa eeka e oteze aromo kane ye madinǝ! Dongdong ngha ebelo epaana eye, pate ka nyimi ondo ote ka a cǝwǝ, wa lyǝ udi.
MAT 18:8 Aa o ara o, na obona o, wa ote ka o lyǝ a madinǝ, mara o core wa ka opere. Wa kala o lyǝ ara e ebeene o dera o maro kaa o ara yende, na obona yende, na ka legǝdǝ, koo bena tareo ola kaa wata lumbuzu ne ka tobona to leere, ka taara te leere teo a pate.
MAT 18:9 Kangza Liizi leo le otezeo ko lyǝ a madinǝ lopa le ka o pere. Wa gwara o lyǝ ara ebene o dera o maro ka liizi le yende, ka o bena o ale akwilǝ ola ka yizi leere.”
MAT 18:10 “Ekena toto, tane zeele kena ka yende baa nyimia ayana na ne. Eyang belo ying, atoma ane o dera apung o nyimia shili ne gonte mainu ma Ate ang omea waya nyimia shili konang were.
MAT 18:11 Obena Kena ka Oromo ka deya ka ka boze andaaka ne wilǝ.
MAT 18:12 “Eya madoola maying? Ondo waya ka emande lewinu, na kayende ka wilǝ, wato baya etuuru torai ka o torai name aa ting oyara aa wa ale ba gera ka yende kanname sang?
MAT 18:13 Wa cǝ kai, eyang dongdong bele oying, wayo kona oleba maleo o kala etuuru torai ka otorai eeka eta e wilǝ ne.
MAT 18:14 Nyimia, Ate oying azaa shili wato kona oleba a kena ka yende ba nyimi ayana na ka wili ne.”
MAT 18:15 “Aa orone o wa yau tambo bo, o ale ka o bele wai epaaka wa yau, ying ngha leere belle. Wa kona epaaka ba bele wai, baa kuriyǝ orone o orona naname.
MAT 18:16 Waata konau ne, o ale ka oromo yende na a leere kane laka aane kone, adorana angmǝ me itǝ ka ma ganggang a begeshe be aromo leere, na a taaro.
MAT 18:17 Wa nyana kona one, o bele akwilǝ ana o tare Ashili, kangza waata kona nee ne, o kuriyǝ wai a nyimi andaaka neta rosa Ashili ne na ondo eesa emate o makeke.”
MAT 18:18 “Eyang dongdong bele oying, pate epaaka e tera a lerambo leena, awa itǝ epaaka a samba o tera me ba zaa shili. Pate epaaka e dinggǝ a lerambo leena, eyo itǝ ka o dinggǝ a zaa shili.
MAT 18:19 “Eyang dongdong wala o bele oying na, aromo leere ba nyimi lerambo leena ne kabare ka tukpwei tone ba za epaaka neya bosa me, Ate ang omea waya nyimia zaa shili wayo nya ne.
MAT 18:20 Pate araaka aromo leere, na a taaro ne gwarnang ba nyimi leze leng, eyang cikǝ legwa kaa ne.”
MAT 18:21 Na Biturusu paka ting Yeso nawa pirkǝ na, “Ateokora, ka wondaa orone ong wa tambo a mi ang pisi wai? Ka o sondaare na?”
MAT 18:22 Na Yeso bekaa na, “Ka o sondaare belle dai, ka o sondaarea o dukǝa etuuru sondaare.
MAT 18:23 “Aza nyimi ayo kedeya togomo te a zaa shili ka ogomo omea waya yeme o eza abalo ocǝ wai ka eeya taara te azara wai.
MAT 18:24 Nangka wa bore obala ocǝ wai me, naa de ka ondo omea ogomo me tare wai emate magu betuuru.
MAT 18:25 O bena wato ama o ara me ne, na ateakwilǝ wai wa ote ka a lishi wai ka ondaye wai ka ayana wai ka pate magogoro ma wai, ka a are uduru me.
MAT 18:26 Na ozara me tunggunu a begeshe be wai a wa bose wai na, “Ateakwilǝ tana o mungi ne, eyang arau ba pat.”
MAT 18:27 A aza obena ateakwilǝ me wa kone egonegone ozara me, nawa baya a wai kaa uduru me.
MAT 18:28 “Nangka ozara me wa ere arakaname, ka o surǝ wai nawa laka oja lezara awai, ka wa tare wai uduru o kap, emate lewinu. Nawa moke lengmelo le wai, a wa beka wai na, “Arang pate epaaka ang taroo.”
MAT 18:29 Na oja lezara me bose wai naa tana wa mungi ne eyang arau.”
