MAT 18:30 Na ozara me ta kabare ne, nyimia na wa ale ka wai na pate wai akwilǝ andaleme, seena wa are emate uduru me.
MAT 18:31 Nangka aja lezara le wai ne kone epaaka eya ale, neta ne kone oleba nyimi ne. Nane ale ba ateakwilǝ one nane bele wai epaaka ozara name wa ya.
MAT 18:32 Na ateakwilǝ me wa rare wai, nawa beka wai na, “Bo ozara oburua wai. Ma bayau ka uduru ooka ang taro aza obena ba de na obosheng,
MAT 18:33 wa ta gwara o kone egonegone o beja be lezara lo nangka maa kona egonegone o sang?”
MAT 18:34 Na ateakwilǝ wai wa mungi ka wai, aa wa ote na a gǝǝzǝ wai, aa wa ote wai na wa are pate epaaka a tare wai.
MAT 18:35 Nyimia kangza Ate ang o nyimia zaa shili wayo ya kaa komana o ying, eeta pisǝ andaa ying kaa lenyong le yende ne.”
MAT 19:1 Nangka Yeso ka mare obeya angmǝ me a pate, naka baya makeke ma Galili aaka lyǝ aa makeke ma Yahudiya, mamea mayo o tara obeno Urdung.
MAT 19:2 Na aromo a cak ne tare kai, naka womza ana makono aa saname.
MAT 19:3 Na maParisa ma yende ne deya a kai adorana ne kedeya kai, nane pirǝ na, “Azaa o baala makili Mosa, wa gwara obena oromo wa pere ondaye o wai aza ekeeya na?”
MAT 19:4 Naka kabare nee na, “Eta tukǝ soola obena, ondooka wa ye ne o bora, wa ye nea ondaleme kaa ondaye sang?”
MAT 19:5 Na akang bekaana, “Aza nyimi, oromo wa arnang kaa iini wai kaa ate a wai, a wa gwarnang ondaye wai. Neya leere kane itǝ lepung le yende.
MAT 19:6 A ale a izi neto itǝ apung a leere ne, leyendea yo za. Epaaka Ashili a gwaara tana oromo wa are ne.”
MAT 19:7 Nane beka kai na, “Nyimia waaza, eyaaka Mosa wa ote na a nya e wela omaro o amare, akang pere ondaaye?”
MAT 19:8 Na Yeso kabare naka bekaa nee na, “Azaa obena eye kaa anyong a katakau waya wa ote na Mosa kabare na e nya e wela opere amare, obora nyimia ta za ne.
MAT 19:9 Eyang bele oying kangza, pate ondooka wa arnang ka ondaye wai, azaa leyau lee taza ne, awa kang ale kawa ana ondaye yende kawa ote odo, wa ya epa e madinǝ naname. Ondooka wa ote ondaye omea a pere wai ba odo, wa ya leyau.”
MAT 19:10 Na atoma kai bekaa kai na, “Nyimia waaza a tera ondaleme kaa ondaye wai, odera o ana ondaye me wa kala.”
MAT 19:11 Naka bekaa nee na, “Komana wa era wata kabare ka oroka me ne, soona andaaka Ashili a kangkama ne.
MAT 19:12 Ana ondo ne zene ka a ngmeng ne agbele, ana ondo aromoa ne ote ne nane itǝ agbele. Ana ondo kangza ne tere o bena neto ana andaaye ne obena neya yeme togomo te zaa shili. Pate ondooka wayo ama o jeka orokaana, awa jeke.”
MAT 19:13 A were name, na ca Yeso ayana aa batebate adorna ka eke ne o ara, a kakang beye angmǝ kaa Ashili aa za one, na atoma kai ne zurki ba andaaka ne deya ka ayana me.
MAT 19:14 Na Yeso bekaa nee na, “Bayana ayana a batebate aa ne deya mi, tane nara nee ne, obena togomo te zaa shili te ebelo ene te.”
MAT 19:15 Na ka eese taara to kare o leba ba za one, aaka ale teweno te kai.
MAT 19:16 Aya zaa nyimi na ondo paka ting Yeso nawa bekaa na, “Ondo baala, obelo edang ka maa eze ang cǝ ebeene o dera o maro?”
MAT 19:17 Na Yeso kabare wai naa, “Eyaaka oya pirǝ ong ba zaa epa edang? Ashili aya belle aye ka edang. Baaya yeme o cǝ ebeene odera o maro, o tare makili ma Ashili maana.”
MAT 19:18 Nawa beka Yeso na, “Makili ma Ashili maa yeme?” Na Yeso bekaa na, “Tana o wong ondo ne, tana o eze leyau, tana o eze bekǝri ne, tana o beye majǝkǝri ne.
MAT 19:19 Nya ate au ka iini o ogongha one. Kangza oo yeme ondooka wa cikǝ ating au, na ukpwei o.”
MAT 19:20 Na Ondasau me bekaa kai na, “Ma eza nyimi ba pat, eya tata mi kangza?”
MAT 19:21 Na Yeso bekaa wai na, “Ba ya yeme o cikǝ zora madinǝ, ale ka o lishi pate magogoro mau, o jeke emate me ka o nya ana o dera eyapa oyo itǝ ondo ocǝ aa zaa shili. O ama o de ka o tareng.”
MAT 19:22 Nangka ondasau me wa kone nyimi, nawa sokoo ale ka o caro lenyong, obena waya ka ocǝ maleu.
MAT 19:23 Na Yeso bekaa atoma kai na, “Eyang dongdong bele oying, wayo poba kaa ondo ocǝ wa lyǝ ba nyimi togomo ta zaa shili.
MAT 19:24 Eyang kang bele oying. Mara orongkoome wa lyǝ a le'o beberkena ka obena ondo ocǝ wa lyǝ ba nyimi togomo to Ashili.”
MAT 19:25 Nangka atoma Yeso ne kone nyimi, na epame tera ne tukpwei maleo, nane bekaana, “Nyimia waaza, mana wa era wa cǝ o boza?
MAT 19:26 Na Yeso laka ne aaka bekaa na, “Enna ara aromo e pobe oya, ara Ashili ekeeya e era eye.”
MAT 19:27 Na Biturusu kabare nawa bekaana, “Ro naana, te arnang ka ekeeya azaa o tare o. Eya teyo cǝ?
MAT 19:28 Na Yeso bekaa nee na, “Eyang dongdong bele oying, a tomore to deya, awereaka Kena ka Oromo yo cikǝ aa ledǝndǝ lee gong le togomo to kai, ying ka e tareng, eyo cikǝ ara to cikǝ be tuuru ka leere, e core angmǝ ba zaa tokwilǝ be tuuru ka leere a maIsrela.
MAT 19:29 Kangza pate ondooka wa baya tokwilǝ, kaa arone andaleme, na arone andaaye, kaa ate, kaa iini, na ayana, na turu, ba za leze leng, wayo cǝ o ripitini liwinu, a wa kang cǝ ebene odera omaro.
MAT 19:30 Bangka nyimi, aromo a cak ana o bora neyo itǝ ana o maare, aa ana o maare neyo itǝ ana o bora.”
MAT 20:1 “Togomo ta zaa shili a kedeya te kaa ateakwilǝ yende, omea wa suri ba leleere nawa jeke ana ogole ba nyimi ara a wai a mati ma inabi.
MAT 20:2 Nangka wa beye ejamane kaa ne ba za o dinari yende konang owere, nawa turki ne ba nyimi ara me.
MAT 20:3 Aa ya gera beru be torai be leleere nawa suri kangza, nawa laka ana ondo ba cikǝ zora epa o eza a bengmǝ ba ara ejamane.
MAT 20:4 Nawa beka ne na, “Ying kangza ale na ba ara a mati ma inabi mang, eyang nya ying epaaka wa gwara a nya ying.” Nane ale.
MAT 20:5 Nangka wa kang surǝ a ongme wa dukǝ tera, kangza kaa beru be o taaro ulyǝlu, nyimia nawa kang jeka ana ogole.
MAT 20:6 Nangka beru be esu beye, nawa kang surǝ nawa laka ana ondo ba itǝ, nawa beka nee na, ‘Eyaka e were ba cikǝ zora epa o eza?’
MAT 20:7 Nane kabare wai na, “Ondo taa wa nya ro ogole ne.” Nawa bekaa nee na, “Ying kangza ale na ba ara a mati ma inabi mang.”
MAT 20:8 Nangka ulyǝlu waye baa cuwu, na ondo ara o mati ma inabi wa bekaa ondo o kangkama o wai a soola ogole o me na, ‘Rare ana ogole me ka o arseze ne epa eka e itǝ e komana, o bore ba ana o maare ba ale ana o bora.’
MAT 20:9 Nangka andaaka ne bore ogole ba ulyǝlu ba cuwu ne de, na komana one a nya wai be dinari be yende.
MAT 20:10 Nangka andaaka a jeke ne ba obora ne de, nane eke lenyong oo bena neyo cǝ o kala o nyimi. Neema na komana one wa cǝ be dinari be yende.
MAT 20:11 Nangka komana one wa cǝ epaaka a nya wai nane wore odera o kona oleba ba ateakwilǝ me,
MAT 20:12 aane beye na, “Andaaka a jeke ne oo maare ogole o beru be yendea belle ne eze, na ba ara ro nangka ba ara ne, ro ka tee were ba aa gole aa nyimi ongme.”
MAT 20:13 Nawa kabare ondo ba nyimi one na, “Oja, anta ma iru ne. Teta te beya na eyang nyau o dinari yende ne?
MAT 20:14 Emba epaeka te beya kaa bo o ale. Mia maa zaka na ma nya ana o maare ba kap ka nangka ma nyau.
MAT 20:15 Anta ka obare kang ye epaaka ang ama oya me ka epa eng sang? Aa bo ota ba kona oleba epaeka ma ya e rere naname ne na?”
MAT 20:16 Baa zaa nyimi ana o maare neyo itǝ ana obora, aa ana obora neyo itǝ ana o maare.”
MAT 20:17 Awereaka Yeso kaa atoma kai neya zala ba Urushalima, na Yeso itǝ kaa ne be daki orona aka beka nee na,
MAT 20:18 “Teya ale ba Urushalima. Aya nya kena ka oromo ba taara ta andaamoole ama magame ma Ashili, kaa ana o baala angmǝ aka Ashili a nya Mosa, neyo core angmǝ ba zaa kai ka a wong kai.
MAT 20:19 Neyo niyi kai ba taara ta maYahuda kane zeele kai, aane ole kai, aane kang gendare kai ba zaa uti. A lengme lo taaro kangza ayo ara kai.”
MAT 20:20 Na iini ayana Zabadi paka ba ting Yeso kaa ayana kai, naka girwǝ ba begeshe be kai, aa ka bose eyapa ba kai.
MAT 20:21 Na Yeso beka kai na, “Eya oya yeme me?” Naka beka kai na, “Ote ayana ang a leere aana ka ne cikǝ, ka yende o ara ore o, aa ka yende o ara o guri o, a nyimi togomo teo.”
MAT 20:22 Na Yeso kabare naka beka ba ayana me na, “Eta rosa epaeka eya bosaza me ne, eyo ama o sa o gǝǝzǝ omea eyang sa na?” Nane bekaa kai na, “Teyo ama.”
MAT 20:23 Naka bekaa ne na, “Eyo dongdong sa a ka poto kang, a obena e cikǝ ba o ara o re na o guri, mia taza ka o bare nya me ne. Ate ang o zaa shili wa babara araname azaa andaaka aa zaka.”
MAT 20:24 Nangka o dangare atoma kai be tuuru ne kone nyimi, na ne mungi ka ayana leere name.
MAT 20:25 Na Yeso rare ne na ka bekaana, “Erose obena agomo a worme ne wore ne legoone, aa na o kangkama agomo me kangza ne wore ne obare.
MAT 20:26 Wato itǝ nyimi ba nyimi oying ne. Ba zaa nyimi pate ondooka waya yeme o itǝ ondo gong ba nyimi oying, seeka wa itǝ ozara oying.
MAT 20:27 Kangza ondooka waya yeme a wa itǝ ondo tare ka ying, seeka wa itǝ ozara oying.
MAT 20:28 Nyimia kangza Kena ka Oromo kata ka deya ka aromo eze kai lezara ne, ka deye adorana kai ka itǝ ozara, na ka nya ebene kai adorana ka boze aromo ba cak.”
MAT 20:29 Nangka Yeso kaa atoma kai neya baya a nyimia Yariko na aromo ba cak ne tare kai.
MAT 20:30 Arǝ a leere neya cikǝ a be dǝki be orona. Nangka ne kone na Yeso yaa kala, nane ara lengmelo nane bekaana, “Ateokora, kona egonegone oro, Kena ka Daoda!”
MAT 20:31 Na aromo ne zurki baa ne kane kome. Kangza nane wale ara lengmelo ne maleo, aane beya na, “Ateokora, kona egonegone oro, Kena ka Daoda!”
MAT 20:32 Na Yeso itǝ aa ka bekaa nee na, “Eya eya yeme ang ye ying?”
MAT 20:33 Nane beka kai na, “Ateokora, teya yeme a te cǝ o gonta!”
MAT 20:34 Ba nyimi okona egonegone one, na Yeso ka moke ayizi ane, na ongmere liizi nane cǝ o gonta, aane tare kai.
MAT 21:1 Nangka Yeso kaa atoma kai ne dukǝ kapeng ka Betapaji kamea ka amara ka Urushalima, ba kulǝ oyara o mati ma Zaitun, na Yeso ka tong atoma kai a leere,
MAT 21:2 naka beka nee na, “Lyǝ na ba kapeng kaa niini ba izi oying. Ee lyǝ eyo laka kurungzǝ baa tera, ka kabana kame. Dinggǝ na e ka ecang.
MAT 21:3 Ondo wa pirkǝ, ying e beka wai na, Ateokora ya yeme one. Wayo kuriyǝ ee aa rabokoro.”
MAT 21:4 A ye nyimia adorana a panza epa eeka ondo beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili Zakariya beke obena,
MAT 21:5 “Ee bekaa kagala ka Sihiyona na, laka, Ogomo oying waya zo deya ba ying! Ondo o nata ukpwei wai, Waya zaa kabana kurungzǝ.”
MAT 21:6 Na atoma Yeso ne ale, nane ye epaaka Yeso ka bekaa ne.
MAT 21:7 Nane de kaa kurungzǝ ka kabana kame, nane nata ne madibi aa zaa one, a ka zale.
MAT 21:8 Na aromo ba cak ne nata madibi mane ba zaa orona, aana ondo gera marane ma mati nane eese ba zaa orona.
MAT 21:9 A okurkǝnǝng aromo ka neya teweno ba izi ka kai kaa andaaka neya dimǝ kai, nane ara angmelo aane beya na, “Hosana Kena ka Daoda! Okona oleba wa itǝ o kando ko deya ba nyimi leze le Ateokora! Hosana o Ashili!”
MAT 21:10 Nangka Yeso ka lyǝ baa nyimi Urushalima na pate apeng me a bitǝkǝrnu, aane beya naa, “Mana waana?”
MAT 21:11 Na aromo aaka neya tare o Yeso bekaana, “Kanna kando ka o beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili Yeso kamea ka surǝa Nazarat o makeke ma Galili.”
MAT 21:12 Na Yeso ka lyǝ akwilǝ Ashili naka tarangga ana o lisǝzǝ kaa ana o eesa magogoro baa nyimi me, naka bitǝkǝri pate matara mana o saara emate me, kaa matara ma o lisǝsǝ egoma e akwilǝ.
MAT 21:13 Naka bekaa nee na, “A wele obena, ‘Ayo rara akwilǝ ang aro beya angmǝ kaa Ashili, na ying e kuriyǝ ai aro baasaza ana o tǝǝru aromo.’ ”
MAT 21:14 Na arǝ kaa agǝdǝ ne deya baa kai a nyimi akwilǝ Ashili naka womza ne.
MAT 21:15 Nangka andaamoole magame ma Ashili, kaa ana o baala angmǝ aka Ashili a nya Mosa ne laka epa o tera ukpwei eeka ka eza, aa ayana yaa saba Ashili ba nyimi akwilǝ Ashili a ne beya na, “Hosana Kena ka Daoda!” Na ne kone oburǝ maleo.
MAT 21:16 Nane bekaa kai na, “Oya konaza epaeka andaana ya beya me sang? Na Yeso beka ne naa, “Ma kona, azaa nyimi eta rosa obena a wele na, “Ba nyimi ongmǝ a abana ayana kaa akaa tata a asa, boa baa ote ka ne saboo sang?”
MAT 21:17 Naka arnang kaa ne, aaka suri ba nyimi apeng me, naka ale ba Betanya, aaka more saname.
MAT 21:18 Nangka ara a sane a kaya kurǝ ba nyimia apeng, na ekomo moke kai.
MAT 21:19 Nangka ka laka uti o uli ba ting orona, naka ale ba uti me naka ta cǝ eyapa o uti me ne soona marane belle. Naka beka uti me na, “Otoo ya ayana kangza ne!” Na ongmere liizi na uti me wa waka.
MAT 21:20 Nangka atoma kai ne laka nyimi, na epame e tere ne ukpwei nane bore be pirǝ na, “Eyaka uti uli na wa waka ba saseya?”
MAT 21:21 Na Yeso ka kabare naka beka ne naa, “Eyang dongdong bele oying maganggang maame, eeya ka o eke lenyong ba Ashili, zora madoola ma yende, epaaka e mana uti uli ona, eya eto eza belle ne, eyo ama o beka ba oyara ona, era, ka o taru ba nyimi opong ogong, a wayo itǝ nyimi.
MAT 21:22 Eeya ka o eke lenyong ba Ashili, pate epaaka e bosa ba Ashili eyo cǝ e.”
MAT 21:23 Nangka Yeso ka lyǝ ba nyimi akwilǝ Ashili, kaya aza obaala naname, na andaamoole magame ma Ashili, ka magonggong ma aromo nane deya kai ka be pirǝ na, “Ka legoone le mana oya eza magogoro maana? Kangza mana wa nyau legoone le me?”
MAT 21:24 Na Yeso ka kabare naka bekaa na, “Mima eyang eza o ying be pirǝ. E kabareng, mima eyang bele oying ka legoone le mana ang eze magogoro maana.
MAT 21:25 O batisma o Yohana, wa surǝ babaa? Ba zaa shili naa, ba aromoi?” Nane dambaraza a tukpwei tone obena, “Te bekaana, wa surǝ shili, kayo bekaa aro na, na eyaka eta e kabare kaa kai ne?”
MAT 21:26 Kangza te bekaana, “Wa surǝ ba aromo, teya kona boome be aromo, obena komana wa rose obena Yohana ondo beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili wai.”
MAT 21:27 Nane kabare Yeso na, “Teta rosa ne.” Na Yeso beka ne naa, “Nyimia mima anta a bele oying ka legoone le mana ang ezeze magogoro maana ne.”
MAT 21:28 “E laka nannia? Oromo yende wa zene kaa ayana leere andaleme. Nawa ale baa ka o bora, nawa beka kai na, “Kena kang ale ka o eza ogole ba ara o inabi.
MAT 21:29 Na kena kame beka na, “Anta ale ne.” Nangka a rabokoro naka sara madoola, aaka ale.
MAT 21:30 Na ate ame wa ale baa ka o leere kame, nawa beka kai epaaka wa beka a ka o bora. Na ka o leere bekaana, “Ma kona ate, eyang ale,” na kata ale ne.
MAT 21:31 Ba nyimi ayana leere me mana wa ye epaeka ate me wa yeme? Nane bekaana, “Ka o bora.” Na Yeso bekaa nee na, “Eyang bele o ying epeng eme, ana o eesa emate e makeke kaa andaaye o lisǝzǝ apung ane neya kaana oying o lyǝ ba togomo ta Ashili.
MAT 21:32 Obena Yohana o batisma wa de nawa wore ying orona o rere, neeta kabare ka wai ne. Ba zaa nyimi na ana o eesa emate makeke kaa andaaye o lisǝzǝ apung ane ne kabare ka wai, aa ying pate ka o laka enna, malo nyimi na eta kabare a pisǝ madinǝ maying ne.”
MAT 21:33 “Angmǝ aa gerpo yendea aana kangza. Oromo yende wa zene ka waye kaa ara o inabi, nawa ringǝri ara me ka odarne, nawa kau le'o le noke ayana inabi a ara me, a kangza wa so odankee ona soola ara me. Malo nyimi nawa nya ana ogole yende lebose le ara me, a wa ale begere.
MAT 21:34 Nangka awere o sende e inabi me wa ye, nawa tong azara wai baa ana ogole me kane embe epaaka e itǝ e wai baa ne.
MAT 21:35 Na andaaka a bose ne ara me, ne meke azara me, nane ole o yende, aa ne wong o yende, aa ne teeze o taaro me.
MAT 21:36 Nawa kang tongha azara yende, amea ne kala obora, na andaaka a bose ne ara me, nane ye ne epaeka ne ye ana obora name.
MAT 21:37 Malo nyimi nawa tong kena ka wai baa ne, a wa eke obena, ‘Neyo laka o gongha kena kang.’
MAT 21:38 Nangka andaaka a bose ne ara ame ne laka kena ka oromo me, nane bekaa tukpwei tone na, “Aha, kando kaana ekeeya ara me aya itǝ a kai. A te wongha kai adorana ara me itǝ a aro.”
MAT 21:39 Na ne moke kai, aane tare kai ba malo o darne, nane wongha kai.
MAT 21:40 O ara aana wa deya, eya wayo ya kaa andaaka a bose ne ara ogole me?”
MAT 21:41 Nane beka kai na, “Wayo wongza ana anyong a buru me, awa bose ana ondo a ara me, andaaka neyo nyaza wai epaaka e itǝ e wai aa nyimi epa eeka ne cǝ.”
MAT 21:42 Na Yeso beka ne naa, “Eta tukǝ kona epaaka a wele ba nyimi angmǝ Ashili sang? O bena, “Lecale leeka ondo sowa wa nyana, leya lee itǝ le o kala ee dang o sowa odo. Onna o eza Ashilia wai, Epa o tera ukpwei aa yizi aro.”
MAT 21:43 “Ba zaa nyimi eyang bele oying, ayo emba togomo ta Ashili ba ying, ka nya a aromo makeke ma yende amea neyo wore o cikǝ o rere.
MAT 21:44 Ondooka wa rizi aza le cale leena, wayo poso. Aa ondooka le cale leme le taru ba zaa wai leyo nyanta wai naa ma'ena.”
MAT 21:45 Nangka ana magame ma moole kaa maParisa ne kone angmǝ me, nane rose obena, kaya beya baa za onea.
MAT 21:46 Na ne gere o moke okai, na boome ba aromo nara ne, obena pate aromo ne jeka kai ondo beya angmǝ kama mawo ma Ashili kai.
MAT 22:1 Na Yeso kang beka ne angmǝ a gerpo na,
MAT 22:2 “A era kedeya togomo ta shili kaa ogomo yende ooka wa eze kena ka wai ozǝnggǝ amare.
MAT 22:3 Na wa tong azara wai kane rare aromo aaka a baale ne o ozǝnggǝ me, na aromo amea a baale ne neta deya ne.
MAT 22:4 Na wa kang tongha azara wai yende nawa beka ne na, “Alena ka e bekaa andaaka a baale ne o ozǝnggǝ na, maa goro na ma core bena be lome be mate eena, epaolya ee yengha, amara ekeeya ane de.”
MAT 22:5 “Na andaaka a belene o amare me ta bala nee ne, na komana ale o ale awai, ondo wa ale ara awai, aa ondo ale ba ara ejamane awai.
MAT 22:6 O dangare one moke azara ame nane ole ne, a ne wong ne.
MAT 22:7 Ogomo me wa munggi aa cak, na wa tong ana otesa ageza aa moole awai, na ne wong aromo me, aane ese apeng ame ka ola aa pat.
MAT 22:8 Na wa bekaa azara awai na, ‘Amara ekeeya o amare me, aa andaaka a bele ne ta gwara ne de ne.
MAT 22:9 Tareze na marona, apate ondooka e laka ee bekaa wai na wa de ara o zǝnggǝ o amare me.’
MAT 22:10 Na azara me ale na ne rare apate andaaka nee laka, ana edang kaa ana odera edang, nyimia na apanza ogiishi me ka ageng.
MAT 22:11 “Aa nangka ogomo me wa lyǝ kawa laka ageng me, na wa laka ondo zora madibi ma ozǝnggǝ.
MAT 22:12 Na wa pirkǝ wai na, ‘Oja, aa wiinia na ba lyǝ arakaana zora o amba madibi ma ozǝnggǝ ne?’ Na oromo me ta ama obeka eyapa ne.
MAT 22:13 “Na ogomo me bekaa azara awai na, ‘Tera na taara ka tobona te wai, e tare wai a nyimi maring maa bo, ara aka ayo ruuzi ka ononza tuuni.’
MAT 22:14 “O bena aromo acakea aa rare, aa aromo a baate aa zaka.’ ”
MAT 22:15 Na maParisa gere orona ooka neyo moke kai aa nyimi angmǝ a kai.
MAT 22:16 Na ne tong ana otare one ka aromo a Hiridus yende, na ne beka ana, “Ondo baala, te rose beka ana bo ondo baala epengngha, o kang baala komaname orona Ashili, ota zaka ondo ne, ba jeka komaname oyende a bo.
MAT 22:17 Na beka aa ro epa eka ba laka, wa gwara te nya Kaisar emate makeke naa, na tana te nya nea?”
MAT 22:18 Yeso ka rose ara aburu aaka aya anyong ane, naka bekaana, “Ying ana anyong aburu! Eya ka eya kedeya ong?
MAT 22:19 “Worenna bemate beeka a arseze oma makeke mane.” Nane ca kai be dinari be me.
MAT 22:20 Na Yeso pirkǝ nee na ‘Mainu ka leze le mana ba azaa benna?’
MAT 22:21 Nane kabare kai na, “Ma Kaisar.” Na Yeso bekaa nee na, “Na nya na Kaisar epa eka e Kaisar e, ee nya Ashili epa eka a Ashili e.”
MAT 22:22 Nangka ne kona nyimi, na epa eme tere ne ukpwei, aane ale o ale one.
MAT 22:23 A lengme leme, na maSadukiya ka ne beyaana ata eere malo ogwǝ ne, na ne pirkǝ kai,
MAT 22:24 nane bekana, ‘Mosa wa bekaa na oromo wa gbwǝ zora ayana, orone o wai cikǝ kaa kandaye kame ka ka ngmengze wai ayana.’
MAT 22:25 Arone sondaare zene aa nyimi oro. Obora wa ana ondaaye, nawa gbwi zora kena, na ondaadimǝ wai cikǝ kaa ondaaye me.
MAT 22:26 Nyimia ondaadimǝ wai o leere, kaa o taaro, nyimia epame e ale a dukǝ pate one aa sondaare.
MAT 22:27 O maare apat, na ondaye me ma wa gbwi.
MAT 22:28 Na nannameena, aa lengme le o era malo ogbwǝ, wayo itǝ ondaaye mana a nyimi one, ka pate one nee cikǝ kaa wai?
MAT 22:29 Na Yeso bekaa nee na, madoola maying ta orona ne, ka eta rose angmǝ Ashili ka awela ne, kangza eta rose legoone le Ashili ne.
MAT 22:30 Lengme le o era malo ogbwǝ, o anza ondaye ta rene ne, aa onya ondaye kaa o oteze one a todo to rene ne, aza obena neyo kurǝ na atoma Ashili odera lepung aaza shili.
MAT 22:31 Azaa o era malo o gbwǝ, eta ee tukǝ o soola epaeka Ashili a beke aying ne na? A bekaana,
MAT 22:32 ‘Mia Ashili a Ibraheng, Ashili a Ishaku, kaa Ashili a Yakubu.’ Ashilia a pate andaaka neya ka ebeene, ana o gbwizǝ tazane.”
MAT 22:33 Nangka aromome ne kona nyimi, na epa eme tere ne ukpwei.
MAT 22:34 Nangka maParisa ne kone ana Yeso ka toza maSadukiya, nane gwaara tukpwei,
MAT 22:35 ondo o baala angmǝ aaka Ashili a nya Mosa aa nyimi one, wa eze Yeso be pirǝ adorana wa cǝ kawa meke kai.
MAT 22:36 Nawa bena, “Ondo o baala, oyeme kala ogongha a nyimi makili ma Mosa?”
MAT 22:37 Na Yeso kabare wai na, “Yeme Ateokora Ashili au kaa pate lenyong leo, kaa pate ebeene o, ka opate madoola mau.”
MAT 22:38 Onna obora kawa kala aa gongha apate.
MAT 22:39 Makili o leere ome kang ya na obora, ‘Yeme ondooka waya ating o na ukpwei o.’
MAT 22:40 Pate o baala o Mosa ka ana o beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili, ma ya azaa makili ma leere maana.”
MAT 22:41 Nangka maParisa ma yende ne kurkǝnǝng ara yende, na Yeso ka pirkǝ ne na,
MAT 22:42 “Eya madoola maying aza Almasipu? Kai kena ka manaa?” Nane kabare kai na, ‘Kena ka Daoda kai.’
MAT 22:43 Na Yeso bekaane na, “Na a wiinia na Daoda beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Obere o Sangsang, na wa rare kai na ‘Ateokora’? Aa wa bekana,
MAT 22:44 ‘Ateokora wa beka aa Ateokora ong na, “Cikǝ o ara o re ong, seeka ma eke ana o nyana o, aa tetau te tobona teo.” ’
MAT 22:45 Na Daoda wa rara Almasipu na ‘Ateokora’, aa wiinia aaka itǝ kena ka wai?
MAT 22:46 Ondo ta wa ama kabare a Yeso ne. O era a lengme leme, ondo ta wa kang ama o pirkǝ okai ne.
MAT 23:1 Nangka aromo ne kurkǝnǝng ba cake kaa atoma kai, na Yeso bekaane na,
MAT 23:2 “Ana obaala makili ma Mosa ka maParisa neya a nya ne uwǝri baala makili ma Mosa.
MAT 23:3 Azaa nyimi, tare na, eza pate epa eka ne beka ying, se na tane ezeze epa eka ne eze ne, ka ne baala aa neta ezeze epa eka ne baala ne.
MAT 23:4 Ne tesa aromo magogoro ma dendeng ka ma poba ana ba o malo, zora bekaana ne kankama ne ko ka lebo.
MAT 23:5 “Ekeeya ene ne ezaa ka aromo laka. Ne ezaza a gwada a molemole ka angmǝ a Ashili aaka a wele kane tese a madong mane ka taara tone, ne dozeze se jǝng se eewo ka ma dukǝ tulung te ne, ba taara te madibi mane.
MAT 23:6 Ne kala ara o eme ne cikǝ ara cisǝ anda mole ara o zǝnggǝ, a ne kang cikǝ ba izi aa nyimi o dandaro Ashili.
MAT 23:7 Aa ne kang yeme a beeze ne okoo ba ara ejamane, aa kang rara ne na, ‘Ana obaala’.
MAT 23:8 A ying, tana a rara ying ana ‘Ana obaala’ ne, ka ondo obaala o ying o yendea wai, aa pate oying arone ai.
MAT 23:9 Tana e rare ondo orambo na ana ‘Ate’ ne. Eya ka Ate a yendea ka aya zaa shili.
MAT 23:10 A tana rara ying ‘Andaano’ ne, obena eya ka ondoono o yendea belle, kaya Almasipu.
MAT 23:11 Wai ka wa kala ogongha ba nyimi oying wayo itǝ ozara oying.
MAT 23:12 Pate ondo oka wa ara ukpwei, ayo jǝpǝrǝ wai. Aa pate ondo oka wa jǝpǝrǝ ukpwei, ayo ara wai.
MAT 23:13 Eyo zitǝ, ying ana o baala makili ma Mosa ka maParisa, kaa ana rendaza! E pate aromo abuudu o lyǝ aa togomo te zaa shili, yingha tukpwei teying eta lyǝ ne, aa kang nara ana o eme ne lyǝ.
MAT 23:14 Eyo zitǝ, ana o baala angmǝ aaka Ashili a nya Mosa ka maParisa, ana o rendaza! E lyeeze magogoro ma andaye aka andaleme ane a gbwizǝ, e beya angmǝ ka Ashili o eo adorana aa laka ying. Azaa nyimi, o zitǝ oying wayo kala o komana.
MAT 23:15 Eyo zitǝ, ana obaala angmǝ aaka Ashili a nya Mosa ka maParisa, kaa ana o rendaza! E taare manyi ma gong, e aleze a makeke macangcang ba ogera ondo o kurǝ Ashili oyende. Aa e cǝ wai, e kang ote wa kala ying o wilǝ.
MAT 23:16 Eyo zitǝ, ying arǝ aaka ne windǝ aromo. E beeze na, ‘Ondo wa tono ka akwilǝ Ashili, eyapa taza ne, aa wa tono ka ozinari o akwilǝ Ashili, otono me yo lya wai.’
MAT 23:17 Ying arǝ, a rara! Oyeng ome kala ogongha, ozinari na, akwilǝ Ashili oka wa kwizǝzǝ ozinari e?
MAT 23:18 E beeze na, ‘Ondooka wa tono kaa ara o esaza Ashili mapapa mo waze, eyapa taa ne, aa pate ondooka wa tono ka epa eka a nata azame, le tono leyo moke wai.’
MAT 23:19 Ying arǝ! O yemea kala ogongha, epa eka aa nya Ashilia na, na a ara o esaza Ashili mapapa mo waze oka wa kwizǝzǝ epa eka a nya mea?
MAT 23:20 Azaa nyimi, oromo wa tono ka ara o esaza Ashili mapapa mo waze, wa tono ka ara o esaza Ashili mapapa mo waze aa pate epa eka a nata azame.
MAT 23:21 Aa Pate ondooka wa tono ka akwilǝ Ashili, wa tono ka wai ka Ashili ka aya nyimi ai.
MAT 23:22 Pate ondooka wa tono ka zaa shili kanza, wa tono kale dǝndǝ le Ashili ka ondo oka waya cikǝ aaza me.
MAT 23:23 Eyo zitǝ, ying ana o baala angmǝ aaka Ashili a nya Mosa ka maParisa, ying ana o rendaza! E nyaza Ashili le yende a nyimi betuuru epa e ecete ka ma nanggo, aa e pere epa eka ekala edang e makili ma Mosa, na obeya epeng, egonegone, ka o eza epa ee kap. Epa eka wa gwara e eza naname zora o baya ma dangare mame.
MAT 23:24 Ying arǝ aka ne windǝ aromo, e lobeze ecǝngci, aa e dongze orankome!
MAT 23:25 Eyo zitǝ, ana o baala angmǝ aaka Ashili a nya Mosa ka maParisa, ying ana o rendaza! E kwizǝzǝ malo topoto ka teso toying, a nyimi a pena le iri, ka o yeme ukpwei.
MAT 23:26 Bo, urǝ oParisa! Bora kwizǝ a nyimi oso ka opoto, adora a malo me ya a sangsang.
MAT 23:27 Eyo zitǝ, ana obaala makili ma Mosa ka maParisa, ying ana o rendaza! Eye na macao maaka a leleme ka egengge epeng. Ma rere olaka oo yanga, aa nyimi a pena kaa cako andaaka ne gbwizǝ kaa kombela madinǝ.
MAT 23:28 Nyimia ba ayizi aromo ying ana okona boome be Ashilia, aa nyimi anyong aying ana o rendaza, kaa ana ara aburu.
MAT 23:29 Eyo zitǝ, ana obaala makili ma Mosa ka maParisa, ying ana o rendaza! E sooze ana o beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili macao, kangza ezeze ejaaga a macau ma ana o kona boome be Ashili.
MAT 23:30 E beeze na, ‘Eya te rene a were a samba, te ta teyo gwara taara kane ba o wonghza ana obeya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili mame ne.’
MAT 23:31 Nyimia e wore bena ying ayana andaaka ne wonghza ana o beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili.
MAT 23:32 Lya na izi, maare na epa eka ma gonggong maying ma bore!
MAT 23:33 Ying ewa, kaa o kurkǝnǝng ewa e buru! Aa wiinia e bisi o gǝǝzǝ Ashili akwilǝ ola?
MAT 23:34 Azaa nyimi ma tongha ying ana o beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili, kaa ana orosa, kaa ana o baala angmǝ aaka Ashili a nya Mosa. E yo wongha ana ondo one, ee gendare ana ondo o uti, aa na ondo eyo ola ne aa nyimi ma dandaro maying, ee tarze ne aa topepeng ee gǝǝzǝ ne.
MAT 23:35 Nyimia aaza oying ayo gera manyau mana o dera madinǝ maaka a oke a lerambo, aa era a manyau ma ondo o sangsang Habila aa ale a Zakariya kena ka Berekiya, kamea e wongha aa tera akwilǝ Ashili ka ara o esaza Ashili mapapa mayo kurǝ aaza oying.
MAT 23:36 Na eyang baala oying, pate manna ma yo mana ayana nanname.
MAT 23:37 Urushalima! Urushalima! Bo ka ba wongze ana o beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili, aa o kang teeze andaaka aa tongha ba bo ka cale! Ka wondaa ma yeme o kurǝ oying nangka katokoro kuruzi ayana kai aa ma beko ma kai, na ee nyana.
MAT 23:38 Na awa nanname aa ba ying akwilǝ me na a itǝ makansǝng!
MAT 23:39 Mi sang eyang baala oying, eto kang lakang ne, se lengme leeka e bekaana ‘Ondo o kona leba ondooka waya deya ka leze le Ateokora.’
MAT 24:1 Nangka Yeso ka suri Akwilǝ Ashili me, kaya nyimi teyeno, na atoma akai de nane wore kai masosowa ma Akwilǝ Ashili me.
MAT 24:2 Na ka bekaa nee na, ‘Eya gonta pate masosowa maana? Eyang dongdong obele ying, ata baya le cale leyende kaa ayo baya aza leyende ne. Ayo bacakare ai aa pat.’
MAT 24:3 Yeso ka ya cikǝ oyara o Zaitun, na atoma akai ne deya kai aa suk, nane beka kai na, ‘‘Bele ro, ngmǝyamea aya eza mapa maana? Eya kangza eyo wore ro odeya o, ka omare lerambo?”
MAT 24:4 Na Yeso kabare nee, naka bekaana, “Eza na a sauwo, tana ondo rende ying ne.
MAT 24:5 Obena aromo a cake neyo deya aa nyimi leze leng, aane beyaa na, ‘Mia Almasipu’, ka ne rendeze aromo aa cak.
MAT 24:6 Eyo kang konaza marooka ma okara kaa ngmǝ acak azaa makara. Tana ekone boome ne, azaa obena dongdong nyimi yo ya, aa omaare tata suri.
MAT 24:7 Aromo apeng neyo gera aromo apeng yende bete, togomo teyo gera togomo te yende bete. Ayo eza ekomo kangza, kaa o zukǝrzu adeze, a kuruwǝ.
MAT 24:8 Aa pate ka nyimi, onna obora o zitǝa belle.
MAT 24:9 “Malo nyimi neyo niyi ying ka gǝǝzǝ ying, aa kang wongha ying. Pate aromo yo nyana ying aza leze leng.
MAT 24:10 A were na mea aromo acake yo rizi, neyo iri tukpwei, aa ne nyana tukpwei.
MAT 24:11 Atoma o rendaza a cake yo susǝ, aa ne rendeze aromo a cak.
MAT 24:12 Azaa waale ogongha araaburu, o yeme aromo acake yo kasarno.
MAT 24:13 Aa pate ondooka wa motana aa ale omaare wayo bisǝ.
MAT 24:14 Ayo kang baala orooka o leba o togomo te Ashili teena a pate kuruwǝ a nyimi lerambo leena. Malo o nyimi o maare de.”
MAT 24:15 “Azaa nyimi, pate awere aaka e laka epa e berebere, o deesa ka ocara, oo ka ondo obeya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili Daniyel wa beye angmǝ azaa me, aa waya itǝ ara aa sangsang. Ondo o soola awa rose.
MAT 24:16 Aa andaaka neya makeke ma Yahudiya songha ne lyǝ aa mayara.
MAT 24:17 Tana ondooka wa ya azaa akwilǝ jipi a jeka eyapa a nyimi akwilǝ me ne.
MAT 24:18 Ondooka waya ara kangza, tana wa kuri aa jeka odibi owai ne.
MAT 24:19 Andaye aaka neya ka etumǝ ka ana lewanyo, neyo zitǝ.
MAT 24:20 Bosa na Ashili tana tesong teying de aa lekoze na lengme le o teseke ne.
MAT 24:21 Aa werename ayo kala o ara ozitǝ, ombela ooka ata aa tukǝ ezame o era obora lerambo aa deya awereena ne. Ato kang sukǝ nyimi ne dakemeeme.
MAT 24:22 Bangka a kashe shengme sheme ne, ondo ta zene ka waa yoo bisǝ ne, obena andaaka Ashili a zaka ne rene, ayo kashe shengme sheme.
MAT 24:23 Awere name pate ondooka wa beka aying na ‘Almasipu waana!’ Koona, ‘Awa niini!’ Tana e kabare ne.
MAT 24:24 Ma Almasipu kaa ana o beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili ma orenda kaa neyo deesa, kane ezeze mapapa ma o tesa ukpwei, adorana ne wilǝrǝ pate ka andaaka Ashili a zake, nyimi waayo ya.
MAT 24:25 Konanna! Ma bekaa ying ka orabo.
MAT 24:26 “Nee bekaa ying na ‘Lakana, awa niini a owake, tana e ale ne.’ Nee kang bekaa ying na, ‘Awaana ara o baasa,’ tana e kabare ne.
MAT 24:27 Nangka malmi eze masanto aa surǝ aa dizi aa alea aza, nyimi o kurǝ o Kena ka Oromo yo itǝ.
MAT 24:28 Pate ara aaka ekeze rene, aya ejogaale kurkǝnǝzǝng ne.
MAT 24:29 “A saseya malo tomore te ozitǝ oo jǝng me, ‘ongme to kang ya masanto ne, oreka kangza wato nya masanto ne. Aa ewerewere yo tǝǝrǝ aa surǝ azaa shili, ayo zukǝ pate obare ooka waya azaa shili.’
MAT 24:30 Awere namea ayo laka o surǝ o Kena ka Oromo aaka surǝ aza shili, pate aleng aa lerambo leena neyo ruuzi, neyo laka Kena ka Oromo aa kaya deya aza mawere, ka obare kaa togomo tee gong.
MAT 24:31 Wayo tongha atoma kai o dera lepung kane ulbi tojebe ajǝng, aa ne kurki andaaka aa zaka o era aa ara o susǝ ongme, kaa ara o tǝǝru ongme, aa kulu arungji kaa kulu ayarbawa o lerambo leena.
MAT 24:32 Jeka na eyapa a uti uli. Aa e bana ee obara o sara, kane sǝǝrǝ marane maa sau, ee rosa obena lekoze le amara naname.
MAT 24:33 Nyimia awereaka ee laka pate epanana, eyo rosa obena awere a amara, aa bengmǝ be abuudu.
MAT 24:34 Ang dongdong ya baala oying, awereena ta kala ne seeka epanana apate eye.
MAT 24:35 Shili kaa deze yo maro, aa angmǝ ang to tukǝ omaro ne dakemeeme.
MAT 24:36 “Ondo ta rosa lengme leme na awereme ne, koona atoma odera lepung ka neya azaa shili, koona Kena kame, seena Ate me belle.
MAT 24:37 Waye na nangka a eze awere a Nuhu, nyimia o kurǝ Kena ka Oromo yo za.
MAT 24:38 Wa kang ya na tomore tennamea zongka manyi maa gong bore, aya lyelyeeza, aa sosoza, aya nyaza aa angza andaaye, aa dukǝ lengme leeka Nuhu wa lyǝ o onggo o taara manyi.
MAT 24:39 Zongka ne rose epa eka eya ale ne, seena manyi maa gong mame lye ne apat. Nyimia o kurǝ o Kena ka Oromo yo za.
MAT 24:40 Awerenamea, ayo mana aromo leere ara a ogole, ayo jeka oyende, aa baya oyende.
MAT 24:41 Ayo laka andaaye leere aa neya nyanta o nyanto, ayo jeka oyende, aa baya oyende.
MAT 24:42 Azaa nyimi, cikǝ na a le'enda, ka eta rosa lengme leeka Ateokora oying ya kurǝ ne.
MAT 24:43 Rosana bena, eeya ateakwilǝ yo rosa awere aka okǝri ya deya akwilǝ wai aa lelyaare, waa yo mora aa le'enda tana a lyǝ akwilǝ awai ka eze bekǝri ne.
MAT 24:44 Ying kangza cikǝ na ka ogoro, Kena ka Oromo ya deya awereaka ata madoola ma nyimi ne.
MAT 24:45 “Ozara o yemea o eza epa edang aa waye ka orosa, ka ateakwilǝ awai yo nya wai le onta le akwilǝ awai, ka wa nyaza odangare azara me epaolya a were aka wa gwara?”
MAT 24:46 O kona oleba ya aza ozara oka ateakwilǝ awai yo kurǝ awa mana wai awa ya eza nyimi.
MAT 24:47 Eyang dongdong baala oying, wa yo ote wai aza ekeeya e wai.
MAT 24:48 Aa ozara name ondo araaburu wa za, wa yo bekaa ukpwei wai na, ‘Ateakwilǝ ta amara ka o deya ne.’
MAT 24:49 Aa wa bore olaza odangare azara me, awa lye, awa soze kaa ana ososoza.
MAT 24:50 Ateakwilǝ ozara me yo deya a lengme leeka ata madoola ma o deya wai ne, awere aka wata rosa ne.
MAT 24:51 Ka wa daara wai lepung ka lesaro, aa wa nya wai epa eka e gwara ka ana araaburu. Aa arame ayo ruuzi ka o nongza tuuni.”
MAT 25:1 Awere name ayo kedeya togomo te shili na agala be tuuru ka ne jeke eru masanto na ne ale a wobe ondaasau.
MAT 25:2 Esu a nyimi one ya ka orosa, aa ondanggare esu ta neye ka wai ne.
MAT 25:3 Ana o dera orosa ne jeke eru masanto mane, aa neta ne onte manau ne.
MAT 25:4 Aa ana orosa kangza ne monte eru masanto mane kaa kagwi ka manau.
MAT 25:5 Ondaasau me ta wa dusung deya ne, pate one na ne bora ungzǝ, na malau jeke ne.
MAT 25:6 “Aa sanini tera le lyaare, na ne kona lengmelo aa rara na, ‘Ondaasau me a waana wa dukǝ! Surǝ na ka e wobe wai!’
MAT 25:7 “Pate agala name na ne ere na ne diisi eru masanto mane.
MAT 25:8 Na ana odera orosa name bekaa ana orosa na, ‘Nyapana ro a manau maaying aa baate, eru masanto maro ya limbuzu!’
MAT 25:9 Na ana orosa bekaana, ‘Ba eza manau maro to bare ro kaa ying ne. Mara e ale ana lisǝzǝme ke embe.’
MAT 25:10 “Aane tata ara o emba manau mame, na ondaasau me dukǝ. Na andaaka neye ka ogoro ne lyǝ ara o zǝnggǝ ka wai, aa kang pate abuudu me.
MAT 25:11 “Malo nyimi na ondanggare agala name dukǝ, nane bekaana, ‘Ateokora, Ateokora, pǝri ro abuudu!’
MAT 25:12 “Na wa kabare nee na, ‘Ang dongdong bele oying, mi anta rosa ying ne.’
MAT 25:13 “Na Yeso maare ka o bekaana, ‘Azaa nyimi, cikǝ na ka ogoro ka eta rosa lengme na awereme ne.’ ”
MAT 25:14 “Togomo te Ashili teyo itǝ naa oromoa ka waya ya ale aa teweno, nawa rare azara wai aa wa eke pate epa eka waya ka e a taara te ne.
MAT 25:15 Wa nya oyende ma talenti esu, oyende ma talenti ma leere, aa oyende o talenti oyende. Wa nya komaname nangka legoone lewai leze. Aa wa ale.
MAT 25:16 Wai ondooka wa emba ma talenti esu mame wa era a saseya nawa ale nawa wanggare nawa cǝ esu aa zame.
MAT 25:17 Nyimia ondooka wa emba ma talenti ma leere, wai kangza wa cǝ ma leere aa zame.
MAT 25:18 Wai ka wa o talenti o yende, wa ale nawa kau le'o a deze na wa baasa o talenti a ateakwilǝ a wai.
MAT 25:19 “Malo rabo, na ateakwilǝ me wa kuri kane bale epa eka nee cǝ.
MAT 25:20 Na ondo name kawa emba ma talenti esu wa paka nawa de ka ma talenti ma yende esu, awa bekaana, ‘Ateakwilǝ, ba nyang ma talenti esu, mi naana ama cǝ esu yende kangza.’
MAT 25:21 “Na ateakwilǝ beka wai ana, ‘Kondo ogole, ozara edang, o dera araaburu. Ba eza edang aza epa e baate, eyang ote o aza epa ecake. Deya ka o cikǝ o kone oleba kaa ateakwilǝ o.
MAT 25:22 “Na ondooka wa embe ma talenti ma leere wa paka, na wa bekaana, ‘Ateakwilǝ, ba nyang ma talenti ma leere, a maana aa ma cǝ ma leere aa zame.’
MAT 25:23 “Na ateakwilǝ bekaa wai na ‘Kondo ogole, ozara edang, odera araaburu. Ba ya edang aza epa a baate. Eyang ote aza epa cake. Deya ka o cikǝ o kone oleba kaa ateakwilǝ o.’
MAT 25:24 “Wai kangza kawa emba o talenti o yende name, nawa paka, nawa bekaana, ‘Ateakwilǝ, ang rose obena bo oromo oka wata eza eceya ka aromo ne, o yeme o senda a ara aka boa ota ba kweene ne, bo ondo o yeme epa eka ota ba zitǝ a zamea ne.’
MAT 25:25 Waya na ma kona boome, na ma ale nama kawa le'o a deze namaa baasa o talenti ooka ba nyang. Na opa owaa waana!’
MAT 25:26 “Na ateakwilǝ kabare wai na, ‘Bo, ozara araaburu, ondo be nau! Orose bena ang shende ara aka mia ta ma kweene ne, aa mi ondo o yeme epa eka anta maa zitǝ azame ne na?’
MAT 25:27 Wa gwara eeya ba eke o talenti ong ara le'eke ka ma deya ang emba opa ong ka eyapa aza me!
MAT 25:28 “Azaa nyimi, emba na o talenti onname a tara te wai, ka e nya ondo betuuru onname.
MAT 25:29 Pate ondooka waya ka epa, ayo wala wai, ka e wala gongha. Ondooka wata ka e ne kangza, kapa kaa baate kamea wa zene, ayo emba a wai.
MAT 25:30 Tare na ozara odera edang oona a nyimi maring maa bitibiti. Arakanamea wayo ruuzi ka onongza tuuni.
MAT 25:31 “Awereaka Kena ko Oromo ya deya nyimi togomo te kai ka pate atoma o dera lepung, awere namea kayo cikǝ a ledǝndǝ le togomo te kai.”
MAT 25:32 Ayo kurki pate aromo lerambo aa begeshe be kai, ayo kang arsaza ne, nangka ana otare ka emande zauze emande epeng aa nyimia ee bo.
MAT 25:33 Ka yo eke emande epeng o ara ore o kai, aa emande ee bo o ara oguri kai.
MAT 25:34 Awerenamea, Ogomo ya bekaa andaaka yo ara ore owai, ‘Deya na, ying ka Ate ang a eke taara azaa oying, emba na togomo teeka Ashili a eke ying ka o rabo obora lerambo.’
MAT 25:35 Oo bena ma kone ekomo, na e nyang epaolya. Ma kone lewe, na e nyang manyi nang se. Ma deya legeng, na e nyang ara ojǝpi akwilǝ ying.
MAT 25:36 Ma ye ngmata, na e ambang madibi. Ma kono na e sooleng. A pateng akwilǝ andaleme, na e de aa laka ong.
MAT 25:37 “Awerenamea andaa sangsang a begeshe be Ashili yo kabare ko bekaana, ‘Ateokora, ngmǝyamea te lakau ka ekomo na te nyau epaolya, na ngmǝyamea te lakau a kona lewe na te nyau manyi ma o sa?’
MAT 25:38 Kangza ngmǝyamea te lakau ogeng na te nyau ara ujǝpi, koona ngmǝyamea te lakau ngmata nate ambau madibi?
MAT 25:39 Ngmǝyamea te lakau a ota zake ne, koona aa pate akwilǝ andaleme, na te de aa laka o?
MAT 25:40 “Ogomo ome yo kabare nee na, ‘Ang dongdong bele oying, pate epa e erere eka e eza arone ang ana, ka o kala aa be baate, aa ee ezangngha.’
MAT 25:41 A werenamea wayo bekaa andaaka ne yo o ara oguri na, ‘Arnanna kaa mi, andaamea neya enda ogǝzǝ Ashili, lyǝ na ola ooka wata lambu ne kaa babare ogomo obere oburu kaa atoma wai.’
MAT 25:42 Ka ma kona ekomo, eta e nyang epaolya ne. Ma kona lewe, eta e nyang manyi ma o sa ne.
MAT 25:43 Ma ya legeng, eta e nyang ara ujǝpi ne. Ma ye ngmata, na eta ambang madibi ne. Ma kono, a pateng akwilǝ andaleme, na eta e balang ne.
MAT 25:44 “Awerenamea neema neyo kabare na, ‘Ateokora, ngmǝyamea te lakau ka ekomo, koona ka lewe, na aa legeng, na ngmata, koona oya kono, koona oyaa akwilǝ andaleme, na teta balau ne?’
MAT 25:45 “Wayo kabare nee na, ‘Ang dongdong bele oying, nangka eta e eze ka yende aa nyimi andaa batebate aana nyimi ying ne, mia eta e ezanne.’
MAT 25:46 “Andaana ya lyǝ ozitǝ o dera omaro, aa andaa sangsang a begeshe be Ashili neya yo lyǝ a ebeene o dera o maro.”
MAT 26:1 Nangka Yeso ka mare o beya apate epaname, na ka bekaa atoma akai ana,
MAT 26:2 “Erose na Ozǝnggǝ Ocakate tata kaa amora aleerea, ayo kang nya Kena ka oromo ka gendare kai a uti.”
MAT 26:3 Na andaamoole magame ma Akwilǝ Ashili kaa andaano aromo ne gwarnang akwilǝ ondo ogong o magame ma Akwilǝ Ashili, ka aa rare wai na Kayafa.
MAT 26:4 Na ne tere nangka neya moke a Yeso asuk ka ne wong kai.
MAT 26:5 Aa ne bekaana, ‘‘Wato gwara awere ozǝnggǝ me ne, adorana tana aromo ne ara o kara ne.”
MAT 26:6 Aa, Yeso kaya apeng a Betanya akwilǝ Siman, ondooka samba waye ka legangca,
MAT 26:7 na kandaaye ka yende de ara Yeso ka kagwi ka a eze kai kaa acale onis aa ka pena ka manau ma owaze olebo ma emate ecake. Awere aaka kaya lya epaolya naka kare kai manau mame ukpwei.
MAT 26:8 Nangka atoma kai ne laka nyimi, na ne kone oburǝ aane bekaa tukpwei tone na, “Onna ocara emate wai!”
MAT 26:9 “Ayya aa lisǝ manau maana, aa yo ci emate acake ka nya ana odera.”
MAT 26:10 Aa nangka Yeso ka rose epa eka neya beyame, na ka bekaa nee na, “Eyaka eya gera kandaye kaana? Enna, epa ererea kaya eza ong.
MAT 26:11 Ana o dera neye legwa kaa ying koonang were, aa koonag werea anto ya legwa kaa ying ne.
MAT 26:12 Okare manau maana aa kaa ezang, kaya goro ongngha o matasakong mang.
MAT 26:13 Ang dongdong ya baale oying, pate ara aka ayo baala orooka olebo ona aa lerambo aa pate, ayo beya orooka azaa epa eeka kandaye kaana kaya ka rintǝ ka kai.”
MAT 26:14 Na ondo a nyimi atoma Yeso lekuri, ka a beya wai ana Yahuda Iskariyoti, wa ale andaamoole magame ma Akwilǝ Ashili,
MAT 26:15 na wa pirkǝ nee na, “Eya nya ong eya maa nya ying kai?” Na ne bale o azorpa etuuru taaro, nane nya wai o azorpo etuuru taaro.
MAT 26:16 O era awere namea wa gere orona ooka wayo nya Yeso.
MAT 26:17 Nangka lengme le o bora le Ozǝnggǝ Oborode Odera o Yisti, na atoma Yeso de nane pirkǝ kai na, “Aruwǝ me oya yeme a te babarau ara olya epaolya ozǝnggǝ ocakate me?”
MAT 26:18 Na Yeso kabare nee na, “Ale na aa nyimi peng ara oromo yende ka e bekaa wai na, ‘Ondo obaala wa bekaana awere a kai a amara, kayo lya epaolya Ozǝnggǝ Ocakate a akwilǝ au kaa atoma a kai.’ ”
MAT 26:19 Na atoma me ne eze akap nangka Yeso ka ote ne, nane kang goro ekeeya azaa Ozǝnggǝ Ocakate me.
MAT 26:20 Nangka ulyǝlu waye, na Yeso cikǝ a lya epaolya ka atoma kai betuuru ke leere.
MAT 26:21 Neya nyimia olya epaolya, naka bekaana, “Ang dongdong bele oying, ondo aa nyimi oying wayo naying.”
MAT 26:22 Na anyong ane caro ajǝng, na komana one bore o pirǝ o kai ayeyende, aane beyaa na, “Anyya, mia na, Ateokora?”
MAT 26:23 Na Yeso kabare na, “Ondooka waya pasa taara oso yende kaa mi, waiya ya nayi ong.
MAT 26:24 Kena ka Oromo kayo gbwǝ nangka a wele angmǝ Ashili azaa kai. Pate ka nyimi, ondooka waya nayi Kena ka Oromo wa lyǝ udi! Wa kala o bena mara taa a ngmengha wai ne.”
MAT 26:25 Na Yahuda ka wa ya nayi kai pirkǝ na, “Ondo obaala, mia na,?’’ Na Yeso kabare wai na, “Bo ma baa beka.”
MAT 26:26 Neya za olya epaolya, na Yeso jeka oborode, na ka wore okona oleba Ashili, aa ka nyeskare, na ka nya atoma akai, aa ka bekaana “Emba, ka e lya. Leena lepung lengha le.”
MAT 26:27 Na ka jeke kaso ka manyi ma o inabi. Malo owore okona oleba Ashili, na ka nya ne aka bekaana, “Sa na aa pate oying.
MAT 26:28 Obena manna manyau mangngha mai, ma owore opanza okabare otono osau, ka ayo oka aza aromo a cake, ka opisǝ madinǝ mane.
MAT 26:29 Eyang baala oying, anta kang sa manyi ma o inabi na ne, seena lengme lenname ka teyo sa ma yende ma sau ka ying a togomo te Ate ang.”
MAT 26:30 Nangka Yeso kaa atoma kai ne beye leera, nane suri, aane ale a oyara o mati ma o Zaitun.
MAT 26:31 Na Yeso bekaane na, “Pate oying eyo songha e bayang aa lelyaare leena, azaa epaeka eyo manang, nangka a wele na, “‘Eyang taba ondo otare ka enama, legwa le emande epeng me yo bacakarna.’
MAT 26:32 Aa malo ara ong malo o gbwǝ, eyang kaana ying a ale a makeke ma Galili.”
MAT 26:33 Biturusu wa bekaa Yeso, “Pate one ne songha azaa epa eeka eyo manau, mi antang tukǝ songha ne.”
MAT 26:34 Na Yeso beka wai na, “Ang dongdong bele o, aa lelyaare leena, zongka orunǝ sene, oyo sangga orosa ong ka taaro.”
MAT 26:35 Na Biturusu bekaa kai na, “Ayaa wongha ong, anto sangga orosa o ne.” Nyimia apate odangare atoma kai ne beke.
MAT 26:36 Malo o nyimia, Yeso kaa atoma kai ne alea ara kaa beya ai na Gasamani. Ara aaka a pilizi ayana o zaitun ne. Naka bekaa atoma kai, “Cikǝ na arakaana, eyang alea sanini kang beye angmǝ kaa Ashili.”
MAT 26:37 Na ka ale ka Biturusu, a ayana Zebadi aleere, Yakubu kaa Yohana, naka bore o caro anyong kaa o kona o burǝ maleu.
MAT 26:38 Aaka kang bekaa nee na, “O caro a nyong ka waya lenyong leng wa era aa wa wongngeng. Cikǝna arakaana ee eza le'enda ka mi.”
MAT 26:39 Nangka ka lya izi a baate, na ka taru ka mayinu a deze, aa ka beye angmǝ kaa Ashili na, “Ate ang, nyimi waayo ya, saareng kaso ka ozitǝ kaana. Pate ka nyimi sang, epa eeka eyang yeme me eya ato yeme ne, soona epa eeka bo oya yeme me.”
MAT 26:40 Ka o kurǝ ara atoma akai, naka mana ne aa aneya malau, na ka bekaa Biturusu na, “E era eta ama le'enda kaa mi, na awere yende ne na?
MAT 26:41 Cikǝ na aa le'enda, ee kang beya na angmǝ kaa Ashili adorana tana e rǝzi aa nyimi okedeya ne. Dongdong lenyong lee kabare, aa lepung kangza leya nyana.”
MAT 26:42 Naka kuri o leere, na ka beye angmǝ kaa Ashili aaka bekaana, “Ate ang, ozitǝ ona waata kala ne seeka ma se wai, a baya aa eze apa eeka bo oya yeme me.”
MAT 26:43 Nangka ka kang kurǝ, aa ka kang mana ne a malau, azaa obena ayizi ane a pena ka malau.
MAT 26:44 Naka sukǝ o baya one, na ka kuri aa beya angmǝ kaa Ashili o taaro, na ka tikǝri angmǝ aaka ka be samba.
MAT 26:45 Na ka kuri ara atoma kai, aaka bekaa nee na, “Etata a malau nanna, eeya teseke na?” Laka na, awere aya, ka ayo nya Kena ka Oromo a taara te ana madinǝ.
MAT 26:46 Erana ka ale. Laka na, ondo nya ong awaana, wa dukǝ.”
MAT 26:47 Zongka ka pate o ngmǝ, na Yahuda, oyende a nyimia atoma betuuru kaa leere name, dukǝ ka aromo a cake, ka masagali, ka sebenda. Andaamoole magame ma Akwilǝ Ashilia kaa andaano aromoa ne tongha ne.
MAT 26:48 Aa ondo o nayi okai wa samba o wore one obena, “Kondo kamea ma beya kai oko ang gambare kai, kaiya karomo kame. Moke na kai.”
MAT 26:49 Ka o dǝkǝ wai na wa paka a Yeso, aa wa bekaana, “Oya cammo na, Ondobaala!” Aa wa beye kai oko ka o gambare.
MAT 26:50 Na Yeso bekaa wai na, “Oja ong, eza epa eka e deya ka bo.” Na aromo de na ne meke Yeso, nane monte kai.
MAT 26:51 Ka o laka nyimi, na ondo a nyimi andaaka Yeso kaye legwa ka ne sǝǝrǝ osagali na wa lope oto o ozara andoo ogong ona magame ma Ashili.
MAT 26:52 Na Yeso bekaa wai na, “Kuriyǝ osagali o a nyimi opano wai. Pate ondooka wa lopa osagali, osagali yo wongha wai.
MAT 26:53 Eya gonta na anta ka o bare kang gera okangkama Ate ang, kangza aa saseya a kawa turki legwa le atoma Ashili o dera lepung, kane kala legwa le ana o tesa geza a moole be tuuru ka leere sang?
MAT 26:54 Na, a wiinia a ngmǝ Ashili itǝ maganggang aaka a wele, ka aa beyaa na dongdong nyimi mea yo ya?
MAT 26:55 Awere name, na Yeso beka a aromo me na, “E surǝa ka masagali ka sebenda ka e mokeng na ondo o tǝǝru a aromo na? Koonang lengme ang ciisǝ a akwilǝ Ashili ang baaleze na eta mekeng ne.
MAT 26:56 Aa pate a eze nyimia adorana a panza epa eka ana o beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili ne wela.” Ka o kona nyimi na pat atoma kai ne song aane baya kai.
MAT 26:57 Na andaaka ne moke Yeso ale ka kai a Keyafa, ondoo gong ana magame ma Ashili, ara aka ana baala a ngmǝ aaka Ashili a nya Mosa kaa andaano ne kurkǝnǝng ne.
MAT 26:58 Na Biturusu tarze kai aa macangcang aa alea nyimi akora ondoo ogong magame ma Ashili. Nangka wa lyǝ nawa cikǝ kaa ana le'enda, ka wa laka nangka ayo maare.
MAT 26:59 Na andaamoole magame ma Ashili kaa anatendaasau, pate one nane gere angmǝ majǝkǝri kaa ayo eza Yeso adorana ne cǝ orona o wongha kai.
MAT 26:60 Pate kaa nyimi na ne ta cǝ ne, o bekaana aromo a cake ne ya beya majǝkǝri azaa kai. Malo me na aromo leere surǝ,
MAT 26:61 ne bekaa na, “Karomo oona wa bekaana, ‘Wa era wa oke akwilǝ Ashili ana, aa wa sowa ai a nyimi tomore te taaro.’ ”
MAT 26:62 Na ondo gong magame ma Ashili ere aa itǝ na wa bekana, “Ota ke epa o beka ne na? Epa ena aa neya beyaa na ba beke pa?”
MAT 26:63 Na Yeso sokong kome. Na ondo o gong magame ma Ashili beka a kai na, “Ma gwarau ka Ashili aka ya ka ebeene, bele ro, ‘Boa Almasipu, Kena ka Ashili.”
MAT 26:64 Na Yeso bekaa wai na, “Nangka ba beka. Aa eyang bele ying, ba ale a izi, eya laka Kena ka Oromo a cikǝ o ara oree Ondo Keeya, aa ka kang deya aza mawere.”
MAT 26:65 Na ondo o gong magame ma Ashili daara madibi ma wai azaa o caro a nyong, aa wa bekaana, “Ka sopa! Eya teya gerame kangza? Ee kona o sopa ooka kaya.
MAT 26:66 Eya madoola maying? Nane kabare na, “Ka gwara a wong kai.”
MAT 26:67 Nane karze kai mawo a mainu, aa ne ola kai, ana ondo kangza nane kpweze kai to maare.
MAT 26:68 Aane beya ana, “Bele ro epa eka ayo eza aa izi, boa baa ya Almasipu. Mana wa olau?”
MAT 26:69 Aa Biturusu ya cikǝ o yanga a tatara akwilǝ ogomo, na ka kazara kagala de naka zundǝ wai, aa ka bekaana wai na, “Bo kangza oya legwa ka Yeso ka o Galili!”
MAT 26:70 Na Biturusu wa sangga a begeshe bene apate, aa wa bekaana, “Mi anta rose epa eka oya beya me ne.”
MAT 26:71 Nangka wa surǝ aa tatara akwilǝ ogomo, na kazara ka ai yende kangza laka wai, na ka beka andaaka ne ya itǝ arame na, “Oromo na waye legwa ka Yeso ka Nazarat!”
MAT 26:72 Na wa kang sangga ka otongzo na, “Anta rosa oromo name ne.”
MAT 26:73 Ka o rabo a baate, na andaaka neya itǝ arame de ane bekaa Biturusu na, “Ma shango tarenene, bo ma oya nyimi one. Obelo angmǝ au, aa pǝro.”
MAT 26:74 Na wa bora angmǝ aburu aza ukpwei wai, aa wa tongzo, aa wa beyaana, “Anta rosa oromo me ne!” Awerename na urunǝ sene.
MAT 26:75 Na Biturusu rintǝ angmǝ a Yeso na, “Zongka orunǝ sene, oyo sangga orosa ong ka taaro.” Na wa surǝ o yanga na wa ruzii a maleo.
MAT 27:1 Nangka ara asane, na pate andaamoole magame Ashili kaa andaano aromo gwaara angmǝ azaa nangka neya wongha Yeso.
MAT 27:2 Nane tere kai, aane ale ka kai aa begeshe be Ogomo Bilatus.
MAT 27:3 Awere aka Yahuda ooka wa nayi kai wa laka aa core Yeso angmǝ wongha, na wa kone oburǝ, nawa kuri ara andaamoole magame ma Ashili kaa andaano, nawa kuriyǝ ne ma azorpa tuuru taaro name.
MAT 27:4 Awa bekaana, “Ma ya madinǝ ka ma nya ondooka wata tambo ne ka wongha kai.” Nane bekaana, “Eya manyi maro? Onna a owa wai.”
MAT 27:5 Na Yahuda me bacakare o azorpa me a akwilǝ Ashili, na wa suri, na wa ale aa wa ye lesara.
MAT 27:6 Azaa nyimi na andaamoole magame Ashili ne shende emate me aa ne bekaana, “Wata gwara aa eke emate eena e a lebengga le akwilǝ Ashili ne, obena emate me e manyau e.”
MAT 27:7 Azaa nyimi na ne nya tukpwei madoola na, ne embe adeze a ondo sowa madaka ka emate me ka a itǝ adeze o taasa a ageng.
MAT 27:8 Nyimia wa ote, a deya o ngmeengme a rareze arame na ugiishi manyau.
MAT 27:9 Azaa nyimia a panza angmǝ a Ondo o beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili Irimiya ka wa beke na, “Ne jeke emate tuuru taaro, emate eeka aromo a Isrela ne kabare na are azaa kai naname,
MAT 27:10 nane embe adeze ondo o sooza madaka ka e, nangka Ateokora ka oteng.”
MAT 27:11 Na Yeso itǝ a begeshe be ondo togomo, na ondo togomo teme kang pirkǝ kai na, “Boo na, boa Ogomo maYahuda na?” Yeso ka kabare na, “Nangka baa beka.”
MAT 27:12 Nangka ne andaamoole magame ma Ashili kaa andaano ne beye kai majǝkǝri, naka ta beke eyapa ne.
MAT 27:13 Na Bilatus bekaa akai na, “Ota ba kona e pate epa eena ane beyau majǝkǝri azame ne?”
MAT 27:14 Na Yeso ta ka kabare na be pirǝ be yende ne, na nyimi tere ogomo ukpwei aa bote.
MAT 27:15 Koonang awere Ozǝnggǝ Ocakate, ondo togomo wa mena aa peere oromo yende aa nyimia andaaka a pate a akwilǝ andaleme, ooka aromo ne zaka.
MAT 27:16 Awere name, ondo zene a akwilǝ andaleme ka a rose wai ka ogirǝ, ka a beya wai na Barabas.
MAT 27:17 Nangka maYahuda ne kurkǝnǝng, na Bilatus pirkǝ nee na, “Mana eya yeme ang pere ying wai? Barabas naa, na Yeso kamea arareze kai na Almasipu?”
MAT 27:18 Obena wa rose na le'ero le ote nane turki Yeso awai.
MAT 27:19 Bangka nyimi kangza, awere aka wa ya cikǝ a ledǝndǝ le cora angmǝ, ondaye wai wa tong na abele wai na, “Karomo kana ta kaa ya eyapa ne. Sǝǝrǝ taara to orooka karomo kaana obena ma zitǝ a tolau kaya kai.”
MAT 27:20 Andaamoole magame ma Ashili kaa andaano ne tarze aromo aa ne baale ne na ne zaka Barabas ka ne cǝ kane wong Yeso.
MAT 27:21 Na ogomo me kang pirkǝ aromo me na, “A nyimi aromo leere aana, mana eya yeme ang pere ying wai?” Na ne bekaana, “Barabas.”
MAT 27:22 Na Bilatus bekaa na, “Na ang wiinia ka Yeso ka rareze kai na Almasipu?” Na pate one kabare na “A gendare kai a uti!”
MAT 27:23 Na Bilatus pirkǝ ne, “Azaa eya? Ombela araaburu ka eza?” Na ne waale o ara angmelo na, “A gendare kai a uti.”
MAT 27:24 Nangka Bilatus wa laka wa era wata ya eyapa ne, kangza a nyong aromo ya waale o caro, na wa mangka manyi na wa kwizǝ taara tewai aa aromo ya gonta, aa wa bekaana, “Mi, ma kwizǝ a taara teng aa manyau ma karomo ka o dera madinǝ kaana. Onna zitǝ oying wai.”
MAT 27:25 Na pate aromo me kabare na, “Baya ozitǝ ome itǝ azaa aro kaa ayana aro.”
MAT 27:26 Awere namea wa pere ne Barabas. Malo oka wa ote na ole Yeso, aa wa nayi kai ka gendare.
MAT 27:27 Na ana otesa ageza aa moole o ogomo ale ka Yeso a akwilǝ togomo, nane kurki pate legwa le ana otesa ageza a moole o makeke mame azaa kai.
MAT 27:28 Na ne lope madibi maaka maya lepung le kai, aa ne amba kai odibi o ganggo o togomo.
MAT 27:29 Na ne pi betageya be ekana, aa ne amba kai ukpwei, aa ne nya kai lebenda le yende o ara ore o kai, na ne kang tungunu a begeshe be kai aa ne zeele kai, aa ne beyaana kai na, “Ashili waloo ne, Ogomo maYahuda!”
MAT 27:30 Aa ne karze kai mawo, nane jeke lebenda lenname nane ola kai kaa le o ukpwei.
MAT 27:31 Nangka ne mare o zeela kai, nane lope kai odibi o togomo te me, aa kuriyǝ kai madibi maaka maya kai a lepung, nane ale ka kai ka ne gendare uti.
MAT 27:32 Ne ya teweno naname, nane gwarnang ka Saminu, oromo a Siyarin. Waya ne ote nawa ana uti o gendare a Yeso.
MAT 27:33 Nangka ne dukǝ ara aka arareze ai na Golgota, araaka a rose ai na ara o cako ukpwei,
MAT 27:34 nane nya kai manyi ma inabi maaka a sakale ka ka o ngmangmang ka ka se. Nangka ka lembe ka leleng, naka nyana o sa me.
MAT 27:35 Malo o gendare a Yeso, nane eze o zawa azaa madibi ma kai kane laka mana yo jeka odibi me.
MAT 27:36 Malo nyimi nane cikǝ arame aa le'enda le kai.
MAT 27:37 A aza uti me, aza kaa ukpwei o kai, nane wele aa kati ka patarake ka yende na, “KANNAA YESO, OGOMO MAYAHUDA.”
MAT 27:38 Nane kang gendare kai legwa kaa akǝri o tǝǝru aromo a leere, oyende o ara ore, aa o yende o ara uguri kai.
MAT 27:39 Ana o kaale ne ne zeele kai, aa ne zuu ukpwei,
MAT 27:40 aa ne beyaana, “Bo ka baa bekaana, ba era o oka akwilǝ Ashili, oo kang sowa ai a nyimi amora taaro, na boza o ukpwei o! Na bo Kena ka Ashili baaza, jipi a uti ogendare me!”
MAT 27:41 Nyimia kangza andaamoole magame ma Ashili ka ana o baala angmǝ aaka Ashili a nya Mosa ka andaano aromo ne zeele kai, aa ne beyaana,
MAT 27:42 “Ka boza ana ondo, aa ka girǝ o boza ukpwei kai. Kai ya Ogomo Isrela sang? Kaa jipi a uti ogendare na nannameena, awere namea te yo kabare ka kai.
MAT 27:43 Ka eke lenyong a Ashili, baya a Ashili me boza kai nanname, aaya yeme a kai, obena ka bekaana kai Kena ka Ashilia kai.”
MAT 27:44 Pate a akǝri o tǝǝru a aromo ka a gendare ne ka Yeso ne beya akai angmǝ a aburu.
MAT 27:45 Na maring meke pate makeke mame aa era o tera ongme aa dukǝ beru be o taaro ulyǝlu.
MAT 27:46 Nangka ongme wa amara ka otaru, na Yeso ara lengmelo ajǝng, na ka bekaana, “Eloi, Eloi, lama sabatani?” Obena, “Ashili ang, Ashili ang, eyaaka ba nyang o malo?”
MAT 27:47 Aromo aa ka neya itǝ a ting arame ne kone nyimi na ne bekaana, “Karomo kaana kaya orara Ileya!”
MAT 27:48 Na ondo a nyimi one song nawa jeke lesuni nawa tǝkǝzǝ a manyi ma marara, nawa ote a lebenda, aa wa nayi Yeso na ka se.
MAT 27:49 Azaa nyimi odangare me bekaana, “Bayana te laka na Ileya yo deya kawa boza kai.”
MAT 27:50 Na Yeso kang ara lengmelo a jǝng, aa ka pere ebeene e kai.
MAT 27:51 Nyimia oyambati ka waya a akwilǝ Ashili wa daro a tera madǝkǝni ma leere, o era obora aaza a jǝpi dizi. Na adeze a zukǝru, aa acale poso.
MAT 27:52 A pǝǝri macao, andaaka ne gbwizǝ kaa ne ye ka boome be Ashili, ne ere ka ebeene,
MAT 27:53 aa komana one susi a ocao o wai. Malo o era Yeso, nane lyǝ a nyimi apeng aa sangsang, aromo acake ne laka ne.
MAT 27:54 Awere aka ondo gong ana otesa geza o Roma, kaa andaaka neya legwa aa enda Yeso ne laka adeze a zukǝrnu kaa pate epa eka ne laka, na pate one kone boome maleo, aa ne bekaana, “Kanna dongdong Kena ka Ashilia kai!”
MAT 27:55 Andaye yende acake ka ne tare Yeso aa surǝ aa Galili aane kangkama kai, ne itǝ aa macang a gontaka pate epa eka eya ale.
MAT 27:56 Aa nyimi one neye, Mariya ka o Magadala, kaa Mariya iini na Yakubu ka Yusupu, aa iini ayana Zabadi kangza.
MAT 27:57 Nangka o ulyǝlu waye, na Yusupu, oromo o Arimatiya ka waya ka o cǝ, wai kangza ondo o tare Yeso waze.
MAT 27:58 Nawa ale aa Bilatus nawa bose na nya wai lepung le Yeso. Na Bilatus ote na nya wai.
MAT 27:59 Yusupu wa jeke lepung leme, nawa pate le ka betu,
MAT 27:60 aa wa lyǝǝrǝ lepung leme a nyimi ocau osau oka wa she eke ukpwei wai ka wa kau a lecale. Nawa turki lecale legong leyende nawa pate begmǝ be ocau me, aa wa ale.
MAT 27:61 Mariya ka o Magadala, kaa Mariya kayende, ne ya zaa ocikǝ a izi ocau me.
MAT 27:62 Ka o sana ara, malo Lengme le Ogoro, na andaamoole magame ma Ashili kaa maParisa gwarnang a begeshe be Bilatus,
MAT 27:63 nane bekaana, “Ogomo, te rintǝ nangka karomo kaaname ka o rendaza aa ka tata a bengma ka beeze na malo tomore to taaro kayo era ka ebeene.
MAT 27:64 Azaa nyimi, ote ka eza le'enda ocau me maleo aa dukǝ tomore te taaro, tana atoma akai de kane kpwi ekeze kai aa ne bekaa aromo na ka era malo ogbwǝ ne. Orenda o maare wayo kala obora o buru.”
MAT 27:65 Na Bilatus bekaa nee na, “Besa na ana otesa geza aa moole, ka e ale kaa e eze le'enda nangka wa gwara.”
MAT 27:66 Nane ale nane ende ocau ome, aa ne ote bewela becapa be ogomo, aa ne baya ana otesa geza me aa le'enda.
MAT 28:1 Malo Lengme le Oteseke lee kala, aa lelere lengme le obora, na Mariya ka o Magadala, kaa Mariya kayende, ne ale a olaka ocau me.
MAT 28:2 Na adeze zukǝrnu a jǝng o otoma Ashili o dera lepung wa sura a zaa shili nawa kinkǝri o cale me aa wa cikǝ aaza me.
MAT 28:3 Waya masanto na o malmi, aa madibi ma wai maya apeng aa pauwo na adoka.
MAT 28:4 Nangka ana le'enda ne laka wai, na boome moke ne maleo, nane kerkeze aa ne tǝǝru aa deze naa nee gbwizǝ.
MAT 28:5 Aa otoma Ashili o dera lepung leme wa bekaa andaaye me na, “Tana e kona boome ne, ang rose obena Yeso kamea a gendare kaya eya gerame.
MAT 28:6 Kata rene ne. Ka era nangka ka beke. Deyana ke laka ara aka a eke kai.
MAT 28:7 Alena a saseya ka e bekaa otoma akai na, obena ka era malo ogbwǝ. Akaname aa ka yo kang kaana oying o ale a makeke ma Galili. Aa sanamea eyo laka kai! Epa eeka ma deya aa bele oying naname.”
MAT 28:8 Nane baya ocau ome a kwarte a nyimi boome, ka okona oleba aa cake, nane song nane bele atoma akai oroka ome.
MAT 28:9 Na Yeso ka o upkwai kai gwarnang ka ne, naka bekaa nee na, “O cikǝ o cammo itǝ ka ying!” Nane paka aa ma'amo aa ne garme tobona te kai, nane girwǝ a begeshe be kai.
MAT 28:10 Na Yeso bekaane na, “Tane kona boome ne, alena ka e bekaa arone ang, ane ale aa makeke ma Galili, asanamea ne yo lakang.”
MAT 28:11 Nangka andaaye me neya nyimi teweno, na ana ondo aa nyimi ana o enda ocau me, nane bele andaamoole ana magame ma Ashili orooka o pate epa eka ee ale.
MAT 28:12 Na andaamoole magame ma Ashili kaa andaano ne kurkǝnǝng, nane tere madoola ma yende, nane nya ana otesa geza aa moole me emate aa cak,
MAT 28:13 aa ne bekaane na, “Bele na aromo na, atoma kai ya ne deya aa lelyaare aa teya malau nane kpwi kai.
MAT 28:14 Orooka ona wa dukǝ teto te ogomo, teyo nya wai angmǝ te kang itǝ ka ying aa nyimia pate o zitǝ.”
MAT 28:15 Nane embe emate me, nane ye epa eka a bekaa nee na ne eze. Orooka ona wa ale kurǝwa a maYahuda aa deya o ngmeengme.
MAT 28:16 Na atoma akai be tuuru kaa leyende name ale a makeke ma Galili, a oyara ooka Yeso ka bekaa ne na ne gwarnang arame.
MAT 28:17 Nangka ne laka kai, na ne girwǝ aa ne sabe kai, aa na ondo ne dambaraza.
MAT 28:18 Na Yeso paka na ka bekaa nee na, “A nyang pate obare azaa shili ka adeze.”
MAT 28:19 Azaa nyimi, ale na ka e baale pate aromo lerambo ka ne tareng, e eza ne batisma a nyimi le ze Ate, ka Kena, ka Obere o Ashili,
MAT 28:20 e baala ne kane tare pate epaeka ma ote ying. Mi naana kangza ang ye legwa ka ying aa ale ka ying o omaare lerambo.
LUK 1:1 Ondoogong Tiyopalas, aromo a cake ne samba o wela aza epa eka Ashili a beke na nannamena e pena a nyimi oro a kazo Yeso,
LUK 1:2 nangka waze o bora andaaka ne laka ka yizi, ka azara o baala angmǝ a Ashili ne nya ro.
LUK 1:3 A wa kang rere a mi, nangka ma tare epame aza Yeso a be ting, kang wele a kap a deya ara au ondooka aromo gonte o gongnga wai.
LUK 1:4 Ma ye nyimia adorana o rose edang angmǝ aka a baalo.
LUK 1:5 A were a Ogomo Hiridus o makeke ma Yahudiya, ondo magame ma Ashili ka a beya wai na Zakariya wa zene, wai ondo akwilǝ ona Abija waye. Kanza pate one ka ondaye wai ne suri akora a Harona, a leze le ondaye mea leye Alisabatu.
LUK 1:6 Pate one a leere neya sangsang a begeshe be Ashili, ane tare angmǝ a Ateokora ka makili ma wai a kap.
LUK 1:7 Pate ka nyimi neta neye ka kena ne, aza o bena Alisabatu ta ngmenza ne, a pate one a leere ne kang onga a shenai.
LUK 1:8 A were aka Zakariya waya gole ka andaane akora Abija o makili ma Ashili.
LUK 1:9 Nangka makili ma na magame ma Ashili maze, na zake wai na wa lyǝ ba akwilǝ a Ashili adorana wa ese mapapa ma o waze o lebo ara o esaza o mai.
LUK 1:10 A were o esaza mapapa ma o waze o lebo, aromo a cake neya o yangga a beya angmǝ ka Ashili.
LUK 1:11 Na otoma Ashili o zaa shili oyende wa deya wai, na wa itǝ a sara ore o esaza mapapa ma o waze o lebo.
LUK 1:12 Nangka Zakariya wa laka wai na wa kerke, a boome meke wai.
LUK 1:13 Na otoma Ashili o zaa shili me bekaana, “Kana o kone boome ne, Zakariya, o beya angmǝ ka Ashili au, a kona, ondaye o Alisabatu wayo ngmenga kena ka lome, ka oyo nya kai leze na Yohana.
LUK 1:14 Oyo kona o leba, ocǝ lenyong le lebo, aromo a cake neyo kona o leba ka ongmenga wai,
LUK 1:15 aza o bena Ateokora a yo ote wai kawa itǝ ondo ogong a nyimia aromo. Kana wa se oloo ne, ka pate epa eka e era e wongze aromo nangka o loo eze, a obere Ashili wayo tare wa kai zongka a ngmeng wai.
LUK 1:16 A Yohana me wayo kuriyǝ ying maYahuda ba cake ara Ateokora Ashili ane.
LUK 1:17 Kanza wayo kala izi Ateokora, a nyimi obere Ashili ka legoone le Ileya ondo beya a ngmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili, ka wa kuriyǝ anyong anate ba ra yana. Ana o dera o kona ngmǝ kane kabare ka o rosa aromo aka ne kone boome ba Ashili. Awa babare aromo kane ende o deya Ateokora.”
LUK 1:18 Na Zakariya pirkǝ otoma Ashili o zaa shili ka o dera o kabare na, “Ma wanea ang rose epa ena? Ka ma samba o onga, a shenai se ondaye ong se lipǝ kanza.”
LUK 1:19 Na otoma Ashili o zaa shili kabare wai na, “Mea Jibrailu, ondo itǝzǝ ba begeshe ba Ashili, a tongang kang beke angmǝ ka bo ang kang belo angmǝ a lebo na.
LUK 1:20 Nannamena ongmǝ o wayo pate oto kang ama o bekaa ngmǝ ne se ngmeeka ba laka epa eka ma belo a e pena, aza o bena ota ba kabare ka angmǝ aka ma bekaa a bo ne, aka a yo pena a were aka ma Zaka.”
LUK 1:21 A aromo amea neya aza o enda Zakariya, ka madoola ma epa eka e ote wai na wa rabo ba akwilǝ Ashili.
LUK 1:22 nangka wa suri o yangga, wa ta wa ama o beya angmǝ ka ne ne, na ne rose o bena Ashili a wore wai eyapa a nyimi name. A wa lya izi ka lerakare awata ama o beya eyapa ne.
LUK 1:23 Nangka wa mare ogole o wai akwilǝ a Ashili a were name, na wa kuri akwilǝ.
LUK 1:24 Malo tomore tome na Alisabatu ondaye wai waye tumǝ, naka baasa o mareka esu,
LUK 1:25 Aka bekaana, “Ateokora wa yang epa ena, a wereena ka wa lakang ka egonegone na wa kwizǝng e zǝng ba nyimi aromo.”
LUK 1:26 A nyimi oreka o taashe e tumǝ Alisabatu, na Ashili tong otoma ai o sure a zaa shili Jibrailu a Nazarat apeng ayende a nyimi a makeke ma Galili,
LUK 1:27 ara kagala kamea kata ka tukǝ o mora ka ondaleme ne. Ka Yusupu waya caasa kai, Yusupu ondo abuudu ana Daoda. Leze le kagala kamea Mariya.
LUK 1:28 Nawa de a kai a wa bekaana, “A beyo ko bo ka ba cǝ o sana ara Ashili. A Ateokora waye legwa ka bo.”
LUK 1:29 Na Mariya kone o burǝ aza ngmǝ me, aka dambaraza aza obela o ko name.
LUK 1:30 Na otoma Ashili o zaa shili bekaa kai na, “Tana o kone boome ne Mariya, ba cǝ o sana ara Ashili.
LUK 1:31 Oyo ya e tumǝ ka ongmeng kena ka lome, ka oyo nya kai leze na Yeso.
LUK 1:32 Kena kame kayo itǝ ondo o gongnga a rare kai na kena ka ondo kala o gongnga. A Ateokora Ashili wayo nya kai ara o cikǝ togomo te abuudu ate a kai Daoda,
LUK 1:33 aka eze togomo te bedake ba za akora a Yakub. Togomo te kai teto ya ka bekazo ne.”
LUK 1:34 Na Mariya pirkǝ otoma Ashili o zaa shili na, “A wiinia a nyimi ye ka anta tukǝ o mora ka ondaleme ne?”
LUK 1:35 Na o otoma Ashili o zaa shili kabare na, “Obere Ashili o rere wayo lyǝ a bo, kanza a legoone le ondo kala o gongnga leyo panzau. Aza nyimi kena ka lome kamea oyo ngmenga a yo rara kai na Kena ka Ashili.
LUK 1:36 Kanza, Alisabatu kamea e gwaara eyapa kaye ka e tumǝ a nyimi le'ona lekai, kando kamea bezena kato ngmenga ne e tumǝ ekai eya nyimi oreka o taashe.
LUK 1:37 A begeshe ba Ashili eyapa ta girǝzǝ ai ne.”
LUK 1:38 Na Mariya kabare na, “Mi kazara ka Ashili kai, baya wa itǝ a mi nangka ba beka.” Ara name na otoma Ashili o zaa shili ale a wa baya kai.
LUK 1:39 A nyimi tomore tonname zora rabo, na Mariya ere a saseya naka meke orona o ale a kapeng ka yende a nyimi mayara o makeke ma Yahudiya.
LUK 1:40 Ka o dukǝ kapeng kame, naka lyǝ akwilǝ Zakariya na ka beye Alisabatu ko.
LUK 1:41 Nangka Alisabatu ka kone oko o Mariya, na kena kamea ka ya lebangi lekai cokomarono, a obere Ashili wa kang tare ka kai.
LUK 1:42 Naka ara lengmelo a jǝng aka bekaa Mariya na, “Boa ondo o kona o leba a nyimi andaye, ondo kona o leba kai kena kamea oyo ngmenga.
LUK 1:43 Eyaka mima ma sana ka iini Ateokora ka deya mi?
LUK 1:44 Rosa o bena, a were ka oko o wa dukǝ teto teng, kena kamea kaya lebangi leng ka cokomarono ko kona o leba.
LUK 1:45 Bo kando ka o kona o leba kai ka ba kabare o bena Ateokora yo ya epa eka wa beka.”
LUK 1:46 A Mariya bekaana, “Lenyong leng sabeze Ateokora,
LUK 1:47 a mi okpwe ong zante o bena Ashili aya ondo boza ong,
LUK 1:48 ka wa rintǝ o nata okpwe o kazara ka wai. Laka pa, nannamena ba ale a izi pate aromo neyo rarang na ondo sana,
LUK 1:49 aza o bekaana ondoogong me wa ezeng epa e gong. Ashili aya ondo o sangsang.
LUK 1:50 Egonegone ai kanza eya kazo ondooka wa tare ai, a ale a pate aromo.
LUK 1:51 Wa ezeze ma gole ma moole ka legoone le wai. Wa bacakareze ana o ara okpwe a nyimi madoola mane.
LUK 1:52 A wa jǝpǝrǝzǝ agomo ana o arsaza tokpwe aza togomo tone andaaka ne jipǝrǝzǝ tokpwe tone a wa zalaraza ne.
LUK 1:53 Wa nya ana o kona e komo etii ka magogoro ma rere a wa tarangga ana ocǝ zora eyapa a taara tene.
LUK 1:54 Wa kankama azara a wai abuudu a Yakubu, o bena wa rintǝ ne egonegone wai.
LUK 1:55 Nangka wa beke anate aro, o era a Ibraheng ka andaame ne tare wai ba dimǝ zora bekazo.”
LUK 1:56 Na Mariya cikǝ ka Alisabatu mareka ma taaro, a malo nyimi aka kuri akwilǝ kai.
LUK 1:57 Nangka tomore to ngmenga Alisabatu te dukǝ, naka ngmeng kena ka lome.
LUK 1:58 Ana o tokwilǝ to ting kai ka ana o gbaara eyapa ka kai kone o bena Ateokora wa wore kai egonegone cak, na ne kone o leba ka kai.
LUK 1:59 A lengme lo riiru ka o ngmenga nane de a core kena kame, a neya nya kai leze na Zakariya, leze le ate a kai,
LUK 1:60 na iini me beke angmǝ na, “Nyimi taza ne. A yo nya kai leze na Yohana.”
LUK 1:61 Na ne kabare kai na, “Ondo a nyimi akwilǝ aying ta zene ka leze le name ne.”
LUK 1:62 Nane beye erara ka ate kena kame, aza o gera nangka a yo rara kena kame.
LUK 1:63 Na wa pirkǝ epa o daara e wela a wa wele na, “Leze le kai ya Yohana.” Na pate epa eme tere ne okpwe.
LUK 1:64 Malo nyimi na ongmǝ wai pǝrnu a leleng le wai dingarnu, na wa lya izi ka o beya angmǝ o saba Ashili.
LUK 1:65 Na epa eme tere ana o tokwilǝ to ting one okpwe, na pate aromo a topepeng te eeno to mayara ma o makeke ma Yahudiya ne be ngmǝ epa ena ane kone ane kang laka.
LUK 1:66 Pate andaaka ne kone nane eke anyong ane, ane bekaana, “Kena kaana kayo ya nannia?” Ka legoone le Ateokora leye azaa kai.
LUK 1:67 Na obere o rere tare ka ate a kai Zakariya aka beke letoma le Ashili na:
LUK 1:68 “O saba itǝ a Ateokora, Ashili aromo aro abuudu a Yakubu, kawa de na wa boze ro aromo a ai.
LUK 1:69 A wa ara ondo legoone lo boza a nyimi akwilǝ ozara ai Daoda,
LUK 1:70 (nangka Ashili a beke a tongmǝ te andaaka ne beya a ngmǝ ka mawo ma ai ka o rabo).
LUK 1:71 O boza a taara te ana o nyana oro ka aza legoone le ana o nyalang kaaro.
LUK 1:72 Ka wa sǝǝrǝ ondo legoone lo boza adorana wa wore egonegone ana magonggong maro. A wa kang panza o tono wai o sangsang,
LUK 1:73 o tono ka wa ye ogonggong oro Ibraheng.
LUK 1:74 O bekaana, a boze ro ba taara te ana o nyana oro, adorana te tare ai zora o kona boome.
LUK 1:75 A nyimi be sangsang ka o cikǝ oka Ashili a kone o leba a begeshe be ai kazo tomore tero.
LUK 1:76 “A bo kena kang, aromo neyo rarau na, ondo o beya a ngmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili ondo kala o gongnga o bena oyo kala izi a Ateokora ka o babare orona o deya kai.
LUK 1:77 O nya o rosa o boza aromo au nangka wa kwizǝ madinǝ ma ne,
LUK 1:78 aza egonegone e jǝng Ashili aro. Aza egonegone ai ongme zaale ba ro a suri azaa shili
LUK 1:79 ka wa nya masanto ba andaame ne cikǝ a maring nyimia ana o cikǝ a boome be o ululu gbwǝ, ka wa tare ka tobona tero a nyimi be cammo.”
LUK 1:80 A kena kame gong aka itǝ ka legoone a nyimi obe re Ashili, a ka ya nyimi o wake zongka ka wore okpwe kai ba buudu a Yakubu.
LUK 2:1 A nyimi tomore tome, Ogomo ogong o Roma Kaisar Agustas waya ogomo ogong a pate makeke ma Roma wa ote o bena a bale pate aromo aka neya nyimi togomo te Roma.
LUK 2:2 (Aya a balo o bora a were e ka Kiriniyas wa ya togomo a makeke ma Suriya.)
LUK 2:3 Na aromo a pate ne kuri a topepeng to ne adorana a bale ne.
LUK 2:4 A Yusupu wa ere apeng Nazarat a nyimi makeke ma Galili na wa ale apeng Baitalami a makeke ma Yahudiya, araaka a ngmeng ogomo Daoda ne. Yusupu wa ale saname aza o bekaana ne abuudu ayende ai ka na Daoda
LUK 2:5 Wa ale ka Mariya kando kamea wa ya caasa me a kaye ka etumǝ, adorana a bale ne.
LUK 2:6 A were aka neya Baitalami, na tomore to ngmenga kai toye,
LUK 2:7 naka ngmeng kena ka kai ka o bora. Naka urǝ kai ka majembele aka nata kai a nyimi o onggo o nyaza emande epaolya, aza o bena a dera odo akwilǝ ageng.
LUK 2:8 A ana o tare ka emande epeng ya za o eza ogole one a lelyaare o wake a ma'amo ka apeng a Baitalami.
LUK 2:9 Na otoma o surǝ a zaa shili wa suri a nyimi one, a masanto ma Ashili ma malmi a nyimi one, nane kala o ara o kona boome.
LUK 2:10 Na otoma Ashili o zaa shili bekaa ne na, “Tane kone boome ne. Ma ca ying oroka o lebo, omea wayo ote aromo a pate kane kone o leba.
LUK 2:11 O ngmeengme na, a nyimi apeng a Daoda, a ngmenga ondo boza o ying Ondooka Ashili a zake Ateokora.
LUK 2:12 Enna eyo itǝ aying epa o kabare, eyo mana kena a pate a nyimi majembele kanza a nata kai a nyimi o onggo.”
LUK 2:13 A saseya na leguki le atoma a Ashili o zaa shili ne suri. Ane mana oyende name, nane saba Ashili ane beye na,
LUK 2:14 “A saba Ashili azaa shili bedake, a nyimi lerambo le Ashili o cikǝ o cammo wa itǝ ka andaaka Ashili kone o leba one.”
LUK 2:15 Nangka Atoma Ashili o zaa shili ne kuri ba zaa shili ane baya ne, na ana o tare ka emande me bekaa tokpwe to ne na, “Era na nanname ka ale o Baitalami ka laka epa eka Ateokora wa bele ro.”
LUK 2:16 Nyimia ne ere a saseya nane mana Mariya ka Yusupu, ka kena kame ane nata kai a nyimi o onggo.
LUK 2:17 Nangka ana o tare ka emande me ne laka kai, nane baale epa eka otoma Ashili o zaa shili wa bele ne ba zaa kena kame.
LUK 2:18 Pate aromo ka ne kone oroka me, na epa eme tere ne okpwe ba za epa eka ana o tare ka emande ne bele ne.
LUK 2:19 Na Mariya onte pate epa eka a beya a lenyong le kai.
LUK 2:20 Ana o tare ka emande me ne kuri, ane beye leera ane saba Ashili, aza epa eka ne kona ka e epa eka ne laka. Nane eze keeya nangka otoma Ashili o zaa shili wa bele ne.
LUK 2:21 A lengme lo riiru, na core kena kame, a nya kai leze na Yeso, leze lee mea otoma Ashili o zaa shili wa nya a ta aya e tumǝ kai ne.
LUK 2:22 Nangka a were o kwizǝ madinǝ ma iini me nangka maYahuda ezeze wa ye na Mariya ka Yusupu ne ale ka Yeso apeng Urushalima adorana a niyi kai ba Ateokora, nangka angmǝ aka Ashili a nya Mosa a beke.
LUK 2:23 Nyimia a wele ba ngmǝ a Ateokora, “Pate kena ka lome ko bora kamea a ngmenga a yo beya kai na kena ka sangsang ka Ateokora.”
LUK 2:24 Nane core egoma leere o wore bekaana ne tare e epa eka angmǝ a Ateokora a beke o kwizǝ madinǝ ma iini.
LUK 2:25 A were me ondaleme yende wa zene apeng a Urushalima ka a beya wai na Siman. Wa ya sangsang lenyong, a wa tare Ashili, kanza wa ya zaa o enda lengme leeka a yo boza aromo a Yahuda. A obere Ashili wa tare ka wai.
LUK 2:26 Na obere Ashili me wa bekaa wai na wato gbwǝ ne seeka wa laka Ondooka Ashili a zake oka Ateokora wa tong.
LUK 2:27 O bero o sangsang me wa tare ka wai na wa lyǝ atatara akwilǝ Ashili, ba were name iini ka ate a Yeso ne de ka kai kane eze e epa eka angmǝ Ashili a beke na ne eze.
LUK 2:28 Na Siman ana kena kame ba taara te wai a wa saba Ashili, a wa beyana,
LUK 2:29 “Ondo o gong Ateokora, ka a yizi ang ma laka ondo o boza,
LUK 2:30 nangka ba beka, baya ozara o wa ale a cammo.
LUK 2:31 Ondo boza ona ka ba nya a pate aromo neya gonta,
LUK 2:32 masanto ma o pari a yizi aworme kanza ka o sana aromo au maYahuda.”
LUK 2:33 Na epa eme tere okpwe ate ka iini kena kame aza epa eka a bekaa ba za kena kame.
LUK 2:34 A Siman me bekaa angmǝ lebo aza one, a wa bekaa Mariya iini kena kame na, “Ashili a Zaka kena kaana ka ka itǝ orona o rizi andaaka ne nyana kai ka o boza ona ondo ba cake a Yahuda aka ne emba kai, kanza wa itǝ e epa eka aromo a cake neto yeme ne.
LUK 2:35 Aza nyimi a yo bangali madoola ma nyongnga cake. Bo ma Mariya oyo kona a kpwaiye na o sagali wa donga lenyong leo.”
LUK 2:36 Kando ka o beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili ka rene kanza, ka a beya kai na Hanatu, ongmenga Panuel ka abuudu ana Ashiru, ka ka she ong. Ka cikǝ ka ondaleme kai shenai sondaare malome a wa gbwi,
LUK 2:37 nyimia ka cikǝ legbwǝri shenai tuuru riiru ka se naaze. Ka ta ka tukǝ baya akwilǝ Ashili ne lelyaare ka letereme aza o gera mainu ma Ashili, ka pateze ongmǝ aka beeze angmǝ ka Ashili.
LUK 2:38 Ka o deya kai ane a were name, naka wore o leba kai ba Ashili a ka beke angmǝ ba za kena kame andaaka neya soola o boza pate aromo a Urushalima.
LUK 2:39 Nangka Yusupu ka Mariya ne mare pate epa eka angmǝ a Ateokora beke, ane kuri apeng ane Narazat a makeke ma Galili.
LUK 2:40 Na kena kame ka gong a kaye legoone, a Ashili tare ka kai a nyimi o rosa, a masanto ma Ashili ma ya zaa o kai.
LUK 2:41 Koonang lenai a ate ka iini Yeso ne aleze ba Urushalima aza o gwarnang o rintǝ o surǝ maYahuda a makeke ma Masar.
LUK 2:42 A were oka Yeso ka dukǝ shenai betuuru ka se leere, nane ale ka kai a gwarnang name nangka makili mane maze.
LUK 2:43 Nangka ne mare o gwarnang ome, aneya orona o kurǝ akwilǝ ane apeng Nazarat, na Yeso kena ka itǝ a dimǝ a Urushalima, ana ate ka iini kai ta rosa ne.
LUK 2:44 Neya madoola ma o bekaana kaye legwa ka ne, nane were a teweno. Malo nyimia nane bore o gera kai ba nyimi arone ane ka ajaa kai.
LUK 2:45 Nangka neta ne laka kai ne, nane kuri ba Urushalima a gera kai.
LUK 2:46 Malo tomore to taaro nane cǝ kai ba nyimi atatara akwilǝ Ashili, aka ya cikǝ a tera ana o baala ngmǝ Ashili, aka ya konaza aka kang eza ne be pirǝ.
LUK 2:47 Pate ondooka wa kone kai na epa eme tǝru a wai a lenyong aza o rosa kai ka nangka ka kabareze.
LUK 2:48 Nangka ate ka iini Yeso ne laka kai, nane kerke ko kona o leba. Na iini kai bekaa kai na, “Kena, eyaka baya ro nanna? Me ka ate au te zitǝ a gera o.”
LUK 2:49 Naka pirkǝ ne na, “Eyaka eya gera ong? Eta rosa o bena ma era anta arnang ka kwilǝ ate ang ne na?”
LUK 2:50 Nane ta rosa epa eka ka ya beya me ne.
LUK 2:51 Naka kuri apeng a Nazarat kaa ne aka tare ngmǝ ane. A iini kai onte pate epaname a lenyong le kai.
LUK 2:52 Na Yeso gongnga a lepung, ka o rosa o cak, kanza a Ashili ka aromo yeme kai.
LUK 3:1 Ashili a bekaa ngmǝ ka Yohana kena ka Zakariya o wake a were aka Ogomo Buntus Bilatus waya togomo ba nyimi makeke ma Yahudiya. A Ogomo Hiridus waya togomo ba Galili. Orone o wai ka lebangi lene leyende tazane Pilibus waya togomo ba Ituriya ka Tarakunitas. A Lisaniyas waya togomo ba Abilenes.
LUK 3:2 A were aka na Hanana ka Kayapa neya agomo magame ma Ashili, a were name Ogomo ogong o Roma Kaisar Tibariya waya ogomo ogong o pate makeke mame ka Roma, a waya nyimi lenai le betuuru ka esu le togomo te wai.
LUK 3:3 Na Yohana ale kuruwǝ a makeke ma ting obeno Urdung, a wa zoole a wa beya na, aromo ne arnang ka madinǝ mane a eze ne o batisma adorana a kwizǝ madinǝ mane.
LUK 3:4 Nangka a wele angmǝ Ishaya ondo o beya a ngmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili o bena: “Ondo ya beya angmǝ a jǝng o wake, ‘Babarana Ashili orona, nayina kai marona mame.
LUK 3:5 A yo panzaza pate mapati, a pose cale amea a ya orona pate ka a'owa Ara a ka orona me wa gendarono a yo nayii wai, araaka orona me wa burǝ, a yo babara wai ka wa rere.
LUK 3:6 A pate aromo neyo laka o boza Ashili.’ ”
LUK 3:7 Nangka aromo a cake ne deya a Yohana ka ye ne o batisma na wa bekaana, “Ying o kurkǝnǝng ewa ee buru. Mana wa zoola ying na e arnang ka epa e buru emea Ashili ya deya ne aying?
LUK 3:8 Ezana epa eka eyo wore o bekaana e arnang ka madinǝ ma ying e kurǝ a Ashili. Kanza ‘Tane beya tokpwe toying na Ibraheng waya ate arone.’ Eyang beelo ying, Ashili ama o nya Ibraheng ayana nyimi acale na.
LUK 3:9 Betemo beya ting uti, pate uti omea wata ngwengza ayana a rere ne, a yo genda wai ka kare a nyimi ola.”
LUK 3:10 Na aromo me pirkǝ na, “Eya teyo ya nanname?”
LUK 3:11 Na Yohana kabare na wa bekaana, “Ondo oka waya ka madibi ma leere, a wa nya ondooka wata ka mai ne oyende, ondooka waya ka epaolya, a wai ma wa nyapa andaaka neta ka e ne.”
LUK 3:12 Ana o eesa emate makeke ne ma nane de adorana a eze ne o batisma. Nane pirkǝ kai o bena “Ondo baala, eya gbara te ye?”
LUK 3:13 Nawa bekaane na, “Tane embe emate makeke ka e kale epa eka a bekaa ying na e embe ne.”
LUK 3:14 Na ana o tesa geza moole pirkǝ wai na, “Aaro kanza eya teya yame?” Nawa bekaa ne na, “Tane ote aromo kane nya ying emate ka legoone ne, kanza tane anane majakari ne, zanta na ka epa eka a arseze ying.”
LUK 3:15 Aromo me neya aza o enda ondo boza, nane bore madoola anyong obena Yohana oromo omea Ashili a bekaana aya tonga ne na?
LUK 3:16 Na Yohana bekaa pate one na, “Mi ang eze ying o batisma ka manyi, ondooka waya deya a malo ong, wa kalang o gongnga, anta bare ang dinggi sejǝng se tokakau to wai ne. Wai wayo eza o batisma o wai ka obere o Ashili kanza ka ola.
LUK 3:17 Epa o saka epaolya ya taara te wai, wayo zeera elya e wai, kanza wayo eke elya a lebengga le wai, a wa ese masuni mame ka ola ome awata lambuzu ne.”
LUK 3:18 Ka angmǝ a cak abelo anna, Yohana zoole aromo a wa baale ne angmǝ lebo Ashili.
LUK 3:19 Na Yohana me kanza wa zoole Ogomo Hiridus, aza epa eka wa eza, wa ana Hirudiya ondaye orone wai Pilibus na wa itǝ ondaye wai, kanza a wa eze magogoro ma buru.
LUK 3:20 O maare ekeeya, Ogomo Hiridus wa wale eza epa eburu, wa ote na moke Yohana na pate wai akwilǝ ana o ezeza epa eburu.
LUK 3:21 Malo oka Yohana wa eze aromo o batisma a pate na wa kang eza Yeso, a were e ka kaya beya ngmǝ ka Ashili, na za a shili me pǝrnu,
LUK 3:22 na o bere orere o Ashili wa japi aza kai naa kagoma. Nane kone lengmelo ale suri aza shili na le bekaana, “Boa kena kang ang yemo, ang kone o leba o ba cak.”
LUK 3:23 A were aka Yeso ka bore ogole kai, kaye ka shenai tuuru taaro ko ngmenga. Aromo ne jeke o bekaana kai kena ka Yusupu kaye, Yusupu kena ka Heli.
LUK 3:24 Heli kena ka Matat, a Matat kena ka Lawi. Lawi kena ka Malki, a Malki kena ka Yana. Yana kena ka Yusupu,
LUK 3:25 a Yusupu kena ka Matatiya. Matatiya kena ka Amos, a Amos kena ka Nahum. Nahum kena ka Asele, a Asele kena ka Najaya.
LUK 3:26 Najaya kena ka Ma'ata, Ma'ata kena ka Matatiya. Matatiya kena ka Shimeya, Shimeya kena ka Yosek. Yosek kena ka Yoda,
LUK 3:27 a Yoda kena ka Yowanan. Yowanan kena ka Reesa, a Reesa kena ka Zerubabel. Zerubabel kena ka Sheyaltiyel, a Sheyaltiyel kena ka Niri.
LUK 3:28 Niri kena ka Malki, Malki kena ka Adi. Adi kena ka Kosama, a Kosama kena ka Elmadama. Elmadama kena ka Er,
LUK 3:29 a Er kena ka Yoshuwa. Yoshuwa kena ka Eliyeza, Eliyeza kena ka Yorim. Yorim kena ka Matat, Matat kena ka Lawi.
LUK 3:30 Lawi kena ka Siman, a Siman kena ka Yahuda. Yahuda kena ka Yusupu, Yusupu kena ka Yonam. Yonam kena ka Eliyakim,
LUK 3:31 Eliyakim kena ka Meleeya. Meleeya kena ka Menna, Menna kena ka Matata. Matata kena ka Natan, a Natan kena ka Daoda,
LUK 3:32 a Daoda kena ka Yese, Yese kena ka Obed, a Obed kena ka Bowaza, Bowaza kena ka Salmon. Salmon kena ka Nashon,
LUK 3:33 a Nashon kena ka Aminadab. Aminadab kena ka Aram, Aram kena ka Hezron. Hezron kena ka Perez, a Perez kena ka Yahuda,
LUK 3:34 a Yahuda kena ka Yakub, Yakub kena ka Ishaku. Ishaku kena ka Ibraheng, Ibraheng kena ka Tera. Tera kena ka Nahor,
LUK 3:35 a Nahor kena ka Serug. Serug kena ka Reyu, a Reyu kena ka Peleg, Peleg kena ka Eber, Eber kena ka Shela,
