LUK 3:36 a Shela kena ka Kenan, Kenan kena ka Arpakshad. Arpakshad kena ka Shem, a Shem kena ka Nuhu. Nuhu kena ka Lamek,
LUK 3:37 Lamek kena ka Metusela. Metusela kena ka Enok, a Enok kena ka Yared. Yared kena ka Mahalalel, Mahalalel kena ka Kenan,
LUK 3:38 a Kenan kena ka Enosh, Enosh kena ka Set. Set kena ka Adamu, a Adamu kena ka Ashili.
LUK 4:1 Yeso ka deye aka suri obeno Urdung obere Ashili wa panza kai, obere Ashili me na wa tare ka kai, a wa ale ka kai o wake.
LUK 4:2 A saname na ogomo obere oburu wa kedeya kai a nyimi tomore tuuru naaze aka ta ka lya eyapa ne, o maare tomore teme na ekomo moke kai.
LUK 4:3 Na ogomo obere oburu bekaa kai na, “Boa baaya dongdong Kena ka Ashili, kuriyǝ lecale leena kale itǝ oborode.”
LUK 4:4 Na Yeso bekaana, “A wela nyimi angmǝ Ashili na ‘Epaolya ta montaza oromo belle ne.’ ”
LUK 4:5 Malo nyimi na ogomo obere oburu wa ana kai na wa ale ka kai azaa kazalo ka yende, na wa wore kai togomo teeka te zene a walau ba nyimi lerambo le ogomo shili.
LUK 4:6 Nawa bekaa kai na, “Eyang nyau pate legoone aza togomo ka epa emea eya nyimi te, obekaana pate te teya taara tong, ma era ang nya komana ondooka ma yeme.
LUK 4:7 Aza nyimi, ba girwǝ o tareng teyo itǝ tateo apat.”
LUK 4:8 Na Yeso bekaana wai na, “Angmǝ Ashili a bekaana, ‘Ateokora Ashili aya bare a girwǝ a tare ai a kang eza ai ogole. Aya ayo girwǝ a eze ai ogole belle.’ ”
LUK 4:9 Na ogomo obere oburu wa ale ka Yeso a Urushalima na wa zale ka kai ara o kala be zaati ba akwilǝ a Ashili. Awa bekaana, “Bo Kena ka Ashili a baaza canko ara kaana ko taru a deze.
LUK 4:10 Aza o bena angmǝ Ashili bekaana, ‘A yo ote atoma Ashili o zaa shili kane wobo ane tare ka bo.
LUK 4:11 Neyo wobo ka taara tene nangka oto jukǝ obona o oo cale ne.’ ”
LUK 4:12 Na Yeso bekaana, “A wela angmǝ Ashili kanza na ‘Tana o kedeya Ashili Ateokora o ne.’ ”
LUK 4:13 Nangka ogomo obere oburu wa mare okedeya Yeso ba kuruwǝ, na wa baya kai a were me suri.
LUK 4:14 Yeso ka kuri ba makeke ma Galili akaa pena ka legoone le obere orere, na oroka azaa kai wa ale kuruwame a makeke mame.
LUK 4:15 Aka baale ne a nyimi madandaro ma o gwarzanang ma mane, na komana sabe kai.
LUK 4:16 Nangka ka ale a apeng Nazarat araaka ka gong ne, na ka lyǝ ba nyimi o dandaro gwarzanang maYahuda a lengme lo teeseke one, nangka ka mena ezaza me. Naka ere a itǝ kaka baale angmǝ Ashili.
LUK 4:17 Na nya kai angmǝ Ashili aka Ishaya ondo o beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili wa be, naka dingi araaka a bekaana,
LUK 4:18 “Obere Ateokora waya mi. Wa zakang kang beye ngmǝ a lebo ana o dera ocǝ. Wa tongang kang ale kang baale andaaka a tesa ne na a yo dinggǝ ne. Arǝ kanza a yo pari ne a yizi. Andaaka a noke ne ane cǝ o era.
LUK 4:19 Kanza ang baale komana me o bekaana a were ka Ashili a yo wore yeme o ai o boza aromo wa dukǝ.”
LUK 4:20 Malo nyimi naka gbwindari angmǝ me, aaka nya ondo eza ogole o dandaro o gwarzanang maYahuda e wela me, aka ale naka cikǝ. Na komana a nyimi arakaname kare kai yizi.
LUK 4:21 Ka bore bekaana, “Angmǝ Ashili ana ka e kona a nannameena a pena o ngmeengme na.”
LUK 4:22 Pate aromo kane zene arame ne kone oleba kai. A epame kang tera ne okpwe ka ngmǝ ka a susi ongmǝ kai. Ane bore opirǝ na, “Kakama a waani e paana ye nanna kena ka Yusupu tazana ne?”
LUK 4:23 Na Yeso bekaane na, “Eng rose o bena eyo bekang angmǝ a gerpo na, ‘Ondo nyaza makang, womza okpwe o, o bekaana, eza epa eka te kona a ba eza a Kaparnahum apeng au Nazarat.’ ”
LUK 4:24 Na kakang bekaana, “Eyang belo ying e peng eme, a ta kabare ka ondo o beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashil a apeng wai ne.
LUK 4:25 Ang wale bele oying ne, a were a Ileya ondo o beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili, a gwari andaye ne zene ane kang ya a nyimi o dera ne gong a nyimi Isrela. A were ame na eze mawo shenai se taaro ka mareka o taashe, ne komo gǝǝzǝ aromo a kuruwǝ a nyimi makeke mame.
LUK 4:26 Pate ka nyimi, a ta atong Ileya a ondo one ne, atong wai ara ogeng ogwǝri ondaye apeng Zaripat a nyimi makeke Sidon.
LUK 4:27 Agangca gong a cak a nyimi a Isrela a were a Elisha ondo o beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili, a ta a womza ondo one ne, soona Naaman oromo makeke ma Suriya.”
LUK 4:28 Pate aromo ka neye o dandaro gwarzanang maYahuda, malo kona epa eka ka beke, nane kone o kara.
LUK 4:29 Ane ere nane sǝǝrǝ Yeso ba nyimi apeng ane, nane ale ka kai e daki oyara oka a soo apeng me ne, adorana ne turki kai a saname kaka rizi a deze ka ka gbwi.
LUK 4:30 Pate ka nyimi naka kale a tera one, aka ale o ale okai.
LUK 4:31 Na Yeso ale a Kaparnahum apeng yende a nyimi makeke ma Galili, ara namea ka lyǝzǝ o dandaro o gwarnazang maYahuda, aka baale ne koonang lengme lo teseke.
LUK 4:32 Na o baala kai wa tere ne okpwe aza obena angmǝ okai aya susǝ ka legoone.
LUK 4:33 A nyimi dandaro gwarzanang maYahuda mame, ondo zene waye ka obere oburu. Na oromo me rurayi a jǝng a Yeso a wa bekaana,
LUK 4:34 “Haing. Eya manyimau ka ro, Yeso karomo ka Nazarat? Ba deya ka o mare legoone le ro na? Ang rose obena boa mana, boa ondo surǝ Ashili.”
LUK 4:35 Na Yeso zurki obere oburu me jǝng aka bekaana, “Kome a set, o surea nyimi lepung le oromo na.” Na obere o buru me tare oromo me a deze aza yizi komana. Nawa suri a wa baya wai zora o jukǝ wai kanza.
LUK 4:36 Pate aromo ka neya rame nane moke ma ngmǝ mane, ane bekaa tokpwe tone naa, “Embele ya karomo kana kaa ya? Ka zurki aka beke obere oburu na suri oromo me, na wa suri.”
LUK 4:37 Epa eka Yeso kaye na oroka wa ale kuruwǝ a pate makeke mame.
LUK 4:38 Malo oka Yeso ka suri ba nyimi o dandaro gwarzanang maYahuda a lengme leng name naka ale ba akwilǝ a Siman. Naka mana ondawa Siman me aka waya kono ka o pimǝ, nane bose Yeso adorana ka womza kai.
LUK 4:39 Na Yeso me zungdǝ kai aka zurki o pimǝ me na o pimǝ me wa pere kai. Ko ya nyimi, naka ere ba saseya aka sele ne epaolya.
LUK 4:40 Nangka ulyǝlu ye, pate andaaka neye ka ana o kombela kono a kapeng kame nane deese kaa ne a ka eese taara aza one ane cǝsǝ lewoma.
LUK 4:41 Ana ondo one neya ka mabere ma buru na ma susi aza legoone le ngmǝ akai, ane gware koko ane beyaana, “Boa Kena ka Ashili.” Aza o bena ne rose o bekaana kaya Yeso, na Yeso zoole ane, aka nare ne o beya ngmǝ.
LUK 4:42 Nangka ara a sane, na Yeso baya apeng me a ka ale araaka aromo ta zene ne. Na aromo dato gere kai kurǝwǝ, nangka ne cǝ kai nane bose kai na tana ka arnang ka ne ne.
LUK 4:43 Na Yeso me bekaa ne na, “Ashili a tongang kang dongdong ale kale toma le lebo le togomo te ai a topepeng toyende kanza.”
LUK 4:44 Na Yeso lya izi ko kaale aka baale aromo a nyimi madandaro ma gwarnang maYahuda a pate makeke ma Yahudiya.
LUK 5:1 Ngmende a Yeso ya itǝ a bengmǝ be lepung leeka a beya le na Janisarata. Na aroma aaka ne kurkǝnǝng a cake ne nonte kai adorana ne kone angmǝ Ashili.
LUK 5:2 Na Yeso laka ma'onggo ma o taara manyi maleere a bengmǝ be lepung, ka ana o meeshe ekwala ane japi aneya kwizǝ majara mane.
LUK 5:3 Na Yeso lyǝ o onggo yende o Biturusu, naka bekaa wai na wa turki o onggo me a nyimi manyi a baate. A nyimi mea ka cikǝ ne aka baale aromo me.
LUK 5:4 Nangka ka mare o baala, naka bekaa Biturusu na, “Waleke o turki o onggo me a ale ara a gerpo, e tare ojara me a manyi ka o meke ekwala.”
LUK 5:5 Na Biturusu bekaana, “Ondoogong, te more a pate lelyaare a gera na teta meke eyapa ne. Nangka ba beka nyimi, eyang ya nangka ba beka.”
LUK 5:6 Nangka neye nyimi, nane meke ekwala a cak, na majara mame bore o taso.
LUK 5:7 Ka o laka nyimi, nane wali andaane kane ya nyimi o onggo leere kane deya ne kankama ne. Nyimia ne de nane lope ekwala me a nyimi ojara nane panza ma'onggo ma leere mo taara manyi ka ekwala, nyimia na ma yemo lyǝ ba tau manyi.
LUK 5:8 Nangka Siman Biturusu wa laka nyimi a wa surǝ nyimi manyi, na wa tunggunǝ a tulung tewai ating Yeso, a wa bekaana, “Arnang ka mi Ateokora, mi ondo madinǝ wai.”
LUK 5:9 Aza o bena wai ka andaaka neye legwa ne kala aro kerke ko laka e kwala e cake kane meke,
LUK 5:10 nyimia ana Yakubu ka Yohana ayana Zabadi ejaa Biturusu ne kanza ne kerke. Na Yeso bekaa a Siman na, “Kana o kone boome ne, ba itǝ ondo o rara aromo kane deya mi o meese ekwala watoza ne.”
LUK 5:11 Nangka ne windi ma'onggo ma o meese ekwala ene o wulu lepung, nane baya ekeeya ene ane tare kai.
LUK 5:12 Ngmende Yeso kaye apeng yende, na oromo yende de a leganca le lya legoone le wai. Nangka wa laka Yeso, na wa girwǝnǝ ka tulung a deze, a wa kang tunggunǝ maiyinu ma wai ating kai. A wa bose kai na, “Ateokora, ba kabare ba era o kpizi leganca leng.”
LUK 5:13 Na Yeso niyi o ara kai, naka meke wai. Aka bekaana, “Ma kabare ya sangsang.” Na leganca pere wai a saseya.
LUK 5:14 Na Yeso windi wai teto na, “Kana o beka a ondo ne, o ale ko wore okpwe o ondo magame ma akwilǝ Ashili, okang nya epa eka a yo esa nangka angmǝ aka Ashili nya Mosa beke. Ya nyimi ko wore aromo bekaana ba woma.”
LUK 5:15 Pate ka o windi teto ka Yeso ka ye, oroka azaa kai wa waleke lya izi ne, na aromo a cake deese a konaza kai, ko gera o bekaana ne woma aza makono mane.
LUK 5:16 Na Yeso ka baya ara name aka gere araaka aromo tazene ne adorana ka beya ngmǝ ka Ashili nangka ka mena a ezaza.
LUK 5:17 Ngmende Yeso kaya baala, na maParisa ma yende ka ana o baala ngmǝ ka Ashili nya Mosa ne deya a suri a topepeng te makeke ma Galili, ka Yahudiya, apeng Urushalima neya rame. A legoone le Ashili lo womzaza ana o dera o kona zake le ye ka kai.
LUK 5:18 Aza nyimi andaleme yende ne de ane ana oromo omea lepung le wai le gbwǝ aza kapengge, aneya nyamalanǝ kane lyǝǝrǝ wai a nyimi odo kane de ka wai ara Yeso.
LUK 5:19 Nangka neta ne cǝ orona oya epa eka neya yeme me ne aza o gongnga aromo. Azaa nyimi nane zale o ogǝnggǝng odo, nane puki ogǝnggǝng me ane jipǝrǝ wai pate ka o penge omea waya tete azame. Nane eke wai a tera aromo a begeshe be Yeso.
LUK 5:20 Nangka Yeso ka laka nangka ne kabare ka kai, naka bekaa oromo me na, “Beja beng, ma kwizau madinǝ mau.”
LUK 5:21 Na maParisa ka ana o baala ngmǝ ka Ashili nya Mosa ne bore o beya angmǝ a tokpwe tone na, “Mana waana ka wa ya beya a ngmǝ a buru aza Ashili? Mana wa era a wa pisi madinǝ bangka Ashili belle ne?”
LUK 5:22 Yeso ka rose madoola ma nyong mane na ka pirkǝ na, “Eyaka eya eza madoola mana a nyongnga ying?
LUK 5:23 Eya kala o dera o poba o beka: O bena a kwizǝ madinǝ mau na, o jeke kapengge kau o yengai?
LUK 5:24 Eyang yeme e rose o bena, mi Kena ka Oromo ang ye ka legoone a lerambo le Ashili leena o kwizǝ madinǝ.” Aka ringgarnu naka beka ondooka lepung le wai le gbwǝ na, “Ma beka bo na era, jeka kapengge kau o ale akwilǝ.”
LUK 5:25 Nawa ong era a itǝ a saseya a pate aromo neya za o gonta, na wa gbwindari kapengge kame a waya tetene, a wa ale akwilǝ a wa ya saba Ashili.
LUK 5:26 Na komana one laka epa boome, ane saba Ashili. Nane wale o kona boome o bekaana, “O ngmeengme te laka epa o kala begeshe be ro.”
LUK 5:27 Malo nyimi a Yeso suri naka laka ondo eesa emate makeke ka a rareze wai na Lawi a waya cikǝ ara o eesa emate makeke mame. Na Yeso bekaa wai na “tareng.”
LUK 5:28 Na Lawi baya e keeya ka e keeya, a wa ere na wa tare kai.
LUK 5:29 Aza nyimi na Lawi rare ozǝnggǝ o gong azaa Yeso akwilǝ wai. Na ana o eesa emate makeke ka aromo yende cake ne epaolya ka ne.
LUK 5:30 Na maParisa ka ana o baala ngmǝ ka Ashili nya Mosa aka neema maParisa mai ne ale ka oroka a ngmang-ngmang ara ana o tare o Yeso. Nane pirkǝ na, “Eyaka e lyeeze e kang soza ka ana o eesa emate makeke ka andaaka ne kanza ana madinǝa ne?”
LUK 5:31 Na Yeso kabare na, “Andaaka neya zake neta aleze ara ondo nyaza makanne, sekona ana o kono belle.
LUK 5:32 Anta ma deya kang rare ana nyongnga sangsang kane kuri a Ashili ne. Ma deya kang rare ana madinǝ kane baya madinǝ mane ane kuri Ashili.”
LUK 5:33 Na aromo yende pirkǝ Yeso na, “Ana o tare o Yohana ko batisma ezeze o meke ongmǝ ko beya ngmǝ ka Ashili, nyimi ana o tare o maParisa kang ezaza, ana o tare o sooze ane lyeeze epaolya zora o pate ongmǝ.”
LUK 5:34 Na Yeso kabare naka bekaa ne na, “E era e ote ejaa ondooka wa surǝ ana ondaye osau na wa pate ongmǝ a neye legwa na?
LUK 5:35 Rosa na o bekaana a were ya deya ka ondo surǝ ana ondaye osau, a yo jeka wai a baya ne, a were name neyo pate ongmǝ.”
LUK 5:36 Naka bele ne angmǝ a gerpo na, “Ondo ta rene ka wa era wa mangka odibi o sau ka wa pate o dibi o kozo ne ne. Waa ya nyimi, a wa itǝ o bekaana wa cara o dibi wai osau naname. Ojembele osau me a wa core o dibi osau wa era wata ale garre ne ka o dibi kozo ome ne.
LUK 5:37 Nyimia ondo wa era wata kare manyi ma o inabi ma sau a leboboto lo ngma a kozo ne. Waya nyimi, a boboto a kozo me poso apat ka manyi mo inabi me oko apat ka ekeeye caro.
LUK 5:38 Manyi mo inabi ma sau, soona kare mai aboboto asau.
LUK 5:39 Ondo ta rene ka wa sa manyi mo inabi ma kozo, a wa yeme ma sau ne, a wa yo bekaana, ma kozo mame kala o leba.”
LUK 6:1 A lengme lo teeseke ka o bosa Ashili leyende le maYahuda, na Yeso ka atoma kai ne dare aa nyimi turu te yuu, nane pose ane torbe makpwe mame ane lye.
LUK 6:2 Na maParisa ma yende pirkǝ na, “Eya e ote na eya eza epa eka makili ma Ashili ma were a Mosa ma nara aza lengme lo teeseke ka o bosa Ashili maYahuda?”
LUK 6:3 Na Yeso kabare ne na, “Ying eta e bale epa amea Daoda ka aromo akai ne ye a were ka ne kone komo sang?
LUK 6:4 Naka lyǝ a kapuki ka Ashili, a ka jeke epaolya mea a eke ana magame ma Ashili naka lye, a ka nya ejaa a teweno te kai.”
LUK 6:5 Na Yeso kang bekaa ne na, “Kena ka Oromo, kaya ateokora o lengme lo teeseke.”
LUK 6:6 A lengme le yende lo teeseke le maYahuda, na Yeso lyǝ o dandaro gwarzanang maYahuda, aka baale ne, a mana oromo yende rame oka o ara wai o re wa waka.
LUK 6:7 A maParisa ka ana o baala ngmǝ aka Ashili a nya Mosa ne kare yizi kane laka na Yeso kayo womza oromo me a lengme lo teeshekea na, adorana ne cǝ epa o meke kai.
LUK 6:8 A mana Yeso rose madoola mane, naka beka oromo omea o ara wai wa waka na, “Era ka o deya ko itǝ ara kaana.” Na oromo me wa ere na wa itǝ arame.
LUK 6:9 Na Yeso bekaa ne na, “Eyang pirkǝ o ying, eya gbara aye a lengme lo teeseke, a eze epa ererea na, a eze epa e buruai? A boze oromo na naa, a baya wai a wa gbwiai?”
LUK 6:10 Naka gonte ne apat aka beka oromo mea na, “Niyi o ara o.” Na wa niyi o ara me awa woma zak.
LUK 6:11 Azaa nyimia na maParisa ka ana o baala ngmǝ aka Ashili a nya Mosa na nyong ane caro ane gbaara ongmǝ aza epa amea neyo ya ka Yeso.
LUK 6:12 Ngmende a nyimi tomore tong name, na Yeso zale oyara ka ka beya ngmǝ ka Ashili, naka more a saname a beya ngmǝ ka Ashili.
LUK 6:13 Ko sana ara, aka rare ana o tare okai, aka zake ne betuuru ka leere, naka bekaana neya atoma kai.
LUK 6:14 Neya Siman ondooka Yeso ka nya wai leze na Biturusu, orone wai Andarawus, Yakubu, Yohana, Pilibus, Batilomi,
LUK 6:15 Matiyu, Toma, Yakubu kena ka Halpa, Siman kaa beya kai na ka ye kale nyong le makeke ma kai.
LUK 6:16 Ka Yahuda kena ka Yakubu, a Yahuda Iskariyoti ondooka wa lye le kirmǝ le Yeso.
LUK 6:17 Na Yeso japi kaa atoma kai, naka itǝ a deze ara aka aromo a cake ana o tarea kai ne zene. Kanza aromo a cake kane sure a makeke ma Yahudiya ka apeng a Urushalima ka makeke maamea maya ting apeng Taya ka Sidon ka neya ting lepung legong,
LUK 6:18 ne de kane kone kai, aa ne cǝ o woma makono mane a pat. Adaamea o bere buru wa gare ne a womza ne,
LUK 6:19 na komana one ere a waya yeme o meke okai aza o bena legoone le obere o rere waya susǝ a kai aka womza ana ma kono mame apat.
LUK 6:20 A Yeso kare atoma kai yizi aka bekaa ne na, “Ying ana o kona o leba, andaaka neye ka o dera, yingnga ana akwilǝ a togomo te Ashili nannamena ka izi.
LUK 6:21 Ying ana o kona o leba, andaaka neya komo nanname na, eyo tiyǝ. Ana o kona o leba ying, ana o ruuzi, eyo zoza.
LUK 6:22 Ying ana o kona o leba a were aka aromo ne nyana ying, ane baya ying e daki, ane kang beya ying majakari, ane nya ying leze le buru, aza o kabare ka kena ka oromo.
LUK 6:23 “Aza nyimi konana o leba a lengme leng name e cankozo ko kona o leba, o bena epa eka eyo cǝ eyo gongnga ba zaa shili. Nyimia magonggong mane ne eze ka ana o beya a ngmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili kane kaana ying.
LUK 6:24 “Aying ana ocǝ nanname e lyǝ udi, aza o bena e samba o emba o leba o ying.
LUK 6:25 Ying ana o tiyǝ nanname e lyǝ udi, eyo cikǝ ka ekomo. Ying ana o tozo nanname e lyǝ udi, eyo kona o burǝ ee ruuzi.
LUK 6:26 Ying ka aromo ya saba oying e lyǝ udi, nyimia magonggong mane ma eze ka atoma o rendaza aromo.
LUK 6:27 “Eyang baala o ying, ana o konaza ong, yeme na ana o nyano ying. Andaaka ne nyane ying, eza na ne epa erere.
LUK 6:28 Nya ne o kono leba, ana o eza o ying majakari. E bosa Ashili aza andaaka ne nya ying ba huuwu.
LUK 6:29 Ondo wa ceeto ba letamo le yende, wangare wai lo leere leme. Ondo wa jekau o dibi ogong, lopa ka nyimi ko nya wai kanza.
LUK 6:30 Pate ondooka wa bosa eyapa abo o nya wai, ondooka wa embe epa bo ka legoone, tana o gera o bekaana wa kuriyau ne.
LUK 6:31 Ya aromo epa eka oya yeme ane yo.
LUK 6:32 “Ee yeme andaaka ne yeme yingnga belle, a wiini a ecǝ o kona o leba? Ana madinǝ nyimia ne yemeze andaaka ne yeme ne.
LUK 6:33 Nyimia e eza epa e rere andaaka ne ezeze yingnga belle, a wiinia e cǝ o kona o leba? Ana madinǝ nyimia ne ezeze.
LUK 6:34 Kanza e nyaza o duru ara andaaka e laka a neyo ara yingnga belle, e wiinia e cǝ o kona o leba? Ana madinǝ nyimia ne nyaza na madinǝ o duru, aza o bena neyo ara kap.
LUK 6:35 Ying kanza yeme na ana o nyano ying, eza na ne epa e rere, e nyaza ne o duru zora obena neyo ara ying. A arakanamea, eyo cǝ epa cak, e kang wore o bena ying ayana Ashili ne, o bena wa eze epa e rere aromo mea neta zanta ka epa e rere ka aya ne ne, ka ana ara a buru, nyimia ying ma wa gwara e eze.
LUK 6:36 Itǝna ane egonegone, nangka ate aying Ashili ondo egonegonea ai.
LUK 6:37 “Tana e beke epa e buru aza ondo ne, ato beka aza oying ne. Kana e nyalang ka ondo ne, ato nyalang ka ying ne. Kana e onte ondo a lenyong ne, ato onta yingnga a lenyong ne.
LUK 6:38 Nya na ana ondo, a Ashili a yo nya ying kapa ko gose ka rere, ka a kare ne ngmet, a zokare, ne ooso aza pena, kakang kare angmǝ ma madibi maying. Ka kapa kamea ba gose ne, ka kaya a yo gose o ne.”
LUK 6:39 Na Yeso bele ne a ngmǝ a gerpo na, “Urǝ wa era wa windi urǝ lebenda na? Wa ya nyimi, a pate one ta kala a le'o ne?
LUK 6:40 “Ondo oka a baala wai, wa era wata kala ondo baala wai ne, a baala wai kawa mare, a wa itǝ na ondooka wa baala wai.
LUK 6:41 “Eyaka oya gonta kapa ka baate a liizi le orone o, ota ba laka o kuturu ka waya nyimia liizi lo ne?
LUK 6:42 A wanea o beka orone o na, orone, baya ang lope kapa ba liizi lo, a bo ota ba ama o laka o kuturu kawa ya bo liizi lo ne? Bo ondo o renda aromo kane eze epa buru, bora ko lope o kuturu kawa ya bo a liizi, o ama o gonta ko lope kapa kamea kaya liizi le orone o.
LUK 6:43 “Uti o rere wa era wata ngmenga yanaa buru ne, nyimia uti o buru wa era wata ngmenga ayana rere ne.
LUK 6:44 A rose koonang uti a yana wai yaa. Ba era ota taza ayana osaya uti o kana ne, kona ayana o inabi uti kana ne.
LUK 6:45 Nyimia oromo o rere sǝrsǝzǝ epa e rere a nyimi epa e rere ka e ya wai a lenyong, nyimia oromo o buru wa sǝrsǝzǝ epa e buru a nyimia epa e buru ka eya wai a lenyong. Epa emea eya lenyong eya susi ongmǝ.
LUK 6:46 “Eyaka e rarezeng na ‘Ateokora, Ateokora,’ eta eza epa eka ma bekaa ne?
LUK 6:47 Eyang bele ying nangka waze, ondooka wa deya mi kawa koneze ngmǝ ang, a wa eze ogole ka ai.
LUK 6:48 Waye na ondo sowa akwilǝ wai, na wa kau deze a surku, a wa bore o sowa azaa cale. A were aka obeno wa pena ka manyi dukǝ akwilǝ me, a era a ta oko ne, aza o bena a sowa ai a woma.
LUK 6:49 Nyimia pate ondooka wa kona angmǝ ang, ka wa ta eza ogole ka epa eka ma bekaa ne, wa tore ondooka wa sowa akwilǝ wai e genge. Obeno w a pena ka manyi, ka ma dukǝ akwilǝ me, a yo oko, a kang caro ba pat.”
LUK 7:1 Malo oka Yeso ka beke epaname a pate aromo ya konaza, aka ere naka ale apeng a Kaparnahum.
LUK 7:2 A nyimi apengme, ondoogong ona tesa geza a moole a Roma waye ka ondo a nyimi azara wai oka waya kono na waya gbwǝ, ondo tesa geza a moole ome yeme ozara me ba bote.
LUK 7:3 A ondoogong ana o tesa geza omea wa tukǝ o kona oroka ba zaa Yeso, na wa tong anateandasau maYahuda, kane bose kai adorana aka de kaka boze ozara wai tana wa gbwi ne.
LUK 7:4 Ko dukǝ one ba Yeso, nane bose kai ba cak, ane bekaana, “Oromo ona wa gwara o kankama wai.
LUK 7:5 Wa yeme aromo aro, kanza a wa sowa ro o dandaro gwarzanang maYahuda.”
LUK 7:6 Na Yeso ale kaa ne. Nangka ne amara ka akwilǝ me, na ondo tesa geza a moole me tong ajaa wai ba Yeso kane bekaa kai na, “Ateokora, tano gare okpwe ne, anta bare o deya akwilǝ ang ne.
LUK 7:7 Epa eka e ote na ma tonga ba bo naname, mi anta bare ang deya bo ne, ba sokoo beka ngmǝ, ozara ong yo woma.
LUK 7:8 Mi ang ya taara te ondo, kanza ka ana o tesa geza a moole cak ba taara tong, ma bekaa ondo one na wa ale, a wa ale, ma beka ondo na deya a wa de, ma beka ozara na wa ye epana, a wa ye.”
LUK 7:9 Nangka Yeso ka kone nyimi, na oroka me taru kai a lenyong, naka wangarno ba ana o tare kai, naka bekaa ne na, “Anta ma cǝ ondo a nyimi Isrela kawa kabare ka Ashili ka lenyong leyende na oromo na ne.”
LUK 7:10 Na aromo amea atong ne kuri ba akwilǝ me, ane mana ozara me a wa woma.
LUK 7:11 Malo nyimi na Yeso ale apeng amea beya ai na Nayin, ana o tare o kai ka aromo a cak ne ale ka kai.
LUK 7:12 Nangka ne amara ka buudu lyǝ apengme, nane laka aromo a surǝ ka ekeze ondasau omea a ngmeng wai a yende ba iini wai, ondaleme ondayeme wa rabo ko gbwǝ. A aromo a cak apengme a neye ka wai.
LUK 7:13 Nangka Ateokora ka laka ondayeme, na egonegone moke kai, naka beka ondayeme na, “Tana o ruuzi ne.”
LUK 7:14 Na Yeso ale naka moke ogǝkǝ o keze me, na ana o anza ekeze me itǝ tiiyi. A Yeso beke keze me na, “Ondasau, ma beka bo na era.”
LUK 7:15 Na ondooka wa gbwi wa ere a cikǝ, a wa bore o beya ngmǝ, na Yeso nya iini me wai.
LUK 7:16 Na boome be moke aromo me ba pate, aa ne saba Ashili. Ane bena, “Ondo o beya a ngmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili o gong wa ere a nyimi aro. Ashili a deya a boza aromo ai.”
LUK 7:17 Na oroka epa eka Yeso ka eza, wa ale ba kuruwǝ a nyimi Yahudiya ka makeke maame maya ma'amo ka maamane.
LUK 7:18 Ana o tare o Yohana ondo batisma nane bele wai epa eka ne kona. Na ka rare anda leere ba nyimi one,
LUK 7:19 Na ka tong ne ba ra Ateokora kane pirkǝ na, “Boa Ondooka Ashili a zake ondooka waya deya na, te eke lenyong ba ondo kawa tata dimǝi?”
LUK 7:20 Nangka ne de ara Yeso, nane bekaana, “Yohana ondo batisma wa tonga ro ka te pirkau na, ‘Boa Ondooka Ashili a zake ondooka waya deya na, te eke lenyong ba ondo kawa tata dimǝi?’ ”
LUK 7:21 A were name, Yeso ka womza ana makono, ka na o bere o buru, a ka nya o gonta aza andaaka neta gonta ne.
LUK 7:22 Na Yeso kabare naka bekaa ne na, “kurǝ na ka e bekaa Yohana epa eka e kona, ka epa eka e laka. A pari a yizi rǝ, a gǝdǝ ya teweno, agangca ne cǝ lewoma, a pari teto te rara na neya konaza, andaaka ne gbwǝ ne era, kanza a beya oroka o lebo ara ana o dera.
LUK 7:23 Ondo kona o leba oromo oka wa ote lenyong le wai a mi.”
LUK 7:24 Malo kurǝ atoma Yohana, na Yeso bore o beya ngmǝ ka leguki le aromo aza Yohana, naka bekaana, “E ale o wake a laka eya? E ale ba laka ma wake ma ehywo mame obere ya pǝbǝ me na?
LUK 7:25 Nyimia wa taza ne, e ale a laka e ya? E ale a laka ondooka wa amba magogoro ma rere na? Ana o ambaza magogoro me mate, o cikǝ o lebo neya akwilǝ ogomoa.
LUK 7:26 Na eya e ale a laka me? Otoma Ashili na? Nyimia waa za, eyang bele o ying, wa kala otoma Ashili.
LUK 7:27 Yohana waya oromo ome angmǝ Ashili a bekaana, “ ‘Ma tonga otoma ong kawa kale a izi, ondooka wayo babaro orona zongka o de.’
LUK 7:28 Eyang belo ying, Yohana kala ko mana o gongnga a nyimi aromo aka a ngmenga. Pate ka nyimi ondooka waya baate akora Ashili wa kala wai.”
LUK 7:29 (Pate aromo amea ne kone oroka Yeso, ka ana o eesa emate makeke, nane kabare o bena, orona Ashili ya kap, aza o bena neya aromo ka Yohana wa eza ne o batisma.
LUK 7:30 Aza nyimi na maParisa ka na o rosa ngmǝ ka Ashili a nya Mosa ne nyane epa eka Ashili a kedeya aza one, o bena ne nyane a Yohana eze ne o batisma.)
LUK 7:31 Na Yeso lya izi ko beya na, “Aromo tomore teena ne tore eya?
LUK 7:32 Neye na bana yanaa a cikǝ ara ejamane ane rare tokpwe to ne, ane beya na, “ ‘Te ulbi ying a uraru na e nyano yowa leera, te beya ying leera le ma'ade na e nyano ruuzi.’
LUK 7:33 Yohana ondo eza o batisma wa de, wata wa lyeeze epaolya ne, wata wa sooze manyi mo inabi ne, ne beya na, ‘Waye ko bere o buru.’
LUK 7:34 Kanza kena ka oromo ka de, aka ya lyeeza aka sooze, ne bekaana, ‘Laka na kando ko lyelyeza ko sosoza, kaja kana o eesa emate makeke, ka ana madinǝ.’
LUK 7:35 Pate ka nyimi andaaka ne kabare ka o ama Ashili, ne wore o bekaana o ama me wai ka maganggang.”
LUK 7:36 OParisa yende rare Yeso kane lye mete akwilǝ wai, naka ale a ka cikǝ aka lya epaolya me.
LUK 7:37 A nyimi apeng ame ondaye yende wa zene kawa cikǝ nyimi madinǝ ma wai. Nangka wa kone na Yeso ka deya a lya epaolya akwilǝ oParisa, na wa de ka manau mo waze o lebo ma emate e cak aka kagbwi.
LUK 7:38 Na ondaye me de, na wa itǝ a malo Yeso ating tobona te kai, a wa ya ruuzi. Nangka mayizi ma wai ma jakazǝ tobona te Yeso, na wa pisi ka sekpwe se wai, a wa lembe tobona te Yeso aza o kona leba, malo nyimi a ondaye me cokome manau ma o waze o lebo a tobona te kai.
LUK 7:39 Nangka oParisa oka wa rare Yeso a lya mete wa laka epa eka ondaye me wa eza, na wa beke a nyimi lenyong le wai na, “Karomo kana kando ka o beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashilia kaaza, kaayo rosa ombela ondaye waana. Kanza kaayo rosa o bena ondaye me ondo madinǝ wai.”
LUK 7:40 Na Yeso bekaa oParisa me na, “Siman, eyang ka epa eka emea eyang bele o.” Nawa bekaana “Beka, Ondo baala.”
LUK 7:41 A Yeso bekaa wai na, “Oromo yende wa zene ka wa tare aromo leere o duru, ondo bora a tare wai o duru emate ogole mareka betuuru ko riiru, ondo leere me a tare wai o duru ogole o mareka tuuri esu.
LUK 7:42 Pate aromo leere me nane ta ama o ara o duru me ne, na oromo me wa baya ne ka emate me, o laka o, mana ba nyimi one, wayo waale a yeme o oromo omea wa baya ne ka emate me?”
LUK 7:43 Na Siman kabare na wa bekaana, “O laka ong ondooka a baya wai ka emate e cake.” Na Yeso kabare naka bekaana, “Maleo. Ba bekaa kap.”
LUK 7:44 Na Yeso laka ondaye me, aka bekaa Siman na, “Ba laka ondaye na? Ma deya ba akwilǝ au, ota ba nyang manyi kang kpizi tobona tong ne, laka ondaye na wa kwizǝ tobona tong ka mayizi ma wai, kanza wa pisǝ ka sekpwe se wai.
LUK 7:45 Ota ba gwara ongmǝ kami ne a were aka ma lyǝ akwilǝ au, laka ondaye na ko lyǝ wai, a wa taru aa lemba tobona tong na wata baya ne.
LUK 7:46 Ota ba cokoma manau okpwe ong ka o wore o emba ka o gongnga ong ne, laka ondaye na wa cokoma manau ma o waze o lebo a tobona tong.
LUK 7:47 Aza nyimi, a kwizǝ madinǝ ma wai ma cake maaka maya wai, wa wore o yeme o cake. Ondo oka a kwizǝ wai ma baate, wa wore o yeme o baate.”
LUK 7:48 Na Yeso bekaa ondaye me na, “A kwizǝ madinǝ mau.”
LUK 7:49 Aromo me ne ya lya epaolya ka kai, nane bore o beya tokpwe tone na, “Mana ondo ona kawa ama o kwizǝ madinǝ ma cake?”
LUK 7:50 Na Yeso bekaa ondaye me na, “Nangka ba kabare ka mi, aza o bekaana ma era ang bozau, ale a cammo.”
LUK 8:1 Malo nyimi, Yeso ka ale a topepeng te moole ka to eeno, aka baale ne angmǝ a lebo o togomo te Ashili. Atoma kai betuuru ka leere neye legwa ka kai,
LUK 8:2 ka andaye yende kanza ka a are ne ka mabere maburu a kang womza ana ondo aza makono mane. Neya, Mariya (kamea beeze na Magadala) kamea sǝǝrǝ kai mabere ma buru o sondaare,
LUK 8:3 ka Yowana kamea ondaleme kai Kuza, wa soole ma gole akwilǝ Ogomo Hiridus, ka Suzana, ka andaye yende ba cake. Andaye me ne kankama Yeso ka ana o tare kai ka epa eka ne zene.
LUK 8:4 Aromo a cake ne ya za o kurkǝnǝng, aneya deesa ra Yeso ane susi a topepeng to yende, naka bele ne angmǝ a gerpo na:
LUK 8:5 “Ondo ogole yende wa ale a wale ebelo e wai. Nangka waya waale ebelo me ne yende taru a zaa orona o tobona. Na itǝzǝ a e, engmeng o wake donge e.
LUK 8:6 Eyende taru nyimi makeke ma o za opoo, nangka e suri, na e waka ko dera be nau be deze.
LUK 8:7 Eyende taru a nyimi kana, na e ere legwa, na e kana me gwatakalanang a e.
LUK 8:8 Eyende kanza e taru a deze a rere, na e gong e kare eyo, na e kala liwinu le epa eka a waale.” Nangka Yeso ka beke nyimi, aka ara lengmelo naka bekaana, “Ekena teto epa eka eya konaza me.”
LUK 8:9 Na atoma aka ka zake pirkǝ kai masanto ma angmǝ a gerpo na.
LUK 8:10 Na ka kabare na, “Ying a kabare o bena e rose o ela o togomo te Ashili, ana ondo ang beya ngmǝ kaa ne ba gerpo adorana, “ ‘Ne gonte, a neto laka ne, aa ne konaze, a neto rosa ne.’
LUK 8:11 “Masanto ma angmǝ a gerpo na mana: Ebelo me eya angmǝ Ashili.
LUK 8:12 Emea e taru ba aza orona neya aromo amea ne kona, na ogomo bere o buru wa deya na wa kwagale angmǝ me anyong ane, adorana neta emba ai kane cǝ o boza ne.
LUK 8:13 Ebelo eka e taru ba ara acale, neya aromo amea ne kona ngmǝ me nane emba ai ko kona o leba a were ka ne kone, kanza ne ta ko ting ne. Ne kabare Ashili a were name, a nangka ne dukǝ a were o kedeya o kabare o Ashili one nane kuri a dimǝ.
LUK 8:14 Ebelo eka e taru a nyimi e kana neya aromo amea ne kona, na a ta rabo ne, a madoola ma o kona o leba, ocǝ ko rere o were ana, aza nyimi nane ta gongnga a nyimi angmǝ me ne.
LUK 8:15 Ebelo e mea e taru aza makeke ma rere neya aromo amea ne kona ngmǝ me, nane embe ka lenyong le yende, ane monte ai, ane motana ai, aza nyimi nane cikǝ nangka Ashili ya yeme me.
LUK 8:16 “A era ta diki beruu be masanto a pate be ka o uruu ne, na eke be a tau o gonggong ne, a diki a eke ara a zaatia adorana aromo ka neya lyǝ ne laka masanto.
LUK 8:17 Pate epa emea a baasa, a yo sǝǝrǝ e, kanza eyapa ta zene ka a baasa e giri o pari ka komana laka ne.
LUK 8:18 Konana, eza na ba sauwo ka epa emea e ya konaza me, ondooka waya ka epa, a yo wala wai ne, ondooka wa dera epa, epa emea wa laka na wa zene, a yo emba a baya wai.”
LUK 8:19 Na iini ka arone Yeso deya laka kai, nane ta ama o dukǝ ting kai ne ko gongnga aromo.
LUK 8:20 Na ondo bekaa kai na, “Iini ka arone au neya itǝ o yangga, neya yemo laka o.”
LUK 8:21 Na ka bekaana, “Pate aromo amea neya arakana, andaame neya konaza angmǝ Ashili, ane eze epa eka angmǝ me a beka, neya ana iini ang ka arone ang.”
LUK 8:22 Nmengde a Yeso ka bekaa atoma kai na, “Deyana ka tare be daki bo sanini o lepong legong.” Nane lyǝ ba nyimi ka onggo ko taara manyi mame ane bore teweno.
LUK 8:23 Aneya nyimi teweno naname, na malau beshe kai, o bero gong kang era a wa dore lepong leme, na epame kala ne nane laka na manyi ya besa one, ka manyi mame ma bore o lyǝzǝ a nyimi o onggo me.
LUK 8:24 Na atoma Yeso ale nane ara kai ane bekaana, “Ondoogong, Ondoogong, manyi yo lya ro.” Naka ere aka zurki obere ka lejǝng le manyi mame, na le itǝ tiiyi e keeya kome a set.
LUK 8:25 Aka bekaa ana o tare o kai na, “O itǝ o ying aza legoone le Ashili me ba?” A nyimi boome ka o kerke nane pirkǝ tokpwe to ne na, “Mana waana? Ka wa ote o bere ka lejǝng le manyi na ne kone kai ane tare kai.”
LUK 8:26 Yeso ka atoma kai neya yenga a nyimi o onggo o taara manyi a ale ba makeke ma Garasina, apeng amea ya o wulu lepong le makeke ma Galili.
LUK 8:27 Yeso kaya za o japi aza o onggo manyi naname, naka gwarnang ka ondooka waye ka o bere o buru, a waya apengme. Ka o rabo ba cake oromo me wa ciisǝ ngmata, awata kang ciisǝ akwilǝ ne, a wa ciisǝ ba macau.
LUK 8:28 Nangka wa laka Yeso, na wa rurayi a wa rizi ating kai, a wa ara lengmelo na, “Eya manyi mang ka bo, Yeso kena ka Ogomo Ashili? Ma bosau kana ogǝzǝng ne.”
LUK 8:29 A Yeso ka rabo ka o bekaa o bero buru ome na wa arnang ka oromo me. Obere me wa rabo ka o peere o wai ba deze, obena a rabo a tesa wai a taara ka tobona, a dato enda wai, wa mena a tasa sejǝng se me, o bero buru me wa aleze ka wai o wake.
LUK 8:30 Na Yeso pirkǝ wai na, “Mana me leze lo?” Nawa kabare na, “Te gong,” o bekaana, o bere o buru ome gong ba nyimia wai.
LUK 8:31 Nane boseze kai a gweregwere kana ka turki ne a le'o le o dera bekazo leemea apateze ana o bere o buru ba nyimi name ne.
LUK 8:32 Edembashe akwilǝ e cake neya gera epaolya arame ating oyara. Na mabere ma buru mame bose kai na ka turki ne kane lyǝ a nyimi one, naka kabare.
LUK 8:33 Nangka mabere ma buru mame ne suri ba nyimi oromo me, nane lyǝ ba nyimia edembashe me, nane ere ka tesong, ane lyǝzǝ a nyimi lepong leme na manyi lye ne apat.
LUK 8:34 Nangka ana o soola edembashe me ne laka nyimi, nane song aa ne ale apeng, aa ne baale epa eka e mane ne apengme ka makeke ma ma'amo,
LUK 8:35 kanza na aromo me suri nane laka epa eka eya ale. Nangka ne de a Yeso, nane mana oromo oka o bere o buru wa surǝ a wai, a cikǝ a ting tobona te Yeso, a wa amba madibi a wa ya rosa epa eka eya ale, nane kone boome.
LUK 8:36 Andaaka a eze epa eme a yizi ane, ne bele aromo nangka a womze ondo o bere o buru me.
LUK 8:37 Na aromo a pate a makeke ma Garasina bose Yeso na ka ale ka baya ne, aza o bena boome be meke ne a cak. Naka zale o onggo manyi aka ale aka baya ne.
LUK 8:38 Na oromo omea a lopa wai o bere o buru, wade na wa bose Yeso na, “Baya ang ale ka bo,” na Yeso kuriyǝ wai, aka beka wai na,
LUK 8:39 “Kurǝ akwilǝ ko beke epa emea Ashili a yau.” Na oromo me ale ba nyimi apeng, a wa baale epa emea Yeso ka ya wai.
LUK 8:40 Ko deya Yeso a surǝ owulu lepung le me, na aromo wobe kai ko zanta, aneya enda o kurǝ o kai.
LUK 8:41 Na oromo yende ka beya wai na Jariyus ondoono dandaro o gwarzanang maYahuda. Wa de na wa girwǝ a begeshe be Yeso, a wa bose kai na ka ale akwilǝ wai.
LUK 8:42 Aza o bena kagala ka wai, ka kaya ka yende kame, ka dukǝ shenai be tuuru ka se leere ko ngmenga, kayo orona o gbwǝ. Na Yeso kabare aka meke orona o ale, aromo ya za o tura kai a kazo gongnga one.
LUK 8:43 Ondaye yende wa zene arame, a wa rabo ka o kono o ooso ma nyau shenai betuuru ka she leere, a wa wonga pate epa taara te wai, na wata cǝ ondo o womza wai ne.
LUK 8:44 Pate ka aromo a cake kane zene, naka deya sauwo ba dimǝ Yeso a ka meke bengmǝ bo dibi kai, na o ngmere liizi, na ma nyau mame baya o ooso.
LUK 8:45 Na Yeso bekaana, “Manamea wa mekeng bengmǝ bo dibi?” Na komana arakaname ta kabare ne. A Biturusu kang bekaana, “Ondoogong, ka aromo a cake na ane ringgari a kuruwǝ komana wa meko.”
LUK 8:46 Na Yeso bekaana, “Mi ma kona ondo a wa mekeng, makang kone legoone a le surǝ mi.”
LUK 8:47 Nangka ondaye me wa laka o bena wa era awata baasa ne, na wa wore okpwe wai ko kerkeze a wa girwǝ a begeshe be Yeso, a komana ya gonta me. A wa beke epa eka e ote na wa meke kai ka nangka wa woma a nyimi o ngmere liizi.
LUK 8:48 Na Yeso bekaa wai na, “Ogala, o kabare ka legoone le Ashili a wa wongzau. Ale ba nyimi o kono leba.”
LUK 8:49 A Yeso ta ka pate ongmǝ kai ne, otoma deya wa surea akwilǝ Jariyus ondoono o dandaro gwarzanang maYahuda, na wa bekaa kai na, “Kagala kau ka gbwǝ, tana o kang gara ondo baala ne.”
LUK 8:50 Nangka Yeso ka kone nyimi, naka beke a Jariyus na, “Kana o kone boome ne, kabare ka Ashili kayo era.”
LUK 8:51 Ko dukǝ akwilǝ Jariyus, naka ta kabare a ondo lyǝ ka kai ne, sena Biturusu, Yohana ka Yakubu, ate ka iini kagala kame.
LUK 8:52 Pate aromo ame ka neya akwilǝ me, nane poro ruuzi ka ekoko, aza kagala kame, na Yeso bekaana, “Tana e ruuzi ne, kagala kame ta ka gbwǝ ne, kaya malauwa belle.”
LUK 8:53 Nane zoze kai a nyimi mazelakong, ka o rosa o bekaana ka samba o gbwǝ.
LUK 8:54 Na Yeso ka meke o ara kagala kame, aka ara lengmelo na, “Kagala era.”
LUK 8:55 Na e beene kuri a kai, aka ere, na Yeso ote na nya kai epaolya ka ka lye.
LUK 8:56 Na anate a kai laka epa o kala legoone lene, a Yeso windi ne teto na kana ne bele ondo epa eka aye ne.
LUK 9:1 Yeso ka rare atoma kai betuuru ka leere ara yende, naka nya ne o bare ba za obere oburu, aa ne womza makono kanza.
LUK 9:2 A ka kang tonga ne ka ne zoole aza togomo te Ashili aa ne womza ana o dera o kona cammo.
LUK 9:3 Aka bekaa ne na, “Kane jeke eyapa a teweno te ying ne, na lebenda, ojeketa, epaolya, ka emate ne, kanza kana e jeke odibi kawa kala oyende ne.
LUK 9:4 Pate akwilǝ aka a emba ying, cikǝ na arame kazo lengme lo baya apengme.
LUK 9:5 A pate ara amea nyana emba o ying, e era o baya apeng ame, e zazame ma sorma ma tobona toying ka wa itǝ bena ne tera tokpwe to ne.”
LUK 9:6 Nane ere aa ne tare topepeng, aa ne zoole, aza oroka o lebo. Aane womza ana okono a kuruwǝ.
LUK 9:7 Na Ogomo Hiridus o makeke ma Galili wa kone pate epa eka eya ale, na wa kone oburǝ bote, aza o bekaana ana ondo ya beyana Yohana ko batisma ka era nyimi ocau.
LUK 9:8 Ana ondo na ondo o beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili Ileya wa era, ana ondo kanza a beyana ondo a nyimi ana o beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili aka ne gbwǝ ko rabo wa era.
LUK 9:9 Na Ogomo Hiridus bekaana, “Ma ote na core okpwe o Yohana. Mana eyang konaza epa ena azaa wai? Nawa gera o laka Yeso.”
LUK 9:10 Nangka atoma Yeso ne kuri, nane baale kai epa eka ne eze. Naka kuri kane e daki aka apeng ka yende ka a beya kai na Betsaida.
LUK 9:11 Nangka aromo me ne kone obena kaye saname, nane tare kai. Naka embe ne aka bekaa ne angmǝ aza togomo te Ashili, kanza aka womza andaaka neya yeme lewoma.
LUK 9:12 O ongme ya amara a wa taru, na atoma betuuru ka leere name ne deya ara kai ane bekaana, “Baya aromo na ane ale a nyimi apeng ka topepeng to ma'amo ka ne gere epaolya ka ara omora. Obena ara ana a te rene aromo ta rene ne a ai ne.”
LUK 9:13 Na Yeso bekaa ne na, “Nyana ne eyapa ka ne lye.” Na ne kabare na, “Pate epa eka teye ka e, eta kala maborode esu ka ekwala e leere ne. Na Ateokora oya yeme ate wiinia kate lye ka aromo na?”
LUK 9:14 Andaleme me belle ne dukǝ magu esu. Na Yeso bekaa atoma kai na, “Bekaana aromo me na ne cikǝ e tuuru sussu.”
LUK 9:15 Na atoma kai, ne tare o bekaa kai, na pate one cikǝ.
LUK 9:16 Na Yeso jeke maborode esu ka ekwala leere name, aka ara okpwe zaa shili, aka bose Ashili aka posea pate. Malo nyimi aka nya atoma kai ka ne areseze aromo me.
LUK 9:17 Pate one ne lye na ne ti, a atoma kai ne shende madangare mame, na ma pene makende betuuru ka ma leere.
LUK 9:18 Ngmende a Yeso ya bosaza Ashili kai a yende, na atoma kai neya sara yende ka kai. Naka pirkǝ ne na, “Aromo beya mi na manamea?”
LUK 9:19 Na atoma kai bekaana, “Ana ondo beyana boa Yohana ka o batisma, ana ondo kang beyana ondo o beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili Ileya, kanza ana ondo beyana ondo a nyimi ana o beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashilia wa era.”
LUK 9:20 Na Yeso bekaa ne na, “Ying e beya mi na manamea?” Na Biturusu kabare na, “Boa Ondooka Ashili a zake na tong.”
LUK 9:21 Na Yeso windi ana o tare o kai teto na, kana ne bele ondo angmǝ aa na ne.
LUK 9:22 Aka kang bekaa ne na, “Kena ka oromo ka yo zitǝ ba cake, a taara te anateandaasau maYahuda, ana magame ma Ashili ma moole, ka ana o baala angmǝ aka Ashili a nya Mosa ne yo nyana kai. Ane wong kai, a lengme lo taaro aka ere.”
LUK 9:23 Naka beka pate one na, “Pate ondo ome waya yeme a wa tareng, a wa nyane okpwe wai, a wa jeke uti o gbwǝ a wa tareng.
LUK 9:24 Kazo ondooka waya yeme ebeene wai nannamena a lerambo le Ashili leena, wayo dera e ba pate, a kazo ondooka wa nyana ebeene wai nannamena a lerambo le Ashili leena aza o bena ba kabare ka mi, wayo cǝ e ba pate.
LUK 9:25 Epa e rere na, oromo wa cǝ ma gogoro ma lerambo le Ashili a wa dere e beene wai?
LUK 9:26 Nyimia a pate ondooka wa kona ezǝng eng ka ezǝng angmǝ ang, Kena ka Oromo kayo kona ezǝng wai a were aka ka deya a nyimi togomo te kai, ka togomo te Ate akai kanza ka te atoma Ashili o zaa shili.
LUK 9:27 Kanza eyang bele o ying, ana ondo ara kaana, neto gbwǝ ne seeka ne laka togomo te Ashili.”
LUK 9:28 Malo tomore o riiru ko bekaa angmǝ ana, na Yeso jeke ana Biturusu, ka Yohana, a Yakubu nane zale oyara ka kai, ka ne bose Ashili.
LUK 9:29 Nangka kaya za o bosaza Ashili na mainu ma kai sara, a madibi ma kai o wonze a yizi.
LUK 9:30 A saseya na ana o beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili a leere ana Mosa ka Ileya suri a neya beya angmǝ ka Yeso.
LUK 9:31 Na ne suri ka madibi maapeng na ma Yeso, a neya beya angmǝ ka kai aza o gbwǝ kai apeng Urushalima omea wayo panza o beka Ashili.
LUK 9:32 Biturusu ka aja kai neya nyimi malau ma lebo, nangka ne ere na ne laka masanto ma Yeso ka ana o beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili a leere ane itǝ ka kai.
LUK 9:33 Nangka aromo name neya arnang ka Yeso, na Biturusu bekaa kai na, “Ondoogong, wa gwara ka teya arakana. Baya a te sowo mapuki ma taaro, oyende a'o oyende o Mosa, oyende kanza o Ileya.” Awata rose epa eka waya beyame ne.
LUK 9:34 Waya za o beya angmǝ naname, na mawere japi na ma pate ne, nangka mawere mame ma pate ne nane kone boome.
LUK 9:35 Na lengmelo suri a nyimi mawere mame na, “Kanna kena kangnga kai, kamea ma Zaka, kona na kai.”
LUK 9:36 Malo lengmelo le name, nane laka Yeso kai ayende. Na atoma kai a taaro ne eke epame anyong ane, ane ta bele ondo a were name epa eka ne laka ne.
LUK 9:37 Ko sana ara ane japi aza oyarame, na aromo a cake mana Yeso.
LUK 9:38 Na ondo a nyimi aromo a cake me rare kai a jǝng na, “Ondobaala, eyang bosa o na o kone egonegone o kena kang, kaya o ngmenga ong belle.
LUK 9:39 Obere o buru gareze kai, ka ka eze bekoko buuwu. Wa ezeze kai na ebeene ya surǝ ka mapunǝ susi akai ongmǝ. Wata baya kai aka pere ne, waya za o cara kai a cake.
LUK 9:40 Ma bosa atoma au nane sǝǝrǝ o bere o buru ome, nane ta ama ne.”
LUK 9:41 Na Yeso kabare na, “Ying aromo tomore teena eta kabare ka Ashili ne e kang eza epa e buru. Eyang cikǝ ka ying tomore to wonda ang kang noke lenyong ka ying? Deya ka oyana me o arakaana.”
LUK 9:42 O yana me ya zo deya naname, na o bere o buru me tabe wai ba deze a wa beye e gwǝgwǝgbwǝ. Na Yeso zurki o bere o buru me aka womza kena kame aka niyi wai ara ate a wai.
LUK 9:43 Pate aromo kane ya arame nane monte tongmǝ tone aza ogole o gong ka Ashili a eza. A komana ya nyimi madoola me epa eka Yeso ka eza, naka beka atoma kai na,
LUK 9:44 “Kona na epa eka eyang beka ying. A yo nya Kena ka Oromo a taara te ana o nyana kai.”
LUK 9:45 Na atoma kai ta rosa angmǝ aka ka bekaa ne. A baasa aa ne na kana ne rose ne, ne kanza neya kona boome bo pirkǝ o kai aza angmǝ me.
LUK 9:46 Na masanggo ere a tera one aza o bekaana, mana wayo itǝ ondo o gong ba nyimi one.
LUK 9:47 Yeso ko rosa madoola mane, naka jeke kena ka baate aka ote kai naka itǝ ating kai.
LUK 9:48 Aka bekaa ne na, “Pate ondooka wa emba kena ka baate kaana aza o bena wa kabare kame, wa embangnga. Kanza pate ondooka wa embang, a wa emba ondooka wa tongang. Pate ondooka wa jǝpǝrǝ okpwe o wai na kena ka teng kaana nyimi oying a pate, waya yo kala o gongnga a pate.”
LUK 9:49 Na Yohana bekaana, “Ondoogong, te laka ondo a wa ya sǝrsǝzǝ obere o buru a nyimi leze lo na te nara wai aza o bekaana wato nyimi orone.”
LUK 9:50 Na Yeso kabare na, “Tane nare wai ne, pate ondooka wata nyana ying ne oyinga wai.”
LUK 9:51 Nangka tomore to kurǝ Yeso aza shili te amara, naka tere o ale apeng Urushalima a lenyong.
LUK 9:52 Naka tong ana o tare o kai yende ka ne lya izi, na ne ale a kapeng ka yende a makeke ma Samariya ka ne babare keeya zongka ka ale.
LUK 9:53 Na aromo apengme ne nyane o emba kai, aza o rosa o bekaana, kaya orona o ale ba Urushalima.
LUK 9:54 Nangka atoma okai Yakubu ka Yohana ne laka nyimi, na ne bekaana, “Ateokora, oya yeme a te ote ola kawa japi zaa shili kawa ese ne a pate na?”
LUK 9:55 Na Yeso ringǝrnu aaka zurki ane,
LUK 9:56 ane ale a kapeng ka yende.
LUK 9:57 Nangka neya za orona, na oromo yende wa bekaa Yeso na, “Eyang tare o a pate ara ame oya ale ne.”
LUK 9:58 Na Yeso kabare wai na, “Egoro neye ka she'o, engmeng kanza neye ka todo tene, mi kena ka o oromo anta ka ara o mora ne.”
LUK 9:59 Aka kang bekaa oromo yende na, “Tareng kang baalo.” Na oromo me wa bekaa kai na, “Ateokora, baya ang ale ka ang taase ate ang suri.”
LUK 9:60 Na Yeso bekaa wai na, “Baya andaaka neta tareng ne, ane taase aromo ane, a bo o ale ka o baale togomo te Ashili.”
LUK 9:61 Na ondo kang bekaana, “Eyang tare o Ateokora, baya ang ale kang bekaa akwilǝ ang na ma ale.”
LUK 9:62 Na Yeso kabare na, “Ondo ta zene kawa bora ogole ka le'abo a wa soole a dimǝ a wa itǝ ondo ogole edang ne, nyimia ondo ta zene oka waya tare ong a wa soole a dimǝ, a wa gwara ka ogole o togomo te Ashili ne.”
LUK 10:1 Malo nyimi, na Ateokora kang zake ana o tarea kai aromo tuuru sondaare ka leere, naka tong ne a lelere kane sha izi kai aa pate araaka kaya yemo ale ne.
LUK 10:2 Naka bekaana, “O shende arame gong, aa na ogole mea ta gongnga ne. Bosana Ondo arame, ka wa tong ana o shende a nyimia ra wai.
LUK 10:3 Ale na eyang tonza o ying na e bana emande epeng a nyimi egana.
LUK 10:4 Tane monte emate ne, tana e ana o jeteka ne, tana e jeke tokakau ne, tana e dangale tokpwe to ying aza o beya aromo o koo aza orona ne.
LUK 10:5 “Pate akwilǝ ka ee lyǝ ne, e bore ko bekaana, ‘Cikǝ naa cammo ana akwilǝ na.’
LUK 10:6 Ondo o cikǝ cammo wa ya akwilǝ me, o cikǝ o cammo o ying wayo cikǝ wai. Wata zane ne, a wa too itǝ nyimi ne.
LUK 10:7 Cikǝ na akwilǝ me, lya na e se pate epaaka ne nya ying, nyimia waaza, Ondo ogole wa gwara a are wai. Tane kaale a tokwilǝ a buuwu ne.
LUK 10:8 “E lyǝ apeng, aromo apengme na embe ying, e lye apat e epamea a ca ying.
LUK 10:9 Womza na ana o dera kona cammo a nyimi apengme, e bekaa ne na, ‘A were e ka Ogomo Ashili yo eza togomo wa amara ka ying.’
LUK 10:10 Pate apeng amea e lyǝ ne, kane ta kabare ka ying ne, tare na marona maapeng me e beya ne na,
LUK 10:11 ‘Ma sorma ma nyimi apenga a ying maame maya tobona te ro, te zazame mai aza o ying. Ka wa itǝ o bena Ashili yo core a ngmǝ aza o ying. Rintǝna o bena, togomo ta shili te amara.’
LUK 10:12 Eyang belo ying, lengme lo maare le togomo ta Ashili, ozitǝ oo ka aromo apengnge na ne yo kona, wayo kala aromo a Saduma o poba.
LUK 10:13 “E lyǝ udi, aromo o Korasin. E lyǝ udi, aromo o Betsaida. Magole ma moole ma Ashili ka a wore mai a nyimi o ying, a eza mai aromo a Taya ka Sidon, aiya ne poro anyong. Ane gwaara ko amba majembele ane cikǝ ba nyimi mato ko karezea mai a topkwe tone. Ka wa wore bena ne baya madinǝ mane ane kuri a Ashili.
LUK 10:14 A lengme lo gwarnang ka Ashili, a yo kona egonegone Taya ka Sidon ba zo ying.
LUK 10:15 Ying ma Kaparnahum. Eya gonta obena e bare ne kala komana o gongnga neyo zala shili na? Nyimia dai. Aya jipǝrǝ ying a deze araaka ana o gbwizǝ zene.
LUK 10:16 “Na Yeso bekaa na o tarea kai na, ‘Pate ondooka wa kona ying, mia wa kona. A pate ondooka wa nyana ying, mia wa nyana. Ondooka wa nyanang, wa nyana ondooka wa tongang.’ ”
LUK 10:17 Aromo tuuru sondaare ka leere me nane kuri ko kono leba, aa ne bekaa Yeso na, “Ateokora, mabere ma buru ma kona ro, a te zoola ne a nyimi leze lo.”
LUK 10:18 Na Yeso kabare naka bekaana, “Ma laka ogomo o bere o buru a wa taru a deze a wa surea zaa shili na o malmi ma were.
LUK 10:19 Kona na, ma nya ying bare ka e itǝzǝ ewa ka enyakara, kanza e kala pate o bare ondoo nyano ying, eyapa e buru to mana ying ne.
LUK 10:20 Pate ka nyimi, tana e kone o leba o bekaana, obere o buru wa kona ying ne, kona na o leba o bekaana a wela seze se ying a nyimia shili.”
LUK 10:21 A were namea, Yeso ka sabe Ashili azo kono leba ko bero rere a Ashili wa nya kai, naka bekaana, “Ma zanta ka bo Ate, Ateokora shili ka deze, azo bena ba baasa e paana ba na o ama ko rosa, na ba pari ara andaaka ne eyapa tazane. Ate, enna eya kala bo.
LUK 10:22 “Ate ang wa nyang keeya a taara teng. Ondo ta rosa mana kena kame ne soona Ate me belle, nyimia kanza ondo ta rosa mana Ate me ne soona kena kame belle, ka andaaka kena kame ka yeme wore a Ai ba ne.”
LUK 10:23 Na Yeso ringgarnu a atoma akai, naka bekaa ne be daki na, “O kono leba ya zo ying ka e laka epa eka e ya gonta me.
LUK 10:24 Eyang baalo ying, ana o beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili ka agomo, ne yeme o laka epa eka eya gonta me, neta ne cǝ o laka me ne. Ne yeme o kona epa eka e kona, neta ne cǝ o kona me ne.”
LUK 10:25 Ngmende ondo o rosa angmǝ ka Ashili a nya Mosa wa ere na wa pirkǝ Yeso, a waya yeme o kedeya kai, na wa pirkǝ kai na, “Ondobaala, ma ya eya ang cǝ ebeene o dera o maro?”
LUK 10:26 Na Yeso kabare na, “Angmǝ Ashili a bena eya? Nannia bo ba laka ai?”
LUK 10:27 Na oromo me kabare na, “ ‘Yeme Ashili Ateokora o, kale nyong leo, ka legoone leo, ka o rosa o, ka ekeeya o,’ o ‘Yeme ondooka waya ma'amo ka bo na okpwe o.’ ”
LUK 10:28 Na Yeso bekaana, “Ba beka a kap, ya nyimi, o yo rabo.”
LUK 10:29 Na oromo me ya yeme o sǝǝrǝ okpwe wai, na wa pirkǝ Yeso na, “Mana ondooka waya ma'amo ka mi?”
LUK 10:30 Na Yeso kabare ka orooka na, “Ondo wa ere a Urushalima a wa ya ale a Yariko, na wa lyǝ a taara te akǝri orona, na ne embe magogoro ma wai, aa ne ole wai, aa ne baya wai na waya gbwǝ.
LUK 10:31 A mana ondo magame ma Ashili waya kala, na wa laka wai, na wa tare daki, a wa kale a wa ba wai.
LUK 10:32 Nyimia ondogole akwilǝ Ashili wa de na wa kale a sara yende kanza.
LUK 10:33 “Malo nyimia na oromo a Samariya waya kala a wa ya ale begere, naaka wa laka wai na wa kone egonegone wai.
LUK 10:34 Nawa ale a wai, na wa kwizǝ wai, a wa kare wai makang ka manau, a wa tere rakeze me. Na wa ana wai na wa eke aza kurungzǝ, a wa ale ka wai akwilǝ a mosa ageng na wa soole wai.
LUK 10:35 Ko sana ara, a wa nya ondo soola akwilǝ o Mosa ageng me emate ogole a mora leere, a wa bekaa wai na, wa soole ondoo kono me. E mate me e sawa, ma era kurǝ, ang yo aro.”
LUK 10:36 Na Yeso pirkǝ na, “O laka o, a nyimi aromo taaro name, mana wa wore o bekaana waya ting ondooka akǝri ne wobe wai?”
LUK 10:37 Na oromo me bekaana, “Ondo name a wa wore egonegone.” Na Yeso bekaa wai na, “Ale ko ye nyimi.”
LUK 10:38 Yeso ka atoma kai neya nyimi teweno naname, na ne dukǝ kapeng kaa mea ondaye yende ka waya rame ka bezea wai na Marta. Marta me ka emba kai ba akwilǝ wai.
LUK 10:39 Marta kaye ka ondo aa dimǝ ka beya wai na Mariya, kamea ka cika ting Yeso aka koneze ngmǝ aka kaya baala me.
LUK 10:40 A Marta ote okpwe kai ba ogole o sela epaolya, zaa nyimia naka ale ba Yeso naka bekaana, “Ateokora, ota bala epa eka karone kang ka ya ne, ka bayang ka o sele epaolya yende na? Beka kai na ka de ka ka kangkamang.”
LUK 10:41 Na Ateokora kabare naka bekaana, “Marta, Marta, ba nara lenyong lo tete aza mayapa cake
LUK 10:42 Epa yende eya aya gera me a bo, Mariya ka Zaka epa o kala o rere, emea ondo wa era wata ama o emba a kai ne.”
LUK 11:1 Ngmende Yeso ka ya beya angmǝ ka Ashili a ara. Malo oka ka mare, na ondo a nyimi atoma a kai wa bekaa kai na, “Ateokora, baala ro nangka teyo beya angmǝ ka Ashili, nangka Yohana ka o batisma ka baale ana o tare wai.”
LUK 11:2 Naka bekaa ne na, “Eeya beya angmǝ ka Ashili, e bekaana: “ ‘Ate, a monte leze lo a sangsang, a togomo to de a komana ka kuruwǝ.
LUK 11:3 Nyaro epaolya o ngmeengme ka o koonang lengme.
LUK 11:4 Pisǝ madinǝ maro, o baale ro nangka teyo pisǝ andaaka ne eze ro epa e buru, nangka bo o ezeze. Tana o baya a te lyǝ a nyimi o kedeya ne.’ ”
LUK 11:5 Naka bekaa ne na, “A mana ondo ying waye ka oja, na wa ale a wai a tera lelyaare. A wa bekaana, ‘Bejaa, kopeng agwataka taaro a lya.
LUK 11:6 Oja ong yende wa surǝ a begere na wa japi a me, a mi naana anta ka epa o nya wai ne.’
LUK 11:7 “A wiinea oja wai oka wa ya nyimi wata kabare na, ‘Tana o gareng ne. Ma samba o pate abuudu a ma tete ka yana ang, ma era anta ama o era kang nyau eyapa ne?’
LUK 11:8 Nyimia, eyang baalo ying, waata era ka wa nya oja o wai epaolya aza obena beja be wai ne, wayo nya wai pate epa eka waya gera me o bena wata wa kona ezǝng o gara wai ne.
LUK 11:9 “Azaa nyimi eyang beya aying, bosaza na Ashili a yo nya ying, gerza na ara ai eyo cǝ, gwarazana buudu a ai a yo pari ying.
LUK 11:10 Pate ondooka wa bosa, a yo nya wai, pate ondooka wa gera wayo cǝ, kanza pate ondooka wa gwara abuudu a yo pari wai.
LUK 11:11 “Mana a nyimi o ying anate, ka o yana wai wa bosa bekwala, a wa nya wai owa?
LUK 11:12 Na o yana wai wa bose lengma, a wa nya wai onyakara?
LUK 11:13 Ying ana epa e buru, e rose nangka e nyaza ayana ying epa e rere, shebari Ate ying o zaa shili wayo nya obere wai andaaka ne boseze wai.”
LUK 11:14 Yeso kaya za o sǝǝrǝ o bere o buru o nara ngmǝ oromo yende. Malo surǝ o bere o buru me, na oromo me bora o beya ngmǝ, na epame tere aromo me okpwe.
LUK 11:15 Na ana ondo one bekaana, “Kakama. Baazabul, ogomo mabere ma buru, wa ya wa nya kai legoone lo sǝǝrǝ o bere o buru.”
LUK 11:16 Ana ondo kadeya Yeso, nane bekaa kai na, kaye epa e mole ka rose bena Ashili ya malo ogole o kai.
LUK 11:17 Yeso ka ka rose madoola mane naka bekaa ne na: “Pate togomo teeka te arnang, teyo caro, aromo akwilǝ ne arnang akwilǝ me a yo rizi.
LUK 11:18 Ogomo o bere o buru wa arnang okpwe wai, togomo te wai yo ya legoone nannia? Ma beka nyimi ko bena e bekaana ka legoone le Baazabul waya ang sǝrsǝzǝ o bere o buru.
LUK 11:19 Ma sǝrsǝzǝ o bere o buru ka legoone le Baazabul, ana o tare o ying sǝrsǝzǝ ka le mana? Nyimia waaza, ana o tare o ying neya yo core ying angmǝ me.
LUK 11:20 A ma sǝrsǝsǝ o bere o buru ka o ara Ashili, na togomo te Ashili te deya ying naname.
LUK 11:21 “A were aka ondo legoone, wa babare okpwe wai ka magogoro ma o kara, a wa ende akwilǝ a wai, okǝri wa era awata kwǝ magogoro ma akwilǝ wai ne.
LUK 11:22 A ondo kala wai a legoone wa deya a wa zala wai ko kara wayo kala wai, a wa jeka magogoro mo kara maaka wa eke lenyong ne a wa beshe magogoro ma oromo me.
LUK 11:23 “Ondooka wata ya lendo ka mi ne ondo nyana onnga wai, nyimia ondooka wata kurǝ ka mi ne, waya bacakara.
LUK 11:24 “Obere o buru wa suraa nyimi oromo, a wa ale a nyimi o wake a gera ara o teseke. Waata cǝ ne, a wa bekaana, ‘Eyang kurǝ ara oromo amea ma surǝ ne.’
LUK 11:25 Wa kurǝ, wayo mana oromo omea na akwilǝ ka aya sangsang a eyapa ta rene ne.
LUK 11:26 A wa yo kurǝ kawa jeke mabere ma buru o sondaare maaka ma kala o bora me ba ara a buru, kane lyǝ ba oromo me aa ne cikǝ a nyimi o wai. Nyimia o maare oromo me wayo kala o bora wai o burǝ.”
LUK 11:27 Nangka Yeso kaya beya angmǝ name, na ondaye yende a nyimi aromo a cak bekaana, “Ondo kona o leba ondaye omea wa ngmengoo aa ba ase a wai.”
LUK 11:28 Na Yeso kabare na, “Wa kala a kona o leba andaaka ne kona angmǝ Ashili ane ezeze ogole ka ai.”
LUK 11:29 Nangka aromo me ne wale o gongnga ne, na Yeso bekaana, “Lenna lepeza le burua le. Ne ya yeme a wore ne ogole o Ashili, a era ta wore ne ne sekona Yonana ondo o beya a ngmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili.
LUK 11:30 Nangka Yonana ogole Ashili waze aromo apeng a Neneba, nyimia mi Kena ka Ashili kaze a wereena.
LUK 11:31 Aya ogong o makeke ma o Sheba wayo era a lengme lo maare kawa beke epa eka wa rose. Ka wa bekaa aromo me na neta neeya epa e woma ne. Aza o bena wa deya awa suri a macangcang ka wa kone o rosa ogomo Suleimanu. A nannamena, ondooka wa kala Suleimanu ya arakaana pate ka nyimi eta e kona kai ne.
LUK 11:32 Aromo apeng Neneba neyo itǝ a lengme lo maare kale peza le wereena kane nyane o rizi one. Ka ne kuri ara Ashili a were e ka Yonana ka baale ne ngmǝ Ashili, a nannamena ondooka wa kala Yonana ya arakana na eta e kurǝ Ashili ne.
LUK 11:33 “Ondo wa era wata diki biru be masanto a wa eke ara aka wayo baasa beene, koona wa pate be ka oso ne. Wayo eke ara a zaati, adorana andaaka neya lyǝzǝ akwilǝ me ane laka masanto.
LUK 11:34 Liizi le oromo leya na masanto ma lepung le wai. A yizi au aya ka edang, lepung lo a pate yo ya ka masanto. A yizi me a ta rera ne, lepung lo a pate yo ya ka maring
LUK 11:35 Soleke na, kana masanto maaka maya ying maringnga mai ne ma lenyong.
LUK 11:36 Azaa nyimi, nyimi lenyong lo leya ka masanto, lepung lo a pate masantoa yoza, a ara maring tozene ne, pate le leyo ya masanto, nangka masanto ma beru ezeze masanto a bo.”
LUK 11:37 Nangka Yeso ka mare o beya ngmǝ ka aromo, na oParisa yende bose kai kane ale a lya epaolya ba akwilǝ wai. Na Yeso kabare o ale naka cikǝ ara o lyeeze epaolya me.
LUK 11:38 Na oParisa me, nangka wa laka Yeso aka ta ka kwizǝ taara zongka ka bore o lya epaolya ne, na epame itǝ a wai ba lenyong.
LUK 11:39 Na Ateokora bekaa wai na, “Lakai, ying maParisa e kpwizizi malo o poto a ka oso, a nyimi me ka madinǝ, e pena ka o nyalang ka epa e buru.
LUK 11:40 Ying a rara. Ondo oka wa eze malo wa ya wa eze nyimi lenyong kanza sang?
LUK 11:41 Nyana andaaka ne dere epa eka eya nyimi oso me, e keeya yo ya ying ba sangsang.
LUK 11:42 “E lyǝ udi ying maParisa, e nyaza Ashili oyende ba nyimi be tuuru e leto, egweng kaa kombela mananggo, a e nyana o eza e epa eka eya kapo kanza ko yeme Ashili. Eeyo eza o maare ka waya o yeme Ashili zora o baya o bora ka waye ka edang.
LUK 11:43 “E lyǝ udi ying maParisa ana okpwe o gong, ying naana e yeme tora to ciisǝ te moole a nyimi o dandaro gwarzanang maYahuda e kang yeme makoo ara ejamane.
LUK 11:44 “E lyǝ udi, e rere o yangga na macau maaka ma wilǝ e kang burǝ na a nyimi macau mame, ka aromo itǝzǝ ne ane ta rosa ne.”
LUK 11:45 Na ondo a nyimi ana o rosa ngmǝ aka Ashili a nya Mosa wa kabare na, “Ondo o baala, ba beka nyimi, a ba lya mainu maro kanza.”
LUK 11:46 Na Yeso kabare na, “Ying ma kanza e lyǝ udi ana o baala angmǝ aka Ashili a nya Mosa. E anza aromo magogoro ma dengdeng ka deketea ne anza aza angmǝ aka Ashili a nya Mosa o poba oya. Aying ka topkwe to ying e era eta kangkama ne ko ka lebo le yende ne.
LUK 11:47 “E lyǝ udi, ka e ezeze nangka magonggong ma ying eze, o sooza macau ma ana o beya a ngmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili, kanza magonggong ma ying neya ne wonze ne.
LUK 11:48 Ying a tokpwe to ying e wore o bena e kabare ka epa eka magonggong ma ying ne eze. Ne wonze ana o beya a ngmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili aying e sooze ne macau.
LUK 11:49 Azaa nyimi, Ashili ba nyimi o rosa ai a bekaana, ‘Eyang tonga ne ana o beya a ngmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili ka atoma Yeso, neyo wonga na ondo one, ane gǝǝzǝ na ondo.’
LUK 11:50 Aza nyimi, aromo tomore toona neyo ana manyau ma ra aburu a pate ana o beya a ngmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili ka a wongze o era o bora lerambo le Ashili.
LUK 11:51 O era bora ka ma nyau ma Habila a deya a ma nyau ma Zakariya, oka a wong a tera ara a sangsang Ashili ka ara o kala be sangsang a Ashili. Eeye, eyang baalo ying, aromo tomore toona neyo ana madinǝ mame ba pat.
LUK 11:52 “E lyǝ udi ying ana o rosa angmǝ aka Ashili a nya Mosa, eta rosa Ashili ne a ekang dame ana o yeme o rosa me orona, e samba o jeka epa mo pari abuudu o rosa. Ying a topkwe to ying eta e lyǝ ne, aying e kang nara andaaka neya lyǝzǝ.”
LUK 11:53 Nangka Yeso ka baya arakaname, na maParisa ka ana baala angmǝ aka Ashili a nya Mosa ne bore o nyana kai ba jǝng ane gare kai ka bepirǝ,
LUK 11:54 adorana ne laka o rizi o kai aza e epa eka ka yo beka.
LUK 12:1 Aya za a nyimi na aromo a cake gwarnang ara yende na ara sau ne. Na ogongnga one oteze nane itǝzǝ ba tokpwe tone. Na Yeso bore bekaa na o tare o kai na, “Ezana a sauwo ko yisti o maParisa, omea ne rendeze aromoa ka wai belle.
LUK 12:2 Eyapa tarene ko pate ka ato pari ne, eyapa tarene ko baasa ka Ashili ta rosa ene kanza.
LUK 12:3 Za nyimi, pate epa eka aromo ne beka suk, a yo kona e oyangga, kanza epa eka ebeya a teto ta aromo a nyimi o todo, a yo beya o yangga nangka komana yo kona.
LUK 12:4 “Ying aja ang, eyang baala o ying, tane kone boome be andaaka ne wonze lepung, malo nyimi ne era ne ta ama o ye eyapa kanza ne.
LUK 12:5 Baya na ang bele ying ondooka eyo kona boome be wai: Kona na boome be Ashili, ondooka malo wonga lepung, waye ka o bare o tare oromo ola. Ang bekaa ying epeng e me, wa gwara e kona boome be wai.
LUK 12:6 E rosa obena e era e lishi e bangbako esu ba zaa emamate leere na? Pate ka nyimi Ashili ta a winǝ ka ondo a nyimi one ne.
LUK 12:7 Konana, Ashili rosa pate ogongnga sekpwe seeka seya tokpwe to ying. Nyimia waaza, tane kone boome ne. E kala e bangbako a cake e keeya.
LUK 12:8 “Eyang baala o ying, pate ondooka wa kabare ka mi a begeshe be aromo, mi ma eyang kabare ka wai a begeshe be otoma Ashili odera lepung.
LUK 12:9 Ondooka wa sanggang o rosa ong a begeshe be aromo, mima eyang sanggang o rosa wai a begeshe ba Atoma surǝ a zaa shili.
LUK 12:10 Pate ondooka wa beya angmǝ aburu aza Kena ka Oromo, Ashili yo kwizǝ madinǝ ma angmǝ me, a pate ondooka wa tambo aza obere Ashili, Ashili to kwizǝ madinǝ ma angmǝ me ne.
LUK 12:11 “A deya ka ying a madandaro ma o gwarzanang maYahuda ka core angmǝ aza o ying, ka ana togomo, ka ana obeka kone, tane zitǝ aza nangka eyo sǝǝrǝ tokpwe to ying ne kona aza epa o bekaa ne.
LUK 12:12 Aza nyimi o bere orere Ashili wayo baala ying epa eka eyo beka a were name.”
LUK 12:13 Na ondo a nyimi aromo beka kai na, “Ondo baala, beka ondo a izi ong kawa are ro epa eka ate aro wa gbwi a wa baya ro ka e.”
LUK 12:14 Na Yeso kabare naka bekaana, “Oja ong, mana wa nyang togomo to cora angmǝ ying ka eyang ara magogoro ma ying?”
LUK 12:15 Naka bele aromo me na, “Konana. Eza na a sauwo ka o kombela o berendo, ocǝ magogoro ma oromo ba cake, waya ta ote ka wa cǝ ebeene o dera omaro ne.”
LUK 12:16 Aka bele ne angmǝ a gerpo yende, “Aye oromo yende ka waye ka ocǝ a sǝǝrǝ epaolya a cake.
LUK 12:17 Nawa bore madoola a lenyong le wai na, ‘Engta ka aro eke epaolya a cake ka ma cǝ ara ang ne, eya eyang ya naname?’
LUK 12:18 “Nawa beka okpwe wai na, ‘Nanname eng rosa epa oya. Eyang posa abenga ang, ang kang sowa a moole moole, kang kare epaolya na a maacǝ, ka magogoro mang pate a nyimi me.
LUK 12:19 Eng kang beka okpwe ong na, “Ahah, nanname oye ka epaolya a cake mame mayo rabo, oyo ya shenai a lyame, baya o teseke, o lye, o se, o kona oleba o.” ’
LUK 12:20 “Na Ashili beka a wai na, ‘Bo orara. A nyimi lelyaare leena oya gbwǝ. Magogoro mana a ba kurǝ okpwe o, mayo itǝ ma mana?’
LUK 12:21 “Na Yeso maare angmǝ ko bekaana, ‘Wayo itǝ nyimi ka pate ondooka wa kurǝ magogoro a cake ma okpwe wai, a begeshe Ashili wata ka eyapa ne.’ ”
LUK 12:22 Na Yeso bekaa na o tare a kai na, “Aza nyimi, eyang bekaa ying tana e eze madoola aza epa eka eyo lya ka madibi maaka eyo amba apung aying ne.
LUK 12:23 Ebene oromo kala epaolya, a lepung le oromo kala magogoro mo amba.
LUK 12:24 Lakana egorogoro, neta waleze ebelo ne, ne ta senda ne, ne ta ka benga ne shebari kagoropate ne. A pate ka nyimi, Ashili nyaza ne epa o lya. Rosa na e kala engmeng edang.
LUK 12:25 Mana a nyimi o ying aza madoola ma wai, wa era a wa waleke tomore to wai ne?
LUK 12:26 Nangka eta ama oya epa e baate na ne, eyaka e ya doola o dangare me?
LUK 12:27 “Laka nangka eburu gongze, ne ta gole ne, ne ta sowa eyapa ne, ne ta dozaza madibi ne, pate ka nyimi eyang bele o ying, Ogomo Suleimanu ka ocǝ a wai, wata wa tukǝ amba madibi ma rere mo kala beburu be yende ne.
LUK 12:28 Ashili a ambaza mawake magogoro ma rere, mamea ayo gonta o ngmeengme, a leere a ese mai ola, shebari ying, eya wa era awata nya ying ne, eyaka e ta eke lenyong Ashili ne?
LUK 12:29 Tane oteze lenyong le ying aza ogera epa ka eyo lya ko sa ne, kane gare topkwe to ying aza e ne.
LUK 12:30 Aromo aka ne ta rosa Ashili ne a lerambo legoone, ne kanazang ba gera magogoro mana. Ying Ate o ying rose na eya yeme me.
LUK 12:31 Eke na lenyong leying a togomo to Ashili, Ashili yo nya ying pate magogoro maana.
LUK 12:32 “Tana e kone boome ne ying ana o tare ong ka eta gongnga ne, aza obena ate aying ya kona leba o nya o ying ocikǝ a nyimi togomo te wai.
LUK 12:33 Lisǝ na epa eka ezene ka e nya ana o dera emate me. E babare tokpwe to ying le'eke leeka le to caro ne, ocǝ omea wato maro ne ba shili. Ara a ka okǝri wa era awata ama okpwǝ me ne, ka ra aka egau ne era neta sheke ne.
LUK 12:34 Ara a ka ocǝ o zene, arame lenyong lo zene kanza.
LUK 12:35 “Cikǝ na e gonte ra zak, tane lambi eru masanto maying ne.
LUK 12:36 Na azara amea neya enda Ateokora one a wa surǝ a ozǝnggǝ o amare. Wa kurǝ kawa gware abuudu, aa ne pari wai a saseya.
LUK 12:37 Eyang baalo ying e peng me, wayo itǝ epa o zanta azara amea Ateokora wa deya wayo mana ne ane ta ne umǝ ne. Eyang belo ying, wayo lopa o dibi wai o gong, a wa bekaa ne kane cikǝ aro lye epaolya, wayo tare ne a yeyende a wa nyaza ne epaolya.
LUK 12:38 Wayo itǝ epa e lebo ka azara name ka Ateokora wa deya ba tera lelyaare na o sana ara a wa mana ne ba zo enda wai.
LUK 12:39 Eyang yeme e rose o bena ate akwilǝ waa rosa a were aka o kari ya deya, wayo cikǝ ko enda awata kabare okǝri wa lyǝ kawa eze bekǝri akwilǝ me ne.
LUK 12:40 Ying ma cikǝna ko enda koonang a were, o bena Kena ka oromo kaya deya a were aka ato rosa ne ko ba baate.”
LUK 12:41 Na Biturusu pirkǝ na, “Ateokora angmǝ gerpo na a ba beka aza aro na, ka komana mei?”
LUK 12:42 Na Ateokora kabare wai na, “Mana ozara name ondooka a kabare ka wai a wa kang ya ko rosa? Waya ome ateokora wai yo beka wai na wa ende akwilǝ wai, a wa kang nya o dangare azara me epaolya a were aka a kedeya. Ebelo ozara name Ateokora wa ale a wa baya wai ka akwilǝ ka azara, kawa nyaza ne epaolya a were e ka wa gwara, na wa ya nyimi.
LUK 12:43 Wayo rera ozara name a Ateokora wai wa deya a wa mana wai a eza nyimi.
LUK 12:44 Eyang bele oying epeng me, wayo ote ozara name kawa itǝ ondo soola magogoro ma wai apat.
LUK 12:45 A ozara name wa beka a lenyong le wai na, ‘Ateokora ong wata dusung deya ne,’ azaa nyimia wa bora o olaza odanggare azara me andaleme ka andaye, kanza a wa taru a lyelyeza ko sosoza ka nyimia madoola wilǝ a wai.
LUK 12:46 Ateokora ozara name wayo deya a lengme leeka ozara me wata madoola ma nyimi ne, a were e ka wata rosa ne kanza. Ateokora me wayo ola wai a jǝng a wa turki wai a nyimi andaaka ne nyano kabare ka Ashili.
LUK 12:47 “Ozara ome a wa rose epa eka ateokora wai wa ya yeme a wa eze, awata babarono o deya ateokora ne na wa ta kang eza epaame a beka a wai ne, a yo ola ozara name a jǝng.
LUK 12:48 Ozara o me wata rose epa eka ateokora wai waya yeme a wa eze ne, na wa eze epa eka e bare a ole wai, a yo ola wai a baate. Pate ondooka a nya wai epa ecake, a yo gera epa ecake a wai. Ondooka a eke wai aza epa egong, a yo gera epa egong ba wai.
LUK 12:49 “Ma deya kang diki ola ba nyimi lerambo le Ashili. O yeme ongnga aiya a samba oromboke me.
LUK 12:50 Eyang ko batisma o zitǝ, omea a yo ezang, lenyong leng leto tete ne sena a ezeng wai.
LUK 12:51 Eya gonta na ma deya lerambo le Ashili ka komana cikǝ a cammo na? Ko ba baate, eyang belo ying, ma deya adorana e arasannang a tokpwe to ying.
LUK 12:52 Epa eka e bora o ngmeengme, a nyimi akwilǝ yende aromo esu neyo arnang ka leere, aromo taaro neyo nyalang ka aromo leere, aromo leere neyo nyalang ka aromo taaro.
LUK 12:53 Ate yo nyana kena ka wai, a kena kanza kayo nyana ate a kai. Iini yo nyana kagala ka wai, a kagala kanza ka yo nyana iini kai. Ondawa wayo nyana ogiri wai, ogiri kanza wayo nyana ondawa wai.”
LUK 12:54 Yeso ka beka aromo a cake me na, “E laka mawere a ma era a kulu araaka ongme taaru ne e bekaana, ‘Ulyǝ yo ngmeza,’ a wa dato ngmeza.
LUK 12:55 Kanza e kono bere o sara o guri wa era, e bekaana, ‘A yo kona a huuwu,’ a wa dato ya nyimi.
LUK 12:56 Ying ana o renda aromo. E ama orosa epa ka eya ale deze ka zaa shili. Eya ka eta ama obeka eyapa azaa were na ne?
LUK 12:57 “Eyaka eta e laka osawa o ying aza epa erere ne?
LUK 12:58 Ondo wa raro aro cora angmǝ cǝ ko laka a ebabara e tata orona, ba nyana e babare, a wa yo ale ka bo ara ondo cora angmǝ. Ondo o cora ngmǝ kanza wayo taro a nyimi aro teesa aromo.
LUK 12:59 Eyang belo o, ba era o ta surǝ arame ne seeka ba are apat epa eka a core na o are, bemate be yende ato kenǝ ne.”
LUK 13:1 A kap a were name aromo yende ka neya rame, nane beke Yeso angmǝ aza aromo yende o makeke ma o Galili ka Ogomo Bilatus wa ote na wonze ne, a were aka neya cora Ashili emande e lebera. Na ma nyau mane sakalnang ka ma emande eka neya cora Ashili me.
LUK 13:2 Na Yeso kabare ne na, “Eya madoola ma o bekaana aromo o Galili ka a wonze neya kala a madinǝ o gwaara ka o dangare one a Galili me na?
LUK 13:3 Nyimia tazane. Eyang bele oying, eta kurǝ Ashili ne, pate o ying kanza eyo gbwizǝ a madinǝ maying.
LUK 13:4 Nyimia kanza ang bele ying angmǝ yende, aromo betuuru ko riiru name ka odo o eo wa noke ne a kapeng ka Siluwanu, eya gonta o bekaana ne kala o dangare aromo a Urushalima a madinǝ na?
LUK 13:5 Nyimia tazane. Eyang bele oying, eeta kurǝ Ashili ne, pate o ying kanza eyo gbwizǝ a madinǝ maying.”
LUK 13:6 Na Yeso bele ne angmǝ a gerpo adorana ne kuri a Ashili obena, “Oromo waye ka uti o nyaza ayana ara a wai, na wa ale a gera ayana uti me, nyimia wata wa cǝ eyapa ne.
LUK 13:7 Nawa bekaa ondo o soola ara ame na, ‘Laka, ongmeengme shenai she taaro naana eyang deesa a gera ayana o saya na anta ma cǝ eyapa ne. Genda wai. Eyaka wa wobe ara?’
LUK 13:8 “Na ondo o soola ara ame kabare na, ‘Ondoogong baya wai o lenai le yende belle, eyang kawa o ringgari o ting me ang kare o gutu ne.
LUK 13:9 Wa kare ayana a lenai le o deya a baya wai. Wata kare ayana ne, a gende wai.’ ”
LUK 13:10 A lengme lo teseke ka o bosa a Ashili, Yeso kaya baala a madandaro ma o gwarzanang maYahuda.
LUK 13:11 A kandaye ka yende ka gǝdǝ kaya araame ka o bere o buru wa tabe kai o shenai betuuru ka o riiru. A wa pota kai naka yeng a guulǝ.
LUK 13:12 Nangka Yeso ka laka kai, naka rare kai na ka deya izi aka bekaa kai na, “Kandaye, eyang arau ka o kono o.”
LUK 13:13 Naka eke o ara o kai azaa kandaye kame, ba saseya naka naakarnǝ aka saba Ashili.
LUK 13:14 Na ondoogong o dandaro gwarzanang maYahuda kone o burǝ aza o bena Yeso ka womza kai a lengme lo teseke ka o bosa a Ashili, na wa beke aromo ka neya rame na, “Shengme o taashe zene seeka se gwara a gole ne. Aza nyimi, deesa na a shengme se me a yo womza ying bangka lengme lo teseke ka o bosa a Ashili.”
LUK 13:15 Na Yeso kabare na, “Ying ana o rendaza aromo. Mana a nyimi o ying wata dingǝzǝ bena belome ka kurunzǝ ka wai a lengme lo teseke a wa ale ka ne ara o sa manyi ne?
LUK 13:16 Waya kandaye kaana kagala ka akora Ibraheng ka ogomo o bere o buru wa tera kai o shenai betuuru ko riiru, wata gwara a womza kai a lengme lo teseke ka o bosa Ashili maYahuda ne na?”
LUK 13:17 Nangka ka beke nyimi, na pate ana o nyana kai nane kone ezǝng, o dangare aromo a pate ne zante ka ogole o Ashili oka ka ya eza me.
LUK 13:18 Na Yeso pirkǝ na, “Nannia togomo te Ashili ze? Ma era ang kedeya te ka eya? Na aromo ka neyo waala o kabareze ka Ashili na?
LUK 13:19 Teya baate-baatea na eyo o mustad, emea oromo jeke kawa kpweene ara a wai. Na e gong a e itǝ uti, na engmeng sooze todo e bana me, nyimia aromo neyo waale o kabareze ka Ashili ne.”
LUK 13:20 Na Yeso kang pirkǝ na, “Ma era ang kedeya togomo te Ashili ka eya?
LUK 13:21 Waye na o yisti o baate oka kandaye ka yende ka jeka naka rǝkǝ ka ma'ena ma o alakama ma cake. Nyimia ma'ena ma o alakama ma gwarnang ka ma o yisti me ka ma biizi ama pene epa emea a kare mai ne ka ma dukǝ kuruwǝ.”
LUK 13:22 Na Yeso kale a topeng to moole ka to eeno, aka baale aromo orona kai o ale a Urushalima.
LUK 13:23 Na ondo pirkǝ kai na, “Ateokora, aromo a baate Ashili a yo boza na?” Na Yeso bekaa ne na,
LUK 13:24 “Waleke na o nyǝmǝlǝnǝ ne adorana e lyǝ abuudu ocǝ ebeene o dera o maro ka aya seto, aza o bekaana aromo a cake neyo gera o lyǝ a neto ama o lyǝ me ne.
LUK 13:25 Ate akwilǝ me wa era kawa pate abuudu, eyo itǝ o yangga e gware kale bose na, ‘Ate akwilǝ pari ro abuudu.’ “Wayo kabare na, ‘Anta rosa ying ne, anta kang rosa araaka e surine ne.’
LUK 13:26 “Aranamea eyo bekaana, ‘Te lye a te se ka bo, a ba dato baala a marona ma peng aro.’
LUK 13:27 “A wa kabare ne na, ‘Ying ana ra a buru, anta rosa ying ne shebari araaka e suri ne, arnang na ka mi.’
LUK 13:28 “A were aka e laka Ibraheng, Ishaku, Yakub ka pate ana o beya a ngmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili a nyimi togomo te a Ashili, aying a yo tare ying o yangga, eyo ruuzi ka o nonza ongmǝ a saname.
LUK 13:29 Aromo neyo deesa ane susi dizi ka aza, ka sara o re ka o guri, ane cikǝ ara o kona o leba a togomo te Ashili.
LUK 13:30 Konana, andaaka neya ana o maare neya yo itǝ ana o bora, ana o bora kanza neyo itǝ ana o maare.”
LUK 13:31 A were name na maParisa ma yende deye ara Yeso ane bekaa kai na, “Era o baya arakana ka o ale a ara. Ogomo Hiridus ya yeme o wonga o.”
LUK 13:32 Naka bekaa ne na, “Ale na ka e bekaa o ogana ara buru name na, o ngmeengme ka leere eyang sǝrsǝzǝ o bere o buru, ang wonze aromo, a lengme lo taaro ang maare ogole ong.
LUK 13:33 Pate ka nyimi eyang lya izi ka teweno teng o ngmeengme ka leere ka ngmena, wata gwara ondo o beya a ngmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili wa gbwi a ara ne sena ba Urushalima.
LUK 13:34 “Ying aromo Urushalima, Urushalima, ana o womza ana o beya a ngmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili, ana o tarangaza ka cale andaaka a tonza ne aying. Ma rabo a gera nangka eyang kurki a aromo aying ara yende, nangka ka tokoro shende ayana kai a mabeko ka ka ende ne. Na e nyana pat.
LUK 13:35 Laka, a yo baya apeng aying makansǝng zora ondo o enda. Eyang beya ying, eto kang lakang ne seeka e bekaana, ‘Ondo kona leba ondo deya a nyimi legoone le Ashili.’ ”
LUK 14:1 A lengme lo teseke ka o bosa Ashili o maYahuda le yende, a Yeso ka ale a lya epaolya akwilǝ a ondo o gong o maParisa, na aromo kare kai yizi a dongdong.
LUK 14:2 Ating kai, ondo wa zene ka tobona ka taara te wai te bizizi.
LUK 14:3 Na Yeso pirkǝ maParisa ka ana o baala angmǝ aka Ashili a nya Mosa na, “Angmǝ aka Ashili a nya Mosa a kabare o womza aromo a lengme lo teseke ka o bosa Ashili na, nyimia taza ne?”
LUK 14:4 Nane kome a set. A Yeso eke ondo o kono me taara, aka womza wai, aka bekaa wai na wa ale.
LUK 14:5 Malo nyimi na Yeso pirkǝ aromo me na, “Ondo oying waya ka kena, koona ka o rungzǝ, a ka kala a le'o a lengme lo teseke ka o bosa Ashili le maYahuda eyo sǝǝrǝ wai a saseya sang?”
LUK 14:6 Nane dera epa o beka.
LUK 14:7 Nangka Yeso ka laka o bekaana ageng ne Zaka ara o cikǝ a woma o gwarnang ara o lya epaolya. Arakanamea ka beke ne lesau na,
LUK 14:8 “Ondo wa bele ying ozǝnggǝ o ana ondaye osau, tana e ale ka e zake ara o cikǝ a zake ne, ba eza a bele ondo kanza kawa kala ying o gongnga.
LUK 14:9 Ondo kala o wa deya, a yo deya ka bekaa bo na, ‘Era ka o nya wai ara o cikǝ au.’ O ale ka o gere ara o cikǝ a baate, aya nyimi oyo kona ezǝng.
LUK 14:10 A rareo ara o lya epaolya, gera ara o cikǝ a baate, ondooka wa rare o wa deya, a wa yo bekaa bo na, ‘Oja, ale ka o cikǝ ara a zake.’ Arakaname a yo zalarau a izi andaaka a bele ne gwarnang ome.
LUK 14:11 Pate ondooka wa ara okpwe o wai, Ashili a yo jipǝrǝ wai, a ondooka wa nata okpwe wai Ashili a yo ara wai.”
LUK 14:12 Na Yeso bekaa oParisa oka wa rare kai ara o lya epaolya na, “Ba ya rare aromo a lya epaolya, tana o rare aja au, arone au, ana akwilǝ au, ka ana emate ne. Ba ya nyimi neema neyo rareo, ka ne areo a ngmende.
LUK 14:13 Ba ya rare aromo ba lya epaolya, rare ana o dera ocǝ, ka gǝdǝ, ka andaaka sara yende a gbwǝ ane, a arǝ,
LUK 14:14 a Ashili a yo nyau o kona o leba. Bekazo be andaana ka ba rare, ne era neta arau ne, seena Ashili ka aye ne a yo arau a lengme le o ara ana o dera madinǝ.”
LUK 14:15 Ka o kona nyimi, ondo a nyimi andaaka neya lya epaolya ka kai bekaana, “Ondo kona o leba ondooka wayo lya epaolya a were ozǝnggǝ o togomo te Ashili.”
LUK 14:16 Na Yeso kabare wai ka angmǝ a gerpo na, “Ondo wa zene kawa sele epaolya ba cake, na wa kang rare aromo ba lyame.
LUK 14:17 Nangka a were o lya epaolya me aye, na wa tong ozara wai kawa rare andaaka a bele ne na, ‘Deyana, epaolya e yenga.’
LUK 14:18 “Na komana one wa tong ka orooka o dera edang o nara wai o ale ara o lya epaolya me. Ondo bora bekaana, ‘Ang surǝ emba ara, eyang ale kang laka ai, aza nyimi anta cǝ o deya ne.’
LUK 14:19 “A ondo bekaana, ‘Ang surǝ a emba ena elome betuuru ogole abara, ang ya orona o ale kang kedeya ne.’
LUK 14:20 “Ondo kanza wa bekaana, ‘Ang surǝ a ana ondaye osau, anta cǝ o deya ara o lya epaolya me ne.’
LUK 14:21 “Na ozara me wa kuri na wa bekaa ate akwilǝ wai pate epa eka a bekaa wai. Na lenyong le ate akwilǝ me caro. Na wa bekaa ozara wai me na, ‘Ale ba saseya a nyimi marona ma moole ka ma eeno apeng ame. Ka o kurki ana o dera, ana o zǝngtǝ, ka arǝ, ka andaaka taara tene te gbwǝ a sara yende, ka o de ka ne arakaana.’
LUK 14:22 “Malo nyimi na ozara me kuri a wa bekaana, ‘Ate akwilǝ, epa eka ba bekaa a mara o eza me, pate ka nyimi tera to cikǝ tata zora aromo.’ ”
LUK 14:23 Na ate akwilǝ bekaa ozara me na, “Ale a nyimi marona ma malo apeng, ka o kurki aromo kane de, adorana akwilǝ me a pene.
LUK 14:24 Eyang baala oying, ondo ta zene ba nyimi andaaka a rare o bora ka wayo lya epaolya emea a sele ne.”
LUK 14:25 Nangka aromo a cake neya tarea Yeso, naka ringgarnu aka bekaa ne na,
LUK 14:26 “Pate ondooka waya yeme o tare ong, awata yemeng o kala ate a wai, ka iini o wai, ka ondaye wai, ka yana wai, ka arone wai andaleme ka andaye. Kanza ka okpwe wai ne, wata bare a wa itǝ ondo tare ong ne.
LUK 14:27 Kanza nyimia pate ondooka waata ana uti o gbwǝ o wai a wa tareng ne, wa era wata ama o itǝ ondo tare ong ne.
LUK 14:28 “A ondo o ying waya yeme o sowa odo o eo, wayo cikǝ suri a wa bale nangka wayo wonga emate aza o sowa odo o eo me, tana wa bore o sowa zora o ya nyimi emate sau wai ne.
LUK 14:29 Wa bora sowa odo o eo me, kawa ta ama o mara me ne, komana wa laka nyimi a wayo zoza wai,
LUK 14:30 ane beyana, ‘Ondo ona wa bora o sowa odo o eo na wa ta wa ama o mara me ne.’
LUK 14:31 “Nyimia kanza ogomo waya ale a kara ka ogomo yende. Wa gwara o bekaana wa cikǝ a wa soleke aromo magu betuuru, ne era ne eze o kara ka aromo magu tuuru leere na?
LUK 14:32 Wato ama ne, wayo tonga ana ondo ogomo omea neya gwarnang a kara ka wai a wa tata a macangcang kawa gere o cikǝ o cammo.
LUK 14:33 Nyimia kanza, pate ondooka wata cikǝ a wa bale epa eka eya malo o tare ong ne a wa baya e keeya emea waye ka ene, wa era wata itǝ ondo tare ong ne.
LUK 14:34 “Ogalu lento, wa arnang ka o lento wai, ara wiinia ka ote wai kawa kang lento?
LUK 14:35 Wa era wata kang eza okang eyapa ne, soona a oke wai, nyimia wayo za, ondooka wata cikǝ a wa bale epa eka e tare malo o tare ong ne. “Ekena teto epa eka eya konaza ne.”
LUK 15:1 Nangka ana o eesa emate makeke ka ana madinǝ ne de kane kone Yeso aka ya baala.
LUK 15:2 Na maParisa ka ana o baala ngmǝ aka Ashili a nya Mosa, ne bore agbwero na, “Karomo kaana ka itǝ kaja kana madinǝ nangka kaya lya epaolya kaa ne.”
LUK 15:3 Na Yeso bele ne angmǝ a gerpo na,
LUK 15:4 “A mana a ondo o ying waye ka emande e peng lewinu naka yende wili. A wata baya e tuuru torai ka o torai ara o lya mawake, a wa ale kawa gere kayende kamea ka wilǝ seeka wa cǝ kai sang?
LUK 15:5 A wa cǝ kai, a wa kone o leba, a wa ana kai o gagaru
LUK 15:6 a wa ale ka kai akwilǝ. A wa rare ejaa wai, ka andaame ne cikǝ legwa ka wai, a wa bekaana, ‘Kangkamanna o kona o leba aza kamande kapeng ka kaa wilǝ na ma cǝ kai.’
LUK 15:7 Eyang baale o ying, nyimia a yo kona o leba a cake azaa shili azaa ondo madinǝ oyende kawa kuri ara Ashili, kawa kala aromo tuuru torai ko torai ka ne ta ne laka edang o kurǝ a Ashili ne.
LUK 15:8 “A mana ondaye waye ka emate eyo emate betuuru, na be yende wili, wayo diki beru be masanto, a wa beshe akwilǝ me, a wa eke oto a soola me kawa zenga wa cǝ.
LUK 15:9 Wa cǝ be, a wa kurki ejaa wai, ka andaame ne cikǝ legwa, a wa bekaana, ‘Kankamang na o kona o leba, nangka ma cǝ bemate beng beeka be wilǝ.’
LUK 15:10 Eyang baale o ying, nyimia a Ashili ka atoma ai o zaa shili neya za o zanta, a were aka ondo madinǝ wa kurǝ ara Ashili.”
LUK 15:11 Na Yeso lya izi ka o beya angmǝ a gerpo na, “Oromo yende wa zene ka waye ka ayana a lome a leere.
LUK 15:12 Na kabaate kame beka ate ane na, ‘Ate, nyang bengmǝ beng a nyimia akwilǝ na.’ Na ate me are komana one bengmǝ be wai.
LUK 15:13 “Malo nyimi a ta a rabo maleo ne, na kena kabaate kame shende pate epa eka a nya kai aa ka baya akwilǝ me. Naka ale a makeke ma yende ma macangcang. A sanamea ka ale naka wilǝrǝ ocǝ o kai a pate a lya o bere zora epa edang.
LUK 15:14 Malo omea ka mare keeya ka ka zene, na e komo e gong e lyǝ a makeke mame, na kena kame lyǝ nyimi o dera maleo.
LUK 15:15 Naka ale a gera ogole o eza ara oromo yende a nyimi makeke mame, na oromo me turki kai a gole ara e dembashe e akwilǝ e wai, aza o bekaana ka ka soole ne aka nyaza ne epaolya.
LUK 15:16 Aza o burǝ ekomo ka e meke kai, naka gere o lya mabutu mamea e dembashe e akwilǝ neya lyame, na ondo ta nya kai ne.
LUK 15:17 “Nangka ka kuri a madoola ma woma, naka bekaana, ‘Eya eena eeyang eza me? Azara ate ang neye ka epaolya kane ta rosa epa o eza ka ee ne, a mi naana ba gbwǝ ka e komo.
LUK 15:18 Eyang era kang kuri ba ra ate ang, kang bekaa wai na, Ate, ma ya madinǝ ara Ashili, a ma wilǝ ara au kanza.
LUK 15:19 Nannamena anta bare a kang rarang na kena kau ne. Kuriyang kang itǝ na oyende a nyimia na o ezaza oo ogole.’
LUK 15:20 Naka ere aka meke orona o kurǝ ara ate a kai. “Aka tata a macangcang, na ate a kai laka kai, na wa rose kai, a wa kone egonegone kai, nyimia na wa song a wa ale ara a kai, na wa meke kena kame a wa kang gambare kai.
