LUK 15:21 “Na kena kame bekaana, ‘Ate, ma ya madinǝ ara Ashili a ma wilǝ a bo kanza. Nannamena anta bare a kang rarenna kena kau ne.’
LUK 15:22 “A nyimi o zanta na ate me rare azara akwilǝ o wai na wa bekaana, ‘Yangkanna na ka ede ka o dibi o rere ka e amba kai. E amba kai becapa a lebo ka tekakau a tobona.
LUK 15:23 A e de ka bena be mole benname ka core, ka lye a zante.
LUK 15:24 Aza o bekaana kena kaana kakang, mashe bena kagbwi na kakang kurǝ, mashe bena ka wili na a kang cǝ kai.’ Nane zante maleo.
LUK 15:25 “A were name, kena ka wai ka gong kamea ka ale ara, a ka ya za o kurǝ akwilǝ. Nangka ka amara ka akwilǝ, aaka kone aya gwara o guulung ka o yowa leera.
LUK 15:26 Na ka rare ozara akwilǝ me oyende, na ka pirkǝ wai epa eka eya za o ale.
LUK 15:27 Na ozara me bekaana, ‘Ondadimǝ o waya wa deya, waya ate au wa ote na a core bena be mole beena, aza o bekaana ondadimǝ o me wa kurǝ akwilǝ zak.’
LUK 15:28 “Ka o kona nyimi na ondaaizi me kone o burǝ cak, a wa nyana o lyǝ akwilǝ. Na ate ane suri na wa nya wai angmǝ a wa bose wai na wa lyǝ nyimi akwilǝ.
LUK 15:29 Na wa kabare ate wai na, ‘Lakai. A nyimi shenai sheena, ma ezau ogole na ozara, anta ma tukǝ nyana epa eka ba tukǝ bekaana ang ye ne. Pate ka nyimi ota tukǝ nya ong kabanaa kamande kang rare ejaa ang kate deya te lye a te eze ozǝnggǝ ne ma.
LUK 15:30 A nangka kena kaana kakau kamea ka ale naka wilǝrǝ ocǝ kai aza andaye o cikǝ okpwe one, ka kurǝ, ba core kai bena be mole beeme.’
LUK 15:31 “Na ate me bekaa kai na, ‘Kena kang, teye legwa ka bo koonang lengme pate epa eka ang zene a ewa e.
LUK 15:32 A epa e rere e obekaana te zanta, a te cǝ lenyong lee sano, aza o bekaana orone o oona tese bena wa gbwi na nannamena wa kurǝ, tese bena wa wili na a cǝ wai.’ ”
LUK 16:1 Yeso ka bele atoma kai angmǝ a gerpo na, “Ondo wa zene oka waye ka ocǝ ka ondo soola ocǝ o wai ka a ana wai angmǝ na wa kpwizizi ocǝ ate akwilǝ me.
LUK 16:2 Na ate akwilǝ me rare ondo soola me a wa pirkǝ wai na, ‘Eya eyang konaza me aza au? Nyang kazo ekeeya aza ogole o, oto kang itǝ ondo soola ocǝ ong ne.’
LUK 16:3 “Na ondo soola me beke a lenyong le wai na, ‘Ate akwilǝ ong ya tarangga ong ara ogole, eya eyang yame? Mi naana anta ama ogole legoone ne, ang kang ya ka ezǝng e lebose.
LUK 16:4 Ang rose epa eka eyang yame zongka ang baya arakana, ka a taranggang ara ogole ong, a were name aromo neyo embang a tokwilǝ to ne.’
LUK 16:5 “Nyimia wa rare komaname ka ate akwilǝ tare wai oduru. Nawa pirkǝ ondo bora na, ‘Nannia ate akwilǝ ang wa taro.’
LUK 16:6 “Nawa bekaana, ‘Magbwi shewinu riiru ma manao.’ “Na ondo o soola ocǝ me bekaa wai na, ‘Cikǝ nannamena o wele na a taro magbwi shewinu she naaze.’
LUK 16:7 “Nawa kang pirkǝ ondo, ‘A bo nannia taro?’ “Na wai kanza wa bekaana, ‘Magadasa ugu yende o alkama.’ “Na ondo soola ocǝ me bekaana, ‘Emba epa eka a wela tera o ying ka o kuriyǝ kawa itǝ shewinu riiru.’
LUK 16:8 “Na ate akwilǝ me sabe ondo soola ocǝ o wai na, Ang rose na ba kpwizizi ocǝ ong, pate ka nyimi ba wore o ama aza o lya izi o. Nyimia aromo amea neta nyimi masanto ne, neye ka o ama o cak o cikǝ ka aromo abelo ane, ka ne kala aromo amea neya masanto o ama.
LUK 16:9 Na Yeso lya izi ka o bekaana, Eyang beya ying na, ezana ogole ka ocǝ o ying ka e gere tokpwe toying ejaa. Nyimia ocǝ name ka wa to ale ka ying o maare ne, Ashili a yo emba ying a tokwilǝ to dera o maro.
LUK 16:10 “Nyimia ondooka wa eza edang aza ocǝ o baate, a yo eke wai ba za ocǝ o gong, kanza ondooka wata eza edang aza ocǝ o baate ne, wa era wata eza edang aza ocǝ o gong ne.
LUK 16:11 Eeta eza edang aza ocǝ a lerambo le Ashili leena ne, a wiinia a Ashili kabare ka o nya o ying ocǝ edang?
LUK 16:12 Kanza eeta e tukǝ eza edang aza o soola magogoro ma ondo ne, a wiinia a Ashili nya ying maaka maye maying?
LUK 16:13 “Oromo wa era wata ama eza lezara ara ate akwilǝ a leere ne. Waya nyimi a wa nyane ondo a wa yeme ondo, wa era wa kang kabare ka oyende a wa zeele o leere me. Ba era o ta ote lenyong ba Ashili ka emate ne.”
LUK 16:14 MaParisa andaaka ne yeme emate, aza o kona epa eka Yeso ka beka, nane ye becorte.
LUK 16:15 Naka bekaa ne na, “Yingnga ana o ote aromo kane laka na e tare Ashili ka edang, a Ashili rose anyong aying. Pate magogoro maame aromo yeme, maye Ashili ta yeme o laka mai ne.
LUK 16:16 “Obaala Mosa ka ana o beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili, a lya izi ka o baala me a deya a were a Yohana o batisma. O era a were a Yohana a zoole aza angmǝ lebo a togomo te Ashili, a komaname ya gera ocǝ o lyǝ a nyimi me.
LUK 16:17 Wa kala o bekaana a deze ka za a shili maro ka o bekaana beyo be wela be yende be dere legoone a nyimi a pate angmǝ a Ashili.
LUK 16:18 “Nangka a wele angmǝ Ashili na, Pate ondooka wa pere ondaye wai, a wa ana oyende, waya eza leyau naname, a nyimi a pate ondooka wa ana ondaye oka wa pere ondaleme wai, leyauwa waya eza me ka wai.
LUK 16:19 “Yeso ka bele ne angmǝ a gerpo na, Aye ondo ocǝ yende ka wa ambaza madibi maa rere nangka agomo ka ana emate ambaza, kanza a wa cikǝ o leba a koonang lengme.
LUK 16:20 Abuudu akwilǝ wai ondo wa ciisǝ ne kaa rareze wai na Liyazaru ondo lebose, a edara ka ma'aza susi a pate lepung le wai,
LUK 16:21 a wa ya gera pate manyesakarong maaka ma tǝǝruzu a deze araaka ondo ocǝ wa lyeeze epaolya ne. E ere o wake ne deese ane lembeze ma gwahu ma wai.
LUK 16:22 “Na a were de aka Liyazaru wa gbwi na Atoma Ashili o zaa shili ne de nane ana wai, ane nya wai aro cikǝ a rere ating Ibraheng. Ondo ocǝ me na wa kang gbwi na taase wai.
LUK 16:23 Akwilǝ ola araaka wa kone o poba ne, na wa ara yizi azaa shili na wa laka Ibraheng a Liyazaru a cikǝ ting wai.
LUK 16:24 Nawa rare na, ‘Ate Ibraheng, kona egonegone ong ka otong Liyazaru kawa ote lebo a nyimi manyi kawa tenkeng a lelengleng adorana lezi, eyang kona a huuwu a nyimi ola ona.’
LUK 16:25 “Na Ibraheng kabare na, ‘Kena, rintǝ a were amea baya lerambo le Ashili baye ka magogoro ma rere, a Liyazaru wata waye ka epa e rere ne. Nanname waya kona o leba a bo oya kona o burǝ.
LUK 16:26 Malo nyimi apat, a tera aro ka bo le'o le gerpo zene. Ondo wa era awata deya ara ying ne kanza ondo wa era awa ta deya ara aro ne.’
LUK 16:27 “Na ondo ocǝ name bekaana, ‘Nyimi waaza eyang bosa o ate Ibraheng, ka otong Liyazaru akwilǝ te ang,
LUK 16:28 o bena eyang ka arone esu andaleme, kawa nya ne angmǝ kana neema ne deya ara o poba a buru na ne.’
LUK 16:29 “Na Ibraheng bekaana, ‘Arone au neya ka andaaka neyo baala ne. Neye ka angmǝ aka Ashili a nya Mosa, ka angmǝ ana o beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili, ane kone ne.’
LUK 16:30 “Na ondo ocǝ wa kabare na, ‘Nyimia tazane ate Ibraheng. Ondo wa era o cau kawa ale ane yo kurǝ a Ashili.’
LUK 16:31 “Na Ibraheng bekaana, ‘Neta kona angmǝ aka Ashili a nya Mosa ka ewela ana o beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili ne, ondo wa era o ocau ma neto kona wai ne.’ ”
LUK 17:1 Na Yeso beke ana o tare o kai na, “O kedeya zene koonang were, a ondooka wa itǝ orona o nyimi, wa lyǝ udi.
LUK 17:2 Mara a tere ondo name lecale lo nyanto a lengmelo a tare wai a nyimi lepung, ka o bena wa ote ondo a nyimi ayana ana kane rizi a madinǝ.
LUK 17:3 Azaa nyimi, ezana a sauwo ka tokpwe to ying. “Ondooka o rose wa kala madinǝ, zurki a wai, a wa konau, o pisi epa emea wa yau a lenyong.
LUK 17:4 A wa caro o nyong ka o sondaare a lengme, a koonang oya nyimi a wa deya bo na, ‘Ma ya epa e buru, kwizǝng madinǝ mang.’ O pisi wai a lenyong lo.”
LUK 17:5 Na atoma Yeso bekaa kai na, “Ahh. Wala ro o kabare ka Ashili ne.”
LUK 17:6 Naka kabare na, “Eeya ka o kabare ka Ashili na o beyo be o mustad ka beya kala be baate, e era e bekaa uti o gong ona na ‘Wa mukurunu kawa ale kawa gata okpwe wai a lepong,’ a wa ye nyimi.
LUK 17:7 “A ondo o ying waya ka ozara kawa eze wai abara ka ena, kona wa soole wai emande epeng. Mana a nyimi o ying wa surǝ ara a wa beka ozara me na, ‘Deya arakana a saseya ka o cikǝ o lye ka mi?’
LUK 17:8 Wato bekaana, ‘Sele e mete, o ende, ma lya ang kang sa, malo me a bo o kang lya o se?’
LUK 17:9 Wa era a wa zante ka ozara me aza o bekaana wa ya epa eka a beka wai na wa ezea belle na?
LUK 17:10 Nyimia ying kanza, malo eza epa eka a bekaana e eze, eyo bekaana, ‘Aro azara o dera ama ai, te eza ogole oroa belle.’ ”
LUK 17:11 A Yeso ka ya orona o ale apeng a Urushalima, naka kale a bekazo be makeke ma Samariya ka ma Galili.
LUK 17:12 Nangka kaya lyǝ a kapeng ka yende, a aromo betuuru ka neye ka leganca, ane itǝ a macangcang ka kai,
LUK 17:13 ane rare kai ka lengmelo a jǝng na, “Yeso ondo ogong, kona egonegone ero.”
LUK 17:14 Naka laka ne aka bekaana, “Ale na ka e wore tokpwe to ying ara na magame ma Ashili.” Nangka ne ale, na pisi ne leganca le ne.
LUK 17:15 Ondo a nyimi one nangka wa laka a wa woma, na wa kuri, a wa saba Ashili ka lengmelo a jǝng.
LUK 17:16 Na wa girwǝ ating tobona te Yeso, a wa kone o leba kai, a wai oromo o makeke ma Samariya waye.
LUK 17:17 Na Yeso pirkǝ na, “Aromo betuurua a womza sang? O dangare o torai ome ya baba?
LUK 17:18 Ondo one tawa kuri kawa sabe Ashili ne soona o geng ona na?”
LUK 17:19 Naka beka a wai na, “Era ka o ale, o kabare ka Ashili au wa wongzau.”
LUK 17:20 Ngmende maParisa ne pirkǝ Yeso na, “Ngmǝyamea togomo te Ashili ya deya?” Na Yeso kabare na, “Togomo te Ashili teta deesa ka nangka eya doola o laka te ne,
LUK 17:21 aromo ne era ane ta bekaana, ‘Ateena, kona ateniini ne,’ aza o bekaana togomo te Ashili teya tera oying.”
LUK 17:22 Naka beke ana o tare o kai na, “A were aya deya ka eyo yeme o laka lengme le yende a nyimi shengme she Kena ka Oromo, pate ka nyimi eto laka lee ne.
LUK 17:23 Aromo neyo bele ying na, ‘Kaya ka niini, kona kaya kaana.’ Kana e tare nee ne.
LUK 17:24 Lengme le Kena ka Oromo, ya deya a yizi komana nangka mawere malmizi, ama nya masanto a kuruwǝ azaa shili ka koonang bekazo.
LUK 17:25 Zongka aye nyimi Kena ka Oromo kayo zitǝ cak kanza aromo a were aana, ne kang nyana kai.
LUK 17:26 “Nangka waze a tomore te Ogonggong Nuhu, nyimi wayo za a tomore te Kena ka Oromo.
LUK 17:27 A nyimi o nyana a Ashili one, a aromo neya lyeeza, ane sosoza, a anza andaye asau, andaye kang aleze a todo na dukǝ lengme leeka Ogonggong Nuhu wa lyǝ a nyimi o onggo manyi o gong. Zora o rosa saseya na o wena manyi mame zale nama wonge aromo a pate.
LUK 17:28 “Nyimia waze aza o nyana a Ashili a tomore te Lotu. Aromo neya lyelyeza, ane sosoza, neya eesa, ane lisizi, neya gasa ebelo ane sooze todo.
LUK 17:29 Lengme leeka Lotu wa baya apeng a Saduma, zora orosa na ola ka arantaane wai a japi a surǝ azaa shili na wonze aromo a pate a lengme leme.
LUK 17:30 “Azaa o nyana a Ashili aromo a wereena, nyimia wayo za zora o rosa one lengme leeka Kena ka Oromo kayo wore okpwe kai.
LUK 17:31 A lengme leng name ondo waya aza akwilǝ a wai, ka magogoro ma wai a nyimi kwilǝ me, kana wa japi kawa jeke mai ne. Nyimia, ondo waya o wake, kana wa kuri akwilǝ a kazo jeka magogoro ma wai ne.
LUK 17:32 Rintǝ epa eka e mana ondaye o Lotu.
LUK 17:33 Pate ondooka wa yeme ebeene wai wayo dera e, ondooka wa dera ebeene wai aza ong, wayo cǝ e.
LUK 17:34 “Ang bele ying, a lengme lo deya ong, aromo leere neyo ya ara o tete yende, a yo jeka ondo a baya ondo.
LUK 17:35 A yo mana andaye leere a nyanta eroko legwa, a yo jeka ondo a baya ondo.”
LUK 17:36 A yo mana andaleme leere ara a ogole, a yo jeka ondo a baya ondo.
LUK 17:37 Nane pirkǝ na, “A ruwǝme Ateokora?” Naka kabare ne ka angmǝ a gerpo na, “Ara a ka e keze zene, arakanamea ejogale kurkǝnǝzǝng ne.”
LUK 18:1 Na Yeso beke atoma kai angmǝ a gerpo adorana ka wore ne obena ne gwara ane beye angmǝ ka Ashili a gweregwere kana ne poro anyong ne.
LUK 18:2 Naka bekaana, “Apeng yende ondo cora angmǝ wa zene, oka wata ka boome ba Ashili ne, kanza awata bala aromo ne.
LUK 18:3 A ondaye yende wa zene apeng ame, omea ogbwǝri waze, na wa aleze a ondo o cora ngmǝ ba gweregwere kale bose na, ‘Nyang epa eka e gwara a tera ong ka ondo nyana ong.’
LUK 18:4 “O bora na wa nyane. Malo oka ondaye me wa gare wai a deesa a gweregwere, na wa beka okpwe wai na, ‘Pate ka o bekaana anta kona boome ba Ashili ne, kanza anta bala aromo ne.
LUK 18:5 Aza o bena ondaye ona wa garang ka o deesa a gweregwere, eyang ya wai epa eka e gwara aye wai, adorana wa bayang ang teeseke.’ ”
LUK 18:6 Na Ateokora me ka bekaana, “Kona na epa eka ondo o cora ngmǝ oka wata kona boome ba Ashili ne wa beke.
LUK 18:7 Ashili a era a ta nya andaaka wa Zaka ne epa eka e gwara ka neya gera me a wai a letereme kale lyaare ne? Wayo nyana o nya one na?
LUK 18:8 Eyang baala o ying, wayo nya epa e rere ba kwarte. Nyimia waaza, a were aka Kena ka Oromo ka deya, kayo cǝ ondooka wa kabare ka kai a lerambo le Ashili na?”
LUK 18:9 Yeso ka beke angmǝ a gerpo aza aromo aka ne jeka tokpwe tone o bena neye ka boome ba Ashili kanza ane zeele o dangare aromo.
LUK 18:10 Naka bekaana, “Anda leere ne ale ba akwilǝ Ashili kane beye angmǝ ka Ashili. Ondo o bora oParisa wai, a o leere me ondo o eesa emate makeke wai.
LUK 18:11 Na oParisa me wa ere a itǝ, na wa bore o beya ngmǝ ka Ashili a wa beye na, ‘Ashili ma zanta ka bo o bena mi anta ya na o dangare aromo ne. Anta ya na akǝri, ana o irizi aromo, ana o gera andaye aromo, mi anta ya na oromo ona ondo o eesa emate makeke ne.
LUK 18:12 A nyimi le sondaare le yende, ang pateze ongmǝ ka leere, ang nyaza be yende a nyimi be tuuru o cǝ ong.’
LUK 18:13 “Ondo o eesa emate makeke na wa itǝ a macang. Wata wa ara okpwe ka wa laka azaa Ashili ne, a wa beye na, ‘Ashili kona egonegone ong, mi ondo madinǝ wai.’ ”
LUK 18:14 Na Yeso bekaana, “Eyang baala o ying, ondo o eesa emate makeke wa kurǝ ba akwilǝ a wai ka o bena Ashili a kwizǝ madinǝ ma wai, wata na oParisa ne. Pate ondooka wa ara okpwe wai, a yo nata wai. Ondo oka wa nata okpwe wai, a yo ara wai.”
LUK 18:15 Na aromo ne deese ka ayana ane ara a Yeso adorana ka eke ne taara kane cǝ o leba. Ka o laka o nyimi na atoma kai, ne zurki ane.
LUK 18:16 Na Yeso ka rare a bana ayana me, aka bekaa atoma a kai na, “Baya na a bana yana ane deye a mi, tana e nare ne ne, togomo te Ashili tatone te.
LUK 18:17 Ang bele ying epeng eme, pate ondooka wata kabare ka togomo te Ashili nangka ka bana kena ka kabare ne, wa era wata lyǝ ba nyimi o te ne.”
LUK 18:18 Ondoono dandaro o gwarzanang maYahuda yende wa pirkǝ Yeso na, “Ondo o baala o lenyong le sangsang, ma wiini a ang cǝ ebeene odera o maro?”
LUK 18:19 Na Yeso pirkǝ wai na, “Eyaka oya beya mi na ondo o baala o lenyong le sangsang, ondo o baala o lenyong le sangsang ta zene ne, Ashili aya belle ondo o baala o lenyong le sangsang.
LUK 18:20 O rose epa eka angmǝ aka Ashili a nya Mosa wa wele, ‘Tana o eze leyau ka andaye ne, tana o wong ondo ne, tana o eze bekǝri ne, tana o beye majakari aza ondo ne, nya ate ka iini o togomo tene.’ ”
LUK 18:21 Na oromo me bekaana, “Ma tare epa eka a beka pate a were ame ma tata ka bana kena.”
LUK 18:22 Ka o kona nyimi, na Yeso bekaa wai na, “Epa e yendea tata ka ba dera. Lisǝ epa eka oye ka e ba pate, ka o areseze ana o dera, oyo itǝ ondo le'eke a cake aza shili. O de ka o tareng.”
LUK 18:23 Nangka wa kone nyimi, na lenyong le wai caro aza o bekaana, waya ka ocǝ a cake.
LUK 18:24 Ka o laka lenyong le wai a le caro, na Yeso bekaana, “Wayo poba a cak ana ocǝ ne lyǝ a togomo te Ashili.
LUK 18:25 Mara o rankome wa lyǝ a le'o le beberkena aza o bena, ondo ocǝ wa lyǝ a togomo te Ashili.”
LUK 18:26 Aromo amea ne kone orooka ona nane pirkǝ kai na, “Nyimia waaza, mana wa era a wa cǝ o boza?”
LUK 18:27 Na Yeso kabare na, “Epa eka e kala legoone le aromo, eta kala legoone le Ashili ne.”
LUK 18:28 Na Biturusu bekaana, “Gwukuu. Aro naana a te baya tokwilǝ tero ka e keeya a te taro.”
LUK 18:29 Na Yeso bekaana, “Eyang dongdong bele o ying, ondo ta zene omea wa baya akwilǝ wai, ka ondaye, ka arone, ka anate, ka ayana, aza ogole o togomo te Ashili,
LUK 18:30 a wa dera ocǝ magogoro nanname. A izi a wa kang cǝ ebeene o dera o maro ne.”
LUK 18:31 Na Yeso ale ka atoma kai ba e daki, naka bekaa ne na, “Teya zala a ale a Urushalima, a sanamea angmǝ aka ana o beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili, ne wele aza Kena ka Oromo a yo pena.
LUK 18:32 A yo nya kai a legoone le taara te Aworme. Neyo zeela kai, ane eseze kai, ane kareze kai mawo. Ane ole kai ane kang wonga kai.
LUK 18:33 Malo nyimi a lengme lo taaro aka ere.”
LUK 18:34 A atoma kai neta ne cǝ masanto ma epa eka ka baale ne ne. Masanto mame a baasa ba ne, neta ne rose epa eka ka baale ne ne.
LUK 18:35 A were aka Yeso ka amara ka apeng a Yariko, a urǝ yende waya cikǝ ba e daki be orona a wa eze lebose.
LUK 18:36 Nangka wa kone aromo aneya kala, na wa pirkǝ epa emea eya ale.
LUK 18:37 Na beka wai na, “Yeso karomo ka apeng Nazarat kaya ya kala.”
LUK 18:38 Nawa rare ka lengmelo a jǝng na, “Yeso kena ka abuudu a Daoda kona egonegone eng.”
LUK 18:39 Aromo amea neya izi nane zurki wai na wa kome, na wa wale o ara lengmelo ba jǝng kanza, a wa beya na, “Kena ka buudu a Daoda, kona egonegone eng.”
LUK 18:40 Na Yeso itǝ aka ote na a de ka oromo ome ara kai. Nangka wa deya ma'amo na Yeso pirkǝ wai na,
LUK 18:41 “Eya oya yeme ang ezo?” Na urǝ ome kabare na, “Ateokora, eyang yeme ang cǝ o gonta ara.”
LUK 18:42 Na Yeso beke a wai na, “Cǝ o gonta ara, o kabare ka Ashili au wa wongzau.”
LUK 18:43 Ka o beka o Yeso nyimi, a wa ong cǝ o gonta ara a saseya, na wa tare kai, a wa sabe Ashili. Nangka aromo ne laka nyimi, na pate one ne sabe Ashili.
LUK 19:1 Yeso ka lyǝ a Yariko, aka ya kala a nyimi apeng naname,
LUK 19:2 na ondooka beya wai na Zaka, oromo ogong a nyimi ana o eesa emate makeke, wai ondo ocǝ kanza.
LUK 19:3 Wa gere o laka o bena mana Yeso, na wata ama ne, aza o bena aromo ne gong arame, a wai kanza waya kpwentiring.
LUK 19:4 Nawa lyǝ izi kato song, na wa zala uti o urǝrǝ orona ka Yeso kaya kala arame, adorana wa cǝ wa laka kai.
LUK 19:5 Nangka Yeso ka dukǝ rame, naka ara okpwe naka beka wai na, “Zaka, jipi a saseya, o ngmeengme, akwilǝ au wa eyang dongdong jipi ne.”
LUK 19:6 Nawa jipi a kwarte, a wa embe kai ka lenyong leyende.
LUK 19:7 Nangka aromo ne laka nyimi, na pate one bebeya a tokpwe tone, nane bekaana, “Gwukuu. Ka jipi akwilǝ ondo madinǝ.”
LUK 19:8 Na Zaka ere a itǝ, na wa bekaa Ateokora na, “Ateokora, laka. Nannamena pate epa eka eyang ka e eyang ara a tera kang nya ana o dera, a pate ondooka ma iri wai, eyang kuriyǝ wai ka naaze epa eka ma emba a wai.”
LUK 19:9 Yeso ka beka wai na, “Ngmeengme na, o boza wa lyǝ akwilǝ ana, o bekaana ba kurǝ a Ashili kanza bo kena ka akora na Ibraheng wai.
LUK 19:10 Kena ka Oromo ka deya dakememe a gera epa eka e wilǝ, ka ka boza e kanza.”
LUK 19:11 Nangka neya konaza epa me, na Yeso ka lyǝ izi ka o baala one angmǝ a gerpo, aka ya ma'amo ka o Urushalima, aneya madoola ma o bena togomo te Ashili taya wore okpwe te nannamena.
LUK 19:12 Naka bena, “Oromo yende akwilǝ togomo wa ale a makeke ma yende ma macangcang adorana a nya wai togomo zongka wa kuri.
LUK 19:13 Nawa rare azara wai betuuru, na wa nya komana one emate, a wa kang bekaa ne na, ‘Wangara na emate me seeka ma kuri.’
LUK 19:14 “Na aromo apeng wai ne nyane wai, nyimia nane tong atoma a malo wai ara ondooka waye ka o bare o nya wai togomo kane bekaana, ‘Teta yeme oromo ona a wa itǝ ogomo oro ne.’
LUK 19:15 “Pate ka nyimi na nya wai togomo, malo oka wa cǝ te na wa kuri, a wa ote na a rare wai azara name ka wa nya ne emate, ka wa laka epa eka ne cǝ aza o wangara me.
LUK 19:16 “Na obora me de a wa bekaana, ‘Ondoogong, bemate be yende beeka ba nyang be windi emate betuuru.’
LUK 19:17 “Nawa kabare ozara me na, ‘Gajeya, ozara ogashe. Nangka ba wore edang aza epa e baate, ma nyau togomo to apeng betuuru.’
LUK 19:18 “Na o leere ome de, na wa bekaana, ‘Ondoogong, bemate beka ba nyang be windi emate esu.’
LUK 19:19 “Nawa kabare wai na, ‘Bo kanza ma nyau togomo to apeng esu.’
LUK 19:20 “Kanza na oyende de na wa bekaana, ‘Ondoogong emba bemate bo. Mashe tere e a kajembelea, nang baasa suk.
LUK 19:21 Aza o bena eyang kona boome bo, obena bo o pobe. O jeeze epa eka ota ba eke ne o kang shende epa eka ota ba gata ne.’
LUK 19:22 “Na ondoogong me kabare na, ‘Bo ozara a ara a buru. Eyang core o angmǝ aza epa eka ba beka, O rose bena mi oromo o poba, ondo omea wa jeeze epa eka wata wa eke ne, ang kang shende epa eka anta ma gata ne?
LUK 19:23 Nyimia waaza, eyaka ota ba eke emate eng ara o eese emate ne, ka ma kurǝ ang cǝ eyapa azame ne?’
LUK 19:24 “Nawa beka aromo ka neya itǝ arame, ‘Emba na bemate beena a wai ka e nya ondoname ka waya ka e betuuru.’
LUK 19:25 “Nane beka wai na, ‘Ondoogong, wa ya ka emate betuuru pa.’
LUK 19:26 “Eyang baala o ying, pate ondooka waye ka eyapa cake, a yo wala wai ne, ondooka waye ka eya baate kanza, a embe kapa ka mea waya ka kai.
LUK 19:27 A ana o nyana ong ka neta yeme ong na ang eze togomo aza one ne, deya na ka ne arakana ka e wongze ne ang yang gonta.”
LUK 19:28 Nangka Yeso ka beka nyimi, na ka kala aka ale Urushalima.
LUK 19:29 Nangka ka amara ka kapeng ka Betapaji ka ko Beta nya, kane ya e daki zuwǝ o mati ma Zaitun, na ka tonga atoma kai a leere,
LUK 19:30 aka bekaa ne na, “Lyǝ na a kapeng kaanini a izi o ying. Ka o lyǝ o ying, eyo laka ka bana ka kurungzǝ ka yende ka o tera, kame a ta a tukǝ ozalame ne. Dinggǝ na kai ka e deene arakana.
LUK 19:31 Ondo oka wa pirkǝ ying na, ‘Eyaka eya dinggǝ a kai?’ E bekaana, ‘Ateokora aro ya yeme a kai.’ ”
LUK 19:32 Na andaaka atong ne ale, nane mana nangka Yeso ka bekaa ne.
LUK 19:33 Neya aza o dinggǝ kai naname, na ana kurungzǝ kame pirkǝ ne na, “Eyaka eya dinggǝ ka kurungzǝ kana?”
LUK 19:34 Nane bekaana, “Ateokora ya yeme a kai.”
LUK 19:35 Nane de ka kai ba Yeso, ane nata madibi mane azaa kurungzǝ kame, ane ana Yeso nane eke azaa kai.
LUK 19:36 Kaya aza o ale naname, na aromo nasa madibi mane azaa orona.
LUK 19:37 Nangka Yeso ka amara ka Urushalima araaka orona wa jipi o zuwǝ o mati ma Zaitun, na o kurkǝnǝng ana o tare okai a cake ne bore o kona oleba, ane saba Ashili kale ngmelo ajǝng aza e pate epa e moole kane laka.
LUK 19:38 Nane bekaana, “Ondo kona o leba ogomo oka waya deya a nyimi leze le Ateokora.” “O cikǝ a cammo aza shili, a o saba itǝ a Ashili.”
LUK 19:39 Pate ka nyimi na maParisa ma yende a nyimi o kurkǝnǝng aromo ne bekaa kai na, “Ondo baala, zurki a o kurkǝnǝng ana o tare o kane kome seete.”
LUK 19:40 Naka kabare na, “Eyang baala o ying, aromo na ne kome a seete, acale ka tokpwe to ai neya saba Ashili.”
LUK 19:41 Nangka ka amara, naka laka apeng a Urushalima, naka ruuzi aza ai.
LUK 19:42 Naka bekaana, “Aiya e rose o ngmeengme na epa eka aya gerame aza o cikǝ a cammo. A nanname a baasa aying.
LUK 19:43 A were ya deya ka ana o nyana o ying neyo ringgari ying ka o sowa lebonggo, ane kang eza o kara ka ying. A ana o tesa a geza a moole neyo ringgari ying a koruwa.
LUK 19:44 Neyo wonza aromo aying a pate. Neto kang baya lecale leyende leeka a soo tedo to ying ne aza le yende ne. A yo ya nyimia aza o bena eta e kabare o bena Ashili a de ka boze ying ne.”
LUK 19:45 Na ka lyǝ a atatara a akwilǝ Ashili, na ka bore o taranggaza ana o lisǝzǝ magororo.
LUK 19:46 Na ka beya ne na, “A wele na, ‘Akwilǝ ang a yo itǝ akwilǝ o beya angmǝ ka Ashili. Na ying e kuriyǝ ai obake akǝri.’ ”
LUK 19:47 Koonang lengme, ka baale aromo a akwilǝ Ashili. A ana magame ma Ashili ma moole, ka ana o baala angmǝ aka Ashili a nya Mosa, ka ana o togomo aza aromo ne gere orona o wongnga kai.
LUK 19:48 Nane dere nangka neyo wongnga kai, obena angmǝ a kai a embe anyong aromo a pate ka neya arame.
LUK 20:1 Ngmende a Yeso ka lyǝ atatara akwilǝ Ashili ka ka baale kanza aka zoole aromo aza orooka o lebo, na ana magame ma Ashili ma moole, ana o baala angmǝ aka Ashili nya Mosa ka anateandaasau ne de.
LUK 20:2 Nane bekaa kai na, “Bele ro orona legoone leeka o ezeze epa ena ne. Mana wa nyau legoone leena?”
LUK 20:3 Na Yeso kabare na, “Eyang eza ying be pirǝ, beleng na,
LUK 20:4 Legoone le ngmǝ a Yohana ondo batisma a suri a Ashili na, aromo ai?”
LUK 20:5 Nane beya tokpwe tone, nane laka o bekaana, “Te bekaana, ‘Wa suri a Ashili,’ a kayo bekaana, ‘Eyaka eta e kabare ka wai ne?’
LUK 20:6 Kanza te bekaana, ‘Wa suri aromo,’ aromo a cake neyo teza ro ka cale, o bekaana komana rose Yohana ondo o beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili wai.”
LUK 20:7 Nane maare ko bekaa kai na, “Teta rosa araaka le suri ne ne.”
LUK 20:8 Na Yeso bekaa ne na, “Mima anta bele o ying ka legoone le mana eyang eza epa eka eya gonta me ne.”
LUK 20:9 Na Yeso ka lyǝ izi ka o baala aromo angmǝ a gerpo na, “Ondo wa rene amea waye ka ara o inabi, na wa nya ana ondo ogole arame a wa ale a begere a makeke ma yende, na wa rabo a saname.
LUK 20:10 Nangka a were o shende e inabi waye, na wa tong ozara wai oyende ana ogole me kawa mangka ayana o inabi me ba ne. Na ana ogole me ne ole wai, aane tarangga wai na wa kuri zora eyapa.
LUK 20:11 Na oromo me wa tong ozara o leere, na ana ogole me kang ola wai na o bora, aane eze wai epa ezǝng aane kang tarangga wai na wa kuri zora eyapa.
LUK 20:12 Na oromo me wa tong ozara o taaro, na ana ogole me ne ole wai aane juki wai aane were wai o yangga.
LUK 20:13 “Na ondo ara o inabi me wa bekaana, ‘Eya eyang ya naname? Eyang tonga kena kang ka lome kamea ang yeme, ang rose obena neyo tare kai.’
LUK 20:14 “Pate ka nyimi nangka ana ogole me ne laka kai nane bekaa tokpwe to ne na, ‘Kando kamea kayo jeka ocǝ me kaana, baya ate wong kai, a ocǝ ondo arame wa itǝ aoro.’
LUK 20:15 Nane wong kai ane tare e keze kai a malo ara inabi. “Eya ondo arame wayo ya ne?
LUK 20:16 Wayo deya ka wa wong ana ogole me, a wa nya ana ondo ara ame.” Nangka aromo ka neya akwilǝ a Ashili ne kone nyimi nane bekaana, “Kana Ashili baya nyimi aye ne.”
LUK 20:17 Na Yeso karene a yizi a dongdong aka pirkǝ na, “Eya bekazo ba ngmǝ epa ena a ana o beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili ne wela? “ ‘Lecale leemea ana o sowa ne nyana, leya le itǝ leeme a waale a yeme me a were o sowa.’
LUK 20:18 Bekazo be angmǝ ana a beya, pate ondooka wa rizi baaza lecale leme a wayo jukǝ okpwe wai a wa poso a nyokonyoko. A lecale leme le taru a wai a were amea a yo core angmǝ azaa wai, a yo nyanta wai kawa itǝ na ma'ena.”
LUK 20:19 Aza o bekaana ne rose na angmǝ a gerpo na aza o bena neta ne kabare ka o baala o kai ne. Na ana o baala angmǝ aka Ashili a nya Mosa ka ana magame ma Ashili ma moole ne gere orona o meke o Yeso a saseya, nane kone boome ba aromo.
LUK 20:20 Na ne gere orona o meke o kai kane ote kai ka ka rizi aza epa eka ka yo beka. Adorana ka lyǝ a taara te ogomo makeke mame. Nane nya aromo anyong a buru yende emate kane itǝ ana o kare o kai a yizi, na aromo me wore o bena ne aromo a rere ne. Na tong ne ba Yeso kane eze kai be pirǝ.
LUK 20:21 Andaaka atong, ne pirkǝ Yeso na, “Ondobaala, te rose o bena o beeze o kang baala e peng, o takang wore o bena o kala yeme a ondo ne, kanza o baale orona Ashili ba kap.
LUK 20:22 Wa rere o bena te are emate makeke a Ogomo ogong o Roma Kaisar na te bayai?”
LUK 20:23 Na Yeso ka ka rose anyong ane a buru naka bekaa ne na,
LUK 20:24 “Woreng na beyo bemate. O ululu ka leze le mana a aza beyo bemate me?”
LUK 20:25 Nane bekaana, “O Ogomo ogong o Roma Kaisar wai.” Naka bekaa ne na, “Nyimi waaza nyana Ogomo ogong o Roma Kaisar epa eka e Ogomo ogong o Roma Kaisar e, e nya Ashili epa e Ashili e.”
LUK 20:26 Nane ta cǝ orona o meke o kai ne aza epa eka ka beka arakaname a nyimi aromo. Na epa eme tere ne okpwe aza o kabare o kap o be pirǝ be ne, nane kome a set.
LUK 20:27 MaSadukiya ma yende, kane beeze na malo o gbwǝ a era ta era ne, ne deye a Yeso ka be pirǝ. Nane bekaana,
LUK 20:28 “Ondo baala, Mosa ondo o beya a ngmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili wa wele ro oroka o bena, ondo wa gbwǝ a wa baya ondaye zora ayana, wa gwara o bena orone o wai ana ondaye me kawa ngmeng wai ayana.
LUK 20:29 A bena, arone yende ne zene neya a sondaare. Ondo o bora a nyimi one wa ana ondaye na wa gbwi zora kena.
LUK 20:30 Na o leere wa ana ondaye me na wa gbwi zora kena.
LUK 20:31 Na o taaro one wa ana ondaye me, nyimia ne anza ondaye me a ale orone o sondaare nane gbwizi zora ayana.
LUK 20:32 O maare na ondaye me wa gbwi.
LUK 20:33 A lengme lo era andaaka ne gbwizǝ, wayo itǝ ondaye mana a nyimi one, nangka pate one a sondaare ne tukǝ o ana o wai?”
LUK 20:34 Na Yeso bekaa ne na, “Aromo a were ana andaleme anza andaye, andaye kanza ne aleze a todo.
LUK 20:35 Pate ka nyimi andaaka neya kap ka were name ane kang bare o era a malo gbwǝ, ne era neta ana andaye ne a andaye kanza ne era ane ta ale a todo ne,
LUK 20:36 ne era neta gbwǝ kanza ne, aza o bena ne itǝ na atoma a surǝ a zaa shili. Ne itǝ ayana Ashili, o bena ne era a malo o gbwǝ.
LUK 20:37 Eta e kabare a kap ne, Mosa wa wore o bena andaaka ne gbwǝ neyo era, wa wele epa eka Ashili a beke, a epa eka Ashili a beke naana, ‘Mea Ashili Ibraheng, ka Ashili Ishaku, a Ashili a Yakub.’
LUK 20:38 Ai Ashili ana o gbwǝ taza ne, ai Ashili a pate andaaka ne gbwǝ a neya tare o kai ka e edang, neye ka ebeene.”
LUK 20:39 Na ana ondo ba nyimi ana o baala angmǝ aka Ashili a Mosa ne bekaana, “Ondo baala ba bekaa kap.”
LUK 20:40 Ondo ta zene kanza kawa ama pirǝ o kai ne.
LUK 20:41 Na Yeso ka pirkǝ aromo a cak na, “Eyaka ana o baala angmǝ aka a Ashili a nya Mosa ne beeze na Ondooka Ashili a zake kena ka abuudu Daoda kai?
LUK 20:42 Daoda ka okpwe kai a nyimi o Seleera ka bekaana: “ ‘Ateokora wa bekaa Ateokora ong na, “Cikǝ a sara ore ong,
LUK 20:43 zongka ang ote ana o nyana o atau legoone lo na o taara atau tobona to.” ’
LUK 20:44 Daoda wa rare kai na, ‘Ateokora.’ Nyimia waaza a wiinia aka ta kala o bena kena ka abuudu a wai ne?”
LUK 20:45 A aromo a pate ya konaza, na Yeso ka bekaa ana o tare o kai na,
LUK 20:46 “Ezana a sauwo ka ana o baala angmǝ aka Ashili a nya Mosa, aza o ara okpwe one. Ne ambaza ma dibi ma moole ane yenga nyimi aromo, ane kang yeme a beye ne oko a nyimi ara ejamane. Kanza ane yeme a nya ne ara o cikǝ a rere ba nyimi madandaro ma o gwarzanang maYahuda, ka ara o cikǝ a rere ara o gwara.
LUK 20:47 Neya ana o lyeeza magogoro ma agbwǝri andaye, ane kang rabo a beya angmǝ ka Ashili adorana a laka ne. Abela aromo name Ashili a yo gǝǝzǝ ne ba cak.”
LUK 21:1 Yeso ka ara okpwe naka laka ana ocǝ yende aneya taara emate a nyimi ara le'eke le emate akwilǝ Ashili.
LUK 21:2 Naka kang laka kagbwǝri kandaye a ka tare eyo emate e batebate leere a nyimi ara le'eke leme kanza.
LUK 21:3 Na ka bekaana, “Eyang baala o ying epeng eme, epa eka kagbwǝri kandaye kaana ka tare ba nyimi me, e kale o dangareme ba pate.
LUK 21:4 Obena pate ana ocǝ name ane nya a baate a nyimi epa e cake ka neya ka e, kai kanza ba nyimi odera naka nya pate emate epaolya kai ka lenyong le yende.”
LUK 21:5 Ana ondo a nyimi ana o tarea kai neya beya angmǝ aza akwilǝ a Ashili, ka nangka a babara ai ka acale emamate, a magogoro maaka a nyaza mo gole akwilǝ me. Na ka bekaa ne na,
LUK 21:6 “Magogoro maana eya gonta me, a were ya deya ka lecale leyende ato baya le aza le yende zora o bacakare ne.”
LUK 21:7 Nane pirkǝ kai na, “Ondo baala, ngmǝyamea aya eza mapapa mana? Eya teyo laka ka te rose bena a were me a amara ko deya?”
LUK 21:8 Naka kabare na, “Doola na ka edang tana ondo wilǝrǝ ying ne. Obena aromo a cake ya deya ka leze leng, ane beye majakari na, ‘Mea Ondooka Ashili a zake,’ ane kang beya na, ‘A were o maare a amara.’ Tane tare ne ne.
LUK 21:9 E kang kona angmǝ o makara ka o ara anyong, tane kerke ne. Seeka a bore o ya a nyimi, a omaare tata izi.”
LUK 21:10 A wereme na Yeso bekaa ne na, “Makeke mayo eza okara ka makeke ma yende, a togomo teyo eza okara ka togomo te yende.
LUK 21:11 Adeze a yo zekimarnu a cake, ka e komo kanza ka makono ato ara cak. A yo kang laka mapa ma boome ka mapa maaka a ta a tukǝ o laka me ne a susǝ aza shili.
LUK 21:12 “Zongka nyimi, neyo gǝǝzǝ ying a cak. Neyo ale ka ying a madandaro ma o gwarzanang maYahuda ka core angmǝ aza o ying. A kang a aleze ka ying a tokwilǝ to pateze ana o eza epa e buru a yo pirǝ ying angmǝ a begeshe ba agomo a batebate ka a moole aza o bena ying e tareng.
LUK 21:13 Nyimia wayo itǝ orona o bele one angmǝ aza ong.
LUK 21:14 Aza nyimi terana anyong aying tana e eze madoola nangka eyo kabare angmǝ aza o ying ne,
LUK 21:15 eyang nya ying angmǝ a woma ka o rosa nangka ana o nyana o ying neto kang ama o itǝ ka ying ne.
LUK 21:16 Pate ana ate ka iini, arone a lome, ana akwilǝ aying, ka ejaa, neyo nyana, ane niyi ying ka wonze ana ondo o ying.
LUK 21:17 Komana wayo nyana ying aza o bena ying e tareng.
LUK 21:18 Pate ka nyimi lekpwi le yende okpwe o ying to wilǝ ne.
LUK 21:19 E itǝ ka legoone eng yang nya ying ebeene o dera o maro.
LUK 21:20 “A e laka apeng Urushalima à á ringgari ai ka ana o tesa geza a moole, e rose o bena a were o posa ai wa amara.
LUK 21:21 Aza nyimi andaaka neyo makeke ma Yahudiya aane song kane zale mayara, andaaka neya nyimi apeng ane suri, kanza andaaka neye a topepeng to batebate to yangga o Urushalima kana ne lyǝ a nyimi apeng ne.
LUK 21:22 A were name a yo itǝ o taasa aza andaaka ne eza epa e buru, kanza angmǝ aka ana o beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili ne wele, a yo pena.
LUK 21:23 Wayo itǝ ka o zitǝ cake andaye aka neye ka e tumǝ ka andaye amea neya nyaza ayana maane a tomore tonname. O mungi Ashili wayo oko aza aromo ana, aane yo zitǝ jǝng.
LUK 21:24 A yo wonga ana ondo one ka o sagali, a yo kang beza odanggare one azara a ale a pate makeke ma lerambo le Ashili. A Urushalima a yo itǝ epa ma zelakong ara aworme ka neyo eza togomo ara o danggare one a ale a were aka neyo dukǝ bekazo be ne.
LUK 21:25 “A yo laka magogoro ma sau, ongme, oreka ka e werewere. Ara kaana a deze, aromo neyo kona o burǝ ane kang kona boome aza behoowo ka o tambalana lepong.
LUK 21:26 Aromo neyo kona boome aza epa eka ne laka eya oko a deze, o bena o bare o nyimi shili Ashili a yo zukarnǝ mai.
LUK 21:27 A were namea komana me wayo laka Kena ka Oromo aka ya deya a nyimi mawere ka o bare okai ka o gongnga kai o cake.
LUK 21:28 E bora o gonta magogoro mana, erana ba itǝ e ara tokpwe toying aza, aza o bena o boza o ying wa amara.”
LUK 21:29 Ka bele ne angmǝ gerpo na, “Laka na uti o saya ka mati ba pate.
LUK 21:30 Ne bora o sǝrsǝzǝ ma rane, eyo laka ka tokpwe toying na lekoze le amara.
LUK 21:31 Nyimia waaza, ba laka pate epa ena eya ale, e rose o bena togomo te Ashili te amara.
LUK 21:32 “Ang bele ying e peng eme, aromo a were ana neto gbwizǝ a pate ne zongka mapapa maana ma wore okpwe mai.
LUK 21:33 Azaa shili ka deze neyo maro angmǝ ang ato maro ne.
LUK 21:34 “Ekena teto. Kana e baya anyong aying aye maring ka o sosoza, kanza ka magogoro ma were anane. Kana e baya a lengme lenname le meke ying eta rosa ne.
LUK 21:35 Lengme lenname ya deya aza pate ondooka waya ka ebeene a pate lerambo le Ashili leena.
LUK 21:36 Ekena teto koonang a were, e beye angmǝ ka Ashili nangka eyo bisǝ a pate epa eka eya deya, kanza nangka eyo ama o itǝ a begeshe be kena ka Oromo ka o kona o leba.”
LUK 21:37 Koonang lengme Yeso ka ale akwilǝ Ashili kaka baale, a koonang lyǝlu aka kuri kaka maare lelyaare ba za oyara o Zaitun.
LUK 21:38 A aromo a cake gwarzanang akwilǝ Ashili koonang leleere kane koneze kai.
LUK 22:1 A were o gwarnang o rintǝ o dera o wonga ayana o bora maYahuda a Masar, wa amara,
LUK 22:2 ana magame ma Ashili ma moole ka ana o baala angmǝ aka Ashili nya Mosa ne gere orona omea neyo wonga Yeso. Ne gere o ya nyimi a ondo ta rosa ne ko bena neya kona boome ba aromo.
LUK 22:3 Na ogomo o bere o buru wa lyǝ ba Yahuda ka a rareze wai na Iskariyoti, waya nyimi atoma Yeso betuuru ka leere.
LUK 22:4 Nawa ale ana magame ma Ashili ma moole ka andaamoole ajawu akwilǝ a Ashili, nane gere nangka wayo nya ne Yeso.
LUK 22:5 Nane kone o leba ba cake, aane eke o bena neyo ara wai emate.
LUK 22:6 Na Yahuda kabare ka nyimi, na wa bore o gera orona oka wayo nya ne Yeso a aromo ta rosa ne.
LUK 22:7 Na lengme lo o gwarnang o rintǝ o dera o wonga ayana o bora maYahuda a Masar wa dukǝ ka a yo core Ashili ka kwete.
LUK 22:8 Na Yeso tong Biturusu, ka Yohana aka bekaa ne na, “Ale na ka e babare ro ara o gwarnang o rintǝ o dera o wonga ayana o bora maYahuda a Masar kate lye a nyimi me.”
LUK 22:9 Nane pirkǝ kai na, “Oya yeme ate babare e a baba?”
LUK 22:10 Naka kabare na, “E lyǝ apengme, eyo gwarnang ka ondaleme yende a wa ana o daka manyi. Tare na wai a ale akwilǝ ka waya lyǝ ne,
LUK 22:11 e bekaa ondo akwilǝ me na, ‘Kando ka o baala ka tonga ro kate pirkau na. Odo ageng ya baba, araaka eyang lya epaolya o gwarnang o rintǝ o dera o wonga ayana o bora maYahuda a Masar ka atoma ang ne?’
LUK 22:12 Wayo wore ying odo ogong oka waya aza o gungǝ, oka a eke e keeya a nyimi me. Arakaname eyo babara e keeya ne.”
LUK 22:13 Nane ale ane mana e keeya nangka Yeso ka bekaa ne. Nane babare epaolya o gwarnang o rintǝ o surǝ maYahuda a makeke ma Masar.
LUK 22:14 Nangka a were ame a dukǝ, na Yeso ka ale ka atoma kai, aane pitǝkǝlnǝ legwa ara o lya epaolya.
LUK 22:15 Na Yeso bekaa ne na, “Ma yeme o lya epaolya o gwarnang o rintǝ o dera o wonga ayana o bora maYahuda a Masar o na ka ying zongka ang lyǝ o zitǝ.
LUK 22:16 Eyang bele o ying, ma era ang takang lya e ne, seeka e laka ebelo e a e pena a nyimi togomo te Ashili.”
LUK 22:17 Naka jeke kagbwi, aka kone o leba Ashili aka bekaana, “Emba na epa eka eya nyimi kagbwi kaana ka e esoze a tokpwe to ying.
LUK 22:18 Eyang bele o ying, ma era ang takang sa kanza ba nyimi e buru o inabi ne seeka togomo te Ashili te de.”
LUK 22:19 Aka jeke o borode, naka kone o leba Ashili aka pose wai, aka nya ne aka bena, “Onna lepung lenga le a nya aza o ying lya na, ezezena nyimi e rintǝng.”
LUK 22:20 Nyimia kanza, malo o lya emete naka jeke kagbwi kame, aka bena, “Epa eka eya nyimi kagbwi kaana eye na otono osau ka wayo bora ka ma nyau mang a were aka a wonga, maaka a yo oka aza o ying.
LUK 22:21 Ang kang beka eyapa, arakana ondooka waya niyi ong a taara te andaaka ne nyaneng waya nyimi ara o lya epaolya ka mi.
LUK 22:22 Kena ka Oromo kayo gbwǝ nangka a beka, kanza ondooka wa niyi kai ana o nyana kai wa lyǝ udi.”
LUK 22:23 Na atoma kai ne bore o pirǝ tokpwe tone na, mana a nyimi aro ka wayo ya nyimi?
LUK 22:24 Na masanggo ere a nyimi one, aza o bena mana wayo itǝ ondo kala ogonga.
LUK 22:25 Na Yeso bekaa ne na, “Agomo aworme neta rose Ashili ne, ne anza ne magogoro ma dendeng, kanza andaaka ne eze togomo aza one ne rareze tokpwe tone na ana o kankama aromo.
LUK 22:26 Tana wa itǝ nyimi ba nyimi o ying ne. Mara ondoogong ba nyimi o ying a wa itǝ na ondobaate, ondoogong a nyimi o ying wa itǝ na ozara.
LUK 22:27 Mana kala o gongnga, ate akwilǝ ka a casa wai epaolya na, ozara oka wa arsezea? Ate akwilǝ oka casa wai epaolya tazane? A mi naana ba nyimi o ying na ozara o arsaza epaolya.
LUK 22:28 Yingnga andaaka e itǝ ka mi a nyimi o kona o zitǝ ong.
LUK 22:29 Nangka ate ang wa nyang legoone le togomo, nyimia ma nya ying,
LUK 22:30 adorana e lye e kang sa ara o lya epaolya a nyimi togomo tong kanza e cikǝ a tora te cikǝ togomo, e eze togomo ba za tokora betuuru ka e leere maYahuda.
LUK 22:31 “Biturusu, Biturusu, ogomo o bere o buru wa gere kedeya o ying a pate, wayo zeera ying nangka a zeere ma'ena ma o alkama, adorana a lope ying atoma ka e itǝ na masuni.
LUK 22:32 Ma bosa Ashili aza o Biturusu, nangka o kabare Ashili au wa to sawa ne. Malo oka ba kurǝ a mi, o kankama o dangare o ying ka neema ne kuri ara Ashili.”
LUK 22:33 Na Biturusu kabare na, “Ateokora, ma tera o bena eyang ale ka bo ara o tesa aromo kanza ka ara o gbwǝ ka bo.”
LUK 22:34 Na Yeso bekaana, “Ang belo, Biturusu, zongka o runǝ wa sene o ngmeengme, oyo sanggang ka taaro na ota rosanne.”
LUK 22:35 Na Yeso pirkǝ atoma kai na, “A were aka ma tong ying zora emate, zora epaolya, zora tekakau, e dera e yapa na?” Nane bekaana, “Teta te dera ne.”
LUK 22:36 Naka bekaa ne na, “Nannamena a were na a sara, eeya ka emate, ka epaolya e jeke ka e onte, kanza ondooka wata ka o sagali ne, a wa lishi o dibi wai kawa embe oyende ne.
LUK 22:37 Eyang bele o ying, angmǝ Ashili aka ondo o beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili Ishaya wa wele a bena, ‘A gwaara kai ka ana madinǝ,’ wa itǝ o bena, waya pena ba za ong. Nyimia, epa eka a wele ba za ong eya za o penze.”
LUK 22:38 Na atoma kai ne bekaa kai na, “Laka, Ateokora, masagali ma leere maana.” Na Yeso kabare na, “Maa bare.”
LUK 22:39 Yeso ka ale aza oyara Zaitun nangka ka mena ezazaa me, na atoma kai ale ka kai.
LUK 22:40 Nangka ka dukǝ rame, aka bekaa ne na, “Beyana angmǝ ka Ashili tana e rizi a nyimi o kedeya ogomo o bere o buru ne.”
LUK 22:41 Naka arnang ka ne na o ewa o wera lecale, naka girwǝ aka beya angmǝ ka Ashili.
LUK 22:42 Aka bekaana, “Ate, ba kabare o arang ka o zitǝ ona a deya ba za ong. Pate ka nyimi tana o tare ka o yeme ong ne, o yeme o waya aya tare me.”
LUK 22:43 Na otoma Ashili o zaa shili wa deya kai na wa kankama kai adorana ka cǝ legoone.
LUK 22:44 Aka ya aza o zitǝ, naka wale legoone lo beya ngmǝ ka Ashili ne, na malane susi a lepung le kai a ma tenkeze a deze na ma nyau.
LUK 22:45 Nangka Yeso ka ere ara o beya ngmǝ ka Ashili, naka kuri araaka atoma kai ne zene, aka mana ne ane umǝ ka o caro anyong cak, aza o bena ne zenga.
LUK 22:46 Naka bekaa ne na, “Eyaka eya malau? Era na ka e beye angmǝ ka Ashili adorana tana e rizi a nyimi o kedeya ogomo bere o buru ne.”
LUK 22:47 Kaya nyimi o beya ngmǝ naname na leguki le aromo deya rame, a oromo o mea a beya wai na Yahuda, ondooka waya nyimi atoma a kai betuuru ka leere, wa kalea ne a izi. Nawa paka ting Yeso adorana wa gwara ongmǝ ka kai o wore o yeme,
LUK 22:48 na Yeso pirkǝ wai na, “Yahuda, o beya o ko ka ongmǝ wa itǝ orona o nya Kena ka oromo na?”
LUK 22:49 Nangka atoma a Yeso ne laka epa eka eya ale, nane bekaana, “Ateokora, te kweze ka masagali ma ro na?”
LUK 22:50 Na ondo one wa kpweene oto ozara ondo magame ma Ashili bedake na wa core.
LUK 22:51 Na Yeso bekaa ne na, “Kana ekang ya nanna ne.” Naka meke oto oromo me aka womza wai.
LUK 22:52 Na Yeso bekaa ana o baala ngmǝ Ashili a were a Mosa, ka ana o endaza akwilǝ Ashili, ka anateandasau, amea ne deya kazo kai, “E surǝ ka masagali, ka se benda ba meke ong na okǝri o womza aromo na?
LUK 22:53 Maye ka ying koonang lengme ba nyimi akwilǝ a Ashili, na eta mekeng ne. Nannamena a were a yingnga. Ka maring ya aza togomo.”
LUK 22:54 Nane meke Yeso ane ale ka kai ba akwilǝ ogomo magame ma Ashili. Na Biturusu tarezene a macangcang.
LUK 22:55 Nangka ne gwaara ola atatara ara o beya angmǝ me a pate aane cikǝ ara yende, na Biturusu cikǝ a wa kondo ola kaane.
LUK 22:56 Na kazara kagala ka yende a nyimi a agala ka neya eza ogole akwilǝ me ka laka Biturusu a cikǝ ating ola me, naka kare wai a yizi aka bekaana, “Ondo ona waye legwa ka Yeso.”
LUK 22:57 Na Biturusu sanggang kai, a wa bekaana, “Kandaye, anta rosa kai ne.”
LUK 22:58 Malo nyimi, a ondo wa kang deya na wa laka Biturusu na wa rose wai, a wa bekaana, “Bo ma oya nyimi one.” Na Biturusu kabare na, “Oromo, mi anta nyimi one ne.”
LUK 22:59 Malo o rabo a baate, na ondo kang bekaana, “Masanggo ta rene ne, oromo ona waye ka kai, wai oromo o makeke Galili waye.”
LUK 22:60 Na Biturusu kabare na, “Oromo, anta rosa epa eka oya beya me ne.” Waya aza o mara o beka nyimi naname na urunǝ wa sene.
LUK 22:61 Na Ateokora ringgarnu naka laka Biturusu. A were name na Biturusu wa rintǝ epa eka Ateokora bekaa wai o bena, “Zongka o runǝ wa sene o ngmeengme, oyo sanggang ka taaro.”
LUK 22:62 Nawa suri o yanga na wa ruuzi a jǝng aza epa eka wa ya.
LUK 22:63 Ana o enda Yeso ne zeele kai, ane ole kai.
LUK 22:64 Nane pate a yizi kai, ane pirkǝ kai na, “Bele ro ondooka wa ceeto.”
LUK 22:65 Nane beye kai angmǝ buru a cak o zeela kai.
LUK 22:66 Ka o sana ra, na andaano maYahuda, neya, anateandasau, ka ana magame ma Ashili ma moole, ka ana o baala ngmǝ aka Ashili a nya Mosa nane gwarnang, ane ale ka Yeso ara o gwara one.
LUK 22:67 Nane bekaa kai na, “Boa Ondooka Ashili a zake na?” Naka kabare ka o bena, “Ma bele ying na, mia Ondooka Ashili a zake eto kabare ne,
LUK 22:68 kanza ma pirǝ ying na, ‘Mia mana?’ Eto kabareng ne.
LUK 22:69 A nanname a ale a izi, Kena ka Oromo kayo cikǝ o ara o re Ashili ondo legoone.”
LUK 22:70 Pate one nane bekaana, “Nyimi waaza, boa Kena ka Ashili na?” Naka kabare ne na, “Epa eka e beka nyimi waze.”
LUK 22:71 Nane bekaana, “Kai ka beka ka ongmǝ o kai, eya teya gera me kanza.”
LUK 23:1 Pate aromo kane gwarnang nane ere aane ale ka Yeso a begeshe be Ogomo Bilatus.
LUK 23:2 Nane bore o anza kai angmǝ na, “Te mana karomo kaana aka wilǝrǝzǝ aromo aro, aka beya ne na tana ne nya Ogomo ogong o Roma Kaisar emate makeke ne kanza aka beya okpwe kai na, kaya Ondooka Ashili a zake na ogomo.”
LUK 23:3 Na Ogomo Bilatus pirkǝ Yeso na, “Boa ogomo maYahuda na?” Na Yeso kabare na, “Ba bekaa kap.”
LUK 23:4 Na Ogomo Bilatus wa bele ana magame ma Ashili ma moole ka leguki le aromo na, “Mi anta ma cǝ epa e buru eka eyang meke me aza karomo kaana ne.”
LUK 23:5 Nane nyane epa eka wa bekaa ne lya izi ko beyana, “O baala kai wa ara anyong aromo a nyimi makeke maYahuda. Ka bore apeng Galili, naka deya ara kaana.”
LUK 23:6 Ka o kona nyimi, na Ogomo Bilatus pirkǝ na kai karomo ka makeke ma Galili kai na.
LUK 23:7 Nangka wa rose o bena Yeso ka suri a araaka Ogomo Hiridus waya togomo ne, na wa turki ne ara a Ogomo Hiridus me, a were name wai Ogomo Hiridus waya apeng Urushalima.
LUK 23:8 Nangka Ogomo Hiridus wa laka Yeso, na wa kone o leba a cak, o bena wa rabo ka o yeme o laka Yeso me, wa koneze oroka o bekaana, ka ezeze epa eka e kala begeshe ba aromo, na wa ya yeme o laka ebelo e.
LUK 23:9 Na Ogomo Hiridus pirkǝ Yeso aza angmǝ cak, na Yeso kata kabare ka eyapa ne.
LUK 23:10 Ana magame ma Ashili ma moole ka ana o baala angmǝ aka Ashili a nya Mosa nane itǝ arame aane beya ngmǝ ka o caro anyong aza Yeso ka o beyana, ka eza mapa ma buru.
LUK 23:11 Na ana Ogomo Hiridus ka ana o tesa geza a moole a wai, ne zeele kai kanza ane beye kai angmǝ a buru. Nane amba kai o dibi o togomo ane kuriyǝ kai ara Ogomo Bilatus.
LUK 23:12 A lengme lennamea Ogomo Bilatus ka Ogomo Hiridus ne itǝ ejaa, o bora neta ne ciisǝ a cammo a tokpwe tone ne.
LUK 23:13 Na Ogomo Bilatus rare andaano maYahuda, neya, ana magame ma Ashili ma moole, ka anate andaasau ka o dangare aromo a pate,
LUK 23:14 na wa bekaa ne na, “E deya ka karomo kaana aza o bena e beeze na ka wilǝrǝzǝ aromo kane nare o cikǝ o cammo. Ma pirǝ kai a begeshe be ying adorana ang cǝ o dera gaashe a kai, nanta ma cǝ epa e buru eka ma era ang meke aza kai ne.
LUK 23:15 Ogomo Hiridus ma wata wa cǝ epa e buru aza kai ne, waya wa ote na wa turki kai ara ong, karomo kaana kata ka ya eyapa o bare ka wong kai ne.
LUK 23:16 Aza nyimi, eyang ote ka ola kai ang pere kai.”
LUK 23:17 A Ogomo Bilatus waye ka o pere oromo yende ka a pate, a were o gwarnang o rintǝ o dera o wonga ayana o bora maYahuda a Masar omea ne mena ka o bosaza me.
LUK 23:18 Na aromo me ka le ngmelo le yende, beke a jǝng na, “Ale na ka karomo kaana ka e wong kai, a pere ro Barabas.”
LUK 23:19 A Barabas a pate wai ara ana o eza epa e buru aza o bekaana wa gereze bete a nyimi apengme, kanza azaa o wonga oromo.
LUK 23:20 Ogomo Bilatus waya yeme o perea Yeso, na wa kang bosa ne.
LUK 23:21 Nane lya izi ka o arsaza a ngmelo na, “A wong kai azaa uti o gendare. A wong kai azaa uti o gendare.”
LUK 23:22 Ka taaro naname ka Ogomo Bilatus beke angmǝ aane na, “Eya e? Karomo kaana kaya eya e buru? Me anta ma cǝ epa e buru ba kai ka e bare o wongnga kai ne. Eyang ote ka ole kai ang pere kai.”
LUK 23:23 Na aromo me ne ara lengmelo ajǝng o bena soona a wong kai aza uti o gendare.
LUK 23:24 Na Ogomo Bilatus kabare ka epa eka neya yeme me.
LUK 23:25 Nawa pere oromo oka a pate a nyimi akwilǝ ana o eza epa e buru, kawa gereze bete a nyimi apeng a wa kang wongnga ondo, waiya ne bose na a pere wai, a wa nya Yeso nangka neya yeme me kane wong kai.
LUK 23:26 Nangka ana o tesa geza a moole neya ale ka Yeso, nane gwarnang ka Siman oromo o Siyarin a waya lyǝ apeng, nane meke wai ane ana wai uti o gendara aromo, a wa tare Yeso a dimǝ.
LUK 23:27 A aromo a cake tare kai, ka andaye yende kane kone egonegone ane kang ruuzi aza o ziyǝ ka Yeso ka ya kona me.
LUK 23:28 Na Yeso ringgarnu naka bekaa ne na, “Andaye o Urushalima, tana e ruuzi aza ong ne, ruuzi na aza tokpwe to ying ka ayana aying.
LUK 23:29 A were aya deya amea eyo bekaana, ‘Ondo kona o leba andaye amea neta ne tukǝ ngmenga ne, a bangi amea a ta ngmengzaza ne kanza a maane mame a ta a tukǝ o asaka mai ne.’
LUK 23:30 A were name “ ‘Neyo beka a mayara na, “Oko na aza aro.” A ma'owa na, “Pate ro.” ’ ”
LUK 23:31 Aka beke angmǝ a gerpo na, “Aromo ne eza mapa maana a were aka uti tata o nyaza, wayo itǝ nannia uti me wa waka?”
LUK 23:32 Aromo leere, ana o eza epa e buru a ale ka ne legwa ka Yeso adorana a wong ne.
LUK 23:33 Nangka ne dukǝ araaka beya ai na, “Ara macako ma okpwe” arakaname a gendare Yeso uti ne. Ka ana o eza epa e buru name, ondo o ara ore, a ondo o ara o guri.
LUK 23:34 Na Yeso bekaana, “Ate, kwizǝ epa e buru ana o nyana ong, o bena neta rosa na mana mi ne.” Ane eke madibi ma kai a tera one nane laka mana waya jeka.
LUK 23:35 Aromo ne itǝ ane gonte, anda gong ane nane zeele kai, ane beya na, “Ka boza na ondo, aka boze okpwe kai ka ya kaaya ondo boza oka Ashili a zake.”
LUK 23:36 Ana o tesa a geza a moole ne de nane zeele kai. Ane niyi kai manyi ma marara ma yana inabi,
LUK 23:37 ane beya kai na, “Boa baya ogomo maYahuda, boza okpwe o.”
LUK 23:38 Aza ka okpwe kai a wele na, “KANDO KAANA KAYA OGOMO MAYAHUDA.”
LUK 23:39 Ondo a nyimi ana o eza epa e buru me ka a gendare ne ka Yeso na wa zeele kai, a wa bekaana, “Boa baya Ondooka Ashili a zake, boza okpwe o ka ro.”
LUK 23:40 A ondo eza epa e buru o leere me wa zurki a wai na, “O kone boome ba Ashili sang, bo ka a gendare uti ona ka kai?
LUK 23:41 Ro teya eesa o poba oka wa gwara ka ro, kai ka ta ka ya epa e buru ne.”
LUK 23:42 A wa bekaana, “Yeso rintǝng a were aka ba lyǝ a nyimi togomo to.”
LUK 23:43 Na Yeso kabare wai na, “Eyang bele o maganggang, o ngmeengme na oyo cikǝ ka mi ara a lebo ang aza shili.”
LUK 23:44 A tera letereme na ye maring a kuruwǝ a makeke mame, nama dukǝ o gendarono ongme,
LUK 23:45 na ongme wata nya masanto ne. Na epa o wobe ara o kala be sangsang akwilǝ Ashili wa daro a tera.
LUK 23:46 Na Yeso ka ara lengmelo a jǝng naka bekaana, “Ate, ma nyau ebeene eng a nyimi taara to.” Ka o bekaa nyimi, aka windi ebeene kai o mare a ka gbwi.
LUK 23:47 Nangka ondo tesa a geza a moole o gong a Roma wa laka epa eka ka ya, na wa saba Ashili a wa bekaana, “Dongdong karomo kaana kando ka o dera madinǝ kai.”
LUK 23:48 Na aromo aka neya gonta epa eka aya eza me arame, nane kuri akwilǝ ka o ola begeshe be ne a nyimi o kona o buru.
LUK 23:49 Pate aromo aka ne rose Yeso ka andaye amea ne tare kai a sura a makeke ma Galili, nane itǝ a macangcang ane gonte epa eka eya ale.
LUK 23:50 Ondo wa zene ka a beya wai na Yusupu, ka waye a nyimi andaano maYahuda, oromo me waye ka edang, a wa kone boome ba Ashili,
LUK 23:51 wata wa kabare ka epa eka andaano maYahuda ne eze ne. Wa de a wa suri a makeke ma Yahudiya apeng a Arimatiya a waya za o enda togomo to Ashili.
LUK 23:52 Nawa ale ba Ogomo Bilatus na wa bose wai na wa nya wai lepung le Yeso.
LUK 23:53 Nawa jipǝrǝ lepung le kai, a wa pate le ka betu a wa ote le ocau oka a coo o cale omea a ta a tukǝ o eza matasokong a wai ne.
LUK 23:54 Lengme leme lo babarono adorana a lyǝ a lengme lo teeseke ka o bosa Ashili maYahuda.
LUK 23:55 Andaye amea ne tare Yeso a surǝ a makeke ma Galili, nane ale ka Yusupu adorana ne laka araaka o cau me wa zene ka nangka a eke lepung le Yeso leme.
LUK 23:56 Nane suri akwilǝ, ane babare manao ma o waze o lebo. A lengme lo teseke nane teseke, nane teseke nangka angmǝ aka Ashili a nya Mosa a bekaana a eze.
LUK 24:1 A lelere aping o lengme le o bora, na andaye me ale ocau me ka magogoro ma owaze o lebo kane babare wai.
LUK 24:2 Nane mana a kinkǝri ocale ome a waya bengmǝ bo ocau me,
LUK 24:3 Nangka ne lyǝ a nyimi me, nane ta mana lepung le Yeso Ateokora ne.
LUK 24:4 Nangka neya madoola aza nyimi, a saseya na andaleme leere suri ating one, aane amba madibi ma o wonza a yizi.
LUK 24:5 A nyimi boome na andaye me tunggunǝ tokpwe tone a deze, na aromo me bekaa ne na, “Eyaka eya gera ondo ebeene a nyimi andaaka ne gbwizǝ?
LUK 24:6 Kata arakana ne, ka era. Rintǝna epa eka ka bekaa ying a makeke ma Galili,
LUK 24:7 ‘O sara ta zene ne a yo nya Kena ka Oromo a taara te aromo madinǝ kane wong kai azaa uti o gendare, a lengme lo taaro aka ere.’ ”
LUK 24:8 Na andaye me ne rintǝ angmǝ Yeso.
LUK 24:9 Nangka ne kuri aane suri ocau me, nane bekaa pate a atoma a Yeso betuuru ka o yende name, ko dangare aromo pate epa name.
LUK 24:10 Ana Mariya ka mea beya kai na Magadala, ka Yowana, a Mariya iini Yakubu, ka o dangare andaye, nane bele atoma kai epa eka eze.
LUK 24:11 Na atoma Yeso ta kabare epa eka andaye name ne bele ne ne, o bena angmǝ ane a ta orona ne.
LUK 24:12 Na Biturusu ere ba wup ka tesong a wa ale o ocau me. Ko dukǝ a wa tunggunu, a wa gokareke nyimi ocau me, na wa laka betu beeka a pate kai ne à á eke a sara yende. Na wa kuri akwilǝ ka madoola ma epa eka eya ale.
LUK 24:13 A lengme lenname, ana o tare a Yeso anda leere neya teweno to ale a kapeng ka yende ka beya kai na Imawus, kamea kata ewa maleo ne ka apeng Urushalima.
LUK 24:14 Neya dano aza epa eka eya ale.
LUK 24:15 Aneya za o dano naname, na Yeso okpwe kai paka ne aka lya izi ko yenga ka ne.
LUK 24:16 A Ashili a pate ne o rosa kai.
LUK 24:17 Naka bekaa ne na, “Eya dano aza eya a nyimi teweno tane?” Nane itǝ ara yende aane caro a mainu.
LUK 24:18 Na ondo a nyimi one ka a beya wai na Kiliyabas wa pirkǝ kai na, “Boa ayende ogeng a apeng Urushalima ko ta rosa epa eka eya ale a tomore teena ne na?”
LUK 24:19 Naka pirkǝ ne na, “Eya ya ale?” Na ne bekaana, “Epa eka e mana Yeso ko Nazarat. Kai kando ka o beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili, angmǝ akai aye ka legoone, a magole ma kai a begeshe ba Ashili ka aromo ma moole.
LUK 24:20 Kanza ana magame ma Ashili ma moole ka andaano a makeke ne core ngmǝ o wong kai aane gendare kai uti.
LUK 24:21 Ro tese eke a lenyong o bekaana, kaya kayo boza maYahuda ka pere ne. Eya kang tata, wa amara ka tomore te taaro naana aza epaana eya ale.
LUK 24:22 Bangka nyimi andaye yende a nyimi aro ne nya ro epa e mole, ne ale o ocau me a leleere aping,
LUK 24:23 pate ka nyimi neta ne mana lepung le kai ne. Nane de aane bekaa ro na ne laka Atoma Ashili o zaa shili nane bekaa ne na ebeene e kuri a kai kanza.
LUK 24:24 Na ana ondo a nyimi aro, ne ale o ocau me nane mana nangka andaye me ne beka, aane ta laka lepung le Yeso me ne.”
LUK 24:25 Na Yeso bekaa ne na, “Ying a rara, andaaka anyong ane ta rosaza eyapa a saseya ka ne kabare pate epa eka ana o beya a ngmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili ne wela angmǝ Ashili ne.
LUK 24:26 A samba o bekaame na Ondooka Ashili a zake kayo zitǝ a marona cake, malo nyimi aka lyǝ ara o kona o leba kai a rere.”
LUK 24:27 Naka baale ne pate epa eka Mosa ka ana o beya a ngmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili ne wele aza Ondooka Ashili a zake.
LUK 24:28 Nangka ne amara ka kapeng ka yende kamea neya ale ne, na Yeso kaye na kaya lya izi ka teweno.
LUK 24:29 Nane paka kai ane nyitǝmǝrǝnu a bose kai na, “Cikǝ ka ro, o lyǝlu waya, a were o taru ongme waya.” Naka tare ne aka cikǝ ka ne.
LUK 24:30 Nangka ne cikǝ aro lya epaolya, naka jeke o borode, aka kone o leba Ashili, aka poseze naka areseze ne.
LUK 24:31 A arakanamea a Ashili a pari ne o rosa kai, a malo nyimi naka wili ane.
LUK 24:32 Nane bekaa tokpwe tone na, “Eyaka anyong aro a ta a pǝrnu ka te rose ko kona o leba a were aka kaya beya ngmǝ ka ro orona, aka ya baala aro angmǝ Ashili ne?”
LUK 24:33 A were name ne ere nane kuri apeng a Urushalima nane mana atoma betuuru ko yende ko dangare ana o tare o kai,
LUK 24:34 a neya beya na, “Nyimi waze, Ateokora ka era aka wore okpwe kai ara Siman Biturusu.”
LUK 24:35 Na aromo leere name ne baale pate epa eka e mane ne orona, ka nangka ne rose kai a were aka ka arseze ne o borode.
LUK 24:36 A neya za o beya ngmǝ aza nyimi, na Yeso okpwe kai ka itǝ a tera one aka beye ne oko na, “O cikǝ a cammo tare ka ying.”
LUK 24:37 Na boome moke ne anyong ane kerkeze, aza o bekaana ne laka bebuu.
LUK 24:38 Naka bekaa ne na, “Eyaka eya kona boome nanna? Eyaka eta e kabare ka Ashili anyong aying ne?
LUK 24:39 Solekena manyuwǝ a taara ka tobona tong. Mea kai ko okpwe ong. Mekenna ka e kone, bebuu ta ya ka enama ka cako ne, nangka me ang zene.”
LUK 24:40 Nangka ka beke nyimi, aka wore ne taara te kai ka tobona tome.
LUK 24:41 Ne tata ko dera o kabare anyong o bekaana neya kona o leba ka epa e moole, naka pirkǝ ne na, “Eya ka epaolya ara kaana na?”
LUK 24:42 Nane nya kai bekwala bemea a eesa,
LUK 24:43 Naka embe be aka lye, aneya gonta kai.
LUK 24:44 Naka bekaa ne na, “Epa ena ma bekaa ying a were aka ma tata ka ying: Eyo pena nangka a wele aza ong a nyimi ngmǝ aka Ashili a nya Mosa, ka ana o beya angmǝ ka mawo ma Ashili, ka Seleera.”
LUK 24:45 Naka pari madoola mane, nane rose angmǝ Ashili ka a wele.
LUK 24:46 Kanza aka bekaa ne na, “Epa ena a wela, na Ondooka Ashili a zake kayo zitǝ ka wong kai aka ere a nyimi o ocau a lengme lo taaro,
LUK 24:47 kanza oroka o kurǝ a Ashili Ka o kwizǝ madinǝ waya a yo beya a nyimi leze le kai a pate lerambo le Ashili a bore apeng Urushalima.
LUK 24:48 Yingnga andaaka e laka ka eyo baala ana ondo.
LUK 24:49 Eyang tonga o ying ka epa eka Ate wa beka. Cikǝ na a nyimi apeng zongka ang nya ying legoone le obere o rere o suri aza shili.”
LUK 24:50 Naka sǝǝrǝ ne a malo peng Urushalima, a kulu kapeng ka Betanya, aramea ka ara taara to kai aza shili aka kare ne o kona o leba.
LUK 24:51 Malo o kare one o leba, naka arnang ka ne, a ana kai a ale azaa shili.
LUK 24:52 Nane tunggunu ane nya kai togomo to kai, ane kuri apeng Urushalima ko kona o leba o cake.
LUK 24:53 Nane cikǝ akwilǝ Ashili koonang lengme, ane saba Ai.
